here is tha femlie line o jesus christ tha sinn o davit an o abraham abraham wus tha faither o isaac isaac tha faither o jacob jacob tha faither o judah an his brithers an judah wus tha faither o perez an zerah an thair mither wus tamar perez wus tha faither o hezron hezron tha faither o ram ram wus tha faither o amminadab amminadab tha faither o nahshon an nahshon tha faither o salmon salmon wus tha faither o boaz an tha mither o boaz wus rahab boaz wus tha faither o obed an tha mither o obed wus ruth obed wus tha faither o jesse an jesse tha faither o king davit davit wus tha faither o solomon bi hir that wus yinst tha wife o uriah solomon wus tha faither o rehoboam rehoboam tha faither o abijah abijah tha faither o asa asa tha faither o jehoshaphat jehoshaphat tha faither o jehoram jehoram tha faither o uzziah uzziah wus tha faither o jotham jotham tha faither o ahaz ahaz tha faither o hezekiah hezekiah wus tha faither o manasseh manasseh tha faither o amon an amon tha faither o josiah josiah wus tha faither o jeconiah an his brithers that wus roon aboot tha time the wur cairriet aff tae babylon an efter the wur cairriet awa tae babylon jeconiah becum tha faither o shealtiel an shealtiel tha faither o zerubbabel zerubbabel wus tha faither o abiud abiud tha faither o eliakim an eliakim tha faither o azor azor wus tha faither o zadok zadok tha faither o akim an akim tha faither o eliud eliud wus tha faither o eleazar eleazar tha faither o matthan an matthan tha faither o jacob an jacob wus tha faither o joseph an joseph wus merriet tae mary an mary wus tha mither o jesus tha yin caad christ that made fowerteen generations in aa frae abraham tae davit fowerteen frae davit til the wur cairriet awa tae babylon an anither fowerteen frae that tae tha cumin o christ an this is hoo tha birth o jesus christ cum aboot his mither mary wus promist tae joseph but afore the cum thegither she fun oot she wus wi a wean an it wus bi tha halie spirit noo joseph hir husban wus a dacent man an he didnae want hir tae be affrontit sae he thocht tae senn hir awa on tha quait he wus thinkin aboot aa this whan lo an behoul an angel o tha loard appeart tae him in a draim an saed joseph sinn o davit dinnae be feart tae tak mary fer yer wife fer tha wean shes cairryin is o tha halie spirit she wull hae a sinn an ye ir tae gie him tha name jesus fer he wull save his ain fowk frae thair wrangdaeins noo aa this wus daen tae bring aboot whut tha loard haed saed throu tha proaphit a virgin wull cairrie a wean a sinn an whan hes boarn hell be caad immanuel mainin god is wi iz whaniver joseph waakent up he daen whut tha angel o tha loard haed toul him tae dae an he tuk mary hame fer tae be his wife but he didnae sleep wi hir til efter tha wean wus boarn an he caad him bi tha name jesus efter jesus wus boarn in bethlehem in judea durin tha time that herod wus king spaemen frae tha east cum tae jerusalem an the axt whar is tha yin that haes bin boarn king o tha jews fer we hae saen his starn in tha east an hae cum fer tae woarship him whaniver king herod heerd this he wus baadlie put aboot an aa jerusalem wi him sae he brocht thegither aa tha jewish fowks heid preeshts an maisters o tha laa an he axt thaim whar tha christ wus tae be boarn in bethlehem o judea the saed fer this is whut tha proaphit writ but you bethlehem in tha lan o judah ye ir bi nae mains tha laist amang tha rulers o judah fer oot o you wull cum a ruler that wull herd ma fowk israel then herod caad tha wise men thegither on tha quait an he fun oot frae thaim whan it wus that tha starn haed cum intae sicht he sent thaim tae bethlehem an he toul thaim luk in iverie airt fer tha wean as shuin as yis fin him wud ye bring me wurd sae as a can gae an woarship him as weel efter the haed heerd whut tha king haed tae say the set aff on thair wye an lo an behoul tha starn the haed saen in tha east went aheid o thaim til it stapt richt ower tha place whar tha wean wus whaniver the saa tha starn the wur hairt gled the cum intae tha hoose the saen tha wee wean wi his mither mary an the bood doon an wurshipt him then the apent thair kists an the set afore him thair gifts o gowld an frankincense an myrrh an bein warnt in a draim no tae gae bak tae herod the tuk anither road bak hame an efter the went awa an angel o tha loard appeart tae joseph in a draim git up he toul him tak aff tae egypt wi tha wean an his mither bide thair til a gie ye tha wurd fer herod is aboot tae hunt oot tha wean fer tae dae awa wi him sae up joseph got he tuk tha wean an his mither wi him in tha middle o tha nicht an he set aff fer egypt he stapt thair til herod deed an aa this brocht aboot whut tha loard haed saed throu tha proaphit oot o egypt a hae caad ma sinn whaniver herod fun oot hed bin haad he wus rippin an he gien oarders fer tae kill aa tha weechils in bethlehem an roon aboot thaim at wus twa yeir oul an unner takkin intae accoont tha time he haed bin telt bi tha spaemen then whut tha proaphit jeremiah saed aforehan wud happen cum aboot a voice wus heerd in ramah greetin an lamentin it wus rachel greetin fer hir weans an she niver devalved acause hir weans wus nae langr wi hir but whaniver herod deed lo an behoul an angel o tha loard appeart in a draim tae joseph in egypt an he saed git up tak tha wean an his mither awa tae tha lan o israel fer tha yins that wus gaun tae kill tha wean is deid sae joseph upt an tuk tha wean an his mither an he went intae tha lan o israel but whan he heerd that archelaus wus tha king o judea in tha ruim o his faither herod he wus feart tae gae thair bein warnt in a draim he pued bak tae tha district o galilee an he went an settelt doon in a toon caad nazareth an sae it cum tae pass whut wus saed bi tha proaphits he wull be caad a nazarene in thaim days jhone tha baptiser cum praichin in tha wiles o judea an sayin turn awa frae yer sins fer tha kingdom o heiven is nearhan jhone is tha yin tha proaphit isaiah spauk aboot tellin thairs a voice cryin oot in tha wiles mak tha wye readie fer tha loard mak his pads strecht fer him jhones claes wus made o kemels hair an he haed a leather belt roon his middle an he leeved bi aitin gresshoppers an wile honey croods gaed oot tae him frae jerusalem alang wi aa tha fowk frae judea an tha hale district o tha river joardan an thaim at confesst thair sins wur baptised bi him in tha joardan river but whan he saa a wheen o pharisees an sadducees cumin tae whar he wus baptisin he saed tae thaim ye sleekit shooer o vipers wha telt ye tae rin frae tha wrath o god thats cumin ye maun show bi tha wye ye leeve that ye hae turnt awa frae yer sins an dinnae be thinkin tae yersels we hae abraham fer oor faither an hae daen wi that a tell ye that oot o thon stanes god can mak weans fer abraham gods hatchit is noo at tha ruit o tha trees an thaim that dinnae gie guid fruit wull be fellt an pitcht intae tha fire am baptisin yis wi watter fer tae show yis hae repentit but thairs yin cumin efter me that is michtier ner me am no fit tae cairrie his buits he wull baptise ye wi tha halie spirit an wi fire his winnowin fork is in his han an he wull redd up his thrashinflure getherin his wheat intae his barn an burnin tha caff wi a fire ye cannae pit oot then jesus cum frae galilee tae tha joardan fer tae be baptised bi jhone but jhone tried tae pit him aff sayin its me that needs tae be baptised bi you an you ir cumin tae me jesus saed jist dae this fer noo fer this is tha richt thing fer iz tae dae tae cairrie oot tha wull o god sae jhone gien in tha minit jesus wus baptised he ris up oot o tha watter an jist wi that tha heivens apent an he saa tha spirit o god cumin doon laik a doo an lichtin on him an a voice cum frae heiven sayin this is ma sinn ma hairts delicht am weel plaised wi him then jesus wus taen bi tha spirit intae tha wulderness fer tae be tempit bi tha deil efter gaun wioot mait fer fowertie days an fowertie nichts he wus gye hungrie tha tempter cum tae him an saed if ye ir tha sinn o god tell thaim thair stanes tae turn intae breid jesus saed bak tae him it is writ man cannae leeve bi breid alane but bi iverie wurd at cums frae tha mooth o god then tha deil tuk him tae tha halie citie an stud him up on tha verie tap o tha hoose o god if ye ir tha sinn o god saed he throw yersel doon fer tha guid buik says he wull tell his angels tae luk efter ye an wi thair hans the wull haud ye up fer fear ye dunt yer fit agin a stane jesus saed bak tae him its in tha buik forbye ye ir no tae temp tha loard yer god an nixt thing tha deil tuk him tae a big heich muntin an lut him see aa tha kingdoms o tha warl in aa thair glorie a wull gie ye aa this he saed if yell jist boo doon an woarship me jesus saed tae him awa or that satan fer it is writ doon ye ir tae woarship tha loard yer god an tae sarve naebodie but him then tha deil lut him be an angels cum an lukt efter him noo whan jesus heerd tha wittins that jhone haed bin put in jail he went bak intae galilee an efter leain nazareth he gaed tae capernaum an he stapt thair capernaum wus bi tha loch in tha district o zebulun an naphtali tae bring aboot whut wus foretoul bi tha proaphit isaiah in tha lan o zebulun an tha lan o naphtali on tha wye tae tha loch on tha ither side o tha joardan in galilee whar tha gentiles leeve tha fowk that sut in tha dairk hae saa a bricht licht an on tha yins leevin in tha lan o tha shedda o deith tha licht haes cum in frae then on jesus begun tae praich turn awa frae yer sins fer tha kingdom o heiven haes cum nearhan ye yin day whan jesus wus waakin alang tha loch shore o galilee he saa twa brithers simon caad peter an his brither andra the wur castin a neyt intae tha watter fer the wrocht at tha fishin cum an follae me jesus saed an a wull mak ye fishers o men an richt awa the layed doon thair neyts an the follaed efter him he gan on frae thair an saen twa ither brithers jeames tha sinn o zebedee an his brither jhone the wur in a boat wi thair faither zebedee mennin thair neyts jesus caad thaim an richt awa the left tha boat an thair faither an the follaed him jesus trevelt aa roon galilee taichin in thair meetin hooses an praichin tha guid wittins o tha kingdom an curin iverie disaise an ailment amang tha fowk wurd aboot him spreed aa ower syria an the brocht tae him aa tha seeck fowk wi aa kines o disaises thaim that wus tormentit or bothert wi ill spirits or tuk fits or fowk that wus paralysed an he made thaim better big croods follaed him frae galilee an tha ten toons an jerusalem an judea an tha district on tha ither side o tha river joardan noo whaniver he saa tha croods he gaed up tha muntin an sut doon his follaers gethert roon him an he stairtit tae taich thaim sayin blisst ir tha puir in spirit fer thairs is tha kingdom o heiven blisst ir tha yins that greet fer the wull be comfortit blisst ir tha yins that ir gentle fer the wull inherit tha irth blisst ir tha yins that hae a hungr an a druith fer whuts richt fer the wull get thair fill blisst ir tha yins that ir merciefu fer the wull be showed mercie blisst ir tha pure in hairt fer the wull see god blisst ir tha yins that warks fer peace fer the wull be caad sinns o god blisst ir tha yins thats traitit ill fer daein whuts richt fer thairs is tha kingdom o heiven blisst ir you whan fowks baadmooth ye an trait ye ill an miscaa ye on accoont o me be joyfu an gled acause yis hae a pooerfu reward waitin fer ye in heiven fer the illtraitit tha proaphits that wus thair afore ye in jist tha same wye yous ir tha saut o tha irth but if tha saut loasses its taste hoo can it git bak its tang it is nae langr onie use but fer tae be throwed oot an thrampt unner fit yous ir tha licht o tha warl a toon bigged on a hill cannae be hid ye dinnae licht a lamp an pit it unner a boul na ye pit it on a stan whar it gies licht tae tha hale hoose in tha same wye let yer licht shine afore iveriebodie sae as the wull see yer guid warks an gie glorie tae yer faither in heiven dinnae be thinkin that a hae cum fer tae dae awa wi tha laa or tha proaphits a hinnae cum fer tae dae awa wi thaim but fer tae fulfill thaim a tell ye tha truith afore heiven an irth passes awa no tha weeest letter ner even tha weeest stroke o a pen wull pass awa frae tha laa afore iveriethin god wants fer it is brocht aboot oniebodie that breks yin o these commauns even tha laist o thaim an lairns ithers tae dae tha same wull be laist thocht o in tha kingdom o heiven but whaiver keeps these commauns an lairns ithers tae dae thaim wull be gye weel thocht o in tha kingdom o heiven fer am tellin yis this less yer guidness gaes beyont that o tha pharisees an tha maisters o tha laa yisll no git intae tha kingdom o heiven thats fer shair yis hae heerd that it wus saed tae fowk lang syne dinnae commit murder an oniebodie that murders wull be judged fer it but am tellin ye oniebodie thats even angrie wi his brither wioot onie caas is gaun tae be judged fer it agane oniebodie that says tae his brither ye eejit ye that bodie wull hae tha heich cooncil tae answer tae an oniebodie that says ye oul fool wull be rinnin tha risk o hell fire sae if ye ir bringin yer offerin tae tha althar an ye mine that yer brither haes ocht agin ye jist lea it doon fornent tha althar awa an mak it up wi yer brither furst then cum bak an gie yer offerin in soart things oot quick wi yer enemie that is takkin ye tae coort dae it while ye ir still wi him on tha wye thair or hell mebbe han ye ower tae tha judge an tha judge cud han ye ower tae tha offysher an ye cud be cloddit intae jail a tell ye tha truith yell no git oot o thair afore yer last pennies pyed yis hae heerd that it wus saed dinnae commit adulterie but am tellin yis that oniebodie that even luks at a wumman wi lust haes aareadie commitit adulterie wi hir in his hairt if yer richt ee maks ye dae wrang hoke it oot an clod it awa its faur better fer ye tae loass tha yin pairt o yer bodie ner fer yer hale bodie tae be throwed intae hell an if yer richt han maks ye dae wrang cut it aff an clod it awa its faur better fer ye tae loass tha yin pairt o yer bodie ner fer yer hale bodie tae gang intae hell its bin saed in tha scriptures as weel oniebodie that divorces his guidwife maun gie hir a notysh o divorce but am tellin ye that oniebodie that pits awa his wife fer ocht ither ner rinnin aff wi anither man he maks hir an adulteress an oniebodie that merries a divorced wumman commits adulterie as weel forbye ye ken that it wus saed tae tha fowk lang syne dinnae brek yer oath but keep tha oaths ye hae made tae tha loard am tellin ye but dinnae sweer ava ether bi heiven fer it is gods throne or bi tha irth fer it is his fitcreepie or bi jerusalem fer it is tha citie o tha michtie king an dinnae sweer bi yer heid fer ye cannae mak even yin o yer hairs white or blek jist let yer ay be ay an yer na na oniethin mair ner this cums frae tha wickit yin yis hae heerd that it wus saed an ee fer an ee an a tuith fer a tuith but a tell ye dinnae fecht agin a wickit bodie if summodie hits ye on tha richt cheek turn tha ither side til him forbye an if summodie wants tae sue ye an tak tha shirt aff yer bak let him hae yer tapcoat as weel if summodie gars ye tae gang yin mile gang twa mile wi him gie tae tha yin that axes ye fer ocht an dinnae turn yer bak on a bodie thats lukkin tha lenn o sumthin yis hae heerd that it wus saed love yer nighber an hait yer enemie but a tell ye love yer enemies an pray fer thaim that traits ye ill that ye micht be childer o yer faither in heiven he maks his sin tae rise on tha wickit as weel as on tha guid an he senns rain on thaim that daes whuts richt as weel as on tha yins that daesnae if ye jist love thaim at loves you whut reward wull ye get shair even tha tex men daes that an if ye onlie pass tha time o day wi yer ain yins whut ir ye daein mair ner ithers even pagans daes tha same dae the no but you maun be perfait jist as yer heivenlie faither is perfait dinnae mak a show afore fowk o onie guid yis dae fer yer faither in heiven wull gie yis nae reward fer that sae whan ye gie ocht tae tha needie dinnae soon tha trumpet tha wye tha hippycrates daes in tha meetin hooses an on tha streets fer tae be weel thocht o a tell ye tha truith the hae got aa tha reward their gaun tae get but whan ye gie ocht tae tha needie dinnae let yer left han ken whut yer richt han is daein sae that yer giein micht be on tha quait then yer faither that sees whut is daen on tha quait wull reward ye an whan yis pray dinnae be laik tha hippycrates fer the love tae stan an pray in tha meetin hooses an on tha street coarners fer aa tae see a tell ye tha truith the hae got aa their gaun tae get but whan you pray gang awa intae a ruim alane shut tha dure an pray tae yer faither in saicret then yer faither at sees whut is daen in saicret wull reward ye an whan ye pray dinnae keep rhymin on an on laik pagans fer they think tha mair the taak tha better the wull be heerd dinnae be laik thaim fer yer faither kens whut ye hae need o afore ye ax him sae this is hoo ye shud pray oor faither that bides abain halie be yer name micht yer kingdom cum shuin an yer wull be daen on irth jist tha wye it is abain gie iz theday eneuch breid tae dae iz an forgie iz oor debts jist as we hae forgien tha yins thats in debt tae us an dinnae road iz intae temptation but save iz frae tha wickit yin fer yours is tha kingdom tha pooer an tha glorie fer iver an iver amen fer if you forgie fowk whan the dae wrang agin ye then yer heivenlie faither wull forgie you as weel but if ye dinnae forgie fowk thair wrangdaeins yer faither wull no forgie you tha wrangs yous hae daen whan ye fast dinnae luk doon in tha mooth as tha hippycrates dae fer the mak thair faces luk miserable jist tae let fowk see ther fastin a tell ye tha truith this is aa tha reward ther gaun tae get but whan ye fast pit oiyle on yer heid an waash yer face sae fowk wull no notysh that ye ir fastin yer faither but wha ye cannae see wull notysh an tha yin that sees whut is daen in hidlins he wull gie ye yer reward dinnae hoord up fer yersels treysures on irth whar moths an roost desthroy an whar thiefs brek in an steal but hoord up fer yersels treysures in heiven whar nether moth ner roost can desthroy ner thiefs brek in an steal fer whut ye think tha maist o wull aye be in yer hairt yer ee is tha lamp o tha bodie if yer ee is guid yer hale bodie is fu o licht but if yer ee is baad yer hale bodie is fu o dairkness if then tha licht wiin ye is dairkness it maun be pitch blek naebodie can sarve twa maisters fer ether hell hait tha yin an love tha ither or hell stick bye tha yin an think naethin o tha ither ye cannae sarve baith god an gowld sae am tellin ye tak nae thocht fer yer life whut yell ait or whut yell drink ner yit aboot yer bodie whut claes yell pit on ye is life no mair impoartin ner mait an tha bodie mair impoartin ner claes luk at tha burds o tha air the dinnae sow ner reap ner hoord awa in barns an yit yer heivenlie faither feeds thaim ir yous no warth faur mair ner thaim ye cannae add a singl oor tae yer life bi worryin aboot it an why dae ye worrie aboot tha claes ye pit on ye luk hoo tha lilies o tha fiel growe they nether wark ner spin yit all tell ye this een solomon cudnae match thaim wi aa his fancie claes an if that is tha wye god pits claes on tha gress o tha fiel thats here theday an throwed intae tha fire themorra dae you dooters no unnerstan that hell luk efter you anaa sae dinnae fash yersels bi sayin whut wull we ait or whut wull we drink or whut wull we pit on iz fer thaim at daesnae know god rin efter aa these things but yer heivenlie faither kens aa ye hae need o seek oot his kingdom an his righteousness furst o aa an aa these ither things wull tak care o thairsels sae dinnae fash yersels aboot themorra fer themorra wull luk efter itsel iverie day haes eneuch bother o its ain dinnae judge ithers sae as yell no be judged yersels fer in tha same wye yis judge ithers yisll be judged that wye yersels an tha misure yis gie wull be tha misure yis get an why dae ye see tha skelf in yer brithers ee but ye dinnae see tha plenk in yer ain ee hoo can ye say tae yer brither let me tak tha skelf oot o yer ee whan luk aa tha time thair is a plenk in yer ain ee ye oul hippycrate ye pu tha plenk oot o yer ain ee furst an then yell be able tae see proper tae tak tha skelf oot o yer brithers ee dinnae gie whuts halie tae tha doags an dinnae scatter yer pearls afore pigs if ye dae the may thramp thaim unner thair feet an then turn an teer ye tae bits keep on axin an it wull be gien tae ye keep on lukkin an yell fin whut yer efter keep on rappin an tha dure wull be apent tae ye fer iveriebodie that axes wull get him that keeps on lukkin wull fin whut hes efter an tae him that keeps on rappin tha dure wull be apent whutch faither amang ye if his sinn axes him fer breid wull gie him a stane or if he axes him fer a fish wull he gie him a snake an sae if sinfu fowk laik yersels know hoo tae gie guid things tae yer weans hoo much mair wull yer faither in heiven gie guid things tae thaim that axes him sae in iveriethin dae tae ithers whut yis wud want thaim tae dae tae yersels fer this is whut tha laa an tha proaphits is aa aboot gae in bi tha nerra gate fer wide is tha gate an braid is tha road that leads tae destruction an monies a yin gaes that wye but nerra is tha gate an reuch tha rodden that leads tae life an thairs no monie that fins it watch oot fer fauss proaphits the cum tae ye lukkin laik hairmless sheep but on tha inside ther naethin but a paak o wolfs yell ken thaim bi thair fruit ay bi whut the dae daes fowk gether grapes frae a thoarn bush or figs frae thristles na in tha same wye iverie guid tree gies guid fruit but a baad tree gies ye baad fruit a guid tree cannae gie baad fruit an a baad tree cannae gie ye guid fruit iverie tree that daesnae gie guid fruit is cut doon an throwed intae tha fire its laik that wi tha fauss proaphits tae yell ken thaim bi whut the dae its no iverie yin that says tae me loard loard thatll git intae tha kingdom o heiven but its onlie him that daes tha wull o ma faither wha is in heiven monies a yinll say tae me on tha day o reckonin loard loard did we no proaphesy in yer name an in yer name did we no drive oot ill spirits an dae a hale lock o miracles then a wull tell thaim strecht a niver knowed ye awa frae me ye wrangdaers sae iverie yin that hears these wurds o mine an heeds thaim is laik a wise man that bigged his hoose on a roak tha rain cum doon tha watter ris an tha wuns got up an hut agin tha hoose yit it didnae faa acause it wus bigged on tha roak but iverie yin that hears these wurds o mine an daesnae heed thaim is laik a gormless man that bigged his hoose on san tha rain cum doon tha watter ris an tha wuns blattert an bate agin thon hoose o his tha hoose faad doon an whut a cresh thair wus whan jesus haed daen sayin these things tha croods wur aa thunnerstruck wi his taichin fer he taicht thaim laik a bodie wi thortie an no laik thair maisters o tha laa whaniver jesus cum doon frae tha braeside big croods follaed him an here cum up this man wi leprosie an he got doon on his knees afore him an saed loard if ye hae a mine tae ye can mak me clain an jesus put his han oot an toucht tha man am wullin he saed be clain an richt awa he wus cured o his leprosie then jesus saed tae him luk here mine ye dinnae tell oniebodie but gang awa an show yersel tae tha preesht gie an offerin fer yer cleansin as moses toul iz in tha laa fer a wutness tae yin an aa that yer weel agane whan jesus wus gaun intae capernaum a centurion cum tae him plaidin wi him an sayin loard ma sarvin man is lyin on his bed at hame hes no weel an cannae move ava hes sufferin sumthin tarrible jesus saed tae him weel am cumin tae mak him better tha centurion saed loard tha laiks o mes no fit tae hae ye cum unner ma ruif but jist say tha wurd an ma sarvin man wull be better agane fer a ken hoo tae tak oarders an a hae sodgers unner me as weel a tell yin tae gang an he gangs an anither yin tae cum an he cums a tell ma sarvin man tae dae this or that an he daes it whan jesus heerd this he wus stoondit an saed tae thaim that follaed him a tell ye tha truith a niver fun oniebodie wi sitch faith in aa israel a say tae ye that monie fowk wull cum frae tha east an tha wast an the wull tak thair place roon tha boord wi abraham isaac an jacob in tha kingdom o heiven but monie o tha yins tha kingdom wus got readie fer the wull be cast oot intae tha dairk whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth then jesus saed tae tha centurion gae it wull be daen fer ye tha wye ye believed it wud an his sarvint got better agane that verie minit noo whaniver jesus cum intae peters hoose he saen peters mitherinlaa lyin in bed wi a faivir he toucht hir han an tha faivir left hir an she got up an stairtit tae sarve an luk efter him an that evenin the brocht tae him a hale lock o fowk that wur bothert wi ill spirits an he driv oot tha spirits wi a wurd an cured aa that wus seeck this wus fer tae bring aboot whut wus spauk throu tha proaphit isaiah he tuk oor ailments on hissel an he cairriet oor disaises noo whan jesus saa tha thrang gethert roon him he toul his follaers tae gang ower tae tha ither side o tha loch then thair wus this maister o tha laa cum up an saed maister a wull follae ye nae metter whar yer gaun an jesus saed tae him foxes hae holes an burds hae nests but tha sinn o man haes naewhar he can caa hame anither o his follaers saed tae him loard let me gang an burie ma faither furst but jesus saed bak tae him follae me an let tha deid burie thair ain deid then he got intae tha boat his follaers got in efter him an awa the went wioot onie warnin a wile stoarm cum up on tha loch an tha waves waasht ower tha boat but jesus slep throu it his follaers cum an waakent him sayin loard save iz or well aa be droont hoo cum yis ir sae feart saed he hae yis nae faith ava then he stud up an chackt tha wun an tha waves an it wus aa peace an quaitness tha men wur dumfoonert an axt whut kine o a man is this tha verie wun an tha waves daes his biddin an whan he got tae tha ither side o tha loch tae tha lan whar tha gadarenes leeved thair wus these twa men cum oot frae tha graveyaird fer tae meet him the wur bothert wi ill spirits an that reuch naebodie cud get bye thaim whut is it ye ir efter wi us sinn o god the guldert hae ye cum here tae torment iz afore tha day o reckonin a bit awa frae thaim a big herd o pigs wus hokin fer food an tha ill spirits plaidit wi jesus gin ye ir gaun tae drive iz oot jist senn iz intae tha herd o pigs thonner he saed tae thaim awa wi ye sae the cum oot o tha men an gaed intae tha pigs an aa tha herd tuk aff doon tha hill heid furst intae tha loch an tha hale lock o thaim deed in tha watter tha yins lukkin efter tha pigs run aff the gaed intae tha toon an toul iveriebodie aa that haed tuk place an whut haed happent tae tha men bothert wi ill spirits then tha hale toon gaed oot tae meet jesus an whan the saen him the plaidit wi him tae lea thair pairt o tha kintrie jesus climmed intae a boat sailed ower tha ither side an cum tae his ain toon the brocht a paralysed man tae him lyin on a bed an whaniver jesus saa tha faith the haed he saed tae tha paralysed man tak hairt sinn yer sins is aa forgien at this some o tha maisters o tha laa saed amang thairsels thats naethin but blesphemie knowin whut the wur thinkin jesus saed hoo cum yis hae sitch wickit thochts in yer hairt is it aisier tae say yer sins is forgien ye or tae say get up an waak but jist sae as yell ken tha sinn o man haes tha pooer tae forgie sins here on irth he then saed tae tha paralysed man up ye get lift yer bed an gae hame an tha man stud up sae he did an he went awa hame whan tha thrang saen this the wur fillt wi wunnerment an the gien glorie tae god fer giein sitchana thortie tae a man whan jesus wus trevelin on frae thair he saa a tex man bi tha name o mattha sittin in his hut follae me he toul him an mattha ris up an follaed him a while later whan jesus wus at a denner at matthas hoose thair wus a hale lock o tex men an ither fowk o ill repute aitin alang wi him an his follaers whaniver tha pharisees saen this the axt his follaers whuts yer maister daein aitin wi thaim tex men an sinners on hearin this jesus saed it is no thaim thats weel needs a docter but thaim thats seeck but awa an lairn tha mainin o this scripture its mercie am efter am no efter secryfice fer a hinnae cum fer tae caa tha guid fowk tae repent a hae cum fer tae caa sinners an it wus then that jhones follaers cum up an axt him hoo is it that tha pharisees an us ir aye fastin but your follaers dinnae fast jesus saed bak tae thaim dae ye think tha waddin guests wud murn while tha bridegruim is still wi thaim thairll cum a day but whaniver tha bridegruim wull be tuk awa frae thaim an its then thell be fastin naebodie patches thair oul duds wi a bit o new claith fer tha patchll pu awa an mak it waur nether wud the poor new wine intae oul wineskins fer if the dae tha skins wull brust tha wine wull rin oot an tha wineskins wull be ruint na the poor new wine intae new wineskins an tha baith o thaim wull keep noo whaniver he wus sayin this a heidyin o tha meetin hoose cum an got doon on his knees afore him an saed ma wee dochter haes deed jist thair noo but cum an pit yer han on hir an shell cum bak tae life an jesus got up an gaed wi him as weel as his follaers an lo an behoul thair wus this wumman that wus bothert wi bleedin fer twal yeir she cum up behin him an toucht tha enn o his cloke fer saed she til hirsel if a can jist touch his cloke a wull be made weel agane jesus turnt roon an saen hir tak hairt dochter dear he saed yer faith haes made ye weel an tha wumman wus hailt that verie minit noo whan jesus cum tae tha hame o tha heidyin o tha meetin hoose he saa tha funeral fluters an aa tha hale thrang foofin an greetin an he saed awa er that tha wee lass is no deid shes jist sleepin but the begun tae lach at him efter tha crood wus put oot tha dure jesus gaed in an tuk tha wee lass bi tha han an she ris tae hir feet an this wus aa tha taak o that hale kintrieside as jesus gaed on frae thair twa blin men follaed him caain oot sinn o davit tak peetie on iz whaniver he went intae his hoose tha blin men cum in tae an he axt thaim dae yis believe a hae tha pooer fer tae dae whut yer wantin ay loard the saed we dae then he toucht thair een an saed itll be daen tae ye accoardin tae yer faith an thair sicht cum bak an the cud see jesus gien thaim a guid warnin an saed luk here dinnae you be tellin oniebodie aboot this but nae shuiner wur the oot than the stairtit tae spreed tha news aboot him aa roon tha hale kintrie an efter the left a man that wus bothert wi ill spirits an cudnae spake wus brocht tae jesus an jesus driv oot tha ill spirit sae tha man that wus dum cud noo spake tha crood o fowk wus dumfoonert an saed we niver saen tha laiks o this in israel afore but tha pharisees saed its tha deil tha heidyin o tha ill spirits that gies him tha pooer tae cast oot ill spirits an jesus trevelt throu aa tha toons an villages taichin in thair meetin hooses praichin tha guid news o tha kingdom an hailin iverie kine o disaise an ailment whaniver he saen tha croods his hairt went oot tae thaim acause the wur aa laik sheep wi nae shepherd troublet on thair lane wi nae road tae turn then he saed tae his follaers thairs a gran hairst waitin but thairs no monie warkers tae gether it in sae keep on axin tha loard o tha hairst tae senn oot mair warkers intae his hairvest fiel he caad his twal follaers thegither an he gien thaim tha pooer tae drive oot ill spirits an tae cure aa kines o disaises an ailments tha names o tha twal possels wus furst simon caad peter an his brither andra then jeames tha sinn o zebedee an his brither jhone philip an bartholomew tammas an mattha tha tex man jeames tha sinn o alphaeus an thaddaeus simon tha zealot an judas iscariot tha yin that bethrayed jesus an jesus sent oot tha twal o thaim an gien thaim thair oarders dinnae be gaun amang tha gentiles or intae onie toon o tha samaritans but rether gae tae tha loast sheep o israel an as ye ir gaun alang praich this tha kingdom o heiven is nearhan heal seeck fowk rise tha deid cleanse thaim wi leprosie drive oot ill spirits ye hae freelie received sae ye maun gie freelie dinnae tak alang onie gowld or siller ner een a copper in yer girthpooch tak nae baag fer tha road ner spare claes ner shune ner a stav fer tha warker is warth his keep whutiver toon or village ye gae intae luk fer some warthie dacent bodie thair an stap ower at his hoose til ye tak yer lave o tha place as ye gae intae this hame or that bid thaim tha time o day if tha hame is warthie let yer blissin be on it if it isnae warthie let yer blissin cum bak tae ye if the dinnae mak yis walcum or gie yis a hearin dicht tha stour aff yer feet whan ye lea that hame or toon a tell ye tha truith tha fowk o sodom an gomorrah wull be better aff on tha day o reckonin ner that toon am sennin yis oot laik sheep amang wolfs sae be as cannie as sarpents an as hairmless as doos be on yer gaird agin men thell han yis ower tae tha cooncils an gie yis a guid whuppin in thair meetin hooses on accoont o me yell be brocht afore guviners an kings as wutnesses tae thaim an tae tha gentiles but whaniver yis ir liftit an brocht tae thrial dinnae be ower enxious aboot whut tae say or hoo tae say it yell be gien tha richt wurds at tha richt time fer itll no be you thats spakin but tha spirit o yer faither spakin throu ye brithers wull han ower thair brithers tae be killt an faithers thair weans an weans wull rise up agin thair faithers an mithers an hae thaim put tae deith as weel yell be haitit bi yin an aa on accoont o me but he that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved whan yis ir persecutit in yin place fly tae anither a tell ye tha truith yell no hae feenished gaun throu aa tha toons o israel afore tha sinn o man cums bak a follaer is no abain his taicher ner a sarvint abain his maister whut mair can tha follaer ax than tae be laik his taicher or tha sarvint tae be laik his maister gin the hae caad tha heid o tha hoose beelzebul weel whut wull the no caa aa tha yins o his hoosehold sae dinnae be afeart o thaim thairs naethin covert ower thatll no cum tae licht ner hid thatll no be kent whut a tell ye in tha dairk spake oot in tha braid daylicht whuts whuspert in yer ear blare it oot frae tha ruiftaps dinnae be feart o thaim that kill tha bodie but cannae kill tha sowl rether be afeart o tha yin that can desthroy baith bodie an sowl in hell ir twa wee sparras no soul fer a pennie yit no yin o thaim wull faa tae tha grun wioot yer faither knowin it fer tha verie hairs o yer heid ir aa coontit sae dinnae be feart yis ir warth mair ner a hale wheen o sparras whaivers no feart tae own me afore men a wull own him tae afore ma faither in heiven but whaiver disowns me afore men a wull disown him afore ma faither in heiven dinnae be thinkin a hae cum tae bring peace tae tha irth na a didnae cum tae bring peace but a sword fer a hae cum tae turn a man agin his faither a dochter agin hir mither a dochterinlaa agin hir mitherinlaa itll be tha yins leevin wi a man that wull be agin him oniebodie that loves his faither or his mither mair ner me is no warthie o me nether is tha yin that loves his sinn or his dochter mair ner me warthie o me an oniebodie that daesnae tak up his cross an follae me is no warthie o me whaiver fins his life wull loass it an whaiver loasses his life on accoont o me wull fin it him that walcums you walcums me an him that walcums me walcums tha yin that sent me oniebodie that maks a proaphit walcum on accoont o his bein a proaphit wull be gien a proaphits reward an oniebodie that maks a guid man walcum on accoont o bein a guid man wull git a guid mans reward an if oniebodie gies even a bicker o coul watter tae yin o these weans acause he is ma follaer a tell ye he wull no be wantin fer a reward thats fer shair efter jesus haed daen giein oarders tae his twal follaers he gaed on frae thair tae taich an praich in tha toons roon aboot noo jhone wus in jail an whaniver he heerd whut christ wus daein he sent twa o his follaers an the axt him ir you tha yin that wus supposed tae cum or shud we be lukkin oot fer some ither bodie jesus toul thaim gae bak an gie jhone an accoont o whut ye hear an see blin fowk can see noo lameters can waak fowk wi leprosie ir made weel deef fowk can hear tha deid leeve agane an tha guid news is praicht tae tha puir an blisst is tha yin that daesnae misdoot me as jhones follaers wur leain jesus stairtit tae taak tae tha croods aboot him whut did yis gang oot intae tha wulderness fer tae see wus it tae see tha rushes sweein in tha wun if no whut did ye think ye wud see oot thair a man aa rigged oot in fancie claes na tha yins in fancie claes its in kings palaces ye wull fin them sae whut did yis gae oot fer tae see wus it a proaphit ay a tell ye an faur mair ner a proaphit this is tha yin tha scriptures taak aboot whan the say listen a wull senn oot ma messenger aheid o ye he wull mak readie tha wye afore ye a tell ye tha truith amangst thaim boarn o a wumman naebodie haes iver leeved thats mair impoartin ner jhone tha baptiser yit tha yin that is laist in tha kingdom o heiven is a better man ner him frae tha time jhone tha baptiser stairtit tae praich up til noo fowk ir tryin tae push thair wye intae tha kingdom o heiven an violent men ir takkin houl o it fer up tae jhones time aa tha proaphits an tha laa foretoul whut wus tae happen an if ye ir wullin tae believe whut a say jhone is tha elijah that wus tae cum let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent whut can a say aboot tha fowk nooadays the ir laik weans sittin doon at tha mairket an caain oot tae tha ithers we played tha whustle fer ye an ye wudnae daunce we sung a dirge tae ye an ye wudnae greet fer jhone wusnae intae aitin ner drinkin whan he cum an the say thairs a baad spirit in him yit tha sinn o man cum aitin an drinkin an the say wud ye luk at him hes a glutton an hes tarrible fand o tha drink sae he is tha freen o tex men an wrangdaers but daein whuts richt proves tha wusdom o gods wyes then jesus stairtit tae tak tae task tha cities whar he haed daen tha maist o his miracles acause the didnae repent sorra tae chorazim an sorra tae bethsaida fer if tha fowk o tyre an sidon haed saen tha warkin o gods pooer as yous hae saen it the wud hae repentit lang syne in seckclaith an eshes but am tellin ye tha fowk o tyre an sidon wull be better aff on tha day o reckonin than yous wull an capernaum you micht think yer weel on yer wye tae heiven na but am tellin ye yell be brocht doon tae hell fer if tha miracles that wus daen in you haed bin daen in sodom it wud be thair tae this day but a tell ye that sodom wull be better aff on tha day o reckonin ner you at that time jesus saed faither loard o heiven an irth a praise ye that ye hae kep these things frae clivir an warliewise fowk an made thaim clear eneuch fer weans tae unnerstan ay faither it haes plaised ye tae dae it this wye ma faither haes gien aa things ower tae me an naebodie unnerstans tha sinn apairt frae tha faither an naebodie unnerstans tha faither apairt frae tha sinn an whaiver tha sinn wants tae reveal him tae cum tae me aa you thats wearie an burdent an a wull gie ye rest tak ma yauk upon ye an lairn frae me fer am gentle an hummle in hairt an yisll fin rest fer yer sowls fer ma yauk is aisie an ma burden is licht at that time jesus gaed throu tha coarnfiels on tha sabbath day his follaers wur hungrie got an the begun tae pluck tha heids aff tha coarn an the et thaim whaniver tha pharisees saen this the saed tae him luk yer follaers ir daein whuts agin tha laa on tha sabbath day he saed bak tae thaim hae ye no read whut davit daen whaniver him an his freens wus hungrie he gaed intae tha hoose o god an him an his freens et tha halie showbreid an thair wus naebodie barrin tha preeshts allooed tae dae this or hae ye no read in tha laa that tha preeshts in tha hoose o god ir allooed tae wark on tha sabbath day an yit their no hel tae accoont fer brekkin tha laa a tell ye wer taakin aboot sumthin mair impoartin ner tha hoose o god here tha scripture says its mercie am efter am no efter secryfice an if ye haed unnerstud tha mainin o these wurds ye wudnae hae saed that ma follaers wus sinners whan the ir no fer tha sinn o man is loard o tha sabbath anaa jesus gaed on frae that place an he gaed intae thair meetin hoose an thair wus a man thair an his richt han wus wuthert lukkin tae hae sumthin agin jesus tha pharisees axt him ir ye allooed tae hail on tha sabbath day jesus saed bak tae thaim if onie o yis haes a sheep an it faas intae a sheuch on tha sabbath wud ye no tak houl o it an pu it oot is a man no warth faur mair ner a sheep ay sae its aa richt tae dae guid on tha sabbath day wi that he saed tae tha man streetch oot yer han sae he streetcht it oot an it wus aa hailt an jist as guid as tha ither yin but tha pharisees gaed oot an the collogued thegither hoo the cud dae awa wi jesus jesus knowin this left that place an a wile thrang o fowk follaed him an he made aa thair seeck fowk better an he gien thaim a warnin no tae tell oniebodie wha he wus this wus tae fulfill whut wus spauk aboot him throu tha proaphit isaiah here is ma sarvint ma hanwaaled yin hes tha yin a love hes tha yin am weel plaised wi all pit ma spirit on him an hell tell oot justice tae tha nations hell no cum argyin or cryin oot nether wull he rise his voice in tha raas a bent reed hell no brek aff an hell no snuff oot a smolderin wick til he leads justice on tae victrie in his name tha nations wull pit thair trust then the brocht him a man bothert wi ill spirits he wus blin an dum an jesus made him better sae he cud baith taak an see aa tha fowk wur thunnerstruck an the saed cud this be tha sinn o davit but whaniver tha pharisees heerd this the saed it is onlie bi beelzebul tha heidyin o tha ill spirits that this fella casts oot ill spirits knowin thair thochts jesus saed tae thaim iverie kingdom divid agin itsel wull gae tae reck an ruin an iverie citie or hoose divid agin itsel wull no stan an if satan casts oot satan he is divid agin hissel an hoo then cud his kingdom stan an if a cast oot ill spirits bi tha pooer o beelzebul bi whut pooer then daes yer ain fowk cast thaim oot sae let thaim be tha yins tae judge ye fer whut ye hae saed but if a cast oot ill spirits bi tha spirit o god it proves that tha kingdom o god is here amang ye or agane hoo can oniebodie git intae a strang mans hoose an cairrie aff his belangins less he furst tyes up tha strang man efter that he can plunner awa him that is no for me is agin me an him that isnae giein me a han tae gether in he micht as weel be scatterin an sae a tell ye men wull be forgien iverie sin an blesphemie but tha blesphemie agin tha spirit wull no be forgien oniebodie that spakes a wurd agin tha sinn o man wull be forgien but oniebodie that spakes agin tha halie spirit wull no be forgien nether in this age ner in tha age tae cum ye can tell a tree bi its fruit gin tha trees guid its fruit wull be guid gin its baad its fruit wull be baad ye sleekit shooer o vipers hoo can ye say ocht thats guid whan yer wickit yersels fer whuts in yer hairt wull cum oot o yer mooth a guid man brings guid things oot o tha guidness stored in his hairt a wickit man brings wickit things oot o his store o wickitness but a tell ye on tha day o reckonin men wull hae tae mak answer fer iverie careless wurd the hae spauk fer bi yer wurds yell be judged no guiltie an bi yer wurds yell be condemned then some o tha pharisees an maisters o tha laa saed tae him maister we want a miraclis sign frae ye he saed bak tae thaim its onlie a wickit an adulterous generation wud luk fer a miraclis sign but thairll be nane gien apairt frae tha sign o tha proaphit jonah fer jist as jonah wus thrie days an thrie nichts in tha belly o a big fish in tha same wye tha sinn o man wull be thrie days an thrie nichts in tha hairt o tha irth tha men o nineveh wull stan up at tha day o reckonin wi this generation an thell condemn it fer they repentit whaniver jonah praicht tae thaim an yit tha yin thats here noo is mair ner onie jonah tha queen o tha sooth wull stan up wi this generation tae be judged as weel on that day an she wull condemn it fer she cum frae tha enns o tha irth fer tae listen tae solomons wusdom an noo yin abain solomon is here an yis ir no listenin whan an ill spirit cums oot o a man it raiks throu tha desert lukkin fer rest but it fins nane then it says all jist gae bak tae whar a wus leevin afore whaniver it gaes bak it fins tha hoose empie swep clain an aa redd up then it gangs an taks wi it seiven ither spirits mair wickit ner itsel an the aa gae in an the settle thair an that man enns up faur waur ner he wus afore thats tha wye itll be wi this wickit generation while jesus wus still taakin tae tha thrang his mither an his brithers stud ootbye lukkin tae spake tae him summodie toul him yer mither an yer brithers ir waitin ootbye lukkin tae spake tae ye but jesus cum bak wi this wha is ma mither an wha ir ma brithers pointin tae his follaers he saed luk thairs ma mither an ma brithers fer thaim at daes tha wull o ma faither in heiven is ma brither an ma sister an ma mither that verie day jesus gaed oot o tha hoose an sut doon bi tha loch shore sitch a thrang o fowk gethert roon him that he got intae a boat an sut in it while aa tha fowk stud bye on tha shore an he toul thaim a hale wheen o things bi parables laik this yin thair wus this fairmer gaed oot tae saa seed an as he wus scatterin it some drapt doon alang tha pad an tha burds flew doon an peckt thaim up thair wus some seed faad doon on roakie grun whar thair wusnae much clye it sprung up quick becas tha clye wus shalla but as shune as it brairdit an tha sin ris tha plants wus scorcht an the wuthert awa acause the haed nae ruits ither seed faad doon amang thoarns an breers that sprung up tuk ower an chokt it yit ither seed faad on guid grun whar it brocht a hairst o a hunner sixtie or thurtie times whut wus sowed let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent his follaers cum tae him an axt fer why dae ye spake tae tha fowk in parables he saed tae you god haes gien an unnerstannin o tha saicrets o tha kingdom o heiven but no tae thaim fer him that haes plentie wull be gien mair an he wull hae mair ner eneuch an him that haes little even whut he haes wull be tuk awa frae him this is tha raison a spake tae thaim in parables tha mair the luk the dinnae see tha mair the hear the dinnae listen or unnerstan isaiahs proaphesie cums aboot in thaim whaniver he says you wull aye be hearin but niver unnerstannin yell aye be seein but niver takkin it in fer tha hairt o these fowk haes becum haird the can harlie hear wi thair ears an the hae shut thair een itherwise the cud see wi thair een the cud hear wi thair ears the cud unnerstan wi thair hairts an the wud turn tae me tae hail thaim but your een is blisst acause they can see an your ears tae acause they can hear fer a tell ye tha truith thairs monies a proaphit an monies a guid man wud hae gien oniethin fer tae see whut yous see but the didnae see it an tae hear whut yous hear but the didnae hear it listen then tae whut tha parable o tha sower mains whan oniebodie hears tha message aboot tha kingdom an daesnae unnerstan it alang cums tha wickit yin an snaps awa whut wus sowed in his hairt this is whut tha seed sowed nixt tha pad stans fer an then tha seed that faad on roakie grun stans fer tha bodie that hears tha message an taks it in richt awa wi a gled hairt but seein as he haes nae ruits it onlie houls wi him fer a wee while whan haird times an trouble cums acause o gods wurd he jist gies up thair an then then tha seed that faad doon amang tha thoarns thats laik a bodie that hears tha message but wi him chasin efter money an tha bothers o this warl tha message gets chokt an it aa cums tae naethin but tha seed that faad doon on guid grun is laik tha bodie that taks tha wurd tae hairt an unnerstans it bringin in a yiel o thurtie sixtie or a hunner times mair ner wus sowed jesus toul thaim anither parable tha kingdom o heiven is laik a man that sowed guid seed in his fiel but whaniver aa tha fowk wus sleepin his enemie cum an sowed geel amang tha wheat an then he tuk aff noo as shune as tha wheat brairdit an tha ears appeart tha weeds cum up as weel an tha fairmers sarvin men cum up tae him maister the saed did ye no sow guid seed in yer fiel whar then did tha weeds cum frae an enemie haes daen this he saed tha sarvints axt him dae ye want iz tae gae oot an pu thaim up na he saed bak tae thaim becas whaniver yer puin oot tha weeds yell mebbe ruit up tha wheat alang wi thaim let thaim baith growe thegither tae tha hairvest an then all tell tha reapers gether up tha weeds furst an tye thaim up in bunnels fer burnin then awa an gether up tha wheat an bring it intae ma barn jesus toul thaim yit anither parable tha kingdom o heiven is laik a wee mustert seed that a man tuk an sowed in his fiel tha mair it stairts aff as a gye wee seed yit whan it growes it becums a big bush an then a tree sae as tha wee burds cum an tuk shilter in its brenches an heres anither yin he toul thaim tha kingdom o heiven is laik yeast that a wumman tuk fer tae mak breid she warkt that wee bit intae a big boul o flure tae tha hale lock o it ris jesus spauk in parables whan he toul tha croods aa these things he didnae say ocht tae thaim wioot uisin a parable this wus tae bring aboot whut tha proaphit saed wud happen a wull taak tae ye in parables a wull tell ye things hid since tha warl begun then he left tha crood o fowk an went intae tha hoose his follaers cum tae him an saed wud ye tell iz whut that parable o tha weeds in tha fiel mains he answert tha yin that sowed tha guid seed is tha sinn o man tha fiel is tha warl an tha guid seed stans fer tha sinns o tha kingdom tha weeds stans fer tha childer o tha wickit yin an tha enemie that sows thaim is tha deil tha hairvest is tha enn o tha warl an tha reapers ir tha angels jist tha wye tha weeds ir pued up an brunt in tha fire thats tha wye itll be at tha enn o tha warl tha sinn o man wull senn oot his angels an thell ruit oot o his kingdom iveriethin that brings aboot sin an aa thaim that daes wrang an tha angels wull fling thaim intae tha fierie furnace whar thair wull be sair greetin an scringein o teeth then tha yins thats daen richt wull shine brichtlie laik tha sin in thair faithers kingdom let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent tha kingdom o heiven is laik treysure hid in a fiel thair wus this man fun it an he went an hid it agane an he wus that plaised aboot it he went an soul aa he haed an he bocht tha fiel an agane tha kingdom o heiven is laik a dailer on tha lukoot fer fancie pearls whaniver he fun yin that wus warth a hale lock awa he went an soul iveriethin he haed an he bocht it or agane tha kingdom o heiven is laik a neyt that the lut doon intae tha loch an it catched aa kines o fish whaniver it wus fu tha fishermen haaled it ashore then the sut doon an the waaled throu it the put tha guid fish intae creels but the throwed tha baad yins awa thats hoo itll be at tha enn o tha warl tha angelsll cum an soart oot tha wickit fowk frae tha guid an thell cast thaim intae tha fierie furnace whar thairll be greetin an scringein o teeth hae ye unnerstud aa these things jesus axt his follaers ay we hae the saed he saed tae thaim weel then iverie maister o tha laa that haes bin schuiled in tha things o tha kingdom o heiven is laik tha guidman o tha hoose that brings oot o his storeruim treysures baith oul an new an whan jesus wus daen tellin these parables he gaed on frae thair an bak tae his hametoon an whaniver he stairtit taichin tha fowk thair in tha meetin hoose the wur aa dumfoonert whar did this man get his wusdom an miraclis pooers frae the axt is this no jist tha cairpenters sinn his mithers caad mary isnt she an ir his brithers no jeames joseph simon an judas shair his sisters ir aa here wi iz sae whar did this bodie get aa this frae an the tuk umrage at him but jesus saed tae thaim a proaphits niver weel thocht o in his hametoon or in his ain hoose an he didnae dae monie miracles thair acause o thair want o faith at that time herod tha tetrarch heerd whut the wur sayin aboot jesus an he saed tae his sarvin men this is jhone tha baptiser he haes ris frae tha deid thats tha raison he haes these miraclis pooers noo afore this herod haed tuk houl o jhone an he haed him tyed up an put awa in jail acause o herodias his brither philips wife fer jhone wus aye tellin him tha laa daesnae alloo ye tae hae hir herod wud hae killt jhone but he wus afeart o tha crood turnin on him acause the lukt on jhone as a proaphit but at herods birthday pairtie tha dochter o herodias daunced afore thaim an plaised herod that much that he swore hed gie hir whutiver she axt fer tha wee lass saed it wus hir mither put hir up tae it jist gie me tha heid o jhone tha baptiser on a platter tha king wus wile annoyt aboot this but acause o whut hed swore an tha yins wi him roon tha table he oardert thaim tae gie hir whut she haed axt fer sae he got thaim tae tak tha heid aff jhone in tha jail the brocht it bak on a platter an the gien it tae tha wee lass an she cairriet it tae hir mither jhones follaers cum an tuk his bodie awa an buriet it then the went an toul jesus whut haed happent whaniver jesus heerd this he went awa in a boat bi his lane tae a quait place but whan tha croods got tae know aboot it the follaed him on fit frae tha toons an whan jesus cum tae lan he fun a quare thrang o fowk fornent him an his hairt went oot tae thaim an he cured thair seeck fowk then as evenin wus draain in his follaers cum tae him an saed this is a richt oot o tha wye place an its gettin late senn tha croods awa sae the can gang tae tha clachans an buy thairsels a bite tae ait jesus saed the dinnae need tae gae awa yous gie thaim sumthin tae ait we hae naethin here but five bannocks an twa fish the reponed weel bring thaim here tae me he saed he oardert tha fowk tae sit doon on tha gress an takkin tha five bannocks an tha twa fish an lukkin up tae heiven he blisst it an brauk tha bannocks then he gien thaim tae his follaers an tha follaers gien thaim tae tha fowk the aa et thair fill an his follaers gethert up twal creels fu o aa tha wee bits that wus left ower tha nummer o thaim that et wus aboot five thoosan men niver mine weemen an weans richt awa jesus made tha follaers get intae tha boat an gae on aheid o him tae tha ither side while he toul tha thrang tae gae hame efter he haed sent thaim awa he went up tha muntin bi hissel fer tae pray at dailygan he wus thair on his lane bi noo tha boat wus aareadie miles awa frae tha lan it wus takkin a hemmerin frae tha waves an tha wun wus agin it cum tha fowerth watch o tha nicht jesus gaed oot tae thaim waakin on tha watter whaniver his follaers saen him waakin on tha watter the wur hairtscarred an trimmlin wi fear the caad oot its a wraith but strecht awa jesus spauk oot an saed tae thaim tak hairt its masel dinnae be feart loard if its you peter saed bid me cum tae ye on tha watter cum on then saed jesus sae peter got doon oot o tha boat he waakt on tha watter an he went nixt jesus but whaniver he saen hoo strang tha wun wus he wus afeart an he stairtit tae sink loard save me he caad oot at yinst jesus raxt oot his han an gript him hae ye nae faith ava he saed why did ye doot me an whaniver the climmed bak intae tha boat tha wun deed doon then thaim that wur in tha boat wurshipt him sayin you are tha sinn o god an thats tha truith o it whan the gaed bak ower tha loch agane the landit at gennesaret an whaniver tha men o that place reconised jesus the sent wurd roon tha hale kintrieside an the brocht aa thair seeck fowk tae him an plaidit wi him tae let thaim jist touch tha hem o his robe an iveriebodie that toucht it wus makkit weel agane then some pharisees an maisters o tha laa cum tae jesus frae jerusalem an the axt him fer why dae yer follaers lea aside tha oul wyes o oor elders the dinnae even waash thair hans afore the ait jesus cum bak wi this an fer why dae you lea aside tha laas o god fer tha sake o yer ain tradeetions fer god gart ye this honour yer faither an yer mither an oniebodie that miscaas thair faither or mither maun be put tae deith but yous say that its aa richt fer a bodie tae tell his faither or mither whutiver halp ye wud hae got frae me a hae vood tae gie tae god an ye say he isnae obliged tae honour his parents wi it bi this ye mak a nonsense o tha wurd o god fer tha sake o yer tradeetion ye hippycrates isaiah got it richt whan he proaphesied this aboot ye this nation honours me wi thair mooth says god but thair hairt is faur awa frae me thair woarships nae use ava thair taichins ir naethin but manmade rules an regulations jesus caad tha thrang tae him an saed listen tae me an unnerstan whut am sayin whut gaes intae a mans mooth daesnae sullie him but whut cums oot o his mooth its that sullies him then his follaers cum tae him an axt dae ye ken that tha pharisees wur gye ill plaised whaniver the heerd this he saed iverie plant ma heivenlie faither haesnae plantit wull be pued up bi tha ruits lea thaim alane the ir naethin but blin guides if a blin man taks anither blin man bi tha airm tha baith o thaim wull faa intae tha sheuch peter saed tae jesus tell iz whut that ither parable wus aboot ir yous slow on tha uptake tae jesus axt thaim dae yis no see that whutiver gaes intae yer mooth gaes intae yer belly an then passes on oot doon tha drain but tha things that cum oot o tha mooth cum frae tha hairt an thats whut sullies a bodie fer oot o tha hairt cums wickit thochts murder an adulterie lustin an thievin blesphemin an slanderin fowk these things is whut sullies a bodie but aitin wioot tha ritual waashin o hans daesnae sullie him then jesus upt an left that place an he went awa tae tha district roon tyre an sidon an this canaanite wumman frae thaim pairts cum tae him cryin oot loard sinn o davit hae peetie on me ma dochter is sufferin sumthin tarrible wi an ill spirit jesus niver saed a wurd sae his follaers cum tae him an plaidit wi him senn hir awa fer shes follaein iz an shell no stap hir yellin oot he saed bak a wus onlie sent tae tha loast sheep o tha hoose o israel tha wumman cum an got doon on hir knees afore him an she saed loard halp me it isnae richt saed he tae tak tha weans breid an clod it tae tha wee dugs ay loard thats richt she saed but still wi aa een tha wee dugs gits aitin tha crumbs that faa frae thair maisters boord then jesus saed bak tae hir wumman sitch an a faith ye hae yell get whut ye axt fer an hir dochter got better that verie oor jesus quit thaim pairts an cum tae tha loch shore o galilee then he gaed up tha side o tha muntin an sut doon an a wile thrang o fowk cum tae him bringin tha lameters tha crippelt blin fowk an dum fowk an a hale lock o ithers an the leed thaim doon at his feet an he made thaim weel agane tha fowk wur stoondit whaniver the wutnesst tha dum spakin tha crippelt makkit weel lameters waakin an tha blin bein able tae see an the gien glorie tae tha god o israel jesus caad his follaers tae him an saed ma hairt gaes oot tae these fowk the hae bin here wi me this thrie days an the hae naethin lef tae ait a dinnae want tae senn thaim awa hame or thell drap wi hungr alang tha road his follaers saed bak tae him whar cud we get eneuch breid oot here in tha wiles tae feed sitch a crood o fowk hoo monie loafs dae yis hae jesus axt seiven the saed an a wheen o wee fish he bid tha crood o fowk sit thairsels doon on tha grun then he tuk tha seiven loafs an tha fish an whaniver he haed gien thenks he brauk thaim intae bits an gien thaim tae his follaers then they gien thaim tae tha crood the aa et thair fill an efter that tha follaers gethert up seiven creels fu o tha leains tha nummer o men that et that day wus fower thoosan niver mine weemen an weans then jesus sent tha thrang awa an he got intae a boat an gaed ower tae tha kintrie roon aboot magadan yin day tha pharisees an sadducees cum tae jesus an tried tae ketch him oot bi axin him tae show thaim a sign frae heiven he saed at dailygan ye say tha weathers gaun tae be guid fer tha sky is rid an in tha moarnin ye say itll be wundie theday fer tha sky is rid an threatinin sae yis can tell tha weather bi tha luk o tha sky but yis cannae wark oot tha signs o tha times a wickit an adulterous generation luks fer a miraclis sign but nane wull be gien it apairt frae tha sign o jonah jesus then left thaim an gaed awa an whaniver the crosst tae tha ither side o tha loch his follaers didnae mine tae tak breid wi thaim luk oot jesus saed tae thaim be on yer gaird agin tha yeast o tha pharisees an tha sadducees the taakt aboot this amang thairsels an saed its becas we didnae bring onie breid wi iz jesus kent whut the wur on aboot sae he saed tae thaim fer why ir ye taakin amang yersels aboot haein nae breid hae yis nae faith ava dae yis still no unnerstan dae yis no mine tha five loafs a gien til tha five thoosan an aa tha baskets o leains yis gethert up efter or tha seiven loafs a gie til tha fower thoosan an hoo monie creels yis gethert up anaa hoo is it yis dinnae unnerstan that a wus no taakin tae ye aboot breid am tellin ye jist be on yer gaird agin tha yeast o tha pharisees an sadducees an then the unnerstud that he wus no tellin thaim tae gaird agin tha yeast uised in breid but agin tha taichin o tha pharisees an sadducees whaniver jesus cum tae tha district o caesarea philippi he axt his follaers wha dae fowk say tha sinn o man is the saed a wheen say jhone tha baptiser some wud say elijah an still ithers jeremiah or yin o tha proaphits but whut aboot yersels he axt wha dae you say that a am simon peter saed bak you ir tha christ tha sinn o tha leevin god jesus saed blisst ir ye simon sinn o jonah fer this wus no revealt tae ye bi onie human bein but bi ma faither in heiven a tell ye frae noo on you ir peter an on this roak a wull big ma kirk an aa tha pooers o hell wull no owercum it a wull gie ye tha keys o tha kingdom o heiven an whutiver ye bine on irth wull be bun in heiven an whutiver ye lowse on irth wull be lowsed in heiven then he bid his follaers no tae tell oniebodie that he wus tha christ frae that time on jesus stairtit tae mak it clear tae his follaers that he maun gae tae jerusalem an he maun suffer monies a thing at tha hans o tha elders tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa he toul thaim that he maun be put tae deith an be ris up tae life on tha thurd day peter tuk him tae tha yin side an begun tae scoul him niver loard he saed this wull niver happen tae you jesus turnt an saed tae peter git ahint me satan ye ir a thripstane tae me fer ye gie nae thocht tae tha things o god yer heids fu o tha things o men then jesus saed tae his follaers if oniebodie wants tae follae efter me he maun ferget aboot hissel aathegither tak up his cross an stick clase tae me fer whaiver wants tae save his life wull loass it but him that loasses his life on ma accoont wull fin it whut guid wull it be fer a bodie if he gets tha hale warl an yit loasses his ain sowl shair thairs naethin a man cud gie tae get bak his ain sowl is thair fer tha sinn o man is gaun tae cum wi his angels in his faithers glorie an then hell reward iverie singl bodie accoardin tae whut the hae daen a tell ye tha truith thairs yins stannin here an its fer sartin thell no dee afore the see tha sinn o man cumin in his kingdom efter six days jesus tuk wi him peter jeames an jhone tha brither o jeames an brocht thaim up intae a heich muntin bi thairsels thair tha hale luk o him wus changed afore thair verie een his face shone laik tha sin an his claes turnt white as tha licht an jist then thair appeart afore thaim moses an elijah an the wur taakin wi jesus peter saed tae jesus loard am gled we ir here tae see this if ye laik a wull pit up thrie shilters yin fer you yin fer moses an yin fer elijah an he wus still taakin whaniver a bricht clood cum roon thaim an a voice frae tha clood saed this is ma sinn that a love wi him am weel plaised listen tae him whaniver tha follaers heerd this the faad doon wi thair faces tae tha grun hairtscarred but jesus cum an put his han on thaim git up he saed dinnae be feart whaniver the lukt up thair wus naebodie thair but jesus an as the wur cumin doon tha muntin jesus warnt thaim dinnae tell oniebodie whut yis hae saen til tha sinn o man haes bin ris frae tha deid tha follaers axt him sae hoo cum tha maisters o tha laa tell iveriebodie that elijah haes tae cum furst afore tha messiah jesus saed deed ay elijah is tae cum furst tae get aa readie fer tha messiah but am tellin ye elijah haes cum aareadie an the didnae ken wha he wus but the daen tae him aa the wantit in tha same wye tha sinn o man is gaun tae suffer at thair hans then his follaers unnerstud it wus jhone tha baptiser he wus taakin tae thaim aboot noo whaniver the cum bak doon tha muntin tae tha crood o fowk a man cum up tae jesus an got doon on his knees afore him loard hae mercie on ma sinn he saed fer he taks fits an is sufferin wile baad monies a time he wud faa intae tha fire or intae tha watter a brocht him tae yer follaers but the cud dae naethin fer him you fowk ir faithless an aisie led jesus saed hoo lang wull a be wi ye afore yis believe hoo lang dae a hae tae pit up wi ye bring tha wee lad here tae me jesus gien tha ill spirit a richt barjin an it cum oot o tha boy an he wus better agane frae that verie minit then tha follaers cum tae jesus whaniver he wus on his ain an axt fer why cud we no cast oot tha ill spirit he saed acause yer faith is sae waik a tell ye tha truith if yis hae faith as smaa as a mustert seed even yisll say tae this muntin shift frae here tae thair an itll shift naethin wull be impoassible fer ye but ye can onlie git rid o this kine o ill spirit bi prayer an fastin whaniver the cum thegither agane in galilee he saed tae thaim tha sinn o man is gaun tae be hannit ower tae men thatll kill him but on tha thurd day hell rise frae tha deid an wi that sorra fillt tha hairts o his follaers efter jesus an his follaers cum tae capernaum tha collectors o tha tex fer tha hoose o god cum up tae peter an axt daes your taicher no pye tha temple tex he daes shairlie he saed noo whaniver peter cum intae tha hoose jesus wus tha furst tae spake oot whut dae ye think simon he axt him wha dae tha kings o tha irth collect thair dues an texes frae frae thair ain fowk or frae ithers frae ithers peter saed bak an jesus saed til him then thair ain yins dinnae hae tae pye dae the weel we dinnae want tae gie onie offence sae gae ye doon tae tha loch an cast oot yer line tak tha furst fish ye ketch apen its mooth an yell fin a coin tak that an gie it tae thaim an itll pye tha tex fer tha baith o iz roon aboot that time tha follaers cum tae jesus an axt wha is tha maist thocht o in tha kingdom o heiven he caad a wean til him an stud him amang thaim an he saed a tell ye tha truith if ye dinnae change yer hale wye o gaun an becum laik wee childer yell niver git intae tha kingdom o heiven sae whaiver maks little o thairsels an becums laik this wean is tha maist impoartin in tha kingdom o heiven an whaiver walcums yin o these weans in ma name walcums me but if oniebodie leads asthray yin o these weans that believes in me it wud be faur better fer him tae hae a millstane hung roon his neck an tae be droont in tha depths o tha sea dear halp tha warl fer tempin fowk tae dae wrang thairll aye be things that maks fowk dae wrang but dear halp tha bodie that daes tha tempin if yer han or yer fit maks ye tae dae wrang cut it aff an cast it awa it is faur better fer ye tae gae tae heiven wantin a han or a fit ner tae hae twa hans or twa feet an be throwed intae tha iverlastin fire an if yer ee maks ye dae wrang pu it oot an cast it awa it is faur better fer ye tae gae tae heiven wantin an ee ner tae hae twa een an be throwed intae tha fire o hell tak tent that ye dinnae luk doon on yin o these weans fer a tell ye that tha angels that luk efter thaim ir alang wi ma faither in heiven an their readie onie minit tae spake up fer thaim tha sinn o man haes cum tae save thaim thats loast whut dae ye think if a man haes a hunner sheep an yin o thaim wanners wull he no lea tha ninetienine on tha hills an gae tae luk fer tha yin that wannert aff an if he fins it a tell ye tha truith he is mair gled aboot that yin sheep ner aboot tha ninetienine that didnae wanner aff in tha same wye ma faither in heiven isnae wullin that onie o these weans shud be loast if yer brither daes ye wrang gae an show him his sin jist atween tha twa o ye if he listens tae ye ye hae wun yer brither ower but if hell no listen tak yin or twa ithers alang sae that as tha scripture says twarthie wutnesses wull testify tae tha truith o iverie wurd spauk an if he wull no listen tae thaim tell it tae tha kirk an if he wull no listen tae tha kirk ether dail wi him tha wye ye wud dae wi a tex man or tha haithen a tell ye tha truith whutiver ye bine on irth wull be bun in heiven an whutiver ye lowse on irth wull be lowsed in heiven agane a tell ye that if twa o ye here on irth agree aboot oniethin ye ax fer itll be daen fer ye bi ma faither in heiven fer whar twa or thrie cum thegither in ma name am thair amang thaim then peter cum tae jesus an axt loard hoo monie times am a tae forgie ma brither whan he daes wrang agin me up tae seiven times jesus saed bak tae him a tell ye no seiven times but mair laik seiventie times seiven sae ye see tha kingdom o heiven is laik a king that wantit his sarvints tae settle thair accoonts wi him an as he stairtit tae dae this a man that owed him a foartune wus brocht tae him an becas he wusnae able tae pye tha maister oardert that baith him an tha wife an tha weans an aa that he haed shud be soul tae pye bak tha debt tha sarvint faad doon on his knees afore him gie me time he plaidit an a wull pye bak iveriethin tha sarvints maister tuk peetie on him wiped oot his debt an lut him gang free but whaniver that sarvint gaed oot he cum on yin o his fella sarvints that owed him twarthie thoosan pun he tuk houl o him bi tha throat an saed you pye me bak whut ye owe me his fella sarvint faad doon on his knees an begged him gie me time an a wull pye ye bak but he wudnae hear o it insteed he gan aff an haed tha man throwed intae jail til he cud pye up whaniver tha ither sarvints saen whut wus gaun on the wur wile annoyt an the went an toul thair maister iveriethin that happent then tha maister caad tha sarvint in you wickit sarvint he saed a wiped oot that debt o yers acause ye begged me tae shud ye no hae tuk peetie on yer fella sarvint tha same wye a tuk peetie on you his maister wus that angrie got he turnt him ower tae tha jailers tae be tortured til he pyed bak aa he owed this is hoo ma heivenlie faither wull dail wi iverie last yin o ye if ye dinnae forgie yer brither frae yer hairt whaniver jesus wus daen sayin these things he left galilee he gaed intae judea an crosst ower tha river joardan big croods follaed him an he hailt tha seeck amang thaim some pharisees cum up tae him an tae pit him tae tha test the axt him is a man allooed tae pit awa his wife fer onie an iverie raison hae ye no read jesus answert that richt frae tha stairt tha creator made men an he made weemen an that he saed fer this raison a man wull lea his faither an his mither an be joint tae his wife an tha twa wull becum as yin an noo the ir nae mair twa seprit fowk but the ir yin sae whut god haes put thegither let nae man pull sinnerie whut fer then the axt him whut fer did moses say that a man cud gie his wife a notysh o divorce an pit hir awa jesus saed moses allooed ye tae divorce yer wifes acause yer hairts wus haird but this wusnae tha wye o it frae tha stairt a tell ye that oniebodie that pits awa his wife fer ocht ither ner rinnin aff wi anither man an then merries anither wumman that man commits adulterie his follaers saed tae him if thats tha wye o it wi a man that haes a wife shair it wud be faur better no tae merrie ava jesus saed its no iveriebodie can hannle that jist thaim thats halpt bi god fer some ir eunuchs acause the wur boarn that wye ithers wur made that wye bi men an ithers haes gien up tha chaunce o merriage acause o tha kingdom o heiven tha yin that can hannle this shud accept it some weans wur brocht tae jesus fer him tae pit his hans on thaim an pray fer thaim his follaers scoult tha yins that brocht thaim but jesus saed alloo tha weans cum tae me an dinnae houl thaim bak fer tha kingdom o heiven belangs tae tha laiks o thaim an efter he put his hans on tha weans tae bliss thaim he gaed on frae thair noo alang cum this man tae jesus an axt him maister whut guid thing maun a dae tae hae iverlastin life whut dae ye main bi guid jesus saed thair is yin alane that is guid if its iverlastin life yer wantin dae whut tha commauns bids ye whutch yins tha man axt jesus saed dinnae murder dinnae commit adulterie dinnae tak whuts no yer ain dinnae tell lees aboot ither fowk gie respeck tae yer faither an yer mither an ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel a hae kep aa these tha young man saed whut else dae a hae tae dae jesus saed bak tae him if ye hae a mine tae be perfait awa an sell aa ye hae got an gie it awa tae tha puir an yell hae walth in heiven then cum bak an follae me whaniver tha young man heerd this he wus doon in tha mooth an went awa fer he wus quare an weelaff then jesus saed tae his follaers a tell ye tha truith it is haird fer a bodie thats weelaff tae git intae tha kingdom o heiven ay am tellin ye it wud be aisier fer a kemel tae gae throu tha ee o a needle ner fer a monied man tae git intae tha kingdom o god whaniver tha follaers heerd this the wur stoondit an axt wha in aa tha warl can be saved then jesus lukt strecht at thaim an saed wi man this is no poassible but wi god aa things ir poassible wi that peter saed bak tae him luk we hae gien up iveriethin tae follae ye whut then wull thair be in it fer us jesus saed tae thaim a tell ye tha truith whaniver tha new warl cums aboot an tha sinn o man sits on his throne o glorie yous that hae follaed me wull sit doon on twal thrones as weel judgin tha twal clans o israel an iverie yin that haes gien up hooses or brithers or sisters or faither or mither or wife or childer or fairm o lan on accoont o me wull git bak a hunner times as much an he wull inherit iverlastin life but monies a bodie thats foremaist noo wull be last then an monie thats last noo wull be foremaist then fer tha kingdom o heiven is laik a fairmer that gan oot at tha scraich o day tae hire men tae wark in his vineyaird he saed he wud pye thaim a siller coin fer tha day an he sent thaim oot intae his vineyaird aboot nine in tha moarnin he gan oot an saen ithers stannin in tha mairket place wi naethin tae dae he toul thaim gae an wark in ma vineyaird as weel an all pye ye a fair wage sae awa the went tha fairmer gan oot an he daen tha same thing aboot nuin an then agane at thrie roon aboot five in tha efternuin he gaed oot an fun still ithers stannin roon in tha mairket place he axt thaim why hae ye bin hangin aboot here aa day lang daein naethin acause naebodie haes tuk iz on the saed he saed tae thaim gae awa noo an wark in ma vineyaird as weel cum dailygan tha fairmer saed tae his lansteward caa tha warkers an pye thaim thair wages stairtin wi tha last yins a tuk on an gaun bak tae tha furst tha warkers that wus hired roon five in tha efternuin they cum an iverie yin o thaim wus gien a siller coin apiece sae whan tha yins cum that wus hired furst the wur lukkin tae git mair but iverie last yin o thaim wus onlie gien a siller coin tha same as tha ithers whaniver the got it the stairtit tae grummle agin tha fairmer thaim men that wus hired last warkt onlie tha yin oor the saed an ye hae traitit thaim tha same as us that haes daen tha maist o tha wark an tholed tha hait o tha day but he saed bak tae yin o thaim freen am bein fair eneuch tae ye did ye no say ye wud wark fer yin siller coin tak whuts yours an aff ye gang fer a want tae gie tha man that wus hired last tha same as a gien you dae a no hae tha richt tae dae whut a laik wi ma ain siller or dae ye begrudge me bein guid tae tha ithers sae tha last wull be foremaist saed jesus an tha foremaist wull be last monie fowk is caad but few singlt oot noo as jesus wus on tha road up tae jerusalem he tuk tha twal follaers aside an he saed tae thaim listen here wer fer jerusalem an tha sinn o man wull be bethrayed tae tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa the wull condemn him tae deith an thell turn him ower tae tha gentiles fer tae be mockt an whuppt an hung up on a cross but on tha thurd day hell rise tae life agane then tha mither o zebedees sinns cum tae jesus an hir twa sinns alang wi hir faain doon afore him she axt a favour o him whut is it ye want he axt she saed wud ye see tae it that yin o these twa sinns o mine wull sit at yer richt han an tha tither at yer left han in yer kingdom ye dinnae ken whut yer axin jesus saed tae thaim can you drink tha cup o sufferin that am gaun tae drink or can ye be baptised wi tha baptisin that a am tae be baptised wi ay that we can the saed jesus toul thaim yisll shairlie drink frae ma cup o sufferin but tae sit at ma richt or ma left han side isnae fer me tae say ma faither haes made thaim places readie fer tha yins hes singlt oot whan tha ither ten follaers heerd aboot this the wur wile angrie wi tha twa brithers but jesus caad thaim thegither an saed ye ken that thaim that rule ower tha gentiles laird it ower thair ain fowk an thair heidyins aye lets thaim know whas tha boss wi you its no tae be laik that na whaiver wants tae be impoartin amang ye maun be yer sarvint an whaiver wants tae be foremaist amang ye maun be yer slave jist tha wye tha sinn o man didnae cum tae be tendit tae but fer tae sarve ithers an tae gie up his life as a ransom fer monie fowk as jesus an his follaers wur leain jericho a big crood o fowk follaed him an lo an behoul sittin on tha bunker o tha road thair wus these twa men that wur blin an whaniver the heerd jesus wus passin bye the cryed oot loard sinn o davit tak peetie on iz tha thrang chackt thaim an toul thaim tae be quait but the guldert aa tha mair sayin loard sinn o davit tak peetie on iz whaniver he heerd thaim jesus stapt then he caad tae thaim whut dae yis want me tae dae fer ye loard the saed we want oor sicht bak his hairt went oot tae thaim an he put his hans on thair een an at yinst the got thair sicht bak an the follaed efter jesus whaniver the wur nearhan jerusalem an the cum tae bethphage on tha moont o olives jesus sent oot twa follaers an he saed tae thaim gae tae tha clachan fornent ye an at yinst yell fin a cuddie tethert thair wi hir cowlt alangside o hir lowse tha raip an bring thaim tae me if oniebodie says ocht tae ye tell him tha loard haes need o thaim an hell senn thaim richt awa this cum aboot fer tae fulfill whut wus spauk throu tha proaphit say tae tha dochter o zion luk see yer king is on his wye tae ye gentle an ridin on a cuddie on a cowlt tha foal o a cuddie tha follaers gan awa an daen as the wur bid the brocht tha cuddie an tha cowlt an the put thair claes on thaim fer jesus tae sit on an thair wus a hale thrang o fowk gethert tha maist o thaim spreedin thair claes on tha road while ithers sneddit brenches aff tha trees an the strewed thaim on tha pad fer him tae ride ower tha croods that gan aheid o him an thaim that follaed behin cryed oot hosanna
