tae tha sinn o davit blisst be tha yin that cums in tha name o tha loard hosanna in tha heichest heiven whaniver jesus went intae jerusalem tha hale citie wus in a stir an the axt wha wud this man be an tha croods saed bak tae thaim this is jesus tha proaphit frae nazareth in galilee jesus went intae tha hoose o god an driv oot aa tha dailers that wus buyin an sellin in tha coortyaird he coupt tha tables o tha siller changers an whammelt tha saits o thaim that wus sellin doos it is writ doon he saed tae thaim that ma hoose wull be caad a hoose o prayer but yous ir turnin it intae a den o robbers tha blin an tha lameters cum tae him thair in tha hoose o god an he made thaim better but whaniver tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa saen tha wunnerfu things he daen an heerd tha verie weans creein oot in tha temple gruns hosanna tae tha sinn o davit weel the got wile angrie dae ye hear whut these weans ir sayin the axt jesus ay he reponed hae yis niver read whut tha scriptures say frae oot o tha mooth o childer an weans ye hae brocht wurds o praise an jesus left thaim an he gaed awa oot o tha citie tae bethanie whar he stapt fer tha nicht at tha scraich o day as he wus on his wye bak tae tha citie he wus hungrie an seein a fig tree bi tha road he gaed up tae it but fun naethin on it apairt frae leafs then he saed tae it may ye niver bair fruit agane an at yinst tha tree wuthert up an whaniver his follaers saen this the wur dumfoonert hoo did tha fig tree weezen up an dee sae quick the axt jesus saed a tell ye tha truith if ye hae faith an ye dinnae doot no alane can ye dae whut wus daen tae thon fig tree but ye cud even say tae this muntin be shiftit frae whar ye ir an cast yersel intae tha sea an itll be daen if ye believe god wull gie ye whut ye ax fer in prayer jesus went bak intae tha temple gruns an while he wus taichin tha heid preeshts an tha jewish elders cum up tae him bi whut thortie ir ye daein these things the axt an wha gien ye tha thortie jesus saed a want tae ax ye yin question if ye gie me an answer then all tell ye bi whut thortie a dae these things jhones baptisin whar did it cum frae wus it frae heiven or wus it jist a notion o man the stairtit tae taak aboot it amang thairsels an the saed if we say frae heiven hell ax iz sae hoo cum yis didnae believe him but if we say frae men then we hae tha fowk tae reckon wi fer the aa houl that jhone wus a proaphit sae the saed bak tae jesus we cannae tell an jesus saed then all no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie a dae these things whut dae ye think aboot this thair wus a man that haed twa sinns he gaed tae tha furst yin an saed sinn aff ye gang an wark theday in tha vineyaird a wull not he saed but later on he renaiged an he did go then tha faither gaed tae tha ither sinn an he saed tha same tae him an he saed bak a wull sir but he niver went noo whutch yin o tha twa daen whut his faither wantit tha furst yin the saed jesus reponed a tell ye tha truith tex men an weemen wi a baad name aboot tha toon wull get intae tha kingdom o god aheid o ye fer jhone cum fer tae show ye tha wye o righteousness an ye didnae believe him but tha tex men an tha weemen wi a baad name they did an even efter ye saa this ye didnae repent an believe him listen tae anither parable thair wus this lanlaird that plantit a vineyaird he fenced it aa roon he dug a winepress in it an bigged a lukoot tooer then he set tha vineyaird tae a wheen o tenantfairmers tae rin an gan awa on a thrip tae anither kintrie an whaniver it wus hairvest time he sent his sarvints tae tha fairmers fer tae collect tha fruit tha fairmers tuk houl o his sarvints the bate yin o thaim the put anither tae deith an the staned a thurd then he sent ither sarvints tae thaim mair ner he sent tha furst time an tha fairmers traitit thaim aa tha same wye last o aa he sent his ain sinn tae thaim hes ma ain sinn shairlie thell hae regaird fer him he saed but whaniver tha tenantfairmers saa tha sinn the saed tae yin anither this is tha boy wull tak ower whan his da dees cum on noo an well dae him in an whutiver his da wus fer leain him wull cum tae us sae the tuk houl o him an throwed him oot o tha vineyaird an put him tae deith weel noo saed jesus whaniver tha laird o tha vineyaird cums whut wull he dae tae thaim fairmers he wull bring thaim wickit fairmers tae a tarrible enn the answert an hell set tha vineyaird tae ithers that wull gie him his share o tha crap at hairvest time jesus axt thaim hae yis niver read in tha scriptures tha verie stane tha masons turnt doon is noo tha coarner stane tha loard hissel haes wrocht this an a wunnerfu sicht it is sae a tell ye that tha kingdom o god wull be tuk awa frae ye an be gien tae a nation that wull produce tha fruit it shud him that faas ower this stane wull be smesht tae bits an whaiver it faas on wull be grun tae pooder whan tha heid preeshts an tha pharisees heerd jesus parables the knowed richtlie he wus gettin at thaim the lukt fer a wye tae hae him arrestit but the wur feart o tha thrang acause tha fowk tuk him fer a proaphit jesus spauk tae thaim agane in parables sayin tha kingdom o heiven is laik a king that got a waddin pairtie readie fer his sinn he sent his sarvints tae tha yins that wus axt tae tha pairtie tae tell thaim tae cum but the wudnae cum wi that he sent some mair sarvints tell thaim that haes bin axt he saed that tha spreeds aa readie ma oxen an ma best fattened kwye haes bin killt an iveriethin is readie their tae cum on aheid tae tha waddin but agane the pyed nae heed an the gan aff tha yin tae his fairm an tha ither tae his bizness an thair wus ithers tuk houl o his sarvints traitit thaim wile baad an put thaim tae deith tha king wus ragein he sent oot his sodgers fer tae desthroy thaim murderers an he brunt thair citie doon then he saed tae his sarvints tha waddin pairtie is readie but tha yins a axt didnae desarve tae cum gang tae tha crossroads an ax oniebodie ye fin tae cum tae tha waddin sae tha sarvints gan oot intae tha raas an the gethert aa tha fowk the cud fin baith saint an sinner til tha waddin haal wus fu o guests but whaniver tha king cum in tae see tha guests he saa a bodie thair that haednae waddin claes on him freen he axt hoo did ye git in here wioot claes fit fer a waddin tha man haed naethin tae say then tha king toul his sarvints bine him han an fit an clod him oot intae tha dairk whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth fer a hale lock o fowk is axt but thairs no monie pickt oot then tha pharisees gaed oot an collogued thegither as tae hoo the cud ketch jesus oot in sumthin he wud say an sae the sent thair ain follaers tae him alang wi some men o herods pairtie maister the saed we ken ye spake tha truith an that ye taich fowk tha wye o god accoardin tae tha truith wioot onie thocht o whut ither fowk thinks o ye ye dinnae mak o yin mair ner tha ither sae tell iz whuts yer thinkin is it richt tae pye texes tae caesar or no but jesus kent thair wickit mines an he saed ye hippycrates fer why ir ye tryin tae ketch me oot show me tha coin ye pye tha tex wi the brocht him a denarius an he axt thaim whase name an laikness is on it its caesars the saed then he saed tae thaim sae gie caesar whut belangs tae caesar an gie god whut belangs tae god whaniver the heerd this the wur dumfoonert sae the left him an gan awa that same day tha sadducees that say thair isnae onie risin frae tha deid the cum an pit a question tae jesus maister the saed moses toul iz that if a man dees wioot leain onie weans his brither maun merrie tha weeda an hae childer fer him noo supposin thair wus seiven brithers amang iz tha oulest gets merriet an he dees an seein thair wur nae weans his wife wus left tae his brither tha same thing happent tae tha saicont brither an tha thurd richt on doon tae tha seiventh an bye an bye tha wumman she deed as weel noo then at tha risin frae tha deid whase guidwife wull she be o tha seiven seein she wus merriet tae thaim aa jesus answert ye ir no richt ava fer ye dinnae ken tha scriptures an ye dinnae ken tha pooer o god at tha risin frae tha deid thair wull be nae mair merryin fer whaniver the dee fowk wull be laik tha angels o god in heiven but consarnin tha risin frae tha deid dae yis no mine readin whut god saed tae ye a be tha god o abraham tha god o isaac an tha god o jacob hes no tha god o tha deid hes tha god o tha leevin whaniver tha croods heerd this the wur stoondit at his taichin hearin that jesus haed left tha sadducees wi naethin tae say tha pharisees got thegither an yin o thaim a thortie on tha laa tried tae ketch him oot wi this question maister whuts tha maist impoartin commaun in tha laa jesus saed ye maun love tha loard yer god wi aa yer hairt an wi aa yer sowl an wi aa yer mine this is tha furst an tha maist impoartin commaun an tha saicont yin is laik it ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel tha hale o tha laa an tha proaphits hing on these twa commauns noo whaniver tha pharisees wus gethert roon him thair jesus axt thaim whut dae ye think aboot tha messiah whase sinn is he tha sinn o davit the answert he saed tae thaim then hoo is it that davit spakin bi tha spirit caas him loard fer he says tha loard saed tae ma loard sit doon at ma richt han tae a pit yer enemies unner yer feet sae if davit caas tha messiah ma loard hoo can he be his sinn as weel an naebodie haed a wurd tae say bak tae him an frae that day on naebodie wud dar ax him onie mair questions then jesus saed tae tha croods an tae his follaers tha maisters o tha laa an tha pharisees sits in moses sait sae ye maun obey thaim an dae iveriethin the tell ye but dinnae dae tha same as thaim fer the dinnae prectis whut the praich the tye up heavie burdens owerwechtie tae cairt an the pit thaim on fowks shooders but they thairsels ir no wullin tae lift a fingr tae halp thaim iveriethin the dae is daen fer men tae see the mak thair phylacteries extrae wide an tha taussels on thair clokes extrae lang the love tae be at tha tap table at faists an tae hae tha best saits in tha meetin hooses the laik men tae touch thair keps tae thaim in tha mairket places an tae caa thaim rabbi but yous ir tae let naebodie caa you rabbi fer yis hae onlie tha yin maister an yis ir aa brithers an dinnae caa oniebodie on irth faither fer yis hae onlie tha yin faither an he is in heiven nether let oniebodie caa ye leader fer yis hae onlie tha yin leader an thats christ tha maist impoartin amang ye maun be yer sarvint fer whaiver sets hissel up wull be brocht doon a peg an whaiver hummles hissel wull be hel in heich regaird wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates fer ye shut tha dure o tha kingdom o heiven in fowks faces you yersels dinnae enter an yisll no alloo thaim tae enter thats tryin tae git in wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates fer ye swallae up weedas hooses an ye mak lang prayers fer a show sae yisll be condemned aa tha mair wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates fer ye trevel ower lan an sea tae git a singl convert an whaniver he cums roon tae yer wye o thinkin ye mak him twice as much a sinn o hell as yis ir yersels wae faa ye blin guides ye say if oniebodie sweers bi tha hoose o god it mains naethin but if oniebodie sweers bi tha gowld o tha hoose o god hell be hel tae his oath ye blin coofs ye whuts mair impoartin tha gowld or tha hoose o god that maks tha gowld halie ye say as weel if oniebodie sweers bi tha althar it mains naethin but if oniebodie sweers bi tha gift on it he is bun bi his oath ye blin men whuts mair impoartin tha gift or tha althar that maks tha gift halie sae tha yin that sweers bi tha althar sweers bi it ay an bi iveriethin on it as weel an him that sweers bi tha hoose o god sweers bi it an bi tha yin that leeves in it an tha yin that sweers bi heiven sweers bi gods throne an bi tha yin that sits on tha throne wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates ye gie a tenth o yer gairden spices yer mint dill an cummin but yis hae neglectit tha mair impoartin metters o tha laa justice mercie an faith gie yer tenth but dinnae ferget tae be fair an kine tae ithers as weel ye blin guides ye strain oot a midge but ye swallae a kemel wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates ye waash tha ootside o tha bickers an tha plates but tha inside o thaims fu o whut ye got bi yer plunnerin an greed blin pharisee furst clain tha inside o tha bicker an tha plate an then tha ootside wull be clain as weel wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates ye ir laik whitewaashed graves that luk quare an nice on tha ootside but on tha inside ther fu o deid mens banes an iveriethin thats no clain in tha same wye on tha ootside fowk wud think ye wur guid leevin but on tha inside yer fu o hypocrisie an wickitness wae faa ye maisters o tha laa an pharisees ye hippycrates fer yis big tombs fer tha proaphits an fancie monuments fer guid men o lang syne an ye say if we haed hae leeved in tha days o oor forefaithers we wudnae hae bin pairtie tae sheddin tha bluid o tha proaphits in sayin that yer wutnesses agin yersels yer bred frae thaim that murdered tha proaphits sae ye ir gang aheid feenish aff whut yer forefaithers begun ye snakes ye shooer o vipers hoo wull ye escape bein condemned tae hell sae am gaun tae senn ye proaphits an wise men an taichers some o thaim yell kill an hing on a cross ithers yell whup in yer meetin hooses an yell hunt thaim frae toon tae toon acause o this on your heids wull faa tha bluid o aa tha upricht fowk that haes iver bin spillt on tha irth frae tha killin o that guid man abel tae tha killin o zechariah sinn o barachiah him that ye murdered in tha hoose o god atween tha halie o halies an tha althar a tell ye tha truith tha judgemen fer aa this wull faa doon on this verie generation o jerusalem jerusalem you that kill tha proaphits an stane thaim thats sent tae ye monies tha time a wantit tae gether yer weans thegither laik a hen gethers hir lachter o wee burds unner hir wings but yis wudnae let me luk yer hoose haes bin forsook an noo its empie fer a tell ye this yell no see me agane til ye say blisst is tha yin that cums in tha name o tha loard as jesus wus waakin awa frae tha temple gruns his follaers cum up an saed tae him wud ye jist luk at thaim biggins dae ye see aa these things he axt thaim am tellin ye no yin stane here wull be left abain tha ither thell aa be tummelt doon an later on as jesus wus sittin on tha moont o olives tha follaers cum tae him on his lane tell iz the saed whan wull aa this cum aboot an whut wull be tha sign o yer cumin an o tha enn o tha age jesus saed bak tae thaim tak heed an dinnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee fer monies a yin wull cum in ma name sayin a be tha christ an thell lead monie fowk aglee ye wull hear tell o wars an o taak aboot wars but dinnae be put aboot fer sitch things maun happen but tha enn is no near jist yit nations wull mak war on ither nations an kingdoms wull rise up agin ither kingdoms thair wull be dirths plagues an irthquakes in monie pairts aa this is onlie tha stairt o tha bairin pains cumin on then yell be hannit ower tae be persecutit an put tae deith an yell be haitit bi aa nations jist fer bein ma follaers at that time a hale lock o fowk wull turn awa frae tha faith an thell bethray an hait yin anither a hale lock o fauss proaphits wull rise up an lead monies a yin asthray an acause wickitness wull be on tha up tha love o maist fowk wull growe coul but tha yin that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved an tha guid news o tha kingdom wull be praicht in tha hale warl as a wutness tae aa tha nations an then tha enn wull cum sae whaniver ye see tha abomination o desolation stannin in tha halie place tha abomination tha proaphit daniel spauk aboot reader yell unnerstan ma mainin here then thaim ats in judea maun tak tae tha hills naebodie thats on his ruiftap shud gae doon tae tak oniethin oot o tha hoose an naebodie thats awa oot in his fiel shud be gaun bak fer his coat in thaim days itll be tarrible fer weemen thats expectin an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht pray tae god that ye dinnae hae tae flee in tha wunter or on tha sabbath fer then thairll be sitch despert sufferin faur waur ner thair iver wus frae tha stairt o tha warl til noo an tha laik o thisll niver be saen agane if thaim days wurnae shoartent thair wud be naebodie left but fer tha sake o tha chosen yins thaim days wull be shoartent at that time if oniebodie says tae ye luk here is tha messiah or thair he is dinnae tak onie heed fer fauss messiahs an fauss proaphits wull rise up an dae michtie signs an wunners an fowk wull be tuk in bi thaim ay an if ther able the wull fool even tha chosen yins as weel luk a hae toul ye aforehan sae as yell know sae then if oniebodie tells ye thair he is oot in tha wulderness dinnae gae oot or hes hidin here in tha hoose dinnae believe it fer jist as tha lichtnin fleshes ower tha lift frae tha east tae tha wast thats whut tha cumin o tha sinn o man wull be laik whariver ye see a crood o vulters ye know thairs a deid bodie thair al at yinst efter tha sufferin o thaim days tha sin wull be dairkint tha muin wull no gie onie licht tha starns wull faa frae tha heivens an tha pooers o tha lift wull be dinnelt an then tha sign o tha sinn o man wull appear in tha heivens abain an aa tha nations o tha irth wull murn thell see tha sinn o man cumin on tha cloods o heiven wi pooer an muckle glorie hell senn his angels oot wi a lood caa o tha trumpet an thell gether his chosen yins frae tha fower wuns frae tha yin enn o heiven tae tha tither noo lairn this lesson frae tha fig tree as shuin as its brenches stairts tae bud an its leafs cum oot ye ken tha simmer is no faur aff in tha same wye whaniver ye see aa these things yell ken tha time is nearhan ay richt at tha verie dure a tell ye tha truith thairs fowks leevin noo thatll no dee afore aa these things haes cum aboot heiven an irth wull pass awa but ma wurds wull niver pass awa hooaniver naebodie knows tha day an tha oor o aa this no even tha angels in heiven ner tha sinn tha faither alane kens it whaniver tha sinn o man cums bak itll be jist laik it wus in noahs day fer in tha days afore tha flood fowk wus aitin an drinkin an gettin merriet richt up tae tha verie day noah went intae tha airk an the kent naethin aboot whut wud happen til tha flood cum an tuk thaim al awa an thats whut itll be laik whaniver tha sinn o man cums bak twa men wull be at wark in tha fiel yin wull be tuk an tha ither left behin twa weemen wull be grindin mail yin wull be tuk an tha ither left behin sae yous keep watchin tae fer yis dinnae ken whut day yer loards cumin ye can be shair o this if ye haed a hoose an ye knowed whut oor o tha nicht a thief wus cumin yed be watchin fer him wud ye no an ye wudnae alloo yer hoose tae be brauk intae sae yous maun be readie tae fer ye dinnae ken tha oor tha sinn o man wull cum wha is a sarvint yed caa faithfu an wise is it no tha yin that tha maister haes put in chairge o tha ither sarvints in his hoose tae gie thaim thair fair share o mait at tha richt time whaniver his maister cums bak onie sarvint ectin laik this wull be a happie man a tell ye tha truith hell pit that sarvint in chairge o iveriethin he haes but jist say that sarvint is wickit an says tae hissel hes a lang time o cumin tha maister an he stairts tae bate up his fella sarvints an tae ait an collogue wi thaim thats fand o tha drink weel tha maister o that sarvint wull cum bak on a day an oor whan tha sarvint isnae lukkin oot fer him an tha maister wull dae awa wi him an pit him alang wi tha hippycrates ye can be shair that whar they wull be thairll be greetin an scringein o teeth then tha kingdom o heiven wull be laik ten lasses that tuk thair lamps an gaed oot fer tae meet tha bridegruim five o thaim wus wutless an five o thaim wus wise tha yins wi nae wut tuk thair lamps but didnae tak eneuch oiyle alang wi thaim tha wise yins but they tuk jars o oiyle alang wi thair lamps tha bridegruim wus a lang time cumin an the aa becum that sleepie the drapt aff at midnicht tha cry rung oot heres tha bridegruim cum on oot an meet him then aa tha lasses waakent up an the trimmed thair lamps tha yins wi nae wut saed tae tha wise yins oor lamps is gaun oot gie iz a drap o yer oiyle na the answert fer mebbe thairll no be eneuch fer iz aa awa tae thaim that sells tha oiyle an buy some fer yersels but while the wur on thair wye fer tae buy tha oiyle here didnae tha bridegruim turn up tha lasses that haed made readie gaed wi him intae tha waddin pairtie an tha dure wus shut efter a while tha ither lasses cum bak sir sir the saed wull ye no apen tha dure tae iz but he answert a tell ye tha truith a know naethin aboot ye an jesus warnt thaim yer tae watch oot al o yis fer ye dinnae ken tha day or tha oor all be bak agane tha kingdom o heiven wull be laik a man gaun aff on his trevels wha caad his sarvints thegither an pit thaim in chairge o aa he haed tae tha yin he gien five baags o siller tae anither twa baags an tae anither jist tha yin baag accoardin tae whut he knowed the cud dae wi it then aff he went on his thrip strecht awa tha sarvint that got tha five baags begun tae put his siller tae wark an he got bak five mair an tha yin wi tha twa baags got twa mair bak as weel but him that haed bin gien jist tha yin baag he gaed aff digged a hole in tha grun an hid his maisters siller noo efter a lang time tha maister o thaim sarvints cum bak an axt thaim tae gie an accoont o whut thed daen wi his siller tha man that haed bin gien tha five baags cum forrit an brocht wi him tha ither five maister he saed ye hannit ower five baags tae me luk a hae got five mair fer ye his maister saed ye hae daen weel ye guid an faithfu sarvint ye hae showed a can trust ye wi wee things sae all pit ye in chairge o a hale lock mair cum alang wi me an share yer maisters happiness tha man wi tha twa baags o siller cum forrit as weel an he saed maister ye hannit ower twa baags tae me luk see a hae got twa mair fer ye his maister saed ye hae daen weel ye guid an faithfu sarvint ye hae showed a can trust ye wi wee things sae all pit ye in chairge o a hale lock mair cum alang wi me an share yer maisters happiness then alang cum tha man that wus gien tha yin baag o siller maister he saed a kent ye wur a haird man ye hairvest whar ye hinnae plantit an ye gether whar ye hinnae sowed sae a wus feart an gaed oot an hid yer siller in tha grun luk heres whut belangs tae ye his maister saed ye uisless guidfernaethin sae ye thocht did ye that a hairvest whar a hinnae plantit an a gether whar a hinnae sowed weel then ye shud hae put ma siller in tha bank sae a wud hae got it bak wi intrest whaniver a cum bak tak tha baag awa frae him he oardert an gie it tae tha yin that haes tha ten fer iverie yin that haes wull be gien mair an hell hae mair ner eneuch an whaiver haes little or naethin even tha wee bit he haes wull be taen awa frae him noo jist cast that guid fer naethin sarvint oot intae tha dairk whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth an jesus went on tae say this whaniver tha sinn o man cums in his glorie an aa tha angels alang wi him hell sit on his throne in heivenlie glorie afore him aa tha nations wull be gethert thegither an hell set apairt tha fowk yin frae tha ither jist laik a shepherd sets apairt tha sheep frae tha gaits he wull pit tha sheep on his richt han an tha gaits on his left then tha king wull say tae tha yins on his richt han cum yous that ir blisst bi ma faither tak houl o yer inheritance tha kingdom makkit readie fer ye frae tha time tha warl begun fer a wus hungrie an ye fed me a haed a druith on me an ye gien me sumthin tae drink a wus an ootsider an ye tuk me in a haednae a dud o claes tae ma bak an ye gien me some a wus seeck an ye lukt efter me a wus in jail an ye cum an visitit me then tha righteous fowk wull say bak tae him loard whan wus it we saa ye hungrie an gien ye mait or wi a druith on ye an gien ye a drink whan wus it we saa ye an ootsider an tuk ye in or wioot a dud an we gien ye some claes whan did we see ye seeck or in jail an went an visitit ye tha king wull answer a tell ye tha truith whutiver ye daen fer yin o tha laist impoartin o these brithers o mine ye daen it fer me an then hell say tae tha yins on his left han awa wi ye yous that ir curst awa intae tha iverlastin fire thats readie an waitin fer tha deil an his angels fer a wus hungrie an yis gien me naethin tae ait a haed a druith on me an yis gien me naethin tae drink a wus a ootsider an yis didnae tak me in a haednae a dud an yis didnae gie me onie a wus seeck an in jail an yis didnae luk efter me an thaim yins wull say as weel loard whan did we see ye hungrie or wi a druith or an ootsider or needin claes or seeck or in jail an we did naethin tae halp ye an hell repone a tell ye tha truith whutiver yis didnae dae fer yin o tha laist impoartin o these brithers o mine yis didnae dae it fer me then awa thell gae intae iverlastin punishment but fer tha righteous fowk itll be intae iverlastin life whaniver jesus haed daen sayin aa these things he saed tae his follaers ye ken tha passower is tha day efter themorra an tha sinn o man wull be hannit ower fer tae be nailt tae a cross then tha heid preeshts an tha elders o tha fowk gethert thegither in tha palace o tha heich preesht a man bi tha name o caiaphas an the cumpluthert fer tae git tha houl o jesus bi some sleekit wye an pit him tae deith but no whan tha faists on the saed or well hae a garevitch on oor hans aa tha while jesus wus in bethanie in tha hoose o simon tha leper an a wumman cum up tae him wi a wee crock o scent perfume that wus wile dear that she poored ower his heid as he wus restin at tha boord but whaniver tha follaers saen this the wur wile angrie why this waste the axt this perfume cud hae bin soul fer a big price an tha siller gien tae tha puir knowin weel whut the wur sayin jesus saed tae thaim dinnae bother tha wumman this is a guid thing she haes daen fer me fer yell aye hae tha puir wi yis but yell no aye hae me whaniver she poored this perfume on ma bodie she daen it fer tae mak me readie fer ma buryin am tellin ye tha truith whariver in tha hale warl this guid news is praicht hir storie wull be toul sae as shell niver be fergot then yin o tha twal tha yin caad judas iscariot went tae tha heid preeshts an he axt thaim whut ir yis wullin tae gie me if a han jesus ower tae yis sae the settelt fer thurtie siller coins frae then on judas wus lukkin fer a chaunce tae han him ower on tha furst day o tha faist o bairmless breid tha follaers cum tae jesus an axt him whar dae ye want iz tae mak tha passower mail readie fer ye he saed gang intae tha citie an yell see this man tell him tha maister says ma time is nearhan an am gaun tae celebrate tha passower wi ma follaers at yer hoose sae his follaers daen jist as jesus haed bid thaim an the made readie tha boord fer tha passower mail whan tha evenin wus weel on jesus wus at tha boord alang wi tha twal an while the wur aitin he saed a tell ye tha truith yin o yis is fer bethrayin me the wur aa fu o sorra whaniver the heerd this an yin efter tha ither stairtit tae say tae him shairlie its no me ye main loard jesus saed thairs yin thats dippt his han in tha boul wi me wull bethray me tha sinn o man maun follae tha road tha scriptures foretoul lang syne but wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays him it wud be faur better fer that man if he haed niver bin boarn then judas tha yin that wus gaun tae bethray him saed shairlie its no me ye main rabbi jesus answert him its you haes saed it while the wur aitin jesus tuk breid in his hans an whaniver he haed gien thenks tae god he brauk it an hannit it tae his follaers sayin tak this an ait it this is ma bodie then he tuk a bicker o wine he gien thenks tae god fer it an he hannit it roon sayin al o yis drink frae this this is ma bluid its a sign o gods new coveynant an its poored oot tae forgie monie thair wrangdaeins a tell ye all no drink o this fruit o tha vine agane na no til tha day a drink a new wine alang wi you in ma faithers kingdom wi that the sung tha passower psaum an the went oot on tae tha moont o olives an then jesus toul thaim this verie nicht al o yis wull faa awa on accoont o me fer as its writ a wull strike tha shepherd an tha sheep o tha flock wull be scattert but efter a hae ris frae tha deid all tak tha foreroad o ye intae galilee an peter spauk oot tha mair tha restll faa awa becas o ye a niver wull a tell ye tha truith jesus saed bak this verie nicht afore tha rooster craas yell say thrie times ower that ye dinnae ken me but peter spauk oot agane een if a hae tae dee alang wi ye a wull niver deny ye an aa tha ither follaers vood tha same then jesus gaed wi his follaers tae a place caad gethsemane an he toul thaim sit here while a gang ower thair an pray he tuk peter an tha twa sinns o zebedee alang wi him an he begun tae be wile sorrafu an gye troublet then he saed tae thaim ma hairts brekkin wi anguish near tae deith yous bide here an stye awaak wi me he gan forrit a weethin then he bood doon wi his face tae tha grun an he prayed ma faither if it is poassible may this cup o sufferin be tuk awa frae me yit its your wull am wantin an no ma ain then he cum bak tae his follaers an he fun thaim sleepin cud you men no keep watch fer yin oor wi me he axt peter watch an pray sae ye dinnae gie in tae temptation tha spirits wullin but tha bodies waik he went awa a saicont time an he prayed o ma faither if thairs naethin else fer it an if a hae tae drink this cup o sufferin may your wull be daen an whaniver he cum bak yinst mair he fun thaim sleepin fer the cudnae keep thair een apen sae he left thaim an he gan awa agane an prayed tha thurd time sayin tha same thing then he cum bak tae his follaers an he saed tae thaim ir yis still sleepin an takkin yer rest but luk here tha time haes cum tha sinn o man is bethrayed intae tha hans o wrangdaers git up noo an well be aff luk ma bethrayers here tha wurds wus harlie oot o his mooth whan up cum judas yin o tha twal alang wi him wus a big thrang airmed wi swords an stavs sent oot frae tha heid preeshts an tha elders o tha fowk noo tha bethrayer haed warkt oot a sign wi thaim tha yin a kiss is tha man yer lukkin tak tha houl o him sae judas gaed strecht up tae jesus an he saed greetins rabbi an he kisst him jesus saed freen dae whut ye cum here fer then tha men cum forrit the tuk houl o jesus an arrestit him wi that yin o tha men wi jesus raxt fer his sword he pued it oot an hut tha sarvint o tha heich preesht an he sneddit aff his lug pit yer sword awa jesus saed tae him fer aa that draas tha sword wull dee bi tha sword dae ye no ken that if a wantit tae a cud caa on ma faither an he wud senn thoosans o angels tae halp me but hoo then wud tha scriptures be fulfilled that say it maun cum aboot tha wye wer seein noo at that time jesus saed tae tha crood am a some soart o a reiver that yis hae cum oot agin me wi swords an stavs fer tae tak me shair a sut in tha hoose o god iverie day taichin an yis niver layed a han on me but this haes aa tuk place sae that whut wus writ bi tha proaphits micht cum aboot then aa his follaers left him an run awa tha yins that haed liftit jesus tuk him awa tae caiaphas tha heich preesht whar tha maisters o tha laa an tha elders o tha fowk haed gethert thegither but peter follaed him a brave wye behin richt up tae tha coortyaird o tha heich preesht he went intae it an sut doon wi tha gairds tae see whut wud happen noo tha heid preeshts an tha hale cooncil wus lukkin fer men that wud wutness agin jesus sae the cud pit him tae deith but the didnae fin onie wi stories that wud dae tha mair monie fauss wutnesses spauk oot bye an bye twa steppit forrit sayin this fella saed a be able tae desthroy tha hoose o god an big it up agane in thrie days then tha heich preesht ris tae his feet an saed tae jesus hae ye nae answer tae these chairges whut hae ye tae say fer yersel but jesus hel his tung an tha heich preesht saed tae him a chairge ye unner oath bi tha leevin god tell iz if ye ir tha christ tha sinn o god its as ye say jesus answert but am tellin yis aa that in a day tae cum yisll see tha sinn o man sittin at tha richt han o tha michtie yin an cumin on tha cloods o heiven then tha heich preesht tore his claes an saed he haes spauk blesphemie whut dae we need onie mair wutnesses fer luk noo ye hae aa heerd his blesphemie fer yersels whut dae ye think he desarves tae be put tae deith the answert then the sput in his face an hut him wi thair fists ithers hut him wi tha flet o thair hans an the saed weel messiah tell iz wha skelpt ye noo peter wus sittin oot in tha coortyaird an this wee sarvin lass cum up til him you wur wi jesus o galilee as weel she saed but he denied it afore thaim aa a dinnae ken whut yer taakin aboot qo he then he slipt oot tae tha gate whar anither lass saen him an saed tae tha fowk stannin roon this fella wus alang wi jesus o nazareth yinst mair he denied it an wi an oath a dinnae ken tha man efter a wee while tha yins that wur stannin thair went up tae peter an saed shairlie ye maun be yin o thaim fer tha wye ye taak gies ye awa then he stairtit cursin an sweerin an sayin a dinnae ken tha man an at that verie minit a rooster craad then peter haed mine o tha wurds jesus haed spauk afore tha rooster craas yell deny me thrie times an he went oot o tha coortyaird greetin sair at tha scraich o day aa tha heid preeshts an tha elders o tha fowk collogued thegither as tae hoo the wud pit jesus tae deith sae the tyed him up the maircht him aff an the hannit him ower tae pilate tha guviner noo judas that haed bethrayed him whaniver he saa that jesus wus condemned he sairlie rued whut hed daen an he gien tha thurtie siller coins bak tae tha heid preeshts an tha elders a hae daen wrang saed he fer a hae bethrayed tha bluid o an innocent man whuts that tae us the saed on yer ain heid be it sae judas throwed tha siller doon in tha hoose o god then he gan oot o tha temple an he went an hung hissel tha heid preeshts gethert up tha coins an saed it is agin tha laa tae pit this intae tha temple kist seein as its tha price o bluid sae the agreed amang thairsels tae uise tha siller fer tae buy tha potters fiel as a buryin grun fer strangers an thats tha raison tae this verie day its caad tha fiel o bluid in this wye tha wurd spauk bi jeremiah tha proaphit cum aboot the tuk tha thurtie siller coins tha amoont pit on his heid bi israel an the uised thaim tae buy tha potters fiel jist as tha loard commaundit while aa this wus gaun on jesus stud afore tha guviner an tha guviner axt him ir you tha king o tha jews jesus answert you hae saed it but whaniver he wus accused bi tha heid preeshts an tha elders he gien nae answer ava then pilate axt him dae ye no hear whut ther chairgin ye wi but jesus niver saed a wurd bak tae him regairdin onie o tha chairges agin him an tha guviner wus stoondit noo it uist tae be at tha passower faist tha guviner wud aye let a prisner oot o jail whutiver yin tha fowk axt fer an that year the haed a prisner iveriebodie haed heerd tell o bi tha name o barabbas sae whaniver tha crood haed gethert thegither pilate axt thaim whutch yin dae yis want me tae let oot tae ye barabbas or jesus that is caad christ fer he knowed richt weel it wus jist oot o spite the haed hannit jesus ower tae him noo as pilate wus sittin on tha judges sait his wife sent him this message hae naethin tae dae wi thon innocent man fer am tellin ye am sair tormentit this day bi a draim a haed aboot him but tha heid preeshts an tha elders taakt tha crood roon sae as the wud ax fer barabbas an hae jesus put tae deith whutch o tha twa dae yis want me tae let oot tae yis then axt tha guviner we want barabbas the answert sae whut am a tae dae wi jesus thats caad tha christ pilate axt an the aa saed bak tae tha cross wi him but whut fer whuts he daen wrang axt pilate but tha thrang jist roared aa tha mair tae tha cross wi him whaniver pilate saen that he wus gettin naewhar but that he wus aboot tae hae a riot on his hans he got some watter an waasht his hans afore tha crood o fowk am no guiltie o this mans bluid saed he on your heids be it aa tha fowk saed let his bluid be on us an on oor childer then he lut barabbas oot tae thaim but he got jesus whuppt an he hannit him ower fer tae be crucyfied then tha guviners sodgers tuk jesus intae tha praetorium an the gethert tha hale regiment roon him the stript him an put a scarlet robe on him an then the plettit thoarns thegither tae mak a croon an the set it on his heid the put a stav in his richt han an the got doon on thair knees afore him mockin him an sayin lang leeve tha king o tha jews the sput on him an the tuk tha stav an hut him ower tha heid agane an agane an efter the haed daen mockin him the tuk tha robe aff him an the put his ain claes bak on him then the tuk him awa fer tae crucyfie him an whaniver the wur on thair wye oot the run intae a man frae cyrene bi tha name o simon an the gart him tae cairrie tha cross the cum tae a place caad golgotha mainin tha place o tha skull thair the raxt wine up tae jesus mixt wi gall but efter tastin it he wudnae drink onie mair noo whaniver tha sodgers haed nailt him tae tha cross the gemmelt amang thairsels tae divide his claes this brocht aboot whut tha proaphit saed wud happen the divid ma dishables amang thaim an the cloddit dice fer ma claes an sittin doon the kep watch ower him thair abain his heid the put up tha chairge agin him that saed this is jesus tha king o tha jews twa robbers wur crucyfied alang wi him yin on his richt han side an tha tither on his left thaim at waakt bye yellt abuse at him shakin thair heids an sayin hey you that saed ye wur gaun tae desthroy tha hoose o god an big it agane in thrie days save yersel if you ir tha sinn o god cum doon aff that cross an tha heid preeshts tha maisters o tha laa an tha elders the daen tha same an the mockt him he saved ithers the saed but he cannae save hissel is he no tha king o israel then jist let him cum doon aff tha cross an well believe in him he trusts in god let god rescue him noo if he wants him fer he saed a be tha sinn o god tha robbers that wur crucyfied wi him hurlt abuse at him as weel frae nuin tae thrie in tha efternuin dairkness cum ower tha hale lan an roon aboot thrie jesus caad oot wi a lood voice eli eli lama sabachthani that mains o god ma god why hae ye forsook me whaniver some o thaim stannin bye heerd this the saed hes caain oot fer elijah an richt awa yin o thaim run an got a sponge he fillt it wi soor wine put it on a lang stick an raxt it up tae jesus fer him tae drink but tha ithers saed jist lea him alane well see noo if elijah cums fer tae save him then jesus cryed oot agane wi a lood voice an he gien up his spirit at that verie minit tha curtin in tha halie o halies wus tore in twa frae tap tae bottom tha irth shuk an tha roaks split tha graves apent an tha bodies o monie halie fowk that haed deed wur ris tae life the cum oot o thair tombs an efter jesus wus ris frae tha deid the went intae tha halie citie an appeart tae a lock o fowk tha centurion an thaim alang wi him that wus gairdin jesus whaniver the saa tha irthquake an aa that haed happent the wur hairtscarred an the saed thair can be nae doot this wus tha sinn o god noo monie weemen wur thair as weel stannin awa bak takkin it aa in the haed follaed jesus frae galilee fer tae luk efter him in amang thaim thair wus mary magdalene an mary tha mither o jeames an joses an thair wus tha mither o zebedees sinns whan it cum evenin thair wus this weelaff man frae arimathea bi tha name o joseph wha hissel haed becum a follaer o jesus an he gan tae pilate an he axt fer tha bodie o jesus an pilate oardert thaim tae gie it tae him joseph tuk tha bodie an he lapt it in a clain linen claith an he layed it in his ain new tomb he haed cut oot o tha roak he rowlt a big stane agin tha mooth o tha tomb an then he gaed awa mary magdalene an tha ither mary wur sittin thair fornent tha tomb tha nixt day tha yin efter tha day o preparation tha heid preeshts an tha pharisees went tae pilate sir the saed whaniver that deceiver wus still leevin we mine him sayin efter thrie days a wull rise agane sae wud ye gie tha oarder fer thaim tae shut that tomb weel tae tha thurd day less his follaers cum an steal tha bodie an tell tha fowk he haes ris frae tha deid then that deception wud be waur ner tha furst tak gairds wi ye saed pilate awa an shut up tha tomb as weel as ye can sae the gaed an made tha tomb safe bi sealin tha stane an leain tha gaird tae keep watch it wus efter tha sabbath at daylicht on tha furst day o tha week an mary magdalene an tha ither mary cum tae luk at tha tomb aa o a suddent thair wus a michtie irthquake fer an angel o tha loard cum doon frae heiven he gaed tae tha tomb an he rowlt bak tha stane an he sut on it he wus bricht as lichtnin an his claes wus white as snaa whaniver the saa him tha gairds at tha tomb shuk wi fear an the becum laik deid men but tha angel saed tae tha weemen dinnae be feart fer a ken that yer lukkin fer jesus that wus crucyfied hes no here hes ris jist as he saed he wud cum an see tha place whar he wus layed oot quick gae an tell his follaers he haes ris frae tha deid an hes awa on aheid o ye intae galilee yell see him thair noo mine whut a hae toul ye sae tha weemen hurriet frae tha tomb the wur afeart yit fu o joy the run tae tell his follaers whan aa o a suddent jesus appeart fornent thaim fair faa ye saed he an the went tae him tuk houl o his feet an wurshipt him then jesus saed tae thaim dinnae be feart gae an tell ma brithers tae gae intae galilee an thell see me thair while tha weemen wur on thair wye some o tha gairds went intae tha citie an toul tha heid preeshts aa that haed cum aboot an whaniver tha heid preeshts haed gethert thegither wi tha elders the collogued amang thairsels an the gien tha sodgers a big amoont o siller an the toul thaim yer tae say tha follaers o jesus cum in tha nicht an stole him awa whan we wur sleepin if tha guviner hears tell o this well taak him roon an keep ye oot o bother sae tha sodgers tuk tha siller an daen as the wur toul an this storie haes gan roon amang tha jews tae this verie day then tha eleiven follaers gaed tae galilee tae tha muntin whar jesus haed toul thaim whaniver the saen him the wurshipt him but some aye haed thair doots then jesus cum tae thaim an saed aa thortie haes bin gien tae me in heiven an on irth sae gang an mak follaers o aa nations baptisin thaim in tha name o tha faither an o tha sinn an o tha halie spirit taichin thaim tae keep aa tha commauns a hae gien ye an know this a be wi ye iverie day ay tae tha verie enn o time this is tha stairt o tha guid wittins aboot jesus christ tha sinn o god jist as it wus writ doon in isaiah tha proaphit listen all senn oot ma messenger aheid o ye an he wull mak readie yer wye fer ye thairs a voice cryin oot in tha wiles mak readie tha wye o tha loard mak his pads strecht fer him an sae it cum aboot tha messenger appeart an it wus jhone tha baptiser he leeved oot in tha wiles praichin an tellin tha fowk the shud be baptised fer tae show the haed turnt awa frae thair sins an tae show the haed turnt tae god fer him tae forgie thaim aa tha fowk frae tha kintrie roon aboot judea an aa tha fowk frae tha citie o jerusalem trevelt oot tae him on tha muir an jhone baptised in tha river joardan thaim at confesst thair sins noo jhone wore claes made o kemels hair wi a leather belt roon his middle an he leeved bi aitin gresshoppers an wile honey an tha message he gien wus this efter me thair wull cum yin that is michtier ner me a am no fit tae lowse his buits fer him a hae baptised yis wi watter but yin wull cum that wull baptise yis wi tha halie spirit at thon time jesus cum frae nazareth in galilee an jhone baptised him in tha joardan an whaniver jesus wus cumin oot o tha watter tha heivens apent up an tha spirit cum doon on him laik a doo an a voice cum frae tha heivens sayin ye ir ma sinn ma hairts delicht an am weel plaised wi ye an at yinst tha spirit put him awa intae tha wulderness he wus oot in tha wiles fer fowertie days aa tha time bein tempit bi satan he wus surroonded wi wile anymals an tha angels lukt efter him noo a while later efter jhone wus put intae jail jesus cum intae galilee praichin tha guid news o god tha time haes noo cum he saed an tha kingdom o god is nearhan turn awa frae yer wrangdaeins an believe tha guid news yin day whan jesus wus waakin alang tha loch shore o galilee he saen simon an his brither andra throwin a neyt intae tha watter fer the wrocht at tha fishin cum an follae me saed jesus an a wull mak ye intae fishers o men an at yinst the layed doon thair neyts an the follaed efter him whan he went on a wee bit he saa jeames an his brither jhone tha sinns o zebedee in a boat mennin thair neyts an at yinst jesus caad thaim tae an the cum awa wi him as weel leain thair faither zebedee wi tha hired hans on tha boat an the gaed intae capernaum an whan tha sabbath day cum roon he went intae tha meetin hoose an begun tae taich tha fowk that heerd him wur aa thunnerstruck wi his taichin fer he taicht thaim laik a bodie wi thortie an no laik tha maisters o tha laa noo thair wus this man in thair meetin hoose wi an ill spirit an he scraicht oot lood lea iz alane whut dae ye want wi iz jesus o nazareth hae ye cum here tae dae awa wi iz a ken richt weel wha ye ir ye ir tha halie yin o god but jesus chackt him an saed houl yer wheesht an cum oot o him an tha ill spirit made tha man trimmle an shake then it gie a scraich an cum oot o him the wur aa thunnerstruck an the axt yin anither whuts this noo is this a new taichin fer een tha ill spirits dae as he tells thaim an afore lang tha hale kintrie roon aboot galilee wus hotchin wi tha news an the left tha meetin hoose rael quick an the went alang wi jeames an jhone til tha hoose whar simon an andra leeved noo simons mainlaa wus doon wi a faivir an as shuin as jesus cum in the toul him aboot hir sae he gaed til hir bedside tuk hir han an puud hir up strecht awa she coolt doon an she stairtit tae sarve an luk efter thaim an that evenin whan tha sin haed set the brocht til him aa tha seeck an aa tha yins wi demons tha hale toon wus gethert at tha dure an jesus cured a quare lock o seeck fowk o thair monie ailments an he driv oot a brave wheen o demons but he wudnae let tha demons spake oot fer the kent wha he wus wile earlie tha nixt moarnin whan it wus still dairk jesus got up an left tha hoose an went awa tae a place whar he cud be on his ain fer tae pray an simon an tha yins wi him went oot tae luk fer him whaniver the fun him the saed tae him iverie yins lukkin fer ye an jesus cum bak wi cum on an well gang awa frae here tae tha toons roon aboot a hae tae praich thair as weel fer thats whut a cum here fer tae dae sae he trevelt aa roon aboot galilee praichin in thair meetin hooses an drivin oot demons an this leper cum tae jesus got doon on his knees an begged him if ye hae a mine tae ye can mak me clain feelin wile sorrie fer tha man jesus put his han oot an toucht him sayin a am wullin yer better richt awa tha leprosie quit him an he wus weel agane sae jesus sent him awa sayin tae him am warnin ye noo awa ye gang but tell naebodie jist show yersel tae tha preesht an gie an offerin fer yer cleansin as moses telt iz in tha laa fer a wutness tae yin an aa that yer weel agane but insteed tha man went an toul al roon whut jesus haed daen fer him this meent that jesus cudnae be saen gaun intae a toon he haed tae stay oot in tha kintrie but fowk still cum frae aa roon tae see him efter a wheen o days jesus cum bak tae capernaum an wurd went roon that he wus bak hame an monie fowk gethert thegither an thair wus sitch a thrang thair wus nae mair ruim even ootbye tha dure an jesus wus praichin tha wurd tae thaim then fower men cum tae tha hoose cairryin a paralysed man an as the cudnae git near tae jesus fer tha thrang the digged a hole in tha ruif abain him then the lut doon tha mat throu tha hole the haed made wi thair seeck freen lyin on it an whan jesus saa whut faith the haed he saed tae tha paralysed man ma sinn yer sins is aa forgien noo some maisters o tha laa wus sittin thinkin this ower hoo cum this man dars tae taak laik this the thocht its naethin but blesphemie wha can forgie sins but god alane but jesus knowed thair thochts an cud read thaim laik a buik he saed tae thaim hoo cum yis ir thinkin laik this is it aisier tae tell a paralysed man yer sins is forgien ye or tae tell him get up an waak an tak yer mat wi ye but jist sae as yell ken that tha sinn o man haes tha pooer tae forgie sins here on irth he saed tae tha paralysed man am tellin ye get up on yer feet tak yer mat an awa hame tae yer ain hoose richt awa up he got gethert up his mat an waakit oot in front o thaim aa iveriebodie thocht that this wus a wunnerfu sicht an gien glorie tae god an saed we hae niver saen tha laik o this afore yinst mair jesus gaed doon tae tha loch shore a big crood gethert roon him an he stairtit taichin tha fowk whan he wus waakin alang he saa alphaeuss sinn levi sittin in tha tex mans hut follae me jesus telt him an levi ris up an follaed him sae it cum aboot whan jesus wus haein a bite tae ait at levis hoose monie tex getherers an sinners wus aitin alang wi jesus an his follaers fer thair wus aye a hale crood alang wi him whaniver tha taichers o tha laa an tha pharisees saen him alang wi tha sinners an tex men the axt his follaers whuts he daein aitin wi tex getherers an sinners whan jesus heerd this he saed tae thaim its no tha fowk thats weel that haes need o a docter but thaim thats seeck a hinnae cum fer tae caa guid leevin fowk its sinners a hae cum tae caa noo jhones follaers an tha pharisees wur keepin a fast an some fowk cum tae jesus an axt him hoo cum tha follaers o jhone an tha pharisees keep a fast but your yins dinnae sae jesus cum bak wi this dae ye think fowk wud sit doon at tha spreed in a waddin faist alang wi tha bridegruim an no tak a bite tae ait na as lang as tha bridegruim is wi thaim the cannae fast but tha day wull cum whaniver tha bridegruim wull be tuk awa frae thaim an cum that day thell keep a fast efter aa ye wudnae shew a bit o new claith that haesnae bin shrunk on tae an oul coat if ye dae tha patch wull teer awa tha sides o tha hole an mak it waur nether wud ye pit new wine intae oul wineskins fer if ye dae tha skins wull brust an tha winell be skailt an baith tha wine an tha skins wull be ruint but ye maun pit new wine intae new skins yin sabbath day jesus wus waakin throu tha coarnfiels an as the wur makkin thair wye his follaers stairtit tae pluck tha heids aff tha coarn an tha pharisees saed tae jesus luk the shudnae be daein that thats agin tha laa on tha sabbath day jesus saed tae thaim hae ye no read aboot whut davit daen whaniver him an his freens wus hungrie an in want did he no gang intae tha hoose o god whan abiathar wus tha heich preesht an did he no ait tha halie showbreid an gie it tae tha ithers wi him forbye shair that wus agin tha laa fer naebodie but tha preeshts cud ait it an jesus went on tae say tha sabbath wus made fer man man wusnae made fer tha sabbath sae tha sinn o man is loard o tha sabbath anaa an jesus went bak intae tha meetin hoose agane an thair wus a man thair an his richt han wus wuthert an tha pharisees kep thair een on him tae see wud he hail tha man on a sabbath day fer if he did the cud hae sumthin agin him jesus saed tae tha man wi tha baad han stan up whar we can aa see ye then he saed tae tha fowk roon him on tha sabbath is it richt tae dae guid or tae dae ill tae save life or tae dae awa wi it but the hel thair wheesht he turnt roon an gien thaim an angrie luk an at tha same time he wus vext the wur that hairdhairtit he saed tae tha man streetch oot yer han sae he streetcht it oot an his han cum as guid as tha ither yin richt awa tha pharisees went oot an collogued wi herods follaers tae see hoo the cud dae awa wi jesus but jesus tuk hissel aff wi his follaers tae tha loch alang wi a wile thrang o fowk that cum frae galilee judea jerusalem an idumea frae tha ither side o tha joardan an even frae tyre an sidon fer wurd o his miracles haed trevelt faur an wide tha crood wus that big jundyin roon him on tha shore that he toul his follaers tae mak a wee boat readie fer him fer he haed hailt that monie fowk that aa tha yins wi an ailment pusht forrit tae touch him an whaniver fowk wi ill spirits saa jesus the faad doon afore him an tha spirits cryed oot you ir tha sinn o god an he aye chairged thaim no tae tell oniebodie wha he wus then jesus went ontae a muntin an he caad tha yins he wantit wi him an the cum tae him an he pickt oot twal tae be wi him that he cud senn oot tae praich an tae hae tha pooer tae hail tha seeck an tae drive oot demons he gien tha twal tha name o possels an this is whut the wus caad simon that jesus caad peter jeames an jhone tha sinns o zebedee jesus caad thaim boanerges mainin sinns o thunner andra philip bartholomew mattha tammas jeames tha sinn o alphaeus thaddaeus simon tha zealot an judas iscariot tha yin that bethrayed jesus sae jesus went bak intae tha hoose whar he wus stappin ower an thair wus that monie fowk croodin roon aboot thaim that the cud get nae peace tae hae oniethin tae ait becas o whut wus happenin jesus freens tried tae tak tha houl o him fer the thocht he wus oot o his mine an some maisters o tha laa cum frae jerusalem saed beelzebul haes taen him ower its tha heidyin o tha demons thats giein him tha pooer tae cast oot ither demons an jesus caad thaim ower tae him an raisoned wi thaim sayin hoo can satan cast hissel oot if a kingdom is divid agin itsel it maun faa sinnerie an if a femlie is divid agin itsel it cannae stan sae if satan rises up agin hissel an is divid then he cannae stan an thats tha enn o him shair naebodie can brek intae a strang mans hoose an ramseck it afore he haes tyed up tha strang man efter that he can plunner awa a tell ye this men can be forgien blesphemies an aa ither kines o wrangdaeins thairll be nae forgiein fer him that spakes blesphemies agin tha halie spirit but fer that sin an tha guilt o it bides fer iver an aye noo jesus saed aa this becas tha fowk cum frae jerusalem wur chairgin him wi haein an ill spirit an tha mither an brithers o jesus cum lukkin him at tha hoose whar he wus stappin an the caad fer him tae cum oot summodie in tha crood sittin listenin tae him toul him yer mither an yer brithers an sisters ir ootbye the ir wantin ye an jesus cum bak wi whas ma mither an whas ma brithers an he lukt at tha crood sittin aa roon him an saed these yins here ir ma mither an brithers fer thaim at daes tha wull o god thems ma brither ma sister an ma mither yinst mair jesus begun lairnin fowk alang tha loch shore a wile thrang o fowk haed gethert roon aboot him sae he got intae a boat that wus oot on tha watter he sut doon an toul tha yins on tha shore a hale wheen o things bi parables amang thaim wus this yin listen here noo thair wus this fairmer went oot tae saa seed whan he wus scatterin tha seed some drapt doon alang tha pad an tha burds flew doon an peckt it up an some fell on roakie grun whar thair wusnae much clye it sprung up quick becas tha clye wus shalla but as shune as it brairdit an tha sin cum oot tha plants wus scorcht an the deed aff acause the haed nae ruits ither seed faad doon amang thoarns an tha thoarns sprung up tuk ower an chokt it sae thair wus nae yiel but a lock drapt on tae guid grun it daen weel an gien a guid hairst thurtie sixtie or a hunner times mair an jesus saed let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent an whan he wus on his ain some o tha fowk that wus alang wi tha twal axt him aboot his parables tha saicret o tha kingdom o god haes bin gien tae ye saed jesus but tae thaim thats ootside tha kingdom a taak in parables sae that the micht aye be lukkin but niver see an aye listenin yit niver unnerstan less the micht turn an thair sins be forgien an jesus saed if ye dinnae unnerstan this parable hoo ir ye gaun tae unnerstan aa tha rest tha bodie that scattert tha seed wus sowin tha wurd o god then some fowk is laik tha seed that faad doon nixt tha pad as shune as the hear tha wurd alang cums satan an taks it oot o thair hairts an its jist tha same wi tha seed that fell on tha staney grun the hear tha wurd an richt awa tak it in wi a gled hairt but the hae nae ruit sae the cannae houl on tae it whan haird times an trouble cums acause o gods wurd an sae the jist gie up an thairs ither fowk akin tae tha seed that wus sowed amang tha thoarns ther aye worryin rinnin efter money an hungrin fer things the hinnae got an sae thairs nae crap fer tha wurd haesnae a chaunce tae growe ither fowk is laik tha seed sowed on guid grun the hear tha wurd tak it tae thair hairts an it gies a guid yiel thurtie sixtie an a hunner times mair an jesus saed tae thaim wud ye iver think o bringin in a lamp an pittin it unner a boul or tha bed na ye wud pit it up on a stan fer thairs naethin hid thatll no be brocht oot intae tha licht an thairs nae saicret thatll no be brocht oot intae tha apen let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent an he saed tae thaim mine hoo yis listen fer tha misure yis gie wull be tha misure yis get ay an itll be even mair fer him that haes plentie wull be gien mair an him that haes little even whut he haes wull be tuk awa frae him an jesus saed tha kingdom o god is jist laik this tha fairmer scatters seed on tha grun day an nicht nae metter if hes up an aboot or sleepin tha seed sprouts up an growes tha mair he daesnae unnerstan whut maks it growe tha seed growes in tha clye itsel furst tha braird shows then tha staaks an then tha heids cums on tha tap o tha staaks then whan tha crap is ripe tha fairmer taks tha heuk tae it fer hairvest time is cum an agane he saed whut dye think tha kingdom o god is laik noo whut storie cud a tell that wud pit it ower tae ye it is laik a wee bit mustert seed plantit in tha grun tha weeest seed o aa but whan it growes it gets bigger an bigger tae its tha biggest plant in tha gairden wi a spreed o brenches tha burds can roost unner in oot o tha sin an jesus toul a hale wheen o parables laik these tae tha fowk tae halp thaim unnerstan he niver saed ocht tae thaim wioot uisin parables but whan him an his follaers wur on thair ain he toul thaim whut it aa mained whan evenin cum roon he saed tae his follaers cmon an well gang ower tae tha ither side o tha loch whaniver tha thrang wus sent hame jesus wus aareadie in tha boat sae the stairtit oot alang wi some ither wee boats fer tha faur side aa at yinst a big wun ris up thair wus a pooerfu stoarm an tha waves wus batin ower tha side o tha boat tae it wus near fu o watter jesus wus sleepin in tha bak o tha boat on a pilla his follaers ris him yellin maister dae ye no care if we aa droon up he got he chackt tha wun an he saed tae tha waves be quait lown doon then tha wun drapt an it wus aa peace an quaitness an jesus saed tae thaim hoo cum yis ir sae feart hae ye nae faith yit efter aa this the wur hairtscarred an saed tae yin anither whut kine o a man is this even tha wun an tha waves daes as he bids thaim sae the went iver tae tha ither side o tha loch tae tha lan whar tha gerasenes leeved an whaniver jesus wus gettin oot o tha boat richt awa a man wi an ill spirit cum oot frae tha graveyaird fer tae meet him this man leeved amang tha tombs an naebodie cud houl him doon no een wi chains fer the wud langelt him han an fit but he puud tha chains sinnerie an tha fetters he brauk apairt naebodie wus strang eneuch tae curb him an he wud sprachle aboot nicht an day amang tha tombs an braes scraichin an cuttin hissel wi stanes whaniver he saen jesus a lang roads aff he run an he faad doon on his knees afore him he guldert at him whut is it ye ir efter wi me jesus sinn o tha maist heich god in tha name o god wud ye quit tormentin me fer jesus haed aareadie saed tae him cum oot o tha man ye ill spirit an jesus axt whut dae the caa ye ma names legion cum tha answer fer thairs a hale lock o iz an he kep on beggin jesus no tae senn thaim awa oot o thon kintrie noo nearhan on tha braeside wus a big herd o pigs hokin fer food an tha spirits plaidit wi jesus senn iz owerbye tae tha pigs let iz gang intae thaim an sae jesus allooed thaim an tha ill spirits cum oot o tha man an the went intae tha pigs an tha herd aa twa thoosan o thaim tuk aff doon tha hill heid furst intae tha loch an tha hale lock o thaim wus droont in tha watter tha yins mindin tha pigs run aff an toul whut haed tuk place tae tha fowk in tha toon an kintrie roon aboot an the aa cum oot tae see it fer thairsels whaniver the cum tae jesus the saen tha man that haed bin taen ower wi tha legion o ill spirits sittin thair quait wi his claes on him an richt in tha heid an the wur hairtscarred thaim at haed saen it toul tha fowk tha ins an oots o whut haed happent tae tha man wi tha ill spirits an aboot tha pigs forbye an tha fowk begun plaidin wi jesus tae quit thair kintrie whaniver jesus wus gettin aboord tha boat tha man that haed bin tuk iver wi ill spirits rhymed on an on at him tae let him gang wi him but jesus wudnae alloo him an he saed tae him awa hame tae yer ain yins an tell thaim tha much tha loard haes daen fer ye an hoo hes haed mercie on ye sae aff tha man went an stairtit tellin fowk roon tha ten toons whut aa jesus haed daen fer him an the wur aa dumfoonert noo whaniver jesus went bak in tha boat tae tha ither side o tha loch a hale thrang o fowk gethert roon him on tha shore an thair wus this man bi tha name o jairus yin o tha heidyins o tha meetin hoose cum up tae jesus an he faad doon on his knees afore him he plaidit sair wi jesus sayin ma wee dochter is deein cud ye no cum an lay yer hans on hir sae shell get better an no dee an jesus went alang wi him a big thrang o fowk follaed him croodin in on him thair wus this wumman amang thaim that haed bother wi bleedin fer twal year she haed tholed a hale lock unner monie docters an efter spennin aa she haed she wus nae better but jist gettin tha waur noo she haed heerd aboot jesus she cum up behin him in tha thrang an toucht his cloke becas she thocht if a cud jist touch his claes a wull be made weel agane sae she did it an strecht aff tha bleedin stapt an she felt in hir bodie that she wus rid o hir bother richt awa jesus kent tha pooer haed gan oot o him he turnt roon tae tha crood an he axt wha toucht ma claes an his follaers cum bak wi this shair luk at aa tha fowk croodin roon ye an ye ir axin wha toucht me but jesus kep lukkin roon tae see wha haed daen it then tha wumman knowin fine weel whut haed happent tae hir cum an faad doon at his feet trimmlin wi fear an toul him tha hale truith dochter he saed til hir yer faith haes made ye weel gang in peace ye ir redd o yer trouble while jesus wus still taakin some men cum up frae tha hoose o jairus yer dochter is deid the saed tae him ye neednae bother tha maister onie mair takkin nae heed o whut the saed jesus toul jairus dinnae be feart jist believe jesus wudnae alloo oniebodie tae gang wi him apairt frae peter jeames an jhone jeames brither whaniver the cum tae tha hame o tha heidyin o tha meetin hoose jesus saa a hale stir amang tha fowk wi thaim aa roarin an greetin he went in an saed tae thaim whuts aa this narration an yowlin aboot tha wee lass is no deid shes jist sleepin but the lacht at him sae he put thaim aa oot an he tuk tha weans mither an faither an tha follaers that wur wi him an he went in whar tha wee lass wus takkin hir bi tha han he saed tae hir talitha cumi mainin wee lass a say tae ye up ye get richt awa tha wee lass got up on hir feet an waakt aboot she wus twal yeir oul at this the wur aa clain flebbergestit he bid thaim on nae accoont tae tell oniebodie ocht aboot it an he toul thaim tae gie hir a bite tae ait efter this jesus quit thaim pairts an went on bak tae his hametoon alang wi his follaers an whaniver tha sabbath day cum roon he stairtit taichin tha fowk thair in tha meetin hoose an monie that heerd him wur stoondit whar did he get aa this frae the axt whuts aa this wusdom that hes bin gien that sitch miracles ir wrocht bi his hans is this no jist tha cairpenter an hes marys sinn isnt he an tha brither o jeames joseph judas an simon is his sisters no here wi iz an the tuk umrage at him but jesus saed tae thaim a proaphits niver weel thocht o in his hametoon amang his freens or in his ain hoose he cudnae dae onie miracles thair apairt frae layin his hans on twarthie seeck fowk an makkin thaim better an he wus tuk bak wi thair want o faith then jesus went roon aa tha villages lairnin tha fowk an caain his twal follaers roon him he sent thaim oot in twas an gien thaim pooer ower tha ill spirits this wus his biddin tak naethin fer tha road apairt frae a stav nae breid nae baag nae copper coins in yer girthpooch pit sannals on yer feet an tak jist tha claes on yer bak whutiver hoose yis ir stappin in he saed bide yer time in it til yis tak yer lave o tha toon an if tha fowk in onie place wull no mak yis walcum or gie yis a hearin dicht tha stour aff yer feet as yis ir leain as a wutness an warnin tae thaim an sae the went oot praichin that fowk shud turn frae thair sins the driv oot monie ill spirits an the anointit monie seeck fowk wi oiyle an made thaim better king herod antipas got wun o this fer tha hale kintrie wus taakin aboot jesus some fowk wur sayin that jhone tha baptiser wus ris frae tha deid an that wus hoo he cud dae sitch michtie warks ithers thocht it wus tha proaphit elijah an yit ithers thocht he maun be a proaphit laik yin o tha proaphits o tha oulden days whaniver herod heerd this he saed thon jhone that a haed tha heid tuk aff hes cum bak tae life agane fer afore this herod haed gien oarders tae hae jhone brocht in tyed up an put in jail he daen this acause o herodias that he haed merriet tha mair she wus his brither philips wife an jhone haed saed tae herod its agin tha laa fer ye tae tak yer brithers wife fer yersel sae herodias haed it in fer jhone she wud hae killt him but she cudnae get at him fer herod haed a guid regaird fer jhone he kent he wus a strecht an halie man sae he kep him oot o hairms wye whan he heerd jhone it bothert him but aa tha same he aye listened tae him wi a gled hairt at lang last herodias got hir chaunce on herods birthday he wus houlin a big spreed fer aa tha heidyins o tha palace tha generls an tha tap men o galilee whan herodias dochter cum in an daunced it plaised herod an thaim that sut alang wi him tha king saed tae hir ax fer ocht ye want an all gie it tae ye he gien hir his wurd on oath ax whut ye wull an all gie it tae ye up tae a half o ma kingdom an she went oot an saed tae hir mither whutll a ax fer an tha mither saed bak tae hir ax fer tha heid o jhone tha baptiser wi that tha dochter run bak in afore tha king an she saed whut a want is tha heid o jhone tha baptiser richt noo on a platter tha king wus wile sorrie but becas o tha oath he haed tuk an acause o tha yins wi him roon tha table he didnae dar gae bak on his wurd sae richt awa tha king sent aff a sodger tae gang an bring tha heid o jhone tha baptiser bak wi him tha man went awa an he tuk jhones heid aff in tha jail he brocht it bak on a platter gien it tae tha lassie an she gien it tae hir mither an whaniver jhones follaers heerd tell o it the cum an tuk his bodie an the layed it oot in a tomb noo tha possels cum bak tae jesus frae thair trevelin an the toul him aa the haed daen an whut the haed lairnt tha fowk an whar the wur at thair wus that monie cumin an gaun that the cudnae even get peace tae hae ocht tae ait sae jesus saed tae thaim cum awa on yer lane tae a quait place an tak it aisie fer a bit sae the went awa in a boat bi thair lane tae a quait place noo monie fowk saa thaim as the wur gaun aff an kent wha the wur sae the run on aheid on thair fit frae oot o aa tha toons an the got thair afore thaim an whan jesus cum tae lan he fun a hale thrang o fowk fornent him an his hairt went oot tae thaim fer the wur laik sheep wannerin wioot a herd tae luk efter thaim an he begun tae lairn thaim monie things an whan it wus wearin late his follaers cum an saed tae him its dailygan an this is a richt oot o tha wye place senn these fowk awa tae tha fairm hooses an clachans roon aboot tae buy thairsels a bite tae ait but jesus saed bak tae thaim yous gie thaim sumthin tae ait an the saed whut wud we buy it wi it wud tak a wee foartune tae buy fer thaim aa whut hae ye tae ait qo jesus awa an fin oot sae awa the gan tae fin oot an the cum bak an toul him we hae five bannocks an twa fish sae jesus bid thaim aa sit doon in locks on tha green gress an the sut doon in groups o hunnerts an fifties an takkin tha five bannocks an tha twa fish he lukt up tae heiven he blisst an brauk tha bannocks an he kep giein thaim tae his follaers tae han oot tae tha fowk an he divid tha twa fish amang thaim aa as weel the aa et thair fill an the gethert up aa tha wee bits o breid an fish eneuch tae fill twal creels thaim five bannocks haed fed five thoosan men richt awa jesus toul his follaers tae get aboord tha boat an tae gang on aheid o him tae tha ither side fornent bethsaida while he toul tha thrang o fowk tae gang hame an efter leain thaim he went up tha muntin fer tae pray at dailygan tha boat wus oot in tha middle o tha loch an jesus wus on his lane on tha lan he saen tha follaers puin haird on tha oars fer tha wun wus blaain agin thaim an aboot tha fowerth watch o tha nicht he gaed oot tae thaim waakin on tha watter he wus aboot tae pass bye thaim but whaniver the saen him waakin on tha watter the jaloused he wus a wraith an the yellt oot fer the aa saen him an the wur hairtscarred strecht awa he spauk oot tae thaim an he saed tak hairt its masel dinnae be feart then he climmed up intae tha boat alangside o thaim an tha wun deed doon the wur aa dumfoonert an thocht it wus ower ocht fer the cudnae mak onie sense o tha miracle o tha bannocks thed wutnesst thair hairts jist wurnae apen tae it an whan the gaed bak ower tha loch agane the cum tae lan at gennesaret an the drapt enchor thonner at tha shore noo whaniver the steppit oot o tha boat richt awa tha fowk kent wha jesus wus the run roon tha hale kintrieside an the stairtit tae cairrie tha seeck on mats tae whariver the heerd he wus at an noo iveriewhar he went intae tha clachans tha toons or oot in tha kintrie the put tha seeck oot on tha grun in an apen place whar he cud see thaim the besocht him tae let thaim touch even tha enn o his robe an aa that toucht it wus makkit weel agane noo thair wus some pharisees an maisters o tha laa that haed cum frae jerusalem an the gethert roon jesus an the fun faut whaniver the saa some o his follaers aitin breid wi hans that wurnae clain thats tae say the haednae waasht thaim tha pharisees an aa tha jews dinnae ait afore waashin thair hans houlin tae tha tradeetion o tha elders whan the cum frae tha mairket the dinnae ait oniethin less the gie it a waash furst an monie anither thing the houl tae as weel sitch as tha richt wye tae clain thair bickers an jugs thair copper kettles an tables then tha pharisees an tha maisters o tha laa axt jesus fer why dae yer follaers leeve wioot onie regaird tae tha wye it wus hannit doon frae oor elders aitin breid wi thair hans no waasht he saed bak tae thaim isaiah got it richt whan he proaphesied aboot yous hippycrates as its writ doon this nation honours me wi thair mooth says god but thair hairt is faur awa frae me thair woarships nae use ava thair taichins ir naethin but manmade rules an regulations fer yis lea aside tha commauns o god an houl on tae tha tradeetions o men laik tha waashin o pots an bickers an monie anither thing yis dae an he went on tae tell thaim yis hae a quare wye o pittin aside tha laas o god sae as ye can houl tae yer ain tradeetions fer moses saed honour yer faither an yer mither an oniebodie that miscaas thair faither or mither maun be put tae deith but yous say that its aa richt fer a bodie tae say tae his faither or mither a cannae gie yis onie halp becas a hae vood tae gie whut a hae tae god an yous let him dae naethin mair fer his faither or mither sae becas o this yis mak a nonsense o tha wurd o god bi yer tradeetion hannit doon an monie anither thing yis dae laik that jesus caad tha thrang tae him agane an saed listen tae me iverie yin o yis an unnerstan this whut gaes intae ye frae tha ootside daesnae sullie ye but its whut cums oot o yer hairt that sullies ye let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent efter he left tha crood o fowk an gan intae tha hoose his follaers axt him aboot this parable ir yous as slow on tha uptake as tha ithers he axt dae yis no see that its no whut yis ait thatll sullie ye fer it daesnae gae intae yer hairt but intae yer belly an then passes on oot doon tha drain bi this jesus wus sayin that onie soart o mait wus clain he went on tae say its whut cums oot o yer hairt that sullies ye fer its frae wiin yer hairt aa tha wickit thochts cum lustin an thievin murder an adulterie greed doonricht baadness deceit filthynis blekinin fowks cherecter blesphemin pride an iverie kine o fuilishnis aa these wickit things cum frae tha inside its thaim that sullies a bodie efter that jesus left galilee an went awa tae tha district roon tyre an sidon he stapt in a hoose an didnae want oniebodie tae ken it but fer him thair wus nae hidin fer richt awa a wumman that haed a wee lass wi an ill spirit cum tae him as shune as she heerd he wus thair she faad doon on hir knees afore jesus an plaidit wi him tae drive tha ill spirit oot frae hir dochter tha wumman wus a greek wi nae jewish breedin frae tha region o syrophoenicia a shud gie tha weans thair fill furst he saed tae hir fer its no richt tae tak tha weans breid an clod it tae tha wee dugs ay loard saed she but still wi aa een tha wee dugs unner tha table gits aitin tha weans crumbs thats a guid answer an becas o it qo he til hir whan ye gae bak hame yell fin tha ill spirit haes left yer dochter an whaniver tha wumman cum hame richt eneuch she fun tha wee lass lyin quait in hir bed an tha ill spirit gan awa efter that jesus left tha district o tyre an he went bak doon tae tha loch o galilee passin throu sidon an tha ten toons on his wye some fowk brocht tae him a man that wus deef an cud harlie taak an the plaidit wi him tae lay his han on him efter takkin him tae tha side awa frae tha thrang jesus put his fingrs intae tha mans ears then he sput an toucht tha mans tung wi his spittle he lukt up tae heiven an giein a big seich he saed tae tha man ephphatha tha aramaic mainin be apent wi that tha mans ears wus apent his tung wus lowst an he stairtit tae spake laik ither fowk jesus gien thaim oarders no tae tell oniebodie but tha mair he warnt thaim tha mair the kep on taakin aboot it fowk wur flebbergestit he haes daen aa things weel the saed he even maks tha deef tae hear an tha dum tae spake roon aboot thon time whaniver a big thrang o fowk haed gethert thegither an the haed naethin tae ait jesus caad his follaers tae him an he toul thaim ma hairt gaes oot tae these fowk acause the hae bin here wi me this thrie days an the hae naethin lef tae ait if a senn thaim awa hame thell drap wi hungr alang tha road fer some o thaim haes cum a lang wye oot here in tha wiles hoo cud we fin eneuch tae fill thaim axt his follaers whut feck o breid hae ye axt jesus an the saed seiven loafs then jesus bid tha crood o fowk sit thairsels doon on tha grun an he tuk tha seiven loafs gien thenks tae god fer thaim brauk thaim up in bits an gien thaim tae his follaers tae han oot tae tha crood an thats whut the daen an summodie haed twarthie wee fish sae he blisst thaim tae an toul his follaers tae gie thaim oot as weel an efter tha fowk haed et thair fill tha follaers gethert up tha fu o seiven creels o leains in aa thair wus aboot fower thoosan fowk thair that day an the wur aa sent bak hame an richt awa jesus got intae a boat alang wi his follaers an the crosst ower tae tha kintrieside roon bi dalmanutha thair wus some pharisees cum oot an the stairtit tae quiz him an axt him tae gie thaim a sign frae heiven the wur jist tryin tae ketch him oot jesus gien a big seich frae deep doon an saed fer why daes fowk in this day an age keep lukkin fer a sign am tellin yis thair wull be nae sign gien tae thaim an he got intae tha boat an left thaim an went ower tae tha ither side o tha loch noo tha follaers didnae mine tae tak breid wi thaim an the haed nae mair than yin loaf atween thaim on tha boat an jesus chairged thaim sayin luk oot fer tha yeast o tha pharisees an tha yeast o herod an the taakt amang thairsels sayin this is aa becas we hae brocht nae breid jesus knowed whut the wur thinkin an he axt thaim why ir yis taakin aboot haein nae breid dae yis no see dae yis no unnerstan yit is yer hairts still that haird yis hae een ir yis blin yis hae ears ir yis deef dae yis no mine ocht ava whaniver a divid tha five loafs amang tha five thoosan hoo monie baskets o leains did yis lift twal the saed an whan a divid tha seiven loafs amang tha fower thoosan hoo monie creels fu o leains did yis lift seiven the answert an jesus saed tae thaim then hoo cum yis still dinnae unnerstan the cum tae bethsaida an some fowk brocht a blin man tae jesus an plaidit wi him fer tae pit his hans on him he tuk tha blin man bi tha han an waakt him oot o tha village an whan he haed sput on tha mans een an put his hans on him jesus axt dae ye see ocht tha man lukt up an saed a can see fowk but the luk laik trees waakin aboot yinst mair jesus put his hans on tha mans een then his een apent wide an his sicht cum bak an he saa iveriethin roon him clear an plain an jesus sent him awa hame sayin dinnae even be gan near tha village an dinnae be tellin oniebodie thair jesus an his follaers gaed on up tae tha villages roon caesarea philippi an on tha wye thair he axt his follaers this wha dae fowk say that a am a wheen wud say jhone tha baptiser the answert some wud say elijah an ithers yin o tha proaphits but whut aboot yersels jesus axt wha dae you say that a am an peter answert you ir tha christ sae ye ir an jesus gien thaim a warnin tae mak shair an tell naebodie aboot him then he begun taichin his follaers that tha sinn o man wud hae tae suffer monies a thing he wud be gien tha coul shooder bi tha elders tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa he maun be put tae deith an efter thrie days he wud rise agane frae tha deid jesus spauk oot apenlie aboot this an peter tuk him tae tha yin side an stairtit tae scoul him fer it but turnin roon an lukkin at his follaers jesus chackt peter git ahint me satan saed he fer ye gie nae thocht tae tha things o god yer heids fu o tha things o men then he caad tha crood thegither alang wi his follaers an saed if oniebodies lukkin tae follae me he maun ferget aboot hissel aathegither tak up his cross an stick clase tae me fer whaiver wants tae save his life wull loass it but him that loasses his life on accoont o me an tha guid news wull save it whut guid is it fer a bodie tae get tha hale warl an yit tae loass his ain sowl thairs naethin a man cud gie tae get bak his ain sowl shair thairs no fer if oniebodie is no wullin tae stan up fer me an ma wurds in this wickit an godless day an age then tha sinn o man wull no stan up fer him whan he cums in his faithers glorie wi tha halie angels jesus saed tae thaim listen thairs yins stud here theday that fer sartin wull no dee afore the see tha kingdom o god cum wi pooer an efter six days haed
