gan bye jesus tuk peter jeames an jhone alang wi him up intae a heich muntin tae be bi thairsels an richt afore thair verie een tha hale luk o him wus changed his claes aa stairtit shinin white as snaa faur whiter than onie bleacher cud iver mak thaim an lo an behoul elijah an moses appeart taakin thegither wi jesus an peter saed tae jesus rabbi am gled we ir here tae see this cum on an well big thrie shilters yin fer you yin fer moses an yin fer elijah fer he didnae know whut else tae say becas the wur scarred oot o thair wuts an a clood cum doon an hid thaim an a voice cum oot o tha clood an saed this is ma sinn that a love listen tae him an aa o a suddent whaniver the lukt roon thair wus naebodie thair but thairsels an jesus an on tha wye doon frae tha muntin he oardert thaim no tae tell oniebodie whut the haed saen til tha sinn o man haed ris up frae tha deid sae the daen as the wur toul but the kep wunnerin amang thairsels whut this risin frae tha deid wus aa aboot an the axt him hoo cum tha maisters o tha laa tell iveriebodie that elijah haes tae cum furst afore tha messiah an he saed bak tae thaim deed ay elijah wus tae cum furst tae get aa readie fer tha messiah then if thats tha wye o it hoo cum its writ doon in tha guid buik that tha sinn o man maun suffer monie things an the wud aa turn agin him but am tellin ye elijah haes aareadie bin an gan an the daen jist whutiver the laikt wi him as tha guid buik saed the wud an whaniver the cum bak doon tae his ither follaers the saa a wile crood roon thaim an some maisters o tha laa thrawin wi thaim an tha crood o fowk wus aa bye thairsels wi excitement whaniver the saa jesus an the run up tae bid him walcum jesus axt tha maisters o tha laa whuts this thraw aboot an yin o tha crood saed bak tae him maister a hae brocht ma sinn tae ye fer he haes an ill spirit an cannae taak an whan it taks hoult o him he gangs intae a fit an he faas doon foamin at tha mooth an scringein his teeth an hes jist wastin awa a axt yer follaers tae rid him o tha spirit an the cudnae dae it an he saed o you faithless fowk hoo lang wull a be wi ye afore yis believe hoo lang dae a hae tae pit up wi ye bring tha wee lad tae me sae the brocht him an whaniver tha spirit saa jesus it sent tha lad intae a fit an he faad tae tha grun rowlin aboot an foamin at tha mooth hoo lang haes he bin laik this jesus axt tha faither an he saed since he wus a wean an monies tha time it haes throwed him intae tha fire an intae tha watter as weel tae dae awa wi him sae if you can dae oniethin ava tak peetie on iz an halp iz jesus saed whut dae ye main bi if a can oniethin is poassible whan a bodie believes an richt awa tha wee lads faither cryed oot loard a dae believe but tak awa tha doots a hae jesus saa that tha crood wus gettin bigger an he gien tha wickit spirit a richt barjin sayin cum oot o him ye deef an dum spirit an stye oot an tha spirit gien a scraich an it throwed tha lad tae tha grun in anither fit jist afore it cum oot o him tha wee fella lukt as if he haed deed an sae tha crood saed hes deid but jesus tuk him bi tha han an halpt him tae his feet an he wus fit tae stan a while later whaniver jesus wus in tha hoose on his ain wi his follaers the axt him whut fer cud we no cast tha ill spirit oot an he saed ye can onlie git rid o this kine bi prayer an fastin sae the left thair an went on throu galilee an jesus didnae want oniebodie tae know whar he wus fer he wantit tae hae time tae taich his follaers he toul thaim tha sinn o manll be hannit ower tae men that wull kill him efter thrie days but hell rise frae tha deid but the cudnae unnerstan whut he wus mainin an the wur feart tae ax him aboot it an he cum tae capernaum an whan he wus in tha hoose the wur stayin at he axt thaim whut wur ye argyin aboot on tha wye here but the didnae say ocht becas the haed bin argyin aboot wha amang thaim wus tha maist thocht o an he sut doon an caad thaim ower an saed tae thaim whaiver wants tae be furst maun tak tha hinmaist place an be tha sarvint o iverie ither bodie an he tuk a wean an stud him amang thaim then he tuk him in his airms an saed tae thaim whaiver walcums yin o these weans in ma name bids me walcum an whaiver bids me walcum walcums no me alane but him that sent me as weel an jhone saed tae him taicher we saa a bodie drivin oot demons in your name an we made him stap fer he wusnae yin o us but jesus saed dae nae sitch thing fer oniebodie that daes a miracle in ma name wull no be quick tae spake agin me fer whaivers no agin iz is wi iz whaiver gies ye a bicker o watter in ma name becas ye belang tae christ a tell ye hell no be wantin fer a reward thats fer shair but if oniebodie leads asthray yin o these weans that believes in me it wud be better fer him if he wus throwed intae tha sea wi a millstane roon his neck an if yer han maks ye dae wrang cut it aff fer it wud be better tae gae tae heiven wi tha yin han than tae hae twa hans an gae tae hell whar tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on aburnin an if yer fit maks ye dae wrang cut it aff fer it wud be better tae hae jist tha yin fit an gae tae heiven than tae hae twa feet an be throwed intae hell whar tha fire niver dees thair tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on aburnin an if yer ee maks ye dae wrang pu it oot fer its better tae gae intae tha kingdom o god half blin than tae hae twa een an be throwed intae hell whar tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on aburnin fer iveriebodie wull be purified wi fire jist as a secryfice is purified wi saut saut is guid but if it loasses its strenth hoo dae ye mak it saltie agane hae saut in yersels dinnae loass yer strenth an leeve at peace wi yin anither jesus then left capernaum an went intae judea an he crosst ower tha river joardan thair a crood o fowk gethert up agane an he taicht thaim as he aye did an some pharisees tae pit him tae tha test axt him is it allooed fer a husban tae pit awa his wife an he answert whut did moses tell yis tae dae the saed moses allooed a man tae write a notysh o divorce tae pit hir awa an jesus saed tae thaim it wus becas yer hairts wus haird that moses gien ye this laa but frae tha stairt o creation god made men an he made weemen sae a man wull lea his faither an mither an be joint tae his wife an tha twa wull becum as yin nae mair twa seprit fowk sae whut god haes put thegither let nae man pull sinnerie but whan the wur bak in tha hoose his follaers brocht up tha metter agane an he saed tae thaim whaiver pits awa his wife an merries anither he commits adulterie agin hir an if a wumman pits awa hir man an gits merriet tae anither she commits adulterie as weel an the brocht weans fer him tae pit his hans on thaim tae bliss thaim but his follaers chackt tha yins that brocht thaim whan jesus saen this he wus wile angrie an saed tae thaim alloo tha weans tae cum tae me an dinnae stap thaim fer tha kingdom o god belangs tae tha laik o these am tellin ye tha truith whaiver daesnae tak tha kingdom o god intae his hairt laik a wean daes wull no get in ava an he tuk tha weans up in his airms put his hans on thaim an gien thaim his blissin noo as jesus wus settin oot agane thair wus this man cum rinnin tae him he bood doon afore jesus an axt him guid maister whut maun a dae tae be shair a get tae heiven an leeve fer iver an jesus saed bak tae him why ir ye caain me guid thairs naebodie guid apairt frae god ye weel ken tha commauns dinnae murder dinnae commit adulterie dinnae tak whuts no yer ain dinnae tell lees aboot ither fowk dinnae be daein fowk oot o ocht an gie respeck tae yer faither an yer mither an tha man saed tae jesus maister a hae daen aa thaim things since a wus nae age jesus lukt at tha man wi love an he toul him yin thing ye hinnae daen gae awa an sell aa ye hae an gie tha siller tae tha puir an yell hae walth in heiven an then tak up yer cross an cum efter me whaniver he heerd this he wus vext an he went awa doon in tha mooth fer he wus quare an weelaff an jesus turnt roon an he saed tae his follaers hoo verie haird it wull be fer weel monied fowk tae enter intae tha kingdom o god whan he saed this his follaers wus aa tuk bak but jesus saed tae thaim agane freens hoo verie haird it is fer thaim at pits thair trust in thair siller tae git intae tha kingdom o god it wud be aisier fer a kemel tae gae throu tha ee o a needle ner fer a monied man tae git intae tha kingdom o god an his follaers wur thunnerstruck then wha in aa tha warl can be saved the axt him jesus lukt strecht at thaim an saed man cannae dae it bi hissel but god can dae it fer wi god aa things ir poassible then peter begun tae spake an he saed tae jesus mine we hae left iveriethin behin an cum efter ye an jesus saed bak tae him a tell ye this thairs naebodie that haes left behin him his hoose or brithers or sisters or mither or faither or wife or weans or fairm o lan fer ma sake an tha sake o tha guid news but hell get a hunner times mair in tha here an noo o hooses brithers sisters mither weans or fairm o lan as weel as a lock o persecution an hell hae life iverlastin in tha warl tae cum an monies a bodie thats foremaist noo wull be last then an monie thats last noo wull be foremaist then an the wur noo on tha road up tae jerusalem wi jesus waakin aheid o his follaers an the wur in awe o him an tha fowk cumin behin wur wile feart an he tuk tha twal tae tha side agane an he begun tae tell thaim whut wus gaun tae happen tae him he saed luk wer gaun tae jerusalem whar tha sinn o man wull be hannit ower tae tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa that wull sentence him tae dee an gie him ower tae thaim thats no jews an the wull jeer him gie him a whuppin spit on his face an kill him but efter thrie days hell rise tae life agane jeames an jhone tha sinns o zebedee cum an saed tae jesus maister thairs sumthin we want ye tae dae fer iz an he saed whut is it yis want the answert let yin o iz sit doon on yer richt han side an tha ither yin on yer left whaniver ye tak yer throne in glorie but jesus saed bak tae thaim yis dinnae ken whut yis ir axin cud yis thole tae drink tha cup o sufferin that a maun drink or tae be baptised wi tha baptisin that all be baptised wi an the saed tae him ay that we can an jesus saed bak tae thaim yis shairlie wull drink frae ma cup an be baptised wi ma baptisin but its no up tae me tae alloo yis tae sit on ma richt han side or on ma left its up tae god tae gie thaim saits tae tha yins the wur meent fer noo whaniver tha ither ten follaers heerd whut jeames an jhone haed axt fer the stairtit tae get wile angrie wi thaim sae jesus caad thaim thegither an saed tae thaim yis aa ken that tha yins that rule ower tha gentiles laird it ower thair ain fowk an thair heidyins aye lets thaim know whas tha boss this is no tha wye it shud be amang you but fer whaiver wants tae be foremaist amang ye haes tae be laik a sarvint an whaiver wants tae be tha heid man haes tae slave fer aa tha rest fer even tha sinn o man didnae cum tae be tendit tae but fer tae sarve ithers an tae gie his life as a ransom fer monie fowk jesus an his follaers trevelt tae jericho an as the wur leain tha toon wi a big crood follaein thaim the saen blin bartimaeus tha sinn o timaeus sittin beggin on tha bunker o tha road whan bartimaeus heerd that jesus o nazareth wus gaun bye he begun tae caa oot jesus sinn o davit tak peetie on me tha fowk chackt him an the toul him tae be quait but he guldert aa tha looder jesus sinn o davit tak peetie on me jesus stapt in his step an toul thaim tae caa tha blin man ower sae the caad him an saed tae him tak hairt git up fer hes caain ye wi that he aff wi his coat lep up an cum tae jesus an jesus axt whut dae ye want me tae dae fer ye rabboni answert tha blin man a want tae be able tae see agane an jesus saed bak tae him gang yer wye yer faith haes made ye hale an al at yinst he wus able tae see agane an he went aff doon tha road efter jesus an whaniver the got near tae bethphage an bethanie on tha ootskirts o jerusalem nixt tha moont o olives jesus bid twa o his follaers tae gang on aheid he saed gae intae tha clachan fornent ye an as shuin as ye gae in yell fin a cowlt tyed up that naebodie haes iver sut on lowse it an bring it here if oniebodie axes ye whut ir ye daein jist tell thaim tha loard haes need o it an yell get it bak afore lang sae aff the went an fun tha cowlt tyed tae a dure ootbye on tha street an the lowsed it noo some o tha yins stannin roon axt thaim whut ir ye daein lowsin that cowlt tha twa follaers answert whut jesus haed toul thaim tae say an tha fowk lut thaim gang on aheid sae the brocht tha cowlt tae jesus an throwed thair claes ower its bak an jesus got up on it an a lock o fowk stannin alang tha road spreed thair claes on tha pad an ither yins cut doon leafie brenches oot o tha fiels an the strewed thaim afore him an afore an behin fowk wur cryin oot hosanna blisst be tha yin that cums in tha name o tha loard blisst be tha cumin kingdom o oor faither davit hosanna in tha heichest heiven sae jesus went intae jerusalem an on intae tha hoose o god an whan he haed lukt roon an haed tuk iveriethin on it sae he went tae see if it haed onie fruit but it haed naethin on it apairt frae leafs fer it wusnae tha richt time o yeir an his follaers heerd him sayin tae tha tree nae man wull iver ait fruit frae you agane the cum tae jerusalem an jesus went strecht intae tha hoose o god an he begun reddin oot tha dailers that wus buyin an sellin in tha coortyaird he coupt tha tables o tha siller changers an whammelt tha saits o thaim that wus sellin doos he wudnae alloo fowk tae cairrie oniethin intae tha hoose o god fer tae be soul an he gien thaim this lesson saed he is it no writ doon ma hoose wull be caad a hoose o prayer fer aa nations but yous hae turnt it intae a den o robbers an whaniver tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa heerd this the wantit tae dae awa wi him fer the wur feart o him becas aa tha fowk wur wile taen on wi his taichin an at dailygan the went oot o tha citie an in tha moarn whaniver the passt tha fig tree it wus aa wuthert ay richt doon tae tha ruits an peter mindit tha day afore an saed luk rabbi tha fig tree ye curst is aa weezened up an deid jesus saed bak tae thaim hae faith in god fer a tell yis this whaiver wull say tae this muntin be shiftit frae whar ye ir an cast yersel intae tha sea if tha same man haesnae onie doot in his hairt but believes in hissel that this wull raelie cum aboot then god wull dae it fer him sae a say tae yis aa tha things yis ax fer in prayer believe yis wull hae thaim an shair eneuch yis wull an whan yis stan up tae pray forgie oniebodie that haes daen yis wrang sae that yer heivenlie faither wull forgie you tha wrangs yous hae daen if yis dinnae forgie ither fowk nether wull yer heivenlie faither forgie yous an the went bak agane tae jerusalem an intae tha hoose o god an as he wus waakin aboot tha heid preeshts tha maisters o tha laa an tha elders cum up tae him an saed bi whut thortie ir ye daein these things an wha gien ye it an jesus saed bak tae thaim a want tae ax ye yin question an whaniver yis gie me tha answer a wull tell yis bi whut thortie a dae these things whaniver jhone wus baptisin wus this frae heiven or jist a notion o man answer me that noo the taakt this ower amang thairsels an the thocht if we say frae heiven then hell say sae hoo cum yis didnae believe him but if we say it wus frae men whut then fer the wur feart tha fowk wud turn on thaim becas they aa thocht jhone wus a proaphit sae the saed we cannae tell an whaniver jesus heerd this he saed then all no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie a dae these things an jesus begun tae taak tae thaim bi parables thair wus this man that plantit a vineyaird saed he an he fenced it aa roon he dug a pit fer a winepress bigged a lukoot tooer an he set tha vineyaird tae a wheen o tenantfairmers tae rin then he tuk aff tae anither kintrie whaniver hairvest time cum roon he sent yin o his sarvints tae tha fairmers tae collect his share o tha fruit an the tuk houl o tha sarvint bate him up an chaist him awa empiehannit sae tha owner sent anither sarvint that wus traitit in tha same shamefu wye onlie a lock waur fer the peltit his heid wi stanes then he sent anither an the killt him an he sent a wheen mair an the ether bate thaim up or killt thaim as weel bi noo tha laird haed naebodie lef tae senn apairt frae his ain dear sinn sae in tha enn he sent him tae thaim thinkin tae hissel hes ma ain sinn shairlie thell hae regaird fer him an tha tenantfairmers saed tae yin anither this boy wull tak ower whan his da dees if we dae awa wi him aa this wull be oors sae the tuk houl o him killt him an throwed his stane tha masons turnt doon is noo tha coarner stane tha loard hissel haes wrocht this an a wunnerfu sicht it is tha releejus heidyins wantit tae hae jesus arrestit but the wur feart o tha thrang the knowed that tha parable he toul wus agin thairsels sae the went awa an left him alane later on the sent some pharisees an men o herods pairtie fer tae ketch jesus oot in whut he saed whaniver the cum pye texes tae caesar or no wull we gie or wull we no gie the wur twa faced but jesus saa throu thaim an axt fer why ir ye tryin tae ketch me oot bring me a denarius til a see an whaniver the brocht it he axt thaim this whase name an laikness is on it its caesars the answert an jesus saed gie caesar whut belangs tae caesar an gie god whut belangs tae god an the wur dumfoonert wi his answer tha nixt tae cum alang wur tha sadducees thaim that say thair isnae onie risin frae tha deid an this is whut the put tae him maister moses writ doon fer iz that if a mans brither dees an leas a guidwife wi nae weans then tha brither maun merrie tha weeda an hae childer fer his deid brither noo whut if thair wus seiven brithers an tha oulest taks a wife an he dees afore the hae onie weans then tha saicont yin merries hir an he dees wioot haein onie weans ether an tha thurd brither tha same an lo an behoul tha hale seiven merries hir wioot haein onie weans an bye an bye tha wumman she deed as weel sae tell iz this at tha risin frae tha deid whase guidwife wull she be seein she wus merriet on tha hale seiven o thaim an jesus cum bak wi this ye ir no richt ava sae yer no fer ye dinnae ken tha scriptures an ye dinnae ken tha pooer o god fer whaniver fowk rise frae tha deid thair wull be nae mair merryin the wull jist be laik tha angels in heiven an consarnin tha risin frae tha deid dae yis gods no tha god o tha deid hes tha god o tha leevin yis ir aa wrang an stannin listenin tae whut wus gaun on wus yin o tha maisters o tha laa he heerd whut a guid answer jesus haed gien an he axt him this o aa tha commauns whut yin is tha maist impoartin an jesus answert bak tha maist impoartin is this an tak heed o israel tha loard oor god is tha yin an onlie god an ye maun love tha loard yer god wi aa yer hairt an yer sowl an aa yer mine micht an main this is tha furst commaun an tha saicont yin is this ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel nae ither commaun is abain these twa an tha maister o tha laa saed tae him weel saed maister its tha truith ye spake fer thair is yin god an nane ither but him an tae love god wi aa yer hairt an mine micht an main an yer nighber as yersel is mair impoartin than aa tha brunt offerins an secryfices ye cud mak whaniver jesus heerd tha sense tha man wus taakin he saed tae him ye ir no faur awa frae tha kingdom o god efter that naebodie wud davit tae say tha loard saed tae ma loard sit doon at ma richt han tae a pit yer enemies unner yer feet noo davit hissel caad tha messiah ma loard sae hoo then can he be his sinn as weel an tha fowk wur gye gled tae listen tae jesus an as he taicht thaim jesus went on tae say watch oot fer thaim maisters o tha laa paradin aboot in thair fancie robes wantin fowk tae touch thair keps tae thaim at weeda haes gien mair ner onie o tha ithers that gien offerins fer the hae aa gien onlie a pittance oot o thair pruch but this weeda puir an aa that she is haes gien aa she haed tae leeve on yin day as wull aa this cum aboot wull thair be onie sign its gaun tae happen an jesus saed tae thaim tak heed an dinnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee fer monies a yin wull cum in ma name sayin a be tha christ an kingdoms wull rise up agin ither kingdoms thair wull be irthquakes in monie pairts an thair wull be dirths ower tha lan tae but aa this is onlie tha stairt o tha bairin pains cumin on ye maun tak heed the wull han yis ower tae tha cooncils an gie yis a whuppin in tha meetin hooses on ma accoont ye wull be stud afore guviners an kings as a wutness tae thaim but afore this tha guid news maun be praicht tae aa tha nations noo whaniver yis ir liftit an brocht tae thrial dinnae be ower enxious aboot whut yis ir gaun tae say but whan tha time cums jist say whutiver god tells yis tae fer then itll no be yous thatll be taakin but itll be tha halie spirit brithers wull han ower thair brithers tae be killt an faithers thair weans an weans wull rise up agin thair faithers an mithers an hae thaim put tae deith as weel yell be haitit bi aa fowk on accoont o me but tha yin that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved but whaniver yis see tha abomination o desolation spauk aboot bi daniel tha proaphit stannin whar it shudnae be then thaim ats in judea maun tak tae tha hills reader yell unnerstan ma mainin here naebodie thats on his ruiftap shud be gaun bak doon tae get ocht oot o it an naebodie thats awa oot intae his fiel shud be gaun bak fer his coat in thaim days itll be tarrible fer weemen thats expectin an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht pray tae god that this daesnae happen in tha wunter fer in thaim days thairll be sitch wile sufferin faur waur ner thair iver wus frae tha time god made tha warl til noo an yell niver see tha laik agane gin tha loard daesnae cut thaim days shoart thairs naebodie wud be saved but its on accoont o his ain chosen yins that hes cut tha days shoart an if oniebodie shud say tae ye at that time luk here is tha messiah or thair hes thonner dinnae tak onie heed fer fauss messiahs an fauss proaphits wull rise up an dae signs an wunners an fowk wull be tuk in bi thaim ay an een tha chosen yins micht be tuk in tae but tak heed a hae toul ye aa this aheid o time sae as yell know but in thaim days efter tha time o sufferin tha sin wull be mirkit an tha muin wull no gie onie licht tha starns wull be faain oot o heiven an tha pooers o tha lift wull be dinnelt an then aa fowk wull see tha sinn o man cumin in tha cloods in michtie pooer an glorie an then he wull senn his angels oot tae gether thegither his chosen yins frae tha fower wuns frae tha ootermaist pairt o tha irth tae tha ootermaist pairt o heiven noo lairn this lesson frae tha fig tree as shuin as its brenches stairts tae bud an its leafs cum oot ye ken tha simmer is no faur aff in tha same wye whaniver ye see these things happenin yell ken tha time is nearhan ay at tha verie dure itsel am tellin ye tha truith thairs fowks leevin noo thatll no dee afore aa these things haes cum aboot heiven an irth wull pass awa but ma wurds wull niver pass awa naebodie kens tha day or oor whan aa this wull happen nether tha angels in heiven ner tha sinn hissel tha faither alane kens tak heed keep a lukoot an pray fer ye dinnae ken whan that time wull be fer tha cumin o tha sinn o man is laik a man gaun tae a faurawa lan that haes left his hoose in tha chairge o his sarvints he gien thaim aa thair ain wark tae dae an he toul tha dureman tae be on tha lukoot fer him cumin bak sae yous be on tha lukoot tae fer ye dinnae ken whan tha laird wull be bak whuther at tha gloamin or at midnicht or in tha wee smaa oors or at tha scraich o day less cumin on ye o a suddent hell fin ye sleepin whut a say tae ye a say tae yin an aa be on tha lukoot it wus twa days afore tha passower an tha faist o bairmless breid an tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa wus colloguin thegither tae git tha houl o jesus bi some sleekit wye fer tae pit him tae deith but no whaniver tha faists on the saed or well hae a garevitch on oor hans yin day whan jesus wus in simon tha lepers hoose in bethanie he wus at tha boord fer a bite tae ait whan a wumman cum in wi a wee crock o scent it wus oyle o pure nard an coast big money brekkin aff tha tap o tha stoup she poored tha oyle ower his heid but some o thaim that wus thair wus sair illplaised an saed yin tae tither whut fer wus this waste o guid nard fer it cud hae bin soul fer mair ner thrie hunner siller coins an tha catter gien tae tha puir sae the turnt an yaukt tha wumman but jesus saed lea hir alane dinnae bother hir fer this is a guid thing shes daen fer me fer yell aye hae tha puir wi yis an ye can be guid tae thaim whaniver ye want but yell no aye hae me wi ye she haes daen aa she cud fer she haes cum aforehan tae anoint ma bodie fer buryin am tellin ye tha truith whariver tha guid news is praicht ower tha hale warl hir storie wull be toul sae as shell niver be fergot an judas iscariot yin o tha twal gaed awa tae tha heid preeshts fer tae bethray jesus intae thair hans an whan the heerd it the wur richt gled an gien thair wurd tae gie him siller fer his wark sae he lukt oot fer a guid chaunce tae han jesus ower on tha furst day o tha faist o bairmless breid whan the aye killt tha passower lamb jesus follaers axt him whar dae ye want iz tae gang tae mak readie fer tha passower mail sae jesus sent oot twa o his follaers intae jerusalem wi thair oarders as ye gang intae tha citie he toul thaim a man cairryin a crockerie jar o watter wull meet ye follae him an say tae tha guidman o tha hoose he gangs intae tha maister says whar is ma ruim whar a can ait tha passower wi ma follaers an he wull show yis a big upstair ruim plenisht an aa ye ir tae mak it readie fer iz thair tha follaers gan oot an awa intae tha citie an the fun it jist as he haed saed sae the made readie tha boord fer tha passower mail whan it wus weel on in tha evenin jesus cum wi tha twal possels as the wur lyin at tha boord an aitin jesus saed a tell ye tha truith yin o yis thats suppin wi me noo is fer bethrayin me the wur aa sorrie whaniver the heerd this an yin bi yin the axt him is it me ye ir taakin aboot an anither yin saed is it me he saed bak tae thaim its yin o yous twal thats dippin his han in tha boul wi me fer a tha sinn o man maun follae tha road tha scriptures foretoul lang syne but wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays me faur better fer that man if he haed niver bin boarn an as the wur aitin jesus tuk breid in his hans an gien thenks tae god then he brauk it an he hannit it tae his follaers sayin tak it this is ma bodie an he tuk a bicker o wine an gien thenks tae god fer it then he hannit it roon an the aa drunk frae it an he saed tae thaim this is ma bluid a sign o gods new coveynant sealed wi ma bluid poored oot fer monie mairk this all drink nae mair o tha fruit o tha vine tae a drink a new wine in tha kingdom o god then the sung tha passower psaum an the went oot on tae tha moont o olives yisll aa faa awa on accoont o me tha nicht jesus saed tae thaim fer as its writ a wull strike tha shepherd an tha sheepll be scattert but efter a hae ris frae tha deid all tak tha foreroad o ye intae galilee an peter saed tae him tha mair tha restll faa awa all no peter jesus saed tae him a tell ye tha truith afore this verie nichts oot an tha rooster craas twice yell say thrie times ower that ye dinnae ken me na saed peter aa tha mair earnest no een if a hae tae dee wi ye a wull niver deny ye an aa alang wi him vood tha same an the cum tae a place bi tha name o gethsemane an he saed tae his follaers sit doon here til a gang an pray an he tuk peter jeames an jhone wi him an a wile dhread an pooerfu hairtsorra cum ower him an he saed tae thaim ma hairts brekkin wi anguish near tae deith yous bide here an stye awaak an gaun forrit a weethin he cast hissel tae tha grun an he prayed that if poassible tha oor o sufferin micht gang bye him abba faither he saed aa things ir poassible wi you nochts abain yer pooer tak awa this cup o sufferin frae me nane tha less its your wull am wantin an no ma ain an he cum bak an he fun thaim sleepin sae he saed tae peter simon ir ye sleepin cud ye no stye awaak even tha yin oor watch an pray sae ye dinnae gie in tae temptation tha spirits wullin but tha bodies waik an agane he gaed awa an he prayed tha same wurds an whaniver he cum bak yinst mair he fun thaim sleepin fer the cudnae keep thair een apen an the didnae ken whut answer tae gie him yit a thurd time he cum bak an he saed tae thaim ir yis aye sleepin an aye takkin yer rest thats eneuch noo luk tha oor haes cum an tha sinn o man is bethrayed intae tha hans o wrangdaers git up noo an well be aff here cums ma bethrayer tha wurds wusnae richt aff his tung whan up cum judas yin o tha twal an alang wi him wus a hale thrang o fowk wi swords an stavs sent oot frae tha heid preeshts an maisters o tha laa an tha elders an tha traiter haed gien thaim a sign him that a kiss saed he is tha man yer lukkin tak tha houl o him an keep him weel gairded as shuin as judas cum he gaed strecht up tae jesus an he saed rabbi an he kisst him then tha ithers tuk houl o jesus an arrestit him an yin o thaim that stud bye tuk oot a sword an he hut tha sarvint o tha heich preesht an he sneddit aff his lug jesus saed tae thaim am a some soart o a reiver that ye hae cum oot agin me wi swords an stavs fer tae tak me shair a wus wi yis iverie day in tha hoose o god taichin ye yit ye niver layed a han on me but whuts writ in tha halie scriptures maun cum aboot an tha hale lock o thaim left him an run awa but thair wus a young man follaein him wi nocht on him but a linen claith wrapt roon his nakit bodie an the tuk houl o him but he run aff scuddybare leain tha claith in thair hans an the tuk jesus awa tae tha heich preesht an aa tha heid preeshts tha elders o tha fowk an tha maisters o tha laa wus gethert thegither an peter follaed him a lang wye behin richt intae tha palace yaird an he sut doon alang wi tha gairds an wairmed hissel at tha apen fire noo tha heid preeshts an tha hale cooncil wus lukkin fer men at wud wutness agin jesus sae the cud pit him tae deith but the cudnae fin onie fer tha mair monies a yin wutnesst agin him whut the cum oot wi didnae cumpluther in tha enn some o tha wutnesses stud up an saed we heerd him oorsels he saed all pu doon this hoose o god bigged bi man an in thrie days all big anither yin an itll no be tha han o man that bigs it but thair stories didnae cumpluther an tha heich preesht ris tae his feet in tha middle o thaim aa an he axt jesus hae ye nae answer tae these chairges whut hae ye tae say fer yersel but jesus hel his tung sae tha heich preesht put anither question tae him ir ye tha christ tha sinn o tha blissit yin an jesus saed a am an ye wull see me tha sinn o man saitit at tha richt han o tha michtie yin an cumin in tha cloods o heiven wi that tha heich preesht tore his claes an saed whut need hae we o onie mair wutnesses yis hae aa heerd his blesphemie fer yersels whut dae yis jalouse o it an the aa saed he desarved tae be put tae deith an some o thaim fell tae spittin on him the put a blinfoul on him an hemmert him wi thair fists sayin tell iz wha hut ye an even tha gairds tuk tae slappin him wi tha flet o thair hans noo aa this time peter wus doon in tha coortyaird an yin o tha heich preeshts sarvin lasses cum bye seein peter wairmin hissel at tha fire she tuk a guid luk at him an saed you wur wi jesus frae nazareth tae sae ye wur but peter wudnae own up tae it a dinnae ken whut yer taakin aboot saed he an he slipt oot intae tha entrie jist then a rooster craad an tha sarvin lass saen him agane an yinst mair she stairtit tellin tha ithers hingin aboot thairs nae doot this mans yin o thaim peter denied it yinst mair an a wee while efter tha yins roon aboot saed tae peter agane ye maun be yin o thaim fer bi tha wye ye taak ye ir frae galilee as gods ma wutness saed peter a sweer a dinnae ken this man at that verie minnit tha rooster craad tha saicont time an richt awa peter haed mine o tha wurds jesus spauk tae him afore tha rooster craas twice ye wull deny me thrie times at tha verie thocht o it he brauk doon an wep sair at tha scraich o day tha heid preeshts got thegither wi tha elders an maisters o tha laa an tha hale cooncil taakt aboot whut the wud dae nixt the tyed jesus up an maircht him aff an hannit him ower tae pilate an pilate axt him ir you tha king o tha jews jesus answert you hae saed it an tha heid preeshts brocht forrit monie chairges agin him but he niver saed a wurd bak sae pilate axt him agane ir ye no fer sayin ocht whut aboot aa these chairges brocht agin ye but whaniver jesus wud say naethin mair pilate wus quare an tuk bak noo iverie yeir at tha passower faist pilate uist tae let yin o tha prisners oot whaiver tha fowk axt fer yin o thaim at tha time a man bi tha name o barabbas wus in fer murder alang wi ither rebels frae tha risin agin tha romans tha thrang gaed up an the axt pilate tae let a prisner oot as he aye daen yinst a yeir pilate axt thaim dae yis want me tae let oot tha king o tha jews fer he knowed richt weel it wus jist oot o spite that tha heid preeshts haed hannit jesus ower tae him but tha heid preeshts egged tha thrang on tae say na no jesus let barabbas oot sae whut wull a dae then wi tha yin yis caa king o tha jews axt pilate agane crucyfie him the cryed oot whut fer whuts he daen wrang pilate axt thaim but tha thrang jist roared aa tha mair crucyfie him noo pilate wus wantin tae plaise tha crood sae he lut barabbas oot tae thaim he haed jesus gien a guid whalin wi a whup an then he hannit him ower fer tae be crucyfied tha sodgers tuk jesus awa tae tha coortyaird o tha guviners big hoose an the brocht thegither tha hale regiment an the rigged him oot in a purple robe an the plettit thoarns thegither intae a croon an the put it on his heid an the begoud tae salute him cryin oot lang leeve tha king o tha jews the hut him ower tha heid agane an agane wi a stav an sput on him the got doon on thair knees afore him an lut on tae woarship him an efter the haed daen makkin a mockerie o him the tuk tha purple robe aff him an put his ain claes bak on an tuk him oot fer tae crucyfie him thair wus this man the caad simon frae cyrene tha faither o alexander an rufus makkin his wye in frae tha kintrie an the gart him tae cairrie tha cross an the brocht jesus tae a place bi tha name o golgotha mainin tha place o tha skull then the put wine mixt wi myrrh tae his mooth but he wudnae tak it an tha sodgers nailt him tae tha cross then the divid his claes amang thaim bi cloddin dice tae see wha wud get whut it wus nine in tha moarnin whaniver the crucyfied him an the put a signboord abain him wi tha chairge tha king o tha jews writ on it the crucyfied twa robbers alang wi him yin on his richt han side an tha tither on his left an sae it cum aboot laik tha scriptures saed aforehan he wus coontit amang tha laa brekkers thaim at waakt bye yellt abuse at him shakin thair heids an sayin hey you ye saed ye wur gaun tae desthroy tha hoose o god an big it agane in thrie days sae cum doon aff that cross noo an save yersel in tha same wye tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa mockt him an saed amang thairsels he saved ithers but he cannae save hissel this christ this king o israel shud cum doon aff that cross noo then well believe an tha twa that wus crucyfied alang wi jesus hurlt abuse at him forbye an dairkness cum ower tha hale lan frae nuin tae thrie in tha efternuin an jist then jesus gien a lood cry eli eli lama sabachthani mainin ma god ma god why hae ye forsook me an some o tha yins stannin nearhan heerd this an saed listen hes caain oot fer elijah yin o thaim run an wat a sponge wi soor wine put it on a lang stick an hel it up fer jesus tae drink lea him alane an well see if elijah cums tae tak him doon qo he an wi anither lood cry jesus gien his last breath tha curtin in tha halie o halies wus tore in twa frae tap tae bottom an whaniver tha centurion that stud fornent jesus heerd him cryin oot an saen tha wye he deed he saed thair can be nae doot this man wus tha sinn o god some weemen wus stannin awa bak takkin it aa in amang thaim wus mary magdalene an mary tha mither o young jeames an o joses as weel as salome these wur tha weemen that uist tae follae jesus an luk efter him whaniver he wus bak in galilee an monie ither weemen that haed cum up wi him tae jerusalem wur thair forbye it wus preparation day tha day afore tha sabbath sae as it wus wearin on tae evenin joseph o arimathea a man weel up in tha cooncil wha wus waitin on tha kingdom o god hissel tuk his courage in his hans an he went up tae pilate fer tae ax fer tha bodie o jesus pilate wus fair tuk bak whan he heerd that jesus wus aareadie deid he caad tha centurion an axt him wus that richt whaniver he heerd frae tha centurion that jesus wus aareadie deid he lut joseph hae tha bodie sae joseph bocht some linen claith tuk doon tha bodie happt it in tha claith an layed it in a tomb cut oot o tha roak then he rowlt tha stane agin tha apenin o tha tomb an mary magdalene an mary tha mither o joses saa whar the layed oot his bodie tha nixt evenin whan tha sabbath wus iver mary magdalene an salome an mary tha mither o jeames bocht sweet smellin oyles fer tae pit on jesus bodie on tha furst day o tha week at tha scraich o day jist as tha sin wus risin the cum tae tha tomb the axt amang thairsels whas gaun tae rowl awa tha stane fer iz frae tha mooth o tha tomb whan the lukt up the saa tha stane haed bin rowlt awa it wus a pooerfu big stane whaniver the went intae tha tomb the saen a young man wi a white robe on him sittin on tha richt han side an the wur thunnerstruck dinnae be sae feart he saed yis ir lukkin fer jesus o nazareth that the crucyfied hes ris hes no here luk fer yersels this is tha place whar the layed him oot but gae noo an tell his follaers an tell peter that jesus is awa on aheid o yis intae galilee yell see him thonner jist as he toul ye tha weemen cum oot frae tha tomb an tuk aff trimmlin an dumfoonert an the niver saed ocht tae oniebodie fer the wur that feart noo whan jesus ris on tha furst day o tha week he showed hissel furst tae mary magdalene that he haed driv seiven wickit spirits oot o an she went an toul thaim that haed bin wi him that wur sairhairtit an greetin whan the heerd that jesus wus leevin agane an that she haed saen him the didnae believe it an efter this jesus appeart lukkin differnt tae twa o thaim waakin oot intae tha kintrie the cum bak an toul tha ithers tae but the wudnae tak thair wurd fer it ether later on jesus showed hissel tae tha eleiven that wur aitin roon tha boord an he chackt thaim fer no haein mair faith an fer no bein wullin tae believe thaim that haed saen him efter he wus ris frae tha deid an he saed tae thaim gang oot intae tha hale warl an praich tha guid news tae aa mankine oniebodie that believes an is baptised wull be saved but oniebodie that daesnae believe wull be condemned whariver believers gangs these miraclis signs wull gae alang wi thaim in ma name the wull drive oot ill spirits an thell spake wi ither leids thell lift snakes up wi thair hans an if the drink onie deidlie puzhion itll no dae thaim onie hairm ava thell pit thair hans on seeck fowk an thell get better agane efter tha loard haed spauk tae thaim he wus taen up intae heiven an sut doon at tha richt han o god then his follaers went oot praichin iveriewhar an tha loard wrocht alang wi thaim an thair message wus bakt up wi miraclis signs amen maist warthie theophilus a hale lock o fowk haes taen it in han tae draa up an accoont o aa tha things that haes cum aboot amang iz the hae brocht thegither whut wus hannit doon tae iz frae yins that saa it aa wi thair ain een richt frae tha stairt an that becum sarvints o tha wurd o god an sae haein lukt intae it aa masel richt frae whaniver tha hale storie begun a thocht it wud be a guid thing fer me tae pit doon a trig accoont fer ye forbye theophilus tae mak ye shair o tha truith o whut ye hae bin lairnt whaniver herod wus king o judea thair wus this preesht caad zechariah noo he belanged til tha preeshtlie connection o abijah an his wife lizbeth hir femlie went bak til tha dochters o aaron as weel an the wur baith upricht in tha loards sicht keepin aa tha commauns an laas o tha loard but the haed nae femlie fer lizbeth cudnae hae weans an tha baith o thaim wus weel up in yeirs yin time whan it wus tha turn o zechariahs connection fer daein thair dutie in tha hoose o god zechariah wus pickt oot bi tha draain o lots laik tha preeshts aye daen in thaim days tae gang intae tha halie o halies an burn incense noo whaniver tha time cum roon fer burnin tha incense aa tha fowk wus ootbye prayin an aa o a suddent an angel o tha loard appeart stannin on tha richt han side o tha althar o incense zechariah wus tuk bak whan he saen tha angel an he wus hairtscarred but tha angel saed dinnae be feart zechariah fer god haes heerd yer prayer an yer wife lizbeth wull gie ye a wee sinn an ye maun caa him jhone yell be quare an gled whan hes boarn an sae wull a brave wheen o ither fowk alang wi ye fer he wull be ootstannin in tha sicht o tha loard hes no tae tak wine or onie ither kine o strang drink an hell be fu o tha halie spirit richt frae his mithers wame an hell gether monie an israelite bak tae tha loard thair god he wull be laik elijah fu o gods spirit an pooer he wull saffen tha hairts o tha faithers tae thair weans turnin contrairie yins tae a richt wye o thinkin an he wull gang afore tha loard tae mak tha fowk readie fer him zechariah axt tha angel hoo cud a be shair whut yer sayins richt fer baith me an tha wife is weel up in yeirs then tha angel saed am gabriel an am cum strecht frae god hissel fer tae gie ye this guid news mairk this weel seein as ye niver believed whut a toul ye yell be struck dum an no be fit tae taak tae tha weans boarn but thisll cum aboot in tha richt time aa tha while tha yins ootbye wus wunnerin hoo cum zechariah wus takkin sae lang in tha loards hoose whaniver he cum oot he cudnae say ocht ava ner taak tae tha fowk the knowed bi tha signs he wus giein he maun hae saen a vision in tha hoose o tha loard but aa tha while he cudnae taak bye an bye whaniver he haed his turn at tha althar daen he went bak hame no lang efter that lizbeth fun oot she wus gaun tae hae a wean an sae she stapt in tha hoose oot o sicht fer five month tha loard haes bin mair ner guid tae me lizbeth saed an am no affrontit onie langr wi haein nae femlie whan lizbeth wus six month gan god sent tha angel gabriel tae tha toon o nazareth in galilee tae a virgin bi tha name o mary that wus trystit tae a man caad joseph descendit frae king davit tha angel saed til hir fair faa ye blisst amang weemen tha loard is wi ye mary wus aa throu hirsel as she tried tae mak sense o whut tha angel haed telt hir dinnae be feart mary tha angel saed fer ye hae fun favour wi god tak tent ye ir fer haein a wean a sinn an ye maun caa him jesus he wull be ootstannin an be caad tha sinn o tha maist heich god an god wull gie him tha throne o his forefaither davit an he wull rule ower israel fer iver an aye an thairll be nae enn tae his kingdom mary axt tha angel hoo can a hae a wean wi me a virgin an niver bin wi a man tha angel toul hir tha halie spirit an tha pooer o god wull cum doon on ye an sae tha wean boarn tae ye wull be halie an wull be caad tha sinn o god an yer cousin lizbeth is fer haein a sinn in hir oul age as weel tha mair fowk thocht she cudnae hae onie but shes in hir sixth month fer thairs naethin ava god cannae dae mary saed weel am tha sarvint o tha loard an all dae whutiver he wants sae jist let it aa cum aboot laik ye say an then tha angel went awa frae hir efter this mary got hirsel readie an heidit aff in a big hurrie tae a toon in tha hills o judea up she cum thonner tae zechariahs hoose an toul lizbeth it wus guid tae see hir whaniver lizbeth heerd tha soon o marys voice tha bairn gien a lep in hir wame an she wus fu o tha halie spirit lizbeth caad oot wi a gled cry tae mary amang aa weemen yer blisst bi god an blisst be tha wean yer fer haein but hoo cum its me haes bin gien sae big an honour wi tha mither o ma loard cumin tae visit me tha minit a heerd yer wairm wurds a cud feel tha bairn in ma wame giein a lep fer joy ye ir in fer a blissin mary fer ye didnae doot tha loard wud dae jist whut he toul ye then mary saed ma sowl gies praise tae tha loard an ma spirit is gled in god ma saviour fer he haes tuk notysh o me a puir sarvin lass an aa generations frae noo on wull caa me blisst tha michtie yin haes daen wunnerfu things fer me an halie is his name his mercie bides wi thaim that houls him in reverence richt doon tha generations hoo pooerfu his michtie airm is that can skail thaim thats fu o thairsels he haes brocht doon tha michtie frae thair heich saits o pooer an liftit up tha doonanoots he haes fed tha hungrie wi guid things an hes turnt tha weelaff yins bak empiehannit he haes lukt efter his sarvint israel an he niver fergets tae be merciefu fer he promist this tae oor faithers tae abraham an aa his childer fer iver an aye then mary stapt ower wi lizbeth fer aboot thrie month afore gaun bak hame noo whan lizbeths time cum fer tha wean tae be boarn she haed a wee sinn wurd wusnae lang gaun roon o hoo guid tha loard haed bin til hir an hir freens an nighbers wus aa wile plaised whaniver tha wean wus echt day oul thair wus a guid turnoot o freens an nighbers at tha circumcisin an the wur aa wantin tae caa him efter his faither but na lizbeth saed he maun hae tha name o jhone whut the saed nane o yer femlie wus iver a jhone sae the axt tha weans faither bi makkin signs whut he thocht tha name shud be he waved fer thaim tae get him sumthin tae write on but the wur aa tuk bak whan he put this doon his name is jhone strecht aff zechariah fun his tung an he stairtit giein praise tae god aa tha fowk roon aboot wus dumfoonert an it wus tha taak o tha hale kintrieside o judea an iveriebodie that heerd aboot it wus wunnerin whut wye this wee fella wud turn oot oniebodie cud see that tha han o tha loard wus upon him then his faither zechariah fu o tha halie spirit stairtit makkin a proaphesie praise tha loard god o israel fer he haes cum doon amang his fowk an pyed tha coast o settin thaim free frae tha line o davits croon he haes brocht iz a michtie saviour jist laik he saed he wud throu tha mooth o his halie proaphits a lang while bak noo we wull be saved frae thaim thats agin aa we dae an frae thaim that cannae stan iz he haes showed mercie tae abraham an tae aa oor forefaithers bi haein mine o his halie coveynant sae noo we can sarve him wioot bein feart o thaim thats wantin tae hairm iz wi us bein halie an in guid stannin in tha ee o tha loard as lang as we leeve an you ma wee sinn yell get caad tha proaphit o tha maist heich god fer yell mak tha wye readie fer tha cumin o tha loard yell tell tha fowk hoo the can get saved bi haein thair sins forgien heivens risin sin is jist aboot tae brek on iz oot o tha guidness o gods hairt giein licht tae thaim that sits in tha dairk shedda o deith an roadin iz intae tha pad o peace jhone wus raired an he becum strang in spirit an he leeved oot in tha wulderness tae tha time cum tae stairt praichin tae israel roon aboot this time tha emperor caesar augustus gien oarders that a heidcoont wus tae be taen o aa tha fowk in iverie pairt o his empire this wus tha furst coont daen whaniver quirinius wus tha guviner o syria an iveriebodie wus haein tae gang tae whar the wur boarn tae pit thair names doon fer it noo acause josephs femlie went bak tae king davit he haed cum frae nazareth in galilee tae bethlehem in judea whar davit wus frae mary his wife tae be trevelt wi him tha mair o bein near hir time but whan the wur thair hir time cum tae hae tha wean an she haed hir furst babbie a sinn she rowlt him up in bits o claith an put him in a manger wi tha fother acause thair wus nae ruim fer thaim in tha ludgin hoose that nicht a wheen o herdmen wus oot in tha fiels mindin thair sheep aa o a suddent an angel o tha loard cum amang thaim an tha hale kintrie wus lichtit up bi tha glorie o tha loard an the wur wile feart but tha angel saed dinnae be feart fer am bringin yis tha best news iver an its fer tha hale warl tha saviour ay tha christ tha loard haes this nicht bin boarn in bethlehem tha toon o davit an this is hoo yell ken him yell fin a babbie rowlt in bits o claith lyin amang tha fother in a manger an aa o a suddent thair wus a hale thrang o angels tha airmies o heiven praisin god an sayin glorie tae god in tha maist heich heiven an peace on irth tae aa fowk that plaises him whaniver tha angels went bak tae heiven tha herdmen saed yin tae anither cum on well gang tae bethlehem an see this wunnerfu thing that haes happent that tha loard haes toul iz aboot the hurriet aff an the fun mary an joseph an thair wus tha babbie lyin in tha manger whaniver the saen him tha shepherds toul whut tha angel haed saed aboot this wean an aa that haed happent an the wur aa thunnerstruck bi whut the heerd frae tha shepherds mary didnae say much but she kep turnin these things ower an ower in hir hairt tha shepherds went bak tae hirdin thair sheep in tha fiels praisin an giein glorie tae god fer whut the haed saen an heerd it haed bin jist tha wye tha angel haed toul thaim echt days on whaniver the circumcised tha wean he wus gien tha name jesus tha name that tha angel saed tae caa him lang afore he wus boarn whan tha time cum roon fer mary an joseph tae dae whut tha laa o moses saed tae dae efter a weans birth the tuk him tae tha hoose o god in jerusalem tae mak thair offerin an tae present him tae tha loard tha laa o tha loard saed that tha furst boarn wee fella aye belangs tae tha loard as weel as this tha laa o tha loard saed that the haed tae offer a secryfice o twa turtle doos or twa young pigeons noo thair wus this man in jerusalem caad simeon that wus a guid godfearin man fu o tha halie spirit an lukkin forrit tae tha cumin o tha messiah acause tha halie spirit haed toul him that he wudnae dee afore he haed saen christ tha loard that day he wus guidit bi tha halie spirit tae gang tae tha hoose o god whan mary an joseph wus thair tae dae whut tha laa saed whaniver he saa tha wean he tuk him up in his airms an praised god an saed noo a can dee contentit fer a hae saen him jist as ye saed fer ma een haes saen tha saviour o tha warl that ye sent fer yin an aa his licht wull shine on aa tha gentiles an he wull be tha glorie o israel jesus faither an mither wus wile tuk bak at whut simeon saed aboot thair wean then simeon gien thaim a blissin an toul mary tha mither tae tak heed o this tha wean wull hae a pooerfu effect on monie a bodie in israel somell rise up an some wull faa he is a sign frae god but a lock o fowk wull hae naethin tae dae wi him this wye aa tha thochts in fowks hairts wull be oot in tha apen an as fer you mary sorra as shairp as a sword wull stab yer hairt then thair wus a wee weeda wumman echtiefower yeir oul caad anna that wus a proaphitess she haed bin merriet tae hir man fer seiven yeir afore he deed she wus a dochter o phanuel o tha tribe o asher she wud stap in tha hoose o god prayin an fastin nicht an day an tae aa thaim that wus lukkin forrit tae jerusalem bein set free she kep on tellin thaim aboot tha wean efter mary an joseph haed cairriet oot aa that needit daen tae keep tha laa the went bak hame tae tha toon o nazareth in galilee an as tha wean wus growein up he wus strang fu o wusdom an blisst bi god noo iverie yeir his faither an mither went tae jerusalem fer tha faist o tha passower an whan he wus twal yeir oul the went up tae jerusalem fer tha faist laik the aye daen whaniver tha faist wus ower his mither an faither set oot fer hame alang wi ither femlies no knowin that jesus haed styed behin in tha citie the jaloused he wus in tha companie an the trevelt on a hale day afore the misst him whan the cudnae fin him amang thair femlie an freens the went bak tae jerusalem tae luk fer him sae in tha enn it wus thrie days afore the fun him an thair he wus sittin in tha coortyaird o tha hoose o god takkin in whut tha taichers wur sayin an quizzin thaim aa that heerd him cudnae believe tha wye he wus answerin an tha much he knowed whan mary an joseph saen him the wur dumfoonert an his mither saed wean dear why hae ye daen this tae iz me an yer faither haes bin worriet seeck lukkin fer ye why wur ye lukkin fer me he axt did ye no ken that a maun be aboot ma faithers bizness here in his hoose but the didnae unnerstan whut he wus taakin aboot jesus went bak doon tae nazareth wi thaim an aye daen as he wus bid but mary kep aa these things in hir hairt an jesus growed up wise an strang an weel plaisin tae god an man noo whan tiberius caesar haed rult fer tha maist pairt o fifteen yeir pontius pilate wus tha guviner o judea herod wus tha tetrarch ower galilee his brither philip wus tha tetrarch ower iturea an trachonitis an lysanias wus tha tetrarch ower abilene an annas an caiaphas wus tha heich preeshts at this time god spauk tae jhone tha sinn o zechariah oot on tha muirs jhone gaed aa roon tha river joardan praichin an tellin tha fowk the shud be baptised fer tae show the haed turnt awa frae thair sins an tae show the haed turnt tae god fer him tae forgie thaim laik yell fin in tha buik o isaiah tha proaphit he spauk o jhone whan he saed a voice is cryin oot in tha wiles mak readie tha wye o tha loard mak his pads strecht fer him iverie glen wull be fillt in an iverie muntin an knowe levelt oot an tha crookit wyes wull be makkit strecht an tha reuch wyes makkit flet an aa leevin fowk wull see tha savin pooer o god sae jhone spauk tae tha thrang o fowk that cum oot tae get baptised wi him ye sleekit shooer o vipers wha telt ye tae rin frae tha wrath o god thats cumin ye maun show bi tha wye ye leeve that ye hae turnt awa frae yer sins dinnae stairt sayin tae yersels we hae abraham fer oor faither an hae daen wi that fer a tell ye that oot o thon stanes god can mak weans fer abraham gods hatchit is noo hoverin at tha ruit o tha trees an thaim that dinnae gie guid fruit wull be fellt an pitcht intae tha fire whutll we dae then tha thrang wus axin him jhone telt thaim tha yin that haes twa shifts shud gie yin tae him that haes nane an tha yin that haes mait shud dae tha same tha tex men cum tae be baptised as weel an the axt jhone maister whut ir we tae dae an jhone telt thaim dinnae ax fowk fer mair ner ye shud an tha sodgers axt him whut shud we dae jhone saed til thaim dinnae squeeze tha last pennie oot o fowk ner blekmail thaim fer thair siller an mak dae wi whut ye get pyed an be gled o it aa tha fowk wus waitin an wunnerin wus jhone mebbe tha christ but jhone toul thaim aa am onlie baptisin wi watter but yinll cum that wull baptise ye wi tha halie spirit an wi fire he is michtier ner me am no fit tae lowse his buits fer him wi his winnowin fork in his han hell redd up his thrashinflure an gether tha wheat intae his barn but hell burn tha caff wi a fire ye cannae pit oot jhone praicht tha guid news in monies a wye tae aa tha fowk but he telt herod tha tetrarch it wusnae richt tha wye he haed tuk herodias his brither philips guidwife an he toul him aff fer aa tha ither wrang things he haed daen as weel an warst o aa herod put jhone in jail whan aa tha fowk wus gettin baptised bi jhone jesus wus baptised as weel an whaniver he wus gettin baptised he wus prayin an tha heivens apent tha halie spirit cum doon on him laik a doo an a voice cum frae heiven sayin ye ir ma sinn ma hairts delicht an am weel plaised wi ye an jesus wus roon aboot thurtie yeir oul whan he stairtit his praichin an taichin he wus fowk thocht tha sinn o joseph that wus tha sinn o heli an heli wus tha sinn o matthat matthat wus tha sinn o levi levi wus tha sinn o melki melki wus tha sinn o an adam wus tha sinn o god an jesus bein fu o tha halie spirit cum bak frae tha joardan an wus taen bi tha spirit intae tha wulderness fer fowertie days he wus tempit bi tha deil an in aa thaim days he didnae ait ocht ava an at tha enn o tha time he wus gye hungrie an tha deil saed tae him if ye ir tha sinn o god tell that stane thair tae turn intae breid an jesus spauk bak tae him an saed it is writ doon that man cannae leeve bi breid alane but bi iverie wurd o god then tha deil tuk him up heich an lut him see aa tha kingdoms o tha warl in a weethin o time tha deil saed tae him aa tha pooer o these kingdoms a wull gie ye an tha glorie that gangs wi thaim fer its mine tae gie tae whaiver a laik gin ye wull jist boo doon tae me it wull aa be yer ain jesus saed til him awa or that satan fer tha guid buik says ye ir tae woarship tha loard yer god an tae sarve naebodie but him an tha deil brocht him tae jerusalem an tuk him up tae tha verie tap o tha hoose o god an saed tae him if ye ir tha sinn o god throw yersel doon frae here fer tha guid buik says he wull tell his angels tae luk efter ye an keep an ee on ye wi thair hans the wull haud ye up fer fear ye dunt yer fit agin a stane an jesus saed bak tae him its in tha buik forbye ye ir no tae temp tha loard yer god an whan tha deil haed stapt aa tha tempin he tuk aff an lut him be fer a while an jesus cum bak in tha pooer o tha spirit intae galilee an he wus tha taak o tha hale kintrie roon aboot an he taicht in thair meetin hooses an he haed a great name amang thaim aa an he cum tae nazareth whar he haed bin raired an as he aye daen he went intae tha meetin hoose on tha sabbath day an stud up fer tae read the gien him tha screed o tha proaphit isaiah an whan he haed apent tha buik he fun tha place whar it wus writ doon tha spirit o tha loard is cum ower me fer he haes anointit me tae tell oot tha guid news tae tha puir he haes sent me fer tae hail tha hairtbrauk tae lowse thaim thats bun tae gie sicht tae tha blin fer tae set free thaim thats trod doon an fer tae praich tha yeir o tha loards grace whan jesus haed rowlt up tha screed he gien it bak tae tha man in chairge an he sut doon an naebodie in tha meetin hoose cud tak thair een aff him an he stairtit aff bi tellin thaim whut ye hae jist heerd frae tha guid buik haes cum aboot theday an aa spauk weel o him an the cud harlie tak in tha wunsum wurds that cum oot o his mooth is this no josephs sinn the axt he telt thaim this nae doot ye wull quote tha oul saw at me docter hail yersel an yell say whut we heerd ye daen in capernaum dae it here in yer ain hametoon as weel an he saed a warrant ye this nae proaphit is iver walcum in his ain hametoon am tellin ye tha truith in tha days o elijah tha heivens wus shut up fer thrie yeir an six month an thair wus a big hungr ower aa tha lan an thair wus monie weedas in israel at tha time elijah wusnae sent til onie o thaim but onlie tae a weeda wumman in serepta near tha toon o sidon forbye thair wus monie lepers in israel in tha time o elisha tha proaphit but nane o thaim wus makkit clain apairt frae naaman frae syria whaniver the heerd these things aa tha fowk in tha meetin hoose wus wile angrie an the ris up an the driv him oot o tha toon an the tuk him up tae tha broo o tha hill whar tha toon wus bigged fer tae throw him doon heid furst but he passt richt throu tha middle o thaim an gaed on his wye then jesus went on doon tae capernaum a toon o galilee an he wus taichin tha fowk thair on tha sabbath day an the wur aa thunnerstruck wi his taichin fer tha wurds he spauk wus pooerfu an in tha meetin hoose thair wus a man that haed a demon an ill spirit in him an he scraicht oot lood hey lea iz alane jesus o nazareth whut dae ye want wi iz hae ye cum here tae dae awa wi iz a ken richt weel wha ye ir ye ir tha halie yin o god but jesus chackt him an saed houl yer wheesht an cum oot o him an tha demon throwed him tae tha grun fornent thaim aa an it cum oot o him an it didnae hurt him ava an the wur aa dumfoonert an taakt amang thairsels an saed did ye iver hear tha laik o it fer wi thortie an pooer he oarders tha ill spirits an at his biddin the cum oot sae jesus wus tha taak o tha hale kintrieside roon aboot an he gaed oot o tha meetin hoose an on tae simons hame noo simons guidwifes mither wus wile baad wi a faivir an the axt jesus fer tae mak hir better he stud ower hir an he chackt tha faivir an it left hir she got up at yinst an stairtit tae sarve an luk efter thaim noo whan tha sin wus gaun doon aa tha yins that haed seeck fowk wi aa kines o disaises brocht thaim tae jesus an he put his hans on iverie yin o thaim an hailt thaim forbye demons cum oot o monie o thaim cryin oot ye ir christ tha sinn o god an he wud chack thaim oarderin thaim no tae spake fer the kent that he wus tha christ whan it wus daylicht he depairtit an went tae a place he cud be on his ain an tha fowk lukt fer him an cum tae him an axt him fer tae stye fer the didnae want him tae lea thaim but he saed tae thaim a maun praich tha guid news o tha kingdom o god tae tha ither toons as weel fer thats why a wus sent sae he kep on praichin in tha meetin hooses o galilee yin day jesus wus stannin bi tha loch o gennesaret an aa tha fowk wus croodit roon him pushin an shuvin fer tae hear tha wurd o god an he saa twa boats pued up bi tha watters edge but tha fishermen wus awa oot o thaim an the wur waashin thair neyts an jesus got intae yin o tha boats whut belanged tae simon an axt him tae pit oot a weethin frae tha lan an he sut doon an taicht tha fowk frae tha boat noo whan he haed daen taakin tae tha fowk he toul simon pit oot tae tha deep watter an let doon yer neyts fer a haal simon saed dominie we hae wrocht aa nicht an tuk naethin but nanethaless all dae as ye bid me an let doon tha neyts an whan the haed daen this the catched a pooerfu lock o fish thair wus that monie that tha nettin stairtit tae cum apairt sae the waved tae thair nighbers in tha ither boat tae cum an gie thaim a han an the fillt baith boats sae fu that the near sunk whaniver simon peter saa this he faad on his knees afore jesus an saed gawa frae me loard fer am a sinfu man whaniver him an aa that wur wi him saa tha haal o fish the cud harlie tak it in an nether cud jeames an jhone tha sinns o zebedee that wur nighberin wi simon jesus saed tae simon dinnae be feart frae noo on its men yell be ketchin whaniver the haed brocht thair boats tae lan the left aa an the follaed efter jesus anither time whan jesus wus in yin o tha toons thair wus this man wile baad wi leprosie whaniver he saen jesus he faad doon afore him an begged him loard if ye hae a mine tae ye can mak me clain an he put his han oot an toucht him sayin a wull shairlie be clain an richt awa tha leprosie wus gan frae him an he chairged him tae tell naebodie but bid him gang an show hissel tae tha preesht gie an offerin fer yer cleansin saed jesus as moses telt iz in tha laa fer a wutness tae yin an aa that yer weel agane but fer aa this tha hale kintrieside taakt aboot him aa tha mair an cum tae hear him in thair droves an tae be cured o thair ailments then jesus tuk hissel awa frae thaim intae a quait place fer tae pray as he wus in tha habit o daein anither day as he wus lairnin tha fowk thair wus pharisees an taichers o tha laa sittin bye the haed cum frae aa tha villages roon aboot oot o galilee an judea an jerusalem an tha pooer o tha loard wus thair fer tae hail thaim an luk see a wheen o men wus bringin a paralysed man on a bed an the wur lukkin fer a wye fer tae bring him intae tha hoose tae lay him doon afore jesus an whan the cudnae fin a road in acause o aa tha thrang the went up on tae tha tap o tha hoose an lut him doon on his bed throu tha ruif in amang tha fowk richt fornent jesus whaniver he saa thair faith he saed ma freen yer sins is aa forgien tha maisters o tha laa an tha pharisees stairtit taakin amang thairsels wha daes he think he is taakin sitch blesphemie wha can forgie sins but god alane jesus knowed whut thair thochts wur an saed tae thaim hoo cum yis ir thinkin laik this is it aisier tae say yer sins ir forgien or tae say get up an waak but noo yell see that tha sinn o man haes tha pooer tae forgie sins here on irth jesus then saed tae tha man that haed bin paralysed get up tak yer bed wi ye an gang awa hame an richt awa he got up afore thaim gethert up his beddin an went aff hame praisin god the cud harlie believe it an the gien glorie tae god yit at tha same time the felt feart an saed we hae saen things theday that ir ower ocht efter this jesus went oot an saa a tex man bi tha name o levi sittin in his hut an jesus saed tae him follae me levi ris up left aa behin him an follaed jesus an levi layed on a big spreed in his ain hoose fer jesus an thair wus a hale lock o tex men an tha laik thair roon tha table wi thaim but tha maisters o tha laa an tha pharisees wus mutterin tae tha follaers o jesus fer why ir ye aitin an drinkin wi tex men an sinners an jesus saed tae thaim fowk that ir hale an hairtie dinnae need a docter but seeck fowk dae a hinnae cum fer tae caa guid leevin fowk tae repentance but a hae cum tae caa sinners some fowk saed tae him jhones follaers ir aye fastin an prayin an sae dae tha follaers o tha pharisees but your yins is aye aitin an drinkin but jesus saed tae thaim ye cannae mak waddin guests fast while tha bridegruim is wi thaim thairll cum a day but whaniver tha bridegruim wull be tuk awa frae thaim an thatll be tha time the wull fast he toul thaim anither parable naebodie taks a piece o claith frae a new coat tae patch an oul yin if he daes tha new patch wull pu awa frae tha oul an forbye the wudnae match an naebodie pits new wine intae oul wineskins fer if ye dae tha new wine wull brust tha oul skins tha wine wull spill oot an tha skins wull be ruint na ye hae tae pit new wine intae new skins then baith wull be aa richt forbye naebodie efter haein drunk oul wine wud richt awa be lukkin new wine fer he wud say tha oul wine is better cum twa sabbaths efter this jesus wus gaun throu tha coarnfiels an his follaers pluckt tha heids aff tha coarn tae ait giein thaim a rub atween thair hans an some o tha pharisees axt thaim hoo cum yis ir daein whuts agin tha laa on tha sabbath day jesus gien tha answer hae ye no read whut davit daen whaniver him an his freens wus hungrie hoo he gaed intae tha hoose o god an tuk an et tha halie showbreid an gien it tae thaim that wus wi him forbye shair that wus agin tha laa fer oniebodie but tha preeshts an he saed tae thaim tha sinn o man is loard o tha sabbath anaa then on anither sabbath he gaed intae tha meetin hoose tae taich tha fowk an thair wus a man thair an his richt han wus wuthert tha maisters o tha laa an tha pharisees kep thair een on jesus tae see wud he hail on tha sabbath sae as tae hae sumthin agin him but he kent richt weel thair thochts an saed tae tha man wi tha baad han stan up whar the can aa see ye an up he got then jesus saed tae thaim daes tha laa say ye shud dae guid or dae ill on tha sabbath shud ye save life or dae awa wi it an lukkin roon at thaim aa he saed tae tha man streetch oot yer han an he did an his han cum as guid as tha ither yin the wur aa richt an maad an wur colloguin wi yin anither whut the cud dae wi jesus bye an bye jesus went oot tae a muntin fer tae pray tae god an he kep at it tha hale nicht lang an whaniver it wus day he caad his follaers tae him an he waaled oot twal o thaim an gien thaim tha name o possels simon that he caad peter forbye an his brither andra jeames an jhone philip an bartholomew mattha an tammas jeames tha sinn o alphaeus simon tha yin the caad a zealot judas jeamess sinn an judas iscariot tha yin that bethrayed jesus later on an he cum doon frae tha muntin wi thaim an tuk his stance on a flet bit o grun an a hale crood o his follaers alang wi a wile thrang o fowk oot o judea an jerusalem an frae alang tha shores o tyre an sidon cum tae hear him an tae be cured o thair ailments an tha yins vext sair wi ill spirits wus aa cured an tha hale crood o fowks wantit tae touch him acause a pooer o guid wus cumin oot o him an curin thaim aa an jesus wi his een on his follaers saed blisst ir tha puir fer yours is tha kingdom o god blisst ir you thats hungrie noo fer yis wull get yer fill blisst ir you thats greetin noo fer yis wull be lachin then blisst ir you whaniver fowk hait ye or gie ye tha coul shooder baadmooth ye or blekin yer name on accoont o tha sinn o man be richt gled on that day an gie a lep fer joy fer yis hae a pooerfu reward waitin fer ye in heiven fer thair faithers daen tha same tae tha proaphits but sorra tae you weelaff fowk fer ye hae got aa ye ir gettin sorra tae you thats fu noo fer yis wull be hungrie sorra tae you that ir lachin fer yis wull be greetin an sorrafu wae faa yis whan aa fowk spakes weel o ye fer thair faithers daen tha same wi tha fauss proaphits but am sayin tae yous thats listenin love yer faes dae guid tae thaim that haits ye bliss thaim that curses ye an pray fer thaim that wushes ye ill wull an if a bodie gies ye a slap on tha cheek turn tha ither side til him forbye an if a bodie is lukkin yer tapcoat aff ye let him hae yer shirt as weel if oniebodie axes ye fer ocht gie it tae thaim an dinnae be lukkin it bak an jist dae tae ithers whut yis wud want thaim tae dae tae yersels an if yis onlie love thaim at loves you thairs naethin parteeclar aboot that even sinners love tha yins that love thaim an if yis dae guid tae thaim at dae guid tae yersels whut credit is that tae yis sinners dae jist tha same an if yis onlie lenn tae thaim at yis ir hopin tae get it bak frae thairs nae thenks in that fer even sinners lenn tae sinners sae as tae get bak tha same agane but love yer faes dae guid an lenn no hopin tae get oniethin bak an yis wull hae great reward an wull be sinns o tha maist heich fer he is kine tae tha ungratefu an tha wickit sae be merciefu jist as yer faither is merciefu dinnae judge ithers an yell no be judged yersels dinnae condemn an yisll no be condemned forgie an yisll be forgien gie an yisll be gien tae a guid misure preest doon shuk thegither an skailin ower wull be gien tae yis fer tha misure yis gie wull be tha misure yis get bak an jesus spauk a parable tae thaim can tha blin lead tha blin wull the no baith faa intae tha sheuch a follaer is no abain his taicher but whaniver he is weel lairnt he wull be jist laik his taicher an why dae ye see tha skelf in yer brithers ee but ye dinnae see tha plenk in yer ain ee hoo can ye say tae yer brither cum here brither let me tak tha skelf oot o yer ee an yit ye cannae see tha plenk in yer ain ee ye oul hippycrate ye pu tha plenk oot o yer ain ee furst an then yell be able tae see proper tae tak tha skelf oot o yer brithers ee a guid tree daesnae gie rotten fruit ner daes a rotten tree gie guid fruit ye know iverie tree bi its ain fruit ye dinnae pick figs frae a thoarn bush ner grapes frae a blekberrie bush a guid man brings guid oot o tha guidness stored in his hairt an a evil man brings evil oot o tha evil in his hairt fer whutiver his hairt is fu o thats whut cums oot o his mooth an why caa me loard loard an no dae whut a say whaiver cums tae me an hears these wurds o mine an heeds thaim all show ye whut he is laik hes laik a man that bigged his hoose an he dug deep an set tha fittins on a roak an whaniver tha river wus in fu spate an swep agin tha hoose it cudnae shift it fer it wus set on a roak but tha yin that hears whut a say an daesnae dae it is laik a man that bigged his hoose wi nae fundations ava an whaniver tha rush o watter hut it tha hale hoose brauk apairt at yinst whan jesus haed daen taakin tae tha fowk he gaed intae capernaum thair wus this centurion thonner haed a sarvin man he thocht weel o that wus seeck an deein whan he heerd tell o jesus he axt some elders o tha jews tae fin oot if jesus wud cum an mak tha sarvin man weel agane whan the cum tae jesus the kep beggin him sayin ye shud dae sumthin fer this man fer he wus tarrible fand o us jews an he even bigged a meetin hoose fer iz he desarves ye tae dae this fer him sae jesus gan awa wi thaim whan he wus nearhan tha hoose tha centurion sent freens oot fer tae tell him loard dinnae bother cumin onie nearder fer am no fit tae hae ye cum unner ma ruif its no fer tha laiks o me tae cum tae you but jist say tha wurd an ma sarvin man wull be weel agane fer a ken hoo tae tak oarders a hae sodgers unner me as weel a tell yin tae gang an he gangs an anither yin tae cum an he cums a tell ma sarvin man dae this an he daes it whan jesus heerd this he wus stoondit at him an he turnt roon tae tha crood cumin efter him an saed am tellin ye a niver fun oniebodie wi sitch faith in aa israel whan tha freens that wur sent oot cum bak tae tha centurions hoose the fun tha sarvin man weel agane tha nixt day jesus went tae a toon caad nain his follaers an a big crood o fowk cum alang wi him whan he cum near tha gate intae tha toon it happent that the wur cairryin oot a deid man a weeda wummans ainlie sinn an a big crood wus follaein hir oot frae tha toon whan tha loard lukt at hir he tuk peetie on hir an he toul hir dinnae greet he cum ower an put his han on tha coffin an tha yins that wur cairtin it stapt he saed cum on young man up ye get tha deid man sut up an stairtit tae taak an jesus gien him bak tae his mither the wur aa hairtscarred an the praised god sayin a pooerfu proaphit haes ris up frae amang iz god haes cum tae halp his fowk oot whut jesus daen that day wus tha taak o tha hale o judea an aa tha kintrie roon aboot jhone heerd aboot aa this frae his follaers an he caad fer twa o thaim an sent thaim tae tha loard fer tae ax wud you be tha yin that wus supposed tae cum or shud we be lukkin oot fer some ither bodie the cum tae jesus an saed jhone tha baptiser sent iz tae ax ye ir you tha yin that wus supposed tae cum or shud we be lukkin oot fer some ither bodie at that oor jesus made a lock o seeck fowk weel agane frae thair ailments he rid thaim o ill spirits an he made fowk that wur blin able tae see agane he toul jhones follaers gang bak an gie jhone an accoont o whut ye hae saen an heerd blin fowk can see noo lameters can waak fowk wi leprosie ir makkit weel deef fowk can hear tha deid leeve agane an tha guid news is praicht tae tha puir an blisst is tha yin that daesnae misdoot me whan jhones messengers went awa jesus stairtit tae taak tae tha croods aboot jhone he axt thaim whut did ye gang oot intae tha wulderness fer tae see wus it tae see tha rushes sweein in tha wun if no whut did ye think ye wud see oot thair a man aa rigged oot in fancie claes na fowk thats weel dresst an leevin it up its in kings palaces ye wull fin them sae whut did yis gae oot fer tae see wus it a proaphit ay a tell ye an faur mair ner a proaphit this is tha yin tha scriptures taak aboot whaniver the say listen all senn oot ma messenger aheid o ye he wull mak readie tha wye afore ye a tell ye thair wus niver a better man boarn o a wumman ner jhone an yit tha yin that is laist in tha kingdom o god is a better man ner him aa tha fowk even tha tex men whaniver the haed heerd this the knowed fer sartin gods wye wus richt fer the haed bin baptised bi jhone but tha pharisees an tha laayers haednae hoult wi gods plan fer thaim they haednae bin baptised bi jhone jesus axt thaim whut wull a say aboot tha fowk nooadays whut kine o fowk ir the the ir laik weans sittin doon at tha mairket caain oot tae yin anither we played tha whustle fer ye an ye wudnae daunce we sung a dirge tae ye an ye wudnae greet fer jhone tha baptiser wusnae intae aitin breid ner drinkin wine whaniver he cum an ye say thairs a baad spirit in him but tha sinn o man cum aitin an drinkin an ye say wud ye luk at him hes a glutton an hes tarrible fand o tha drink sae he is tha freen o tex men an wrangdaers but whan fowk daes whuts richt the prove tha wusdom o gods wyes noo yin o tha pharisees axt jesus fer his denner sae jesus went hame wi him fer a bite tae ait an tuk his place at tha boord an thair wus this wumman wi a baad name aboot tha toon an whaniver she heerd that jesus wus aitin at tha pharisees hoose she brocht a wee crock o scent wi hir an as she wus behin him greetin hir tears stairtit tae faa on jesuss feet tha wumman dryed his feet wi tha hair o hir heid an she kisst thaim as she poored tha scent ower thaim noo whaniver tha pharisee that haed axt him tae cum saen this he thocht tae hissel if this man wus a proaphit he shud hae kent whut soart o a wumman this is that toucht him he shud a knowed shes a baad wumman jesus toul him a want tae tell ye sumthin simon simon saed maister whut hae ye tae tell me thair wus this man saed jesus that wud hae lent siller tae fowk an twa men owed him tha yin owed him five hunner siller coins an tha ither owed him fiftie noo whan nane o tha twa haed eneuch siller tae pye him bak tha moneylender toul thaim it wus aa richt an he lut thaim aff whut yin o thaim dae ye think wud laik him tha maist simon saed tha yin that he lut aff that owed him tha maist a suppose says jesus ay thats richt ye hae saed it then jesus lukt ower at tha wumman an saed tae simon dae ye see this wumman a cum intae yer hoose an ye niver gien me onie watter fer ma feet but she haes waasht ma feet wi hir tears an dichtit thaim wi hir hair ye didnae show that ye wur gled tae see me bi giein me a kiss but this wumman haesnae stapt kissin ma feet sin a cum in ye niver even thocht o pittin a drap o oyle on ma heid but this wumman haes poored scent aa ower ma feet a tell ye hir monie wrangdaeins haes bin forgien fer she haes showed that much love tae me tha yin that haes bin forgien a wee bit wull onlie love a wee bit an jesus saed tae tha wumman yer wrangdaeins ir forgien tha ither fowk thair at tha table stairtit tae taak amang thairsels sayin whut kine o man is this that can een forgie wrangdaeins then jesus saed tae tha wumman yer faith haes saved ye gang weel efter this jesus trevelt roon aa tha toons an villages praichin an tellin o tha guid news o tha kingdom o god an tha twal wus wi him forbye thair wur sartin weemen that haed bin cured o wickit spirits an ailments thair wus mary caad magdalene seiven ill spirits cum oot o hir an johanna tha guidwife o chuza that run herods hoose an susanna an monie mair that wur aye giein whut the haed tae luk efter jesus noo a wile thrang o fowk cum frae toon efter toon tae gether roon him an he toul thaim this parable thair wus this fairmer went oot tae saa seed an as he wus skailin it some drapt doon alang tha pad an it got waakit iver an tha wile burds peckt it up some faad on roakie grun an it wus nae shuiner abraird tae it wuthert awa fer want o watter an some faad doon amang thoarns an breers an tha thoarns sprung up tuk ower an chokt it an ither seed faad on guid grun an it growed weel an tha hairst wus guid aboot a hunner times mair than wus saad whan he haed toul thaim aa this he caad oot let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent an his follaers axt whuts this parable aboot an he saed tae thaim tae you god haes gien an unnerstannin o tha saicrets o his kingdom but tae tha ithers a taak in parables these fowk micht aye be lukkin but the niver see an aye listenin but the niver unnerstan noo heres tha mainin o tha parable tha seed is tha wurd o god tha seed that faad doon nixt tha pad stans fer tha fowk that hears tha wurd but then alang cums tha deil an he taks it oot o thair hairts sae that the ir stapt frae believin an cannae be saved tha seed on tha roak stans fer tha yins that gie ear til gods wurd an tak it in wi a gled hairt but it haes nae ruit an daesnae houl wi thaim fer whan haird times cum alang the gie up an the hae nae mair mine o it an tha seed that fell amang tha thoarns thats laik fowk that hears tha wurd o god an the cairrie on fer a weethin but in tha enn aa tha warls bothers tha
