catter an tha guid times staps thaim growein up strecht an sonsie but tha seed that faad on guid grun thats laik fowk that ir warthie an guid an gie ear til tha wurd o god the houl it in thair hairts til in tha enn the reap a rich hairst naebodie lichts a lamp an pits a jar ower it or pits it unner a bed ye set it oot whar fowk can see it whan the cum in fer thairs naethin hid that wull no be toul an thairs naethin put awa that wull no be brocht oot intae tha apen mine hoo ye listen fer him that haes plentie wull be gien mair an him that haes little even whut he thinks he haes wull be tuk awa frae him noo jesus mither an his brithers cum tae see him but the cudnae get near tae him fer aa tha crood o fowk jesus wus toul yer mither an brithers ir waitin ootbye lukkin tae see ye but he cum bak wi ma mither an ma brithers ir tha yins that listen tae tha wurd o god an follae it yin day jesus got intae a boat wi his follaers an he saed tae thaim cmon an well gang ower tae tha ither side o tha loch sae the put oot noo while the wur oot on tha watter jesus lay doon fer a sleep an it begun tae get wile stoarmie an tha boat begun tae tak on watter an it wus tarrible dangeris his follaers went up tae him an waakent him dominie dominie the caad oot well be droont an jesus ris an he chackt tha blowsterin wun an waves aa at yinst tha wun drapt an tha stoarm wus ower whar is yer faith he axt thaim an the wur feart an the wunnert an the saed tae yin anither whut kine o a man is this that can mak een tha wun an tha waves dae as he bids thaim jesus an his follaers cum tae tha lan whar tha gerasenes leeved strecht ower tha loch frae galilee an whaniver he wus gettin oot o tha boat thair wus this man cum up tae him frae tha toon he wus fu o demons an haed bin rinnin roon fer a lang time wi naethin on him an leevin in tha graveyaird rether than a hoose whan he saen jesus he faad at his feet an guldert whut is it ye ir efter wi me jesus sinn o tha maist heich god am beggin ye quit tormentin me fer ye see jesus haed bid tha ill spirit tae lea him alane betimes it haed made him brek awa frae his gairds an tha chains the haed bun him up wi an it haed driv him oot intae tha wiles an jesus axt him whut dae the caa ye am caad legion saed he fer monie demons haed tuk houl o him an tha demons kep on beggin jesus no tae be put intae tha blek pit noo a big herd o pigs wus oot hokin fer food on tha braeside an tha demons begged tae be sent intae tha pigs an jesus allooed it sae tha demons cum oot o legion an the went intae tha pigs tha herd tuk aff doon tha hill heid furst intae tha loch an tha hale lock wus droont an whaniver tha yins that wur lukkin efter tha pigs saen whut haed happent the run aff an toul iveriebodie in tha toon an kintrie roon aboot an tha fowk that heerd cum oot tae see fer thairsels an whan the cum tae jesus the fun tha man tha demons haed cum oot o legion wus sittin thair quait at tha feet o jesus he haed his claes on an wus in his richt mine an the wur wile scarred an thaim that haed saen tha hailin o tha man wi tha demons toul tha ithers aa aboot it an aa tha fowk frae tha lan o tha gadarenes begged jesus tae gang awa fer the wur wile feart sae jesus heidit aff tae tha boat fer tae gae awa bak ower the loch tha man tha demons went oot o besocht jesus that he cud gae alang wi him but jesus toul him tae lea an saed gang awa hame an tell tha fowk aboot tha great things god haes daen fer ye sae tha man went hame an he toul tha hale toon whut jesus haed daen fer him noo whaniver jesus cum bak a crood o fowk bid him walcum fer the wur aa waitin on him then a man caad jairus a heidyin o tha meetin hoose cum an faad doon at jesus feet beggin wi him tae cum tae his hoose fer his ainlie dochter a wee lass o twal yeir oul wus deein but as jesus wus gaun thair tha thrang wus croodin roon him an thair wus this wumman amang thaim that haed bother wi bleedin fer twal yeir but naebodie cud dae oniethin fer hir she cum ahint jesus an she toucht tha enn o his cloke an strecht awa tha bleedin stapt wha toucht me axt jesus whan naebodie owned up tae it peter saed dominie fowk ir pushin an shuvin aa roon ye an ye ir wunnerin wha toucht ye saed jesus summodie haes toucht me fer a felt tha pooer gang oot o me tha wumman seein that she cudnae hide cum an faad doon afeart an trimmlin at his feet an afore tha hale fowk she toul whut fer she haed toucht him an hoo she haed bin makkit weel at yinst then jesus saed dochter yer faith haes hailt ye fair ye weel tha wurds wusnae richt aff jesus tung whan this man cum frae tha hame o tha heidyin o tha meetin hoose an saed tae him jairus yer dochter is deid dinnae bother tha maister onie mair whan jesus heerd this he toul him dinnae be feart jist believe an she wull be hailt an whan jesus cum tae tha hoose tha yins he allooed tae cum in wi him wur peter jhone an jeames alang wi tha faither an mither o tha wee lass noo the wur aa greetin an wailin fer hir but jesus saed be quait shes no deid shes jist sleepin an the stairtit tae lach fer the kent she wus deid hooaniver jesus tuk hir bi tha han an caad oot cum on chile up ye git an hir spirit cum bak an at yinst she got up an he toul thaim tae gie hir a bite tae ait tha mither an faither cudnae believe thair een but jesus toul thaim on nae accoont tae say tae oniebodie whut haed happent efter jesus caad his twal follaers thegither he gien thaim pooer iver aa tha demons an pooer tae cure aa kines o disaises an he sent thaim oot tae praich tha kingdom o god an tae hail tha seeck an he toul thaim tak naethin wi ye fer tha road nether stav tae studie ye ner baag tae cairrie ocht in ner breid ner siller an nae spare claes whan ye gang intae a hoose stap ower thair tae its time tae tak yer lave o that toon an whar yer no walcum yer tae lea that toon an yer tae dicht aff een tha stour o yer feet as a wutness an warnin tae thaim an aff the went gaun frae village tae village praichin tha guid news an hailin thair an thonner noo whan herod tha tetrarch heerd aboot aa tha things that jesus wus daein he wus fair fasht acause some fowk saed that jhone tha baptiser wus ris frae tha deid some thocht that yin o tha oultime proaphits haed cum bak tae life an ithers thocht it wus mebbe elijah but herod saed a haed tha heid tuk aff jhone but whas thon am hearin sitch things aboot an he wus ower enxious tae see jesus an tha possels whan the cum bak toul jesus aboot aa tha things the haed daen an he tuk thaim aff bi thair lane tae a quait place near tha toon caad bethsaida but tha croods kent this an follaed him an he bid thaim walcum an taakt tae thaim o tha kingdom o god an brocht hailin tae thaim that haed need o it noo at dailygan tha twal cum tae him an saed senn aa tha croods o fowk awa sae that the can gang an fin ludgins an a bite tae ait fer thairsels in tha clachans an fairm hooses roon aboot fer wer in a richt oot o tha wye place here but jesus toul thaim yous gie thaim sumthin tae ait an the saed we hae naethin but five bannocks an twa fish or mebbe we shud try an buy sumthin fer aa these fowk thair wur aboot five thoosan men an jesus saed tae his follaers mak thaim aa sit doon in groups o aboot fiftie sae the bid thaim aa sit doon then he tuk tha five bannocks an tha twa fish an lukkin up tae heiven he blisst it an brauk it an he kep giein it tae his follaers tae han oot tae aa tha fowk efter the haed aa et thair fill the gethert up aa tha wee bits eneuch tae fill twal creels yin day jesus wus prayin alane tha mair his follaers wus nearhan an he axt thaim wha dae tha croods say that a am the saed a wheen o fowk say jhone tha baptiser some wud say elijah an ithers agane say that yin o tha proaphits frae lang syne haes cum bak tae life an whut aboot yersels he axt wha dae yous say that a am peter spauk up you ir tha christ o god an he gien thaim a warnin an bid thaim no tae tell oniebodie an he toul thaim tha sinn o man maun suffer monies a thing an be gien tha coul shooder bi tha elders tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa an he maun be put tae deith an be ris up tae life on tha thurd day an he saed tae thaim aa if oniebodie wants tae follae efter me he maun ferget aboot hissel aathegither tak up his cross iverie day an stick clase tae me fer whaiver wants tae save his life wull loass it but him that loasses his life on accoont o me wull save it fer whut guid is it fer a bodie tae get tha hale warl an yit desthroy hissel bodie an sowl fer if oniebodie is no wullin tae stan up fer me an ma wurds then tha sinn o man wull no stan up fer him whan he cums in his glorie an tha glorie o his faither an tha halie angels tae am tellin ye strecht thairs yins stud here theday that fer sartin wull no dee afore the see tha kingdom o god yin day aboot echt days efter he haed saed these things he tuk peter jeames an jhone up intae a muntin tae pray an whaniver he wus prayin tha hale luk o him wus changed an his claes wus glancin white turnt an then thair wus these twa men taakin wi him it wus moses an elijah fu o heivenlie splendour an the taakt aboot tha wye he wud dee in jerusalem but peter an tha ithers wi him haed drapt aff tae sleep an whaniver the waakent up the saa his glorie an tha twa men stannin wi him an as tha twa men wus leain jesus peter saed dominie am gled we ir here tae see this cum on an well big thrie shilters yin fer you yin fer moses an yin fer elijah but he wus jist rannerin whan peter wus taakin a clood cum doon an the wur loast in it an the wur hairtscarred whan that happent an a voice cum oot o tha clood sayin this is ma sinn tha yin a hae chose listen tae him whan tha voice haed stapt taakin the lukt an thair wus nae yin thair but jesus an at tha time the didnae breathe a wurd o whut the haed saen tae onie yin nixt day whan the haed cum doon aff tha hill a hale crood o fowk cum tae meet him an this man caad oot frae tha crood maister a beg ye wud ye tak a luk at ma sinn hes tha ainlie chile a hae an a wickit spirit is aye takkin houl o him an whan it daes he lets oot a gulder an he stairts tae fit an foam at tha mooth an its onlie efter hes bin hurt baad that it leas him a brocht him tae yer follaers tae rid him o tha spirit but the cudnae dae it an jesus saed you fowk ir sae faithless an aisie led hoo lang wull a be wi ye afore yis believe hoo lang dae a hae tae pit up wi ye bring yer sinn here tae me jist as tha wee lad wus cumin he faad doon tae tha grun fittin an jesus gien tha wickit spirit a richt barjin an hailt tha wee lad an gien him bak tae his faither the wur aa pure dumfoonert at tha pooer o god but whiles the aa wunnert at tha things jesus did he saed tae his follaers wull yis tak heed tae whut am sayin an let it sink in tha sinn o man is gaun tae be pit intae tha pooer o men but the didnae unnerstan whut he wus sayin an the cudnae fethom it oot yit the wur feart tae ax him whut he meent then the begun queeryin amang thairsels wha wud be tha maist thocht o amang thaim an jesus knowin whut the wur thinkin tuk a wean an set him doon aside him an he saed tae thaim whaiver maks this chile walcum in ma name walcums me an oniebodie that walcums me walcums him that sent me tha yin regairdit o nae accoont amang ye thats tha yin thatll hae tha maist honour jhone saed tae him dominie we saa a bodie drivin oot demons in your name an we made him stap fer he isnae yin o us but jesus saed dae nae sitch thing fer oniebodie thats no agin ye is wi ye an as tha time wus cumin roon fer jesus tae lea tha irth he set hissel tae gang up tae jerusalem an he sent some messengers on up aheid o him an the went aff tae a samaritan village fer tae mak readie fer his cumin but tha fowk thonner wudnae mak him walcum acause the cud see he wus bent on gaun tae jerusalem whaniver jeames an jhone heerd this the saed loard let iz caa doon fire frae heiven an burn thaim aa up jist as elijah did but jesus toul thaim aff an saed ye hae nae unnerstannin ava fer tha sinn o man haesnae cum tae desthroy mens lifes but tae save thaim sae the went on tae anither village an sae it wus as the wur on thair wye this bodie saed tae jesus a wull follae ye nae metter whar yer fer saed jesus tae him foxes hae holes an burds hae nests but tha sinn o man haes naewhar he can caa hame an he saed tae anither yin follae me but he saed loard let me gang an burie ma faither furst but jesus saed bak tae him let tha deid burie thair ain deid but awa you gang an praich tha kingdom o god an yit anither yin saed loard all follae ye but let me gang an say aa ma guidbyes tae ma fowk bak hame but jesus toul him oniebodie that stairts tae ploo an keeps lukkin behin him is nae guid tae tha kingdom o god efter aa this tha loard caad oot seiventie mair follaers an sent thaim oot aheid o him twa bi twa tae aa tha toons an places whar he wus gaun tae visit hissel an he saed tae thaim thairs a gran hairst waitin but thairs no monie warkers tae gether it in sae keep on axin tha loard o tha hairst tae senn oot mair warkers intae his hairvest fiel noo awa yis gang but mine ye am sennin yis oot laik lambs amang wolfs dinnae cairrie a pooch ner a baag ner een spare shune an dinnae stap tae blether wi oniebodie on tha road whutiver hoose yis gang intae say furst god bliss this hoose wi peace if thairs peacelovin fowk thair yer blissin wull bide wi thaim an if thair isnae onie yer blissin wull cum bak tae ye stap in tha yin hoose an ait an drink whut the set afore ye fer a warker is warth his wages dinnae flit aboot frae hoose tae hoose an whaniver yis gang intae a toon if the bid yis walcum ait aa the set afore ye an hail tha seeck fowk thair an say tae thaim tha kingdom o god haes cum nearhan ye but if ye gang intae a toon an the dinnae bid ye walcum gang oot intae tha raas an tell thaim een tha stour o yer toon that clegs oor feet we dicht it aff as a warnin tae ye but well hae ye know that tha kingdom o god haes cum nearhan ye a tell ye tha fowk o sodom wull be better aff on tha day o reckonin ner that toon sorra tae chorazim an sorra tae bethsaida fer if tha fowk o tyre an sidon haed saen tha warkin o gods pooer as yous hae saen it the wud hae repentit lang syne an sut doon in seckclaith an eshes hooaniver tha fowk o tyre an sidon wull be better aff on tha day o reckonin than yous wull an capernaum you micht think yer weel on yer wye tae heiven na but am tellin ye yell be brocht doon tae hell then he saed tae his follaers whaiver listens tae yous is listenin tae me an whaiver turns his bak on you turns his bak on me an whaiver turns his bak on me turns his bak on tha yin that sent me whan tha seiventie cum bak the wur hairt gled an toul jesus loard even tha ill spirits haed tae dae whut we bid thaim in yer name an he saed tae thaim a saa satan faain frae heiven laik a flesh o lichtnin luk noo a hae gien yis tha thortie tae thramp on snakes an scorpions an tae owercum tha pooer o satan yer enemie thairs naethin wull be able tae dae yis onie hairm nanethaless haein pooer ower ill spirits is no tha thing tae be gled aboot but rether be gled that yer names is writ doon in heiven an thair an then jesus wus owercum wi tha joy o tha halie spirit an he caad oot faither loard o heiven an irth a praise ye that ye hae kep these things frae clivir an warliewise fowk an made thaim clear eneuch fer weans tae unnerstan ay faither it haes plaised ye tae dae it this wye ma faither haes gien aa things ower tae me an naebodie kens wha tha sinn raelie is apairt frae tha faither an naebodie fu kens tha faither apairt frae tha sinn an whaiver tha sinn wants tae reveal him tae an whan jesus wus on his ain wi his follaers he turnt tae thaim an saed blisst ir tha een that see whut ye see all tell ye this thairs monie proaphits an kings wud hae laikt tae see whut yous see an the didnae see it an tae hear whut yous hear but the didnae hear it yin day a thortie on tha laa stud up an axt jesus a question tae pit him tae tha test maister whut can a dae tae be shair all hae iverlastin life an jesus saed bak tae him whut daes tha laa o moses say whuts yer unnerstannin o it he answert an saed ye maun love tha loard yer god wi aa yer hairt an yer sowl an yer mine micht an main an yer nighber jist as much as yersel an jesus saed tae him ay thats tha richt answer dae this an yell leeve but he wantit tae keep hissel aheid o tha argyment an he saed tae jesus ay but wha is ma nighber an jesus saed yin time thair wus this man trevelin frae jerusalem tae jericho an he wus set upon bi robbers that stript him o his claes an gien him a richt hemmerin an left him half deid an bi chaunce a preesht cum alang an whan he saen him he slipt bye on tha ither side o tha road an efter this a levite cum bye he stapt an lukt at tha man an gaed bye on tha ither side as weel then a samaritan treveler cum tae whar he wus an whan he saen him his hairt went oot tae him an he went ower tae him an rowlt up his sairs poorin on oyle an wine tae aise thaim an sut him on his ain baist an brocht him tae an inn an lukt efter him tha nixt moarnin whan he wus leain he tuk oot twa siller coins an gien thaim tae tha innkeeper an saed tak guid care o him an if ye ir oot o poaket all mak it up tae ye whan a cum bak saed jesus noo whutch o these thrie wus nighber tae tha bodie that got tha hemmerin frae tha robbers an tha laayer saed tha yin that tuk peetie on him then jesus saed you gang awa an dae tha same as jesus an his follaers waakit on the cum tae a village an a wumman caad mairtha walcumed him intae hir hame she haed a sister mary that settelt hirsel doon at his feet an hung on iverie wurd he haed tae say but mairtha wus aa o a flooster ower aa that needit tae be daen an she saed loard can ye no see ma sister haes lef me tae dae aa tha wark tell hir tae cum an gie iz a han an jesus answert och mairtha ye ir gettin yersel aa warkt up aboot a hale lock o things ye see need daen but onlie yin thing raelie metters mary haes waaled whuts best an itll no be taen awa frae hir yinst whan jesus wus oot prayin yin o his follaers saed tae him efter he haed quit loard lairn iz hoo tae pray jist tha wye jhone did wi his follaers an he saed tae thaim whan ye pray say oor faither that bides abain halie be yer name micht yer kingdom cum shuin an yer wull be daen on irth jist tha wye it is abain gie iz theday eneuch breid tae dae iz an forgie iz oor wrangdaeins laik we forgie thaim that daes wrang agin us an dinnae road iz intae temptation but save iz frae aa ill then jesus saed tae thaim sayin ye went tae a freens hoose in tha middle o tha nicht an saed tae him cud a borra thrie loafs o breid acause a freen o mine haes cum tae visit an thairs nae mait in tha hoose an sayin tha freen caas oot dinnae bother me tha dures lockt an me an tha weans is in bed am no gettin up tae gie ye oniethin even he daesnae get up an gie him whut hes lukkin if ye keep on knockin lang eneuch hell rise an gie him aa he needs an a say keep on axin an it wull be gien tae ye keep on lukkin an yell fin whut yer efter keep on rappin an tha dure wull be apent tae ye fer iveriebodie that axes wull get him that keeps on lukkin wull fin whut hes efter an tae him that keeps on rappin tha dure wull be apent if a sinn axes breid frae onie o yis thats a faither wull he gie him a stane or if he axes a fish wull he gie him a snake or if he axes an egg wud he offer him a scorpion an sae if sinfu fowk laik yersels know hoo tae gie guid things tae yer weans hoo much mair wull yer heivenlie faither gie tha halie spirit tae thaim that axes him yinst jesus wus castin oot a dum spirit frae a man an whaniver tha demon left him an tha man that wus dum stairtit tae taak tha fowk wur dumfoonert but some o thaim saed he casts demons oot throu tha pooer o beelzebul tha heidyin o tha demons but ithers tried tae ketch him oot bi axin fer a sign frae heiven an jesus knowin whut wus in thair mines saed a kingdom divid agin itsel wull gae tae reck an ruin an a hoose divid agin itsel wull faa doon sae if satan is divid agin hissel his kingdom cudnae stan cud it hoo then can ye say that a cast oot demons throu tha pooer o beelzebul if yis say that a cast oot ill spirits bi tha pooer o beelzebul bi whut pooer then daes yer ain fowk cast thaim oot sae let thaim be tha yins tae judge ye fer whut ye hae saed but if a wi tha fingr o god cast oot ill spirits it proves that tha kingdom o god is here amang ye whaniver a strang man thats weelairmed gairds his castle his belangins is safe but whaniver a strangr man attecks an gets tha better o him he taks awa aa tha armour he lippens on an tha belangins is aa divid oot him thats no for me is agin me an him that isnae giein me a han tae gether in he micht as weel be scatterin whan an ill spirit cums oot o a man it raiks throu tha desert lukkin fer rest an whan it daesnae fin onie it says all jist gae bak tae whar a wus leevin afore sae tha spirit gaes bak tae tha hoose it left an fins it swep clain an aa redd up then it luks fer seiven ither spirits mair wickit ner itsel an the aa gae in an settle thair an that man enns up faur waur ner he wus afore an while jesus wus taakin a wumman in tha getherin caad oot blisst is tha wumman that gien ye birth an nurst ye as a wean an he saed bak tae hir but mair blisst ir tha yins that hear tha wurd o god an heed it mair an mair fowk wus jundyin roon him an he begun tae praich tae thaim sayin wer leevin in evil times wi evil fowk the keep lukkin fer a sign but nane wull be gien thaim apairt frae tha sign o jonah tha proaphit fer jist as jonah wus a sign tae tha ninevites in tha same wye a tha sinn o man wull be a sign tae this generation tha queen o tha sooth wull stan up on judgemen day wi tha men o this generation an she wull condemn thaim fer she cum frae tha enns o tha irth fer tae listen tae solomons wusdom yit yin abain solomon is here noo an their no listenin tha men o nineveh wull stan up in that day as weel wi this generation an thell condemn it fer they repentit whaniver jonah praicht tae thaim an yit yin abain jonah is here noo naebodie lichts a lamp an pits it unner a boul fer tae hide its licht but the pit it up on a stan whar aa can see its licht yer ee is tha lamp o yer bodie an if yer ee is guid yer hale bodie is fu o licht but whan yer ee is baad yer hale bodies fu o dairkness noo tha licht ye think ye hae tak heed that its no dairkness an sae if ye be aa fu o licht wi nae wee dairk coarners yer hale bodie wull be glowin laik whan a bricht licht shines on ye an while he wus taakin a pharisee axt him tae his hoose fer a bite tae ait an he went in an sut doon tha pharisee got a gunk whan he saa that jesus didnae waash afore denner but tha loard saed tae him yous pharisees waash tha ootside o tha bickers an plates but inside yer fu o greed an wickitness ye coofs hae ye no tha sense tae know that god made tha inside as weel as tha ootside gie tae tha puir oot o whut ye hae on yer ain plate an then yell be clain throu an throu listen here wae faa ye pharisees ye gie a tenth o yer gairden spices sitch as mint an rue but ye hae neglectit justice an ye dinnae love god but ye shudnae ferget tae be fair an kine tae ithers an tae love god as weel as giein yer tenth wae faa ye pharisees fer ye aye laik tae hae tha best saits in tha meetin hooses aye wantin fowk tae touch thair keps tae ye in tha mairket places ay wae faa ye pharisees maisters o tha laa an hippycrates fer yis ir laik graves wi nae mairkins that men waak ower wioot knowin then yin o tha laayers saed tae jesus maister ir ye gettin at us as weel he saed yer in fer bother tae yous laayers fer yis gie men burdens ower wechtie tae cairt an ye dinnae lift a fingr yersels tae gie a han wae faa ye fer yis big fancie monuments on tha graves o tha verie proaphits that yer faithers killt lang syne yer faithers killt thaim but yous bigged tha monuments sae ye maun gae alang wi whut the daen god then in his wusdom saed a wull senn thaim proaphits an possels the wull kill a wheen o thaim an gie tha rest a haird time sae tha bluid o aa tha proaphits spillt frae tha beginnin o tha warl yous fowk leevin noo hae it on yer heids frae tha killin o abel tae tha killin o zechariah atween tha althar an tha hoose o god ay am tellin yis yousll pye fer this ay yer in fer bother tae yous laayers fer yis hae taen awa tha key tae unnerstannin yis hinnae uised it yersels an yis hae kep ither fowk frae uisin it as weel whaniver jesus quit taakin tha pharisees an tha maisters o tha laa wus wile angrie an heckelt him tryin tae get him tae cum oot wi sumthin that the cud fin faut wi fer tae get him arrestit mainwhile thoosans o fowk gethert up sae thrang that the wur thrampin yin anither jesus spauk furst o aa tae his follaers an toul thaim be on yer gaird agin tha yeast o tha pharisees fer the let on tae be guid an ther faur frae it thairs naethin covert ower thatll no cum tae licht ner hid thatll no be kent sae whutivers taakt aboot in tha dairk wull be heerd in tha braid daylicht an whut ye hae whuspert aboot behin shut dures wull be blared oot frae tha ruiftaps listen freens dinnae be feart o thaim that kill tha bodie fer efter that thairs naethin mair the can dae but all warn ye noo wha ye shud fear fear him that haes tha pooer tae kill an then tae throw intae hell ay a tell ye fear him shair five wee sparras ir soul fer a wheen o happence ir the no an god daesnae ferget onie o thaim but even tha verie hairs o yer heid ir aa coontit sae dinnae be feart yis ir warth mair ner a hale wheen o sparras an am tellin ye whaivers no feart tae tell fowk the belang tae me tha sinn o man wull own him tae afore tha angels o god but oniebodie that daesnae admit tae bein a follaer o mine wull be denied bi me afore tha angels o god an whaiver spakes a wurd agin tha sinn o man wull be forgien but whaiver spakes ill agin tha halie spirit wull no be forgien whan yis ir brocht afore tha meetin hoose offyshals an heidyins dinnae be ower enxious aboot yer answer or whut tae say fer tha halie spirit wull pit tha wurds in yer mooth whan tha time cums an yin o tha crood saed tae him maister wud ye hae a wurd wi ma brither an ax him tae share wi me whut wus lef tae iz an he saed tae him freen wha gien me tha richt tae settle a differnce atween you an yer brither an jesus saed tae thaim tak heed that yis ir no aye wantin things that ither fowk hae fer a mans life is no jist a metter o whut he gethers aboot him an he toul thaim this parable yin time a weel tae dae fairmer haed a guid hairst an he swuthered aboot whut he wus gaun tae dae fer he haed nae ruim tae store it aa sae he saed tae hissel a ken whut all dae all tummle ma barns an big yins thatll houl aa ma grain an guids an all say tae masel a hae plentie lef bye me tae dae me fer monie a yeir sae all jist ait drink an hae a guid time tae masel but god saed ye ir a fool fer yell be caad awa this verie nicht an whall get aa tha stuff ye hae lef behin in tha same wye tha mans a fool that gethers up stuff fer hissel an haesnae stored up tha richt soart o treysure wi god an jesus turnt tae his follaers an saed am tellin ye yis ir tae tak nae thocht fer yer life or yer bodie whut tae ait or whut tae pit on ye thairs mair tae life ner mait an claes luk at tha craws the nether sow ner reap an hae nae barns tae store oniethin in yit the get eneuch tae dae thaim fer god feeds thaim ir yous no warth mair tae him than a wheen o burds ye cannae add an oor tae yer life bi worryin aboot it sae if ye cannae dae a wee thing laik that why worrie yersel aboot oniethin else noo tak tha lilies ye see hoo the growe the dinnae wark an the dinnae spin yit all tell ye this een solomon wi aa his fancie claes cudnae match thaim an if god pits claes on tha gress in tha fiel thats here theday an throwed intae tha fire themorra dae you dooters no unnerstan that hell luk efter you anaa sae dinnae worrie aboot mait or drink dinnae bother yer heids aboot it its thaim at daesnae know god that rin efter sitch things but yer faither abain kens whut ye hae need o but yous ir tae seek oot his kingdom an tha ither things wull tak care o thairsels dinnae be scarred wee flock fer yer faither wants tae gie ye tha kingdom sell aff whut ye hae an gie tha siller tae tha puir an this wull coont as treysure stored up in strang safe moneybaags in heiven whar itll nether be stole bi thiefs ner et wi moths fer whut yis think tha maist o wull aye be in yer hairt be aa dresst up an readie wi tha hoose lit up ect laik men waitin on thair maister tae cum bak frae tha waddin sae that whan he knocks yis can apen tha dure tae him richt awa whaniver tha maister cums blisst ir tha yins he fins watchin an waitin a tell yis this hell get hissel readie sit thaim doon an he hissel wull sarve thaim an lea tha mait oot afore thaim tha maister wull mebbe cum bak in tha wee smaa oors or at tha scraich o day but if he fins thaim readie an waitin whaniver he cums the wull be blisst aa richt ye can be shair o this if ye haed a hoose an ye knowed tha day an oor a thief wus cumin yed be lukkin oot fer him wud ye no ye wudnae alloo yer hoose tae be brauk intae sae yous maun be readie fer ye dinnae ken tha oor tha sinn o man wull cum then peter saed loard did ye main these things fer iveriebodie or jist fer us an tha loard saed am taakin tae onie wise an faithfu sarvint whase maister is able tae lea him in chairge o tha ither sarvints in his hoose tae gie iveriebodie thair fair share o mait at tha richt time onie sarvint ectin laik this whaniver his maister cums bak wull be a happie man all tell ye this hell pit that sarvint in chairge o iveriethin he haes but if tha sarvint says tae hissel hes a lang time o cumin tha maister an he aits an gets drunk an he stairts tae bate up aa tha ither sarvints weel noo tha maister wull cum bak on a day an oor whan hes no lukkin oot fer him an tha maister wull dae awa wi that sarvint he wull trait him jist laik an unbeliever an that sarvint that knowed richtlie whut tae dae an didnae dae whut he wus toul bi tha maister an mak readie hell get yin guid whalin but tha yin that did wrang whaniver he didnae unnerstan whut he shud a daen hell get aff aisie tha mair he daesnae desarve it god wull ax a lock frae thaim thats bin gien a lock tha mair the hae bin gien tae luk efter tha mair the wull hae tae answer fer am cum tae kinnel a fire on irth an a wush it wus aareadie lit a hae a tarrible baptisin aheid o me an awfu testin tae its aa ower dae ye think a cum tae bring peace on irth deed na its deveesion a bring frae noo a hoose wi five fowk wull be divid wi thrie agin twa an twa agin thrie tha faither wull be divid agin tha sinn an tha sinn agin tha faither tha mither agin tha dochter an tha dochter agin tha mither tha mitherinlaa agin tha dochterinlaa an tha dochterinlaa agin tha mitherinlaa an jesus saed tae tha crood o fowk whaniver ye see cloods cumin in frae tha wast ye ken wer fer haein rain an richt eneuch doon it cums an whan tha wun blaas frae tha sooth ye ken wer in fer a scorcher an sae it is yous hippycrates yis can read tha luk o tha sky aa richt but yis cannae see tha signs aa roon aboot ye o whuts tae cum why dae yis no see fer yersels whuts richt if oniebodie pits tha blame on ye an taks ye tae coort ye shud dae yer best tae settle tha metter oot o coort if ye dinnae then yell be up afore tha judge an hell turn ye ower tae tha offysher an yell enn up in jail fer if thats tha wye it enns up yell no git oot o thair afore yer last pennies pyed at that parteeclar time jesus wus toul that pilate haed killt some fowk frae galilee while the wur offerin secryfices in tha hoose o tha loard he saed tae thaim dae ye jalouse tha yins that suffert laik this haed daen mair wrang ner aa tha ither galileeans na a tell ye this if yis dinnae repent tha hale lock o yisll perish as weel or whut aboot tha echteen that deed in siloam whaniver tha tooer cum doon on tap o thaim dae ye jalouse that thair wrangdaeins wus waur ner aa tha ither yins in jerusalem na a tell ye this if yis dinnae repent tha hale lock o ye wull perish forbye then jesus toul thaim a parable thair wus this man haed a fig tree plantit in his vineyaird yin day he cum tae it tae see if thair wus onie fruit on it but he fun nane sae he saed tae tha gairdner luk here this thrie yeir a hae cum lukkin fer figs on this tree an thairs nane on it cut it doon its a waste o guid grun tha gairdner saed lea it alane sir gie it anither yeir all dig roon it an gie it a guid dressin o dung if thairs onie figs on it nixt yeir weel an guid an if no well cut it doon fer ye noo yin sabbath day whan jesus wus taichin in yin o tha meetin hooses thair wus a wumman that haed bin baad fer echteen yeir acause o an ill spirit she wus bent dooble an cudnae stan up strecht ava whan jesus saa hir he caad hir an saed tae hir wumman yer redd o yer seeckness an yer noo free an he put his hans on hir an she stud up hir fu heicht an gien praise tae god but tha heidyin o tha meetin hoose wus angrie acause jesus haed hailt tha wumman on tha sabbath day an he saed tae tha fowk ye hae six days tae dae aa yer wark cum tae be hailt on yin o thaim days an no on tha sabbath an this is hoo tha loard answert him yis oul hippycrates shair dae yis no lowse yer kye an yer cuddies frae tha staal on tha sabbath an tak thaim oot tae watter thaim wus it no richt that on tha sabbath a shud set free this wumman o tha femlie o abraham that haes bin hel in bondage bi satan this echteen yeir this put his enemies tae shame tha hale lock o thaim an aa tha fowk wus hairt gled at aa tha wunnerfu things he daen then jesus saed fer whut laik is tha kingdom o god wha shud a compare it wi it is laik a wee mustert seed that a bodie tuk an plantit in his gairden an it growed intae a tree a tree big eneuch fer wee burds tae tak shilter in its brenches an he saed agane fer whut laik is tha kingdom o god whut shud a compare it wi its laik a wee taste o yeast that a wumman pits in a big boul o flure an it spreeds aa throu it tae tha hale lock o it is ris an he gaed throu tha toons an villages taichin as he went aye heidin on nixt jerusalem an summodie axt him wull thair jist be a wheen o fowk saved loard an he saed tae thaim aa dae aa ye can tae get in bi tha nerra dure fer monies a yin wull try an get in an no be fit tae fer yinst tha heid o tha hoose haes got up an lockt tha dure yell be stannin ootbye rappin an caain oot sir wull ye no apen tha dure tae iz an hell cum bak wi am tellin ye a know naethin aboot ye or whar yis cum frae then yell say but we et an drunk alang wi ye an ye hae taicht iz doon oor loanins but hell cum bak wi a tell ye a dinnae know a thing aboot ye or whar ye cum frae ye rapscallions ye git oot o ma sicht tha hale lock o yis thairll be greetin an scringein o teeth whaniver ye see abraham an isaac an jacob an aa tha proaphits in tha kingdom o god an yous aa shut oot an fowk wull cum frae aa airts an tak thair place roon tha boord in tha kingdom o god but tak heed thairs yins thats last thatll be furst an thairs ither yins thats furst thatll be last jist then some pharisees cum up an saed tae him get oot o here if ye want tae leeve fer herod haes it in mine tae kill ye gang tell thon sleekit oul fox saed jesus tae thaim that all be keepin on castin oot ill spirits an hailin tha seeck theday an themorra an tha day efter that all hae daen whut a wus sent tae dae nanethaless theday themorra an tha nixt day a maun gang on ma road fer it wudnae dae fer a proaphit o god tae dee ootside o jerusalem o jerusalem jerusalem ye kill tha proaphits an stane thaim thats sent tae ye monies tha time a wantit tae gether yer weans thegither laik a hen gethers hir lachter o wee burds unner hir wings but yis wudnae let me luk yer hoose is empie noo but a tell ye this yisll no see me agane til ye say blisst is tha yin that cums in tha name o tha loard yin sabbath day jesus went fer a bite tae ait at tha hoose o yin o tha heidyins o tha pharisees an the wur aa keepin thair ee on him an fornent him wus this man wi his bodie aa swallt up sae jesus axt tha laayers an pharisees daes tha laa alloo ye tae hail fowk on tha sabbath day or no the haed nae answer tae that sae he layed his han on tha man an he hailt him an sent him awa an he turnt tae thaim an saed jist say yin o yis haed a cuddie or a coo that faad doon intil a wal wud ye no gae an pu it oot strecht aff sabbath day or no the cudnae gie him onie answer tae that ava whan jesus saa tha fowk thair aa makkin fer tha best saits in tha hoose he toul thaim this parable whaniver ye get an invite tae a waddin dinnae be settin yersel doon at tha tap table fer anither bodie mair impoartin ner yersel micht be cumin tae it sae then tha yin that axt baith o yis tae tha waddin wud hae tae say tae ye wull ye gie this man yer sait ye wudnae know whar tae pit yersel wud ye an yell hae tae shift tae tha bak o tha ruim but whan ye get an invite gang an sit doon at tha bak an whan tha yin that invitit ye sees ye he wull say freen whut ir ye daein awa bak thair cum on up here tae tha front then aa tha ither fowk thair wull see that ye ir summodie whaiver sets hissel up as summodie tha loardll bring him doon whaiver taks tha hummle place wull be gien tha place o honour then jesus turnt tae tha yin that haed gien him tha invite an saed whan ye gie a denner or a pairtie dinnae be caain yer freens or yer brithers yer femlie or yer weelaff nighbers acause the wull onlie pye ye bak bi invitin ye in return but whan ye gie a big swaree caa aa tha puir tha lameters tha halt an tha blin fowk the cannae pye ye bak but god wull bliss ye an gie ye yer reward whan he rises tha upricht fowk frae tha deid whan yin o thaim that wus sittin at table wi jesus heerd this he saed tae him blisst is tha yin that wull sit doon tae ait in tha kingdom o god then jesus saed tae him yinst thair wus this man giein a big pairtie an he axt a hale lock o fowk tae it an whan tha time fer tha big pairtie cum roon he sent his sarvin man oot wi a message fer tha yins that wus axt ye ir tae cum noo fer iveriethins readie but the stairtit yin an aa tae mak excuses tha furst yin saed a hae jist bocht a bit o lan an a hae tae gang an luk at it a beg ye tae let me aff anither yin saed a hae bocht five yauk o kye an a hae tae gang an try thaim oot a beg ye tae let me aff an anither saed luk a hae jist got merriet a cannae cum sae saed jesus tha sarvin man cum an gien an accoont o it tae his maister then tha maister o tha hoose wus wile angrie an he toul his sarvin man gang oot quick intae tha raas an tha entries an bring in tha puir tha lameters tha blin an tha halt fowk later on tha sarvin man cum bak an saed maister a hae daen as ye bid me yit thairs still ruim fer mair an tha maister toul his sarvin man gang oot intae tha roads an loanins dinnae tak na fer an answer mak thaim cum fer a want ma hoose fillt an all tell yis this qo he nane o thaim that wur invitit at tha furst wull iver sup wi me big croods wus follaein jesus an he turnt tae thaim an saed if onie man cums tae me an pits his faither or his mither his wife or his weans his brithers or sisters ay or even his ain sel afore me he cannae be ma follaer whaiver daesnae tak up his ain cross an cum efter me cannae be a follaer o mine jist say yin o yis haes a mine tae big a tooer wud he no sit doon furst an coont tha coast tae see if he haes eneuch tae feenish it efter he haes put in tha fittins if he fins hes no able tae feenish it aa tha fowk roon aboot wull mak fun o him wull the no the wull say this man stairtit tae big an wusnae able tae feenish tha jab or agane if a king wus gaun tae war wi anither king wud he no sit doon furst an jalouse if he wud be able wi ten thoosan sodgers tae bate him thats cumin agin him wi twuntie thoosan if he fins hes no able then while his enemie is a lang road aff hell senn a gobetween tae him an ax fer terms o peace jist in tha same wye whaiver o yis wull no gie up aa ye hae cannae be ma follaer saut is guid but if it loasses its taste hoo dae ye mak it saltie agane it is nether fit fer tha lan ner tha midden fowk jist clod it oot let him that haes ears in his heid tak tent noo tha tex men an tha wrangdaers gethert roon tae gie him thair ear an tha pharisees an tha maisters o tha laa kep grummlin an the saed this man is weel in wi wrangdaers an een gaes in fer a bite tae ait wi thaim sae jesus toul thaim this parable an he saed say a man amang yis haed a hunner sheep if he loast yin o thaim wud he no lea tha ninetienine oot on tha muirs an gang efter tha yin that wus loast til he fins it an whan he haes fun it hes gye gled an he pits it on his shooder an he heids awa hame wi it an whan he gets hame he caas thegither his freens an nighbers an he says tae thaim cum on an see ir yis no hairt gled wi me a hae fun ma loast sheep a tell yis jist in tha same wye thair wull be mair joy in heiven ower yin wrangdaer that repents o his wrangdaein mair ner ower ninetienine that thinks the dinnae need tae repent or agane if a wumman haed ten siller coins an she loast yin o thaim wud she no tak a bricht licht redd up tha hoose an luk in iverie neuk an crannie tae she fins it an whaniver shes fun it she caas thegither hir freens an nighbers an she says cum on an see ir yis no hairt gled wi me a hae fun ma loast coin a tell yis jist in tha same wye thairs joy amang tha angels o god ower yin wrangdaer that turns frae his wrangdaein jesus went on tae say thair wus this man wi twa sinns tha youngr yin saed tae his faither can a hae noo whut ye wur fer leain me in yer wull sae tha faither divid whut he haed atween tha twa o thaim a wheen o days later tha youngr yin gethert up aa his belangins an he went aff tae a fauraff kintrie he spent aa roon him in wile leevin aboot tha time his money run oot thair wus a wile baad famine ower tha hale lan an he wus starvin wi hungr sae he hired hissel oot tae a local fairmer that sent him oot tae his fiels tae feed pigs tha young fella wus that hungrie got he wus near aitin tha husks he wus feedin tae tha pigs an naebodie gien him ocht ava whan he cum tae his senses he thocht tae hissel ma faithers sarvints bak hame haes eneuch tae ait an tae spare an here a am deein wi hungr all git up an all gae hame tae ma faither an all say a hae sinned agin heiven an agin yersel an am nae langr fit tae be caad yer sinn wud ye no tak me on as yin o yer hired hans sae he ris up an he went bak hame tae his faither but whan he wus yit a lang roads aff his faither saa him cumin an his hairt went oot tae him an he run an throwed his airms roon him an he kisst him tha sinn saed tae him a hae sinned agin heiven an agin yersel an am nae mair fit tae be caad yer sinn but tha faither saed tae his sarvints rin bring oot tha guid robe an pit it on him pit a ring on his fingr an shune on his feet an bring forrit tha kwye we wur fattenin up an kill it fer wer gaun tae hae a big pairtie fer this sinn o mine wus deid an noo hes bak tae life agane he wus loast but noo hes fun sae tha pairtie begun noo while aa this wus gaun on tha ouler sinn wus oot warkin in tha fiels an whan he cum near tha hoose he heerd aa tha music an dauncin sae he caad yin o tha sarvints an he axt him whut wus gaun on tha sarvint toul him yer brither haes cum hame an yer faither haes killt tha wee kwye we wur fattenin fer hes gled tae hae his sinn hame safe an siccar tha ouler brither wus rippin an he wudnae gae intae tha hoose sae his faither cum oot an tried tae taak him roon but he saed tae his faither luk a hae wrocht haird fer ye aa these yeirs an no yinst hae a no daen yer biddin aa this time ye niver even gien me a wee goat tae hae a swaree wi ma freens yit whan this waster o a sinn o yers cums hame efter skailin yer money aa roon him on baad weemen an tha laik ye gae an kill tha best kwye aboot tha place fer him an tha faither saed ma sinn ye ir aye wi me an aa that a hae is yours its onlie but richt we shud be joyfu an gled fer this brither o yers wus deid an noo hes bak tae life he wus loast but noo hes fun an jesus went on tae say tae his follaers yinst thair wus a weelaff man that haed a bodie lukkin efter his affairs an summodie toul him that this owerseer wus squannerin iveriethin sae tha weelaff man confrontit him aboot this an he saed whuts this a hear aboot ye gie an accoont o whut ye hae daen fer all no hae ye aboot tha place onie mair then tha owerseer saed tae hissel whutll a dae whan a hae nae studie wark am no fit tae dig an a wud be affrontit tae beg a know whut all dae sae that fowk dinnae gie me tha coul shooder whaniver a loass ma jab yin bi yin he caad in tha fowk that wur in debt tae his boss an he axt tha furst yin hoo much dae ye owe tha maister a hunner barrels o oyle saed he sae tha owerseer toul him tak yer bill sit doon thair quick an pit doon fiftie an tae anither he saed an whut dae ye owe a hunner baags o wheat saed he sae tha owerseer saed tae him luk here tak yer bill an pit doon echtie baags tha maister o tha crookit owerseer haed tae gie credit tae him fer tha wye he haed o gettin in wi fowk fer tha fowk o this warl ir whiles mair langheidit in thair dailins than tha yins that hae saen tha licht an am tellin ye yis shud uise yer warlie siller tae mak freens in tha warl an sae whan moneys nae mair use tae ye yis wull be gien a walcum intae yer iverlastin hame if yis ir faithfu in wee things then yis wull be faithfu in bigger yins in tha same wye him thats no strecht in wee things wull no be strecht in big things if yis cannae be trustit wi warlie walth wha wull trust yis wi tha true riches o heiven if ye cannae be trustit wi ither fowks money wha wull gie ye money o yer ain tae luk efter a slave cannae sarve twa maisters fer ether hell hait tha yin an love tha ither or hell stick bye tha yin an think naethin o tha ither ye cannae sarve baith god an gowld an tha pharisees that laikt thair money heerd aa this an the stairtit tae geg him but he saed tae thaim yous ir tha yins that try tae prove yersels richt in tha sicht o fowk but god knows whuts in yer hairts fer tha things thats tarrible weel thocht o bi men wud be a scunner tae god afore jhone fowk leeved bi tha laa o moses an tha proaphits but noo tha kingdom o god is praicht an iveriebodies pushin thair wye in but that daesnae main that tha laa daesnae stan fer it daes in iverie wee point its as strang an studie as heiven an irth thegither whaiver pits awa his wife an gets merriet agane is committin adulterie an whaiver merries hir thats divorced commits adulterie as weel an jesus went on tae say yin time thair wus this weelaff man that dresst up in fancie claes an leeved iverie day in tha lap o luxurie an then thair wus this puir beggar covert wi sairs caad lazarus that lay at his gate lazarus wus hopin that tha rich man wud gie him tha leains frae his table whiles tha doags wud cum an lick his sairs in tha enn tha beggar deed an tha angels cairriet him awa tae be wi abraham tha rich man deed forbye an wus buriet an whan he wus sufferin sair in hell he cud see abraham an lazarus thegither a lang wyes aff an he cryed oot tae thaim an saed faither abraham tak peetie on me an senn lazarus tae dook tha enn o his fingr in tha watter tae cool ma tung doon fer am tormentit wi tha bleeze o this fire but abraham saed ma sinn dae ye mine tha time whan ye wur leevin on irth you haed iveriethin an lazarus haed naethin an noo hes at peace an ye ir tormentit an apairt frae aa that thairs a big deep sheuch atween iz baith sae that we can hae nae dailins wi yin anither then tha rich man saed faither abraham wud ye no senn lazarus tae ma faithers hoose tae warn ma five brithers sae that the dinnae enn up here in torment laik masel but abraham saed bak tae him the hae bin aareadie warnt bi moses an tha proaphits let thaim tak heed tae that warnin an tha rich man saed na faither abraham but if summodie frae tha deid appeart tae thaim the wud turn awa frae thair sins an bak tae god but abraham saed if the dinnae heed whut moses an tha proaphits toul thaim then itll no mak onie differnce if summodie cum bak tae thaim frae tha deid yin day jesus saed tae his follaers thairll aye be temptation tae dae wrang but dear halp tha yin that daes tha tempin it wud be faur better fer him if a millstane wus hung roon his neck an he wus drapt intae tha sea rether ner him leadin yin o these puir wee craiters asthray listen here if summodie daes ocht agin ye tell him he shudnae hae daen it an if he says hes sorrie then forgie him an if he keeps on daein ye wrang seiven times a day an is sorrie iverie time then ye maun still forgie him an tha possels saed tae tha loard show iz hoo we can hae mair faith an tha loard saed if yis haed faith as smaa as a mustert seed even yis cud say tae this mulberry tree cum oot bi tha ruit an plant yersel in tha sea an richt awa itd dae whut its toul whaniver yer sarvin man cums in frae tha plooin an mindin tha beese ye wudnae say tae him sit yersel doon quick an hae a bite tae ait rether ye wud tell him tae clain hissel up an sarve you furst an then tak his ain efter a doot ye wudnae say thenks tae yer ain man fer daein whut hes pyed tae dae in tha same wye whan ye dae ma biddin ye shud say wer naethin oot o tha ordinarie fer we hae daen nae mair ner we haed tae an sae jesus went on tae jerusalem follaein tha mairch atween samaria an galilee as he went intae yin o tha villages he saa ten men that wur lepers stannin a wyes aff an the caad oot tae him jesus maister tak peetie on iz an whaniver he saa thaim he saed awa tae tha preeshts an let thaim luk at ye an lo an behoul as the went thair wye the wur hailt an yin o thaim whan he saen he wus cured turnt bak an cryed oot at tha tap o his voice praise god then he faad doon at jesus feet an gien thenks an tha man wus a samaritan sae he wus did a no cure ten men axt jesus whars tha ither nine hae nane o thaim cum bak tae gie thenks tae god apairt frae this foreigner jesus saed tae tha man rise up an gang yer wye yer faith haes made ye weel yin time whaniver tha pharisees axt jesus whan gods kingdom wud cum he toul thaim yis cannae say here it is or thair it is tha kingdom o god is aareadie here amang yis sae thairs nae use lukkin fer it cumin an he saed tae his follaers tha day wull cum whan yisll want tae see tha sinn o man yisll luk fer me an all no be here fowk micht say hes here or hes thair but tak nae notysh an dinnae rin efter thaim fer jist as tha lichtnin fleshes ower tha lift thats whut laik itll be tha day tha sinn o man cums bak but afore that hell hae tae suffer sair an tha fowk roon him noo wull turn agin him whaniver tha sinn o man cums bak itll be jist laik it wus in noahs day fer fowk wus aitin an drinkin an gettin merriet richt up tae tha verie day noah went intae tha airk then tha watter floodit an aa wur droont it wull be tha same as it wus in tha time o lot the et an the drunk an the cairriet on wi thair bizness o buyin sellin fairmin an biggin but tha verie day that lot went oot o sodom fire an brimstane cum doon frae heiven an the wur aa killt tha same wull happen tha day yis see tha sinn o man cum bak on that day naebodie shud lea his ruiftap an be gaun bak doon fer ocht in his hoose an naebodie shud lea his fiel ether tae gae bak hame mine whut happent tae lots guidwife whaiver houls on tae his life wull loass it an whaiver gies up his life wull aye hae it am tellin yis in that nicht twa fowk wull be in tha yin bed yin wull be tuk an tha ither lef behin twa weemen wull be grindin mail thegither yin wull be tuk an tha ither lef behin twa men wull be in tha fiel tha yin wull be tuk an tha ither lef behin an his follaers axt him whar wull this tak place an jesus toul thaim whar ye see a crood o vulters ye know thairs a deid bodie aboot ay sae whaniver ye see tha signs am taakin aboot then yell know weel eneuch jesus toul his follaers this parable that meent that the shud aye pray an no gie up an it went laik this thair wus this judge in a big toon that haed nae fear o ether god ner man an haed nae thocht fer oniebodie in that same toon thair wus this weeda wumman that kep on cumin tae tha judge sayin wud ye mak shair a get a fair dail in tha coort frae tha yin thats agin me at tha stairt tha judge niver bothert fer a lang time he did naethin but then he saed tae hissel tha mair a dinnae fear god or care aboot fowk still wi aa a wull halp oot this weeda wumman fer shes giein me that much bother am scunnert wi hir aye rinnin tae me tha loard went on yis unnerstan whut tha baad judge is sayin dae yis no think god wull tak tha pairt o his ain fowk that cry oot tae him day an nicht hell no keep pittin thaim aff sae hell no am tellin yis hell no be lang in seein justice daen but whaniver tha sinn o man cums bak a wunner wull he fin oniebodie wi faith on tha irth an he toul anither parable tae tha yins that wus fu o thairsels an thocht the wur aa richt an lukt doon on ithers thair wus twa men went up tae tha hoose o god fer tae pray yin wus a pharisee an tha ither wus a tex man tha pharisee ris tae his feet an prayed tae hissel o god a thenk ye that am no laik ither fowk ner fer that metter laik thon tex boy ower thonner a dinnae chait fowk a dae naethin wrang an a keep tae me ain wife a fast twice in tha week an a gie a tenth o aa a hae but tha tex man stud awa bak an wudnae as much as lift his een tae heiven but he bate his breesht in sorra an saed o god hae mercie on me fer am naethin but a sinner a tell ye this tex man an no tha pharisee went doon tae his hoose in guid stannin wi god fer tha yin that thinks a lock o hissel wull be brocht doon but tha yin thats hummle wull be liftit up an as weel the brocht wee weans tae jesus sae that he cud pit his hans on thaim tae bliss thaim but whaniver tha follaers saen this the chackt tha fowk but jesus toul thaim tae cum on aheid an saed alloo tha weans tae cum tae me dinnae stap thaim fer tha kingdom o god belangs tae tha laik o these am tellin ye whaiver daesnae tak tha kingdom o god intae his hairt laik a wean daes wull no get in ava yinst an impoartin bodie axt him guid maister whut maun a dae tae be shair a get tae heiven an leeve fer iver an jesus saed bak tae him why ir ye caain me guid thairs naebodie guid apairt frae god ye weel ken tha commauns dinnae commit adulterie dinnae murder dinnae tak whuts no yer ain dinnae tell lees aboot ither fowk an gie respeck tae yer faither an yer mither an tha bodie saed bak tae him a hae daen aa these things since a wus onie age whan jesus heerd this he saed tae tha man thairs jist yin thing ye still hae tae dae sell aa ye hae an gie tae thaim that haesnae much an yell hae walth in heiven an then cum bak an follae me noo whaniver tha man heerd this he wus doon in tha mooth fer he haed a wile lock o money an whaniver jesus saa tha wye tha man tuk it he saed hoo verie haird it is fer thaim that haes money tae git intae tha kingdom o god fer it wud be aisier fer a kemel tae gae throu tha ee o a needle ner fer a monied man tae git intae tha kingdom o god an tha yins that heerd it axt wha in aa tha warl can be saved then an jesus saed thaim things men cannae dae gods mair ner fit tae dae wi that peter saed mine we hae left iveriethin behin an follaed ye an jesus saed tae thaim am tellin yis oniebodie that haes left his hoose his faither an mither brithers wife or weans fer tha sake o tha kingdom o god wull dae weel an hae plentie in this warl an in tha warl tae cum he wull hae iverlastin life then he tuk tha twal tae tha side an he saed tae thaim see here wer gaun up tae jerusalem an aa thats bin writ doon bi tha proaphits aboot tha sinn o man wull tak place thair fer hell be hannit ower tae tha gentiles fer thaim tae mak fun o him trait him ill an spit on him an the wull gie him a whuppin an kill him but on tha thurd day he wull rise tae life agane but the didnae unnerstan onie o tha things he saed fer tha mainin wus hid frae thaim an the jist cudnae tak it in noo whan jesus wus cumin up tae jericho on tha ootskirts a blin man wus sittin beggin on tha bunker o tha road whan he heerd tha thrang gaun bye he axt whut it wus aa aboot an the toul him jesus o nazareth is cumin tha blin man cryed oot jesus sinn o davit tak peetie on me an tha yins that went afore jesus scoult tha beggar an the toul him tae be quait but he guldert aa tha mair sinn o davit tak peetie on me an jesus stapt an saed bring tha blin man tae me an whan the did jesus axt him whut dae ye want me tae dae fer ye an he saed loard a want tae be able tae see agane an jesus saed bak tae him hae yer sicht yer faith haes made ye hale richt awa he cud see agane an he follaed jesus giein glorie tae god an whaniver aa tha ither fowk saa this the gien praise tae god as weel an jesus cum tae tha toon o jericho an wus trevelin throu it noo thair wus this man caad zacchaeus that wus a heid tex man an he wus quare an weelaff an he wus wantin tae see fer hissel whut jesus wus laik but he wus a wee man an he cudnae get near jesus fer tha crood sae he run awa on aheid an shinned up a sycomore fig tree alang tha wye tae hae a guid luk at jesus whan he wus gaun bye an whan jesus cum tae tha tree he lukt up an saed til him zacchaeus git doon or that richt noo fer am gaun tae yer hoose tha day sae zacchaeus lep doon oot o tha tree an tuk him hame an gien him a wile guid walcum aa tha fowk saen this an stairtit tae pass remairks sayin hes stappin ower wi a wrangdaer oniehoo zacchaeus stud up an toul jesus a tell ye whut loard all gie tha half o whut a hae tae thaim at haes need o it an if a hae got oniethin bi chaitin all pye it bak fower times ower an jesus saed salvation haes cum tae this hoose tha day fer this man is a sinn o abraham as weel a masel tha sinn o man hae cum tae luk fer thaim ats loast an tae save thaim an tha hale crood tuk tent o whut jesus wus sayin an as jerusalem wus nearhan he stairtit tae tell thaim a parable fer fowk thocht that tha kingdom o god wus gaun tae cum aboot at yinst he toul thaim this a weel boarn man went awa tae a fauraff lan he wus tae hae hissel crooned king an then he wus tae cum bak agane afore he went but he caad ten o his sarvin men an gien each o thaim yin gowld coin an he saed tae thaim tak this catter an mak tha maist o it tae a cum bak but he wusnae weel thocht o amang his ain fowk an sae the sent oot wurd efter he went awa sayin we dinnae want this man tae rule ower iz but he got tae be king aa tha same an he cum bak hame then he oardert tha sarvin men tae gie an accoont o hoo the haed daen wi tha catter he haed gien thaim tha furst yin toul him loard yer coin haes made ten mair weel daen saed tha king ye ir a guid sarvint ye hae showed a can trust ye in wee things all gie ye ten cities tae rin an tha saicont yin cum an saed loard yer coin haes made five coins an tha king saed all gie ye five cities tae rin wi that anither yin cum up an saed luk loard heres yer coin a hae kep it lapt up in a cloot a wus feart o ye fer ye ir a haird man tae dail wi ye tak whut daesnae belang tae ye an ye hairvest whut ye hinnae plantit tha king cum bak wi ye uisless guidfernaethin frae yer ain mooth ye hae condemned yersel sae ye thocht a wus a haird man did ye takkin whut didnae belang tae me an hairvestin whut a haednae plantit weel ye cud hae put ma siller intae tha bank hoo cum ye didnae then whaniver a cum bak it cud hae made me a wee bit o intrest wi that tha king toul thaim that wur stannin roon aboot tak his coin frae him an gie it tae him that haes tha ten but the saed tae him loard shair he haes ten coin saed tha king all tell ye this iverie yin that haes wull be gien mair an whaiver haes little or naethin even whut he haes wull be taen awa frae him but as fer thaim that wur agin me an wudnae hae me fer king bring thaim here tae me an kill thaim fornent me efter tellin thaim aa this jesus went on aheid alang tha road up tae jerusalem an whaniver he wus cum near til bethphage an bethanie nixt tha hill caad tha moont o olives he sent on twa o his follaers sayin tae thaim awa intae thon clachan fornent iz whan yis git thair yell fin a cowlt tyed up that naebodie haes iver sut on lowse its raip an bring it til me if onie yin axes yis hoo cum yis ir lowsin tha cowlt jist tell thaim tha loard haes need o it noo tha twa that went fun it jist as the haed bin toul an as the wur lowsin tha cowlt tha yins it belanged tae axt thaim whut ir ye daein lowsin that cowlt saed tha twa tha loard haes want o it an the brocht it tae jesus an pittin thair claes on tha cowlts bak the tuk houl o it tae jesus got on wi that as jesus made his wye alang tha fowk spreed thair claes doon afore him on tha pad an whaniver he wus cumin nearhan tha pad doon frae tha moont o olives his follaers stairtit shoutin oot wi joy tha hale lock o thaim praisin god fer aa tha miracles the haed saen an cryin oot blisst is tha king that cums in tha name o tha loard peace in heiven abain an glorie in tha heichest an some o tha pharisees amang tha thrang saed tae jesus maister scoul yer follaers an tell thaim tae quit it but he cum bak wi this am tellin yis if they ir quait een tha stanes thairsels wull cry oot jesus wus cumin near tae jerusalem noo an whan he saa tha citie he begun tae greet an he saed och if ye onlie haed hae knowed whut wud bring ye peace tha day but na ye didnae an noo its hid frae yer een fer tha time wull cum whan thaim thats agin ye wull big dykes aa roon ye an fence ye in frae aa sides yell be flettent intae tha grun an aa yer fowk alang wi ye thell no lea yin stane on anither fer ye didnae ken tha day that god cum tae ye an yinst he got tae jerusalem whut jesus daen wus this he went strecht intae tha hoose o god an he begun reddin oot tha dailers frae tha coortyaird it is writ doon he saed tae thaim that ma hoose wull be a hoose o prayer but yous hae turnt it intae a den o robbers an efter that iverie day jesus stairtit lairnin tha fowk in tha hoose o god an tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa alang wi tha heidyins amang tha fowk the wur oot tae get rid o him but the cud dae naethin aboot it fer he wusnae iver on his lane an aa tha fowk hung on his iverie wurd on yin o thaim days as jesus wus lairnin tha fowk that wur in tha hoose o god an praichin tha guid news tha heid preeshts tha maisters o tha laa an tha elders amang tha fowk cum up tae him an saed tell iz this bi whut thortie ir ye daein these things an wha gien ye it an he cum bak wi a hae a question tae ax you as weel jist tell me this jhones baptisin wus it frae heiven or wus it jist a notion o man an the taakt aboot it tae yin anither an saed if we gie tha answer frae heiven he wull say hoo cum yis didnae believe him then but if we say frae men aa tha fowk wull clod iz wi stanes fer the hae nae doot that jhone wus a proaphit sae the toul him that the cudnae tell whar jhones baptisin haed cum frae an jesus saed tae thaim then all no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie a dae these things he turnt tae tha fowk an toul thaim this parable thair wus this man plantit a vineyaird an he set it tae a wheen o tenantfairmers tae rin afore gaun awa fer a lang time tae anither kintrie an whaniver hairst time cum roon he sent a sarvin man tae tha fairmers tae get a taste o tha fruit frae thaim but the bate up tha sarvin man an chaist him awa empiehannit sae he sent anither sarvin man but the creesht him as weel wur wile baad til him an sent him awa wi naethin agane he sent anither yin oot an the hurt him an flung him oot tae then tha laird o tha vineyaird saed whut wull a dae a know all senn ma ain sinn that a love the ir shair tae hae regaird fer him but whaniver tha tenantfairmers saen tha sinn the taakt it ower an saed this is tha boy that wull git aa this here whan his da dees if we kill him aa this cud be oors sae the put him oot o tha vineyaird an killt him an jesus axt whut dae yis think tha laird wull dae on thaim noo all tell yis he wull cum an desthroy thaim fairmers an set tha vineyaird tae ithers whan tha fowk listenin tae jesus heerd this the saed this shud niver cum aboot but jesus lukt at thaim strecht in tha ee an axt whut then is tha mainin o this scripture tha verie stane tha masons turnt doon is noo tha coarner stane aa tha yins that faa ower thon stane wull be smesht tae bits an whaiver it faas on wull be grun tae pooder tha maisters o tha laa an tha heid preeshts lukt fer a wye tae tak houl o him thair an then fer the kent he haed spauk agin thaim in this parable but the wur feart o whut tha fowk wud dae keepin a quare clase ee on him the sent yins that lut on the wur honest fer tae spie on him the wur hopin tae ketch him oot in sumthin he saed fer the wantit tae be able tae han him ower tae tha pooer o tha roman guviner these yins that wur spiein on jesus axt him sayin maister ye taak an taich whut is richt ye dinnae mak o yin mair ner tha ither but ye taich gods wye an tha truith tell iz is it richt fer iz tae pye tex tae caesar or no but jesus saa throu thaim an he saed dinnae try me oot let me see a denarius noo whase name an laikness is on it its caesars the saed then gie caesar whut belangs tae caesar saed he an gie god whut belangs tae god that settelt thaim the wurnae able tae ketch him oot afore tha fowk fer whut he haed saed an the haed tae be quait fer his answer flebbergestit thaim an sartin sadducees thaim that say thair isnae onie risin frae tha deid the cum an pit a question tae jesus maister the saed moses writ doon fer iz that if a mans brither dees an leas a guidwife wi nae weans then he maun merrie tha weeda an hae childer fer his deid brither noo whut if thair wus seiven brithers tha oulest gets merriet an he dees wioot haein onie weans sae tha saicont brither he merries tha weeda an he dees as weel still nae weans an tha thurd merries hir an in tha same wye aa seiven brithers merries hir an dees leain nae femlie ava an in tha enn tha wumman she deed as weel noo at tha risin frae tha deid whase guidwife wull she be fer she wus merriet on tha hale seiven o thaim jesus cum bak wi this men an weemen o this warl get merriet but thaim that ir coontit fit tae be pairt o tha risin frae tha deid an tha nixt warl thair wull be nae mair merryin fer thaim thell be laik tha angels an the cannae dee the ir childer o god an childer o tha risin frae tha deid but even moses whaniver he writ aboot tha burnin bush he showed that tha deid rises agane fer he caas tha loard tha god o abraham an tha god o isaac an tha god o jacob lang efter the wur aa deid hes no tha god o tha deid hes tha god o tha leevin fer iveriebodies leevin in gods een an some o tha maisters o tha laa saed weel spauk maister but naebodie ava wud dar ax him onie mair questions then jesus axt thaim hoo can the mak oot that tha messiah is tha sinn o davit fer davit hissel says in tha buik o psaums tha loard saed tae ma loard sit doon at ma richt han tae a mak o yer enemies a stool fer unner yer fit sae davit caas tha messiah ma loard hoo can he be his sinn then whaniver aa tha fowk wus listenin jesus saed tae his follaers dinnae tak heed o tha maisters o tha laa fer the ir fand o paradin aboot in fancie robes an the love fowk tae touch thair keps tae thaim in tha mairket places the laik tae hae tha best saits in tha meetin hooses an tae be at tha tap table at faists the halp thairsels bi daein weeda weemen oot o aa the hae an the mak lang screeds o prayers jist fer show but yis can be shair it wull gang waur wi thaim on tha day o reckonin jesus lukt up an saa tha weelaff fowk pittin thair offerins intae tha kist in tha hoose o god then he saen this puir weeda wumman drappin in twa pennies am tellin yis tha truith qo he this puir weeda haes gien mair ner onie o tha rest o thaim aa these yins hae onlie gien a pittance oot o thair pruch intae tha kist but this weeda puir an aa that she is haes gien aa she haed tae leeve on some o thaimins that wur wi him wur taakin amang thairsels aboot tha wye tha hoose o god wus aa daen up wi its bricht bonnie stanes an coastlie ornyments gien in bi fowk but jesus saed tha day wull cum whan aa these stanes wull be tummelt doon an no yin stane wull be left abain tha ither an the axt him maister whans aa this fer happenin then an wull we hae onie sign o it cumin jesus cum bak wi this tak heed an dinnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee fer monies a yin wull cum in ma name sayin a be tha christ or tha time is cum dinnae pye thaim onie heed whan yis hear tell o wars an fechtin dinnae be feart fer sitch things maun cum aboot furst but tha enn is no near jist yit then he saed tae thaim nations wull mak war on ither nations an kingdoms wull rise up agin ither kingdoms thair wull be michtie irthquakes dirths an plagues in differnt pairts an fleysum sichts an pooerfu signs frae heiven hooaniver afore aa this cums aboot thell be takkin houl o yis persecutin yis an turnin yis in at tha meetin hooses thell clod yis intae jail an dreg yis up afore kings an guviners jist fer bein ma follaers thisll be yer chaunce tae wutness tae yin an aa sae pit yer mine tae it then an dinnae fash yersels aforehan aboot whut kine o answer yis ir gaun tae gie fer a wull pit tha richt wurds in yer mooth an gie yis tha wut tae uise thaim sae nane o yer enemies wull be able tae stan up tae yis or say a wurd agin yis yisll even be hannit ower bi thaim that is clase tae yis yer mither an faither yer brithers yer freens an nighbers an some o yis wull be killt an yisll be haitit bi aa fowk on accoont o me but no een yin hair o yer heid wull cum tae onie hairm dinnae gie up thole aa that cums at ye an yisll fin rael life noo whan yis see tha airmies gethert aa roon jerusalem then yis wull ken that tha time fer it tae be tummelt doon is nearhan then thaim ats in judea maun tak tae tha hills an thaim ats in jerusalem maun flee oot o it an thaim ats ootside tha citie shudnae try tae get in fer thatll be tha day o gods punishment an whut wus foretoul bi tha proaphits maun cum aboot in thaim days itll be tarrible fer weemen thats expectin an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht thairll be a wile baad time o sufferin aa ower tha lan an gods angr wull be agin this fowk some o thaim wull be killt bi tha sword ithersll be tuk awa an skailt amang aa tha nations o tha warl an jerusalem wull be thrampt doon bi haithen feet tae tha time o tha gentiles cums tae an enn thairll be quare signs in tha sin an tha muin an tha starns an doon here on tha irth tha fowk o aa tha nations wull be hairtscarred an at thair wuts enn wi tha souch o tha roarin sea an tha waves fowkll be that feart thell be takkin dwams acause o whut the see cumin on tha warl fer tha verie pooers o tha lift wull be shuk oot o kilter an then aa fowk wull see tha sinn o man cumin in a clood wi aa his pooer an muckle glorie whaniver aa these things stairts tae cum aboot stan up strecht lift up yer heids fer yisll shuin be delivert oot o hairms wye an he toul thaim this parable tak a luk at tha fig tree or onie ither tree whan tha leafs cum oot yis ken wioot bein toul tha simmers no faur aff sae whan yis see these things happenin yis can be shair tha kingdom o god is nearhan a tell yis tha truith thairs fowks leevin noo thatll no dee afore aa these things haes cum aboot heiven an irth wull pass awa but ma wurds wull niver pass awa tak care yis ir no bluthert or yer heids turnt wi wile leevin an dinnae fash yersels aboot tha worries o this life dinnae alloo that day tae cum doon on yis o a suddent laik a thrap wud dae fer thon day wull cum on iveriebodie leevin in tha hale warl sae aye keep an ee oot then an pray yis micht be strang eneuch tae stan afore tha sinn o man an be spared aa these things that ir gaun tae happen iverie day jesus went tae tha hoose o god tae taich tha fowk but he spent iverie nicht on tha moont o olives an aa tha fowk cum at tha furst licht tae listen tae him in tha hoose o god noo tha faist o bairmless breid caad tha passower wus nearhan an tha heid preeshts an maisters o tha laa wus colloguin thegither hoo tae get rid o jesus on tha quait fer the wur feart o whut tha fowk micht dae then satan cum intae tha hairt o judas tha yin caad iscariot that wus yin o tha twal an judas went tae tha heid preeshts an offyshers o tha temple gaird an taakt aboot hoo he micht han jesus ower tae thaim the wur weel plaised an struck a dail wi him tae gie him siller fer his wark sae judas made a paction an he lukt fer a guid apenin tae han jesus ower tae thaim whaniver thair wus nae crood aboot noo tha day o bairmless breid cum alang whan tha lambs wus killt fer tha passower an jesus bid peter an jhone tae gang on aheid fer tae mak readie tha passower mail fer thaim tae ait thegither the axt him whar wud ye hae iz mak it readie an he saed tae thaim tha minit yis cum intae tha citie a man cairryin a crockerie jar o watter wull meet yis follae him tae tha hoose he gangs intae an say tae tha guidman o tha hoose tha maister says whar is tha ruim whar a can ait tha passower wi ma follaers an he wull show yis a big upstair ruim plenisht an aa yis ir tae mak it readie thair the went an the fun it jist as he haed saed an the made readie tha boord fer tha passower mail an whaniver tha time cum tae stairt jesus tuk his place at tha boord an tha possels alang wi him an he saed tae thaim a hae bin langin wi aa ma hairt tae ait this passower mail wi yis afore a suffer fer am tellin yis aa noo all no ait it agane tae tha kingdom o god is cum then he tuk tha bicker in his hans gien thenks tae god an saed tak this an shair it oot amang yis fer a tell yis this frae noo on all no drink o tha fruit o tha vine afore tha kingdom o god haes cum an he tuk tha breid as weel an whaniver he haed gien thenks tae god he brauk it an hannit it tae thaim an saed this is ma bodie gien fer you dae this in mine o me in tha same wye efter supper he tuk tha bicker o wine an saed this bicker is a sign o gods new coveynant sealed wi ma bluid poored oot fer you but tak heed tha yin thats gaun tae gie me up is at tha boord alang wi me fer masel tha sinn o man a maun dee accoardin tae gods plan but wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays me then the begun tae taak amang thairsels axin whutch yin o thaim wud dae sitch an a thing an thair wus a thraw on amang thaim as tae whut yin o thaim shud be tha maist heich jesus toul thaim amang tha gentiles kings laird it ower thair ain fowk an thair heidyins gets tha name o daein guid but wi yous its no tae be laik that amang yous tha maist heich shud be laik tha maist hummle an a heidyin shud be laik a sarvint fer whut yins mair impoartin amang yis him thats sittin at tha boord or tha yin that sarves him is it no tha yin thats at tha boord ay ye wud think that wud be richt but no here fer a am amang yis as yin that sarves yous ir tha yins that hae stud bye me in reuch times an jist as ma faither haes gien a kingdom tae me sae a masel wull gie you tha richt tae ait an drink at tha boord in ma kingdom an yisll sit doon on thrones an judge tha twal clans o israel an wi that he went on tae say simon simon listen tae me satan haes axt tae hae yis aa fer tae riddle ye as wheat but a hae prayed fer ye simon that yer faith wull houl oot an whan ye hae turnt bak tae me ye ir tae haud up yer brithers an peter saed loard am readie tae gang tae jail wi ye or een tae dee wi ye am tellin ye peter saed jesus tha rooster wull no craa themorra moarnin afore ye hae saed thrie times ower that ye dinnae ken me an he went on tae say tae thaim aa whan a sent yis oot wi nae pooch nae baag an nae shune did yis want fer ocht an the saed naethin ava but noo saed jesus if yis hae a pooch or a baag tak thaim wi yis an if ye hinnae a sword sell tha coat aff yer bak an buy yin its writ doon in tha scriptures he wus coontit amang tha laa brekkers an a tell yis that whut wus writ doon thair aboot me maun cum aboot deed ay it wull aa cum aboot an the saed loard heres twa swords saed he bak tae thaim thatll dae an jesus cum oot o tha hoose an made his road tae tha moont o olives as he wus in tha habit o daein an his follaers went alang wi him whan he got tae tha place he toul thaim pray that whan ye ir tempit ye dinnae gie in tae it he went awa as faur as ye cud clod a stane an he got doon on his knees an prayed sayin faither if ye ir wullin wud ye tak this cup o sufferin awa frae me aa tha same no ma wull but yours be daen then an angel frae heiven appeart til him an gien him strenth an bein in a wile agonie jesus prayed mair an mair frae tha hairt tae tha sweit wus faain aff him tae tha grun laik big draps o bluid whan he wus daen prayin he got ontae his feet an went bak tae his follaers he fun thaim sleepin aa wore oot wi sorra an he saed tae thaim whut ir yis sleepin fer git up an pray less ye gie in tae temptation tha wurds wus harlie oot o his mooth whan up cum a hale thrang o fowk an judas yin o tha twal wus at tha heid o thaim he waakit up tae jesus an he gien him a kiss o greetin but jesus saed tae him judas wud ye bethray tha sinn o man wi a kiss whan jesus ither follaers saa whut wus aboot tae happen the saed loard shud we tak oor swords tae thaim an yin o thaim hut tha sarvint o tha heich preesht an he sneddit his richt lug aff but jesus saed houl on nae mair o that an he put his han on tha ear an hailt tha man then jesus saed tae tha heid preeshts tha offyshers o tha temple gaird an tha elders that haed cum oot tae tak houl o him am a some soart o a reiver that yis hae cum oot wi swords an stavs agin me whan a wus wi yis iverie day in tha hoose o god yis niver layed a fingr on me but this is tha time fer yous tae ect tha pooer o dairkness is ower yis noo then the tuk houl o jesus an led him oot an brocht him tae tha heich preeshts hoose peter wus follaein behin keepin his distance an the kinnelt a fire in tha middle o tha coortyaird an the sut doon thegither an peter amang thaim an thair wus this wee sarvin lass tuk a clase luk at him in tha lowe o tha fire this man wus wi him tae saed she but peter saed na na lass a dinnae know him efter a while anither yin saa him an saed ye ir yin o thaim tae but peter saed man na am naethin o tha soart an aboot an oor efter that anither yin insistit this fella wus shairlie wi him fer wioot a doot hes frae galilee tae but wi that peter saed man a dinnae know whut ye ir taakin aboot an tha wurds wusnae richt aff his tung whan a rooster craad an tha loard turnt an lukt at peter an peter haed mine o hoo tha loard haed saed tae him afore tha rooster craas in tha moarnin ye wull deny me thrie times an peter went oot o tha coortyaird greetin sair noo tha men houlin jesus wur mockin him an giein him a guid whalin an the put a blinfoul on him the hut him on tha face an axt weel proaphit tell iz wha skelpt ye an the caad him iverie name unner tha sin then at tha scraich o day aa tha elders o tha fowk gethert thegither baith tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa the led jesus awa tae thair cooncil an the saed tae him if ye ir tha christ tell iz an he saed bak tae thaim if a dae tell yis yisll no believe me an if a ax yis oniethin yisll no gie me an answer oniehoo but frae this time forrit tha sinn o man wull be saitit at tha richt han o tha michtie yin an the aa saed sae ye ir tha sinn o god then an jesus saed bak tae thaim weel ye saed it yersels whut mair pruif dae we need the axt noo we hae heerd it fer oorsels frae his ain mooth then tha cooncil tha hale lock o thaim tuk jesus an brocht him up tae pilate an the stairtit tae bring chairges agin him an saed we fun this man leadin tha fowk asthray tellin thaim no tae pye onie tex tae caesar makkin hissel oot tae be christ tha messiah an a king pilate axt jesus ir you tha king o tha jews an jesus saed bak tae him you hae saed it then pilate saed tae tha heid preeshts an tha thrang o fowk a cannae fin oniethin agin this man but the kep on at pilate sayin this man is stirrin up naethin but bother wi tha things hes bin lairnin tha fowk tha lenth an breadth o tha lan frae galilee richt doon tae here whan pilate heerd this he axt ach daes he cum frae galilee
