then an as shuin as he fun oot that jesus cum unner herods thortie he sent him up tae him fer herod happent tae be in jerusalem hissel at tha time noo whan herod saa jesus he wus hairt gled fer he haed heerd aa aboot him an haed bin langin tae see him he haed hoped he micht see him daein some miracle sae he axt jesus a hale lock o questions but jesus niver saed a wurd bak an tha heid preeshts an tha maisters o tha laa wus stannin aboot hoochin an yellin thair accusations agin jesus herod alang wi his sodgers jeert an made little o him riggin him oot in a braw fancie goon an the sent him agane tae pilate that verie day herod an pilate becum guid freens afore that thair wus nae love loast atween thaim sae pilate caad thegither tha heid preeshts an ither releejus heidyins alang wi aa tha ordinarie fowk an he saed tae thaim yis hae brocht this man afore me sayin that he wus stirrin up fowk an casin bother a hae examined him afore yis aa an a hae fun naethin wrang ava as faur as whut yis say he haes daen na herod didnae ither fer he sent him bak tae iz listen tae me this man haes daen naethin tae warrant bein put tae deith sae all gie him a whalin tae lairn him a lesson an let him gang fer he maun let yin wrangdaer gang at tha faist then tha hale crood o thaim yellt oot awa wi this man let barabbas oot noo barabbas haed bin put in jail fer murder an riotin in jerusalem pilate wantit tae let jesus gang free sae he spauk agane tae thaim aa but the kep on cryin oot crucyfie him crucyfie him pilate saed tae thaim a thurd time why whut wrang haes he daen a dinnae fin oniethin tae pit him tae deith ower all gie him a whalin an let him gang but tha hale thrang shoutit aa tha mair that jesus shud be crucyfied an tha crood an tha heid preeshts got thair ain wye sae pilate gien in tae whut the wantit he daen as the axt him an he let gang tha man that haed bin put in jail fer riot an murder but jesus he hannit ower tae thaim the cud dae whut the wantit wi him as the led jesus awa the clappt hans on simon frae cyrene that wus makkin his wye in frae tha kintrie the put tha cross on his shooder an the gart him tae cairrie it behin jesus a hale crood o fowk wus follaein ahint him an amang thaim a lock o weemen that wur batin thair breeshts an lamentin ower whut wus gaun tae happen tae jesus but jesus turnt roon tae thaim an saed dochters o jerusalem dinnae greet fer me greet fer yersels an yer weans fer luk tha days no faur aff whan the wull be sayin blisst ir tha weemen thats barren an tha wames that niver bair weans an tha breeshts that niver gie milk in that day the wull stairt sayin tae tha muntins faa doon on iz an tae tha hills cover iz ower noo if the wud dae that whaniver tha tree is in fu leaf an growein weel whut wull the dae whan tha trees ir wuthert twa ithers as weel that wur crimnals wur led oot tae be put tae deith alang wi jesus an whan the cum tae tha place caad calvarie the crucyfied him thair an tha twa crimnals alang wi him yin on tha richt han side tha tither on tha left an jesus saed faither forgie thaim fer the dinnae ken whut ther daein an tha sodgers gemmelt fer his claes pairtin thaim amang thairsels aa tha while tha fowk stud bye lukkin on but tha heidyins o tha jews giekt at him sayin he saved ithers let him save hissel if hes gods messiah tha chosen yin tha sodgers jeert him tae cumin up an offerin him soor wine an the saed tae him if you ir tha king o tha jews save yersel an the put up a signboord abain him an it saed in tha greek tha latin an tha hebrew this is tha king o tha jews noo yin o tha crimnals hingin alangside o him yellt abuse at him ir ye no tha messiah he axt save yersel an iz forbye but tha ither yin gien aff tae him an axt him dae ye no fear god seein as ye ir condemned tae dee as weel we ir jist gettin whut we desarve fer whut we hae daen but this man haes daen naethin wrang ava an wi that he saed loard jesus keep mine o me whan ye cum intae yer kingdom saed jesus bak tae him a tell ye tha truith yell be wi me in paradise this verie day bi this time it wus nuin an dairkness cum ower tha hale lan tae thrie in tha efternuin tha licht o tha sin wus blekt oot an tha curtin hingin in tha halie o halies wus torn in twa then jesus cryed oot wi a lood voice faither a gie ma spirit up intae your hans an wi that he gien his last breath noo whan tha centurion saen whut wus daen he gien glorie tae god an saed thon man wus a guid man thats fer shair an aa tha fowk that cum tae see whut wus gaun on whan the saa whut wus daen the bate thair breeshts in sorra an went awa an aa jesus freens alang wi tha weemen that follaed him frae galilee stud awa bak takkin it aa in noo thair wus a man caad joseph a coonciller a guid an dacent man that haednae gan alang wi thair deceesion tae kill jesus he wus frae arimathea a toon o tha jews an he wus bidin his time waitin on tha kingdom o god tae cum joseph went tae pilate an axt fer tha bodie o jesus an he tuk it doon frae tha cross lapt it in linen claith an layed it in a tomb cut oot o tha roak whar naebodie haed bin layed afore an it wus late in tha day on friday tha day fer gettin readie fer tha sabbath tha weemen that haed cum wi jesus frae galilee follaed efter an the tuk heed o tha tomb an hoo his bodie wus layed oot thair the went awa an made up spices an ointments an then the stapt thair wark fer tha sabbath day accoardin tae tha commaun o god on tha furst day o tha week at tha scraich o day tha weemen cum tae tha tomb an brocht tha spices the haed makkit readie an thair wus ither yins alang wi thaim an the fun tha stane rowlt awa frae tha tomb the went in but tha bodie o tha loard jesus wus naewhar tae be saen an the wur wile fasht aboot it aa o a suddent thair wur twa men stannin bye in bricht claes tha weemen wus hairt feart an bood doon wi thair faces tae tha grun an tha men saed fer why ir yis lukkin tha leevin amang tha deid hes no here hes ris dae yis no mine hoo he taakt tae yis bak in galilee sayin tha sinn o man maun be gien intae tha hans o sinfu men tae be crucyfied an tha thurd day rise agane ay richt eneuch the saed thats jist whut jesus toul iz wud happen sae the cum awa frae tha tomb an toul tha eleiven possels aa that haed cum aboot an the toul aa tha rest o thaim as weel it wus mary magdalene an johanna an mary tha mither o jeames an ither weemen that wur wi thaim that toul these things tae tha possels an the didnae believe thaim an thocht the wur taakin blethers then peter got up an run tae tha tomb an stoopit doon an keekt in he saa tha linen claiths lyin bye thair lane an he went awa wunnerin tae hissel whut haed cum aboot that same day twa o jesus follaers set oot fer tha village o emmaus six or seiven mile frae jerusalem an the wur taakin tae yin anither aboot aa tha goinson an whan the wur taakin aboot it an tryin tae unnerstan it jesus hissel cum up alangside o thaim an waakit wi thaim the saa him aa richt but the didnae ken wha he wus an he saed tae thaim whut wur ye taakin aboot thair alang tha road the cum tae a stap lukkin doon in tha mooth an yin o thaim caad cleopas saed tae him ye maun be a stranger in jerusalem if ye hinnae heerd ocht o whuts bin happenin thair in tha last wheen o days saed he tae thaim whut things an the saed did ye no hear aboot jesus o nazareth a proaphit michtie in his wurds an daeins afore god an aa tha fowk an aboot hoo oor heid preeshts an heidyins hannit him ower the passt a sentence o deith on him an nailt him tae a cross sae the did we haed thocht he wus tha yin that wud redeem israel oniehoo its thrie days since this happent ay an parteeclar weemen frae amang iz that wur up earlie at his tomb tuk iz bak whan the saed the cudnae fin his bodie an the cum bak an toul iz thed saen a vision o angels sayin jesus wus leevin an sartin o thaim that wus amang iz went tae tha tomb an richt eneuch the fun it jist as tha weemen haed saed jesus wusnae thair then jesus saed tae tha twa o thaim ye coofs yis ir slow tae tak in aa that tha proaphits spauk aboot the saed that christ wud hae tae dree aa these things afore he gaed intae his glorie did the no an stairtin wi moses an aa tha proaphits he made plain tae thaim whut aa tha scriptures saed aboot hissel an whan the cum nearhan tha village whar the wur gaun he lukt as if he wus gaun on furder but the coaxt him sayin wud ye no stap wi iz fer its dailygan an itll be dairk shuin sae he went in wi thaim an it cum aboot as he sut doon tae ait wi thaim that he tuk breid blisst it an brauk it an gien it tae thaim an aa o a suddent thair een wus apent an the kent wha he wus an wi that jesus wus nae mair tae bi saen the saed tae yin anither did it no set oor hairts alow whan he taakt tae iz on tha road an apent up tha scriptures tae iz sae the ris up tha same oor an the went bak tae jerusalem an fun tha eleiven gethert thegither an thaim that wur wi thaim tha loard is ris richt eneuch the wur toul an simon haes saen him an tha twa frae emmaus toul aa that haed happent on tha road an hoo the knowed it wus jesus tha minit he brauk tha breid an jist as the wur taakin thair stud jesus in tha middle o thaim aa an he saed tae thaim peace be wi yis but the wur aa hairtscarred an afeart an thocht the haed saen a wraith an he saed tae thaim fer why ir yis put aboot an why aa tha doots wiin yersels tak a luk at ma hans an ma feet its masel hannle me an see fer a wraith haesnae flesh an banes as yis see a hae an efter sayin this he showed thaim his hans an his feet an the wur that blythesum an dumfoonert the cud harlie tak it in an he axt thaim hae yis ocht tae ait in tha hoose the gien him a bit o brannert fish an a wee bit o honeycomb an he tuk it an et it afore thaim then he saed tae thaim this is whut a toul ye whaniver a wus still amang yis that aa tha things that wur writ doon consarnin me in tha laa o moses tha proaphits an tha psaums maun cum aboot then he apent thair mines tae unnerstan tha scriptures sayin tae thaim its writ doon that tha christ maun suffer he maun dee an rise frae tha deid tha thurd day an that wi ma thortie yis ir tae praich this message tae aa nations repent o yer sins an god wull forgie yis yis ir tae stairt frae jerusalem yous hae saen these things sae yis ir wutnesses o thaim aa noo listen tae me a wull senn upon yis tha gift ma faither promist but yous ir tae stap here in jerusalem tae yis ir claithed wi pooer frae abain an jesus led thaim oot tha lenth o bethanie an thair he liftit up his hans an blisst thaim an it cum aboot that while he wus blissin thaim he pairtit frae thaim an he wus taen up intae heiven an the wurshipt him an the went bak tae jerusalem wi blythesum hairts an the spent aa thair time laudin an blissin in tha hoose o god richt at tha stairt ye haed tha wurd tha wurd wus thair alang wi god an tha wurd wus god he wus thair alang wi god richt frae tha stairt iverie last thing wus made throu him athoot him naethin ava wus iver made in him wus life an this life wus tha licht o mankine tha licht beams in tha mirk but tha mirk cannae pit it oot thair wus this man sent oot frae god bi tha name o jhone an he cum fer tae be a wutness tae tha licht sae that acause o him aa fowk micht believe noo he wusnae thon licht hissel but he cum fer tae be a wutness tae tha licht tha true licht him that gies licht tae iverie man wus cumin intae tha warl he wus in tha warl but tha mair it wus o his makkin tha warl didnae ken wha he wus he cum tae his ain lan but his ain fowk wantit naethin tae dae wi him yit tae aa thaim that did tak him in an trustit on his name he gien thaim tha richt tae be makkit childer o god childer that wus no boarn bi tha wye o nature ner bi tha wull o flesh an bluid ner bi tha notion a husban micht hae na but childer that wus boarn o god tha wurd cum tae be flesh an bluid an leeved amang iz we hae saa his glorie tha glorie o tha yin an ainlie that cum frae tha faither fu o grace an truith jhone gien wutness o him he caad oot cryin thons him a wus taakin aboot whaniver a saed him that cums efter me is abain me fer he wus thair afore iver a wus boarn oot o tha fu guidness o his hairt we hae aa got yin blissin on tap o anither tha mair tha laa wus gien throu moses grace an truith cum throu jesus christ naebodie haes iver saen god it is gods yae sinn wha bides in tha hairt o tha faither that haes showed him tae fowk noo tha day tha jews sent preeshts an levites frae jerusalem tae ax jhone wha he wus here is whut he saed tae thaim he wus aye apen aboot it an toul thaim strecht am no tha christ sae the axt him wha ir ye then wud ye be elijah na am no qo he ir ye tha proaphit we ir waitin on na saed he at tha enn o it the speered wha ir ye gie iz yer answer tae tak bak tae thaim that sent iz whut hae ye tae say fer yersel jhone answert wi tha wurds o isaiah tha proaphit am tha voice o yin caain oot in tha wiles mak tha road readie fer tha loard cumin noo some pharisees that haed bin sent speered him mair gin yer no tha christ ner elijah ner tha proaphit hoo cum yer baptisin fowk then a baptise wi watter jhone answert but thairs yin stud amang ye that yis dinnae know him that cums alang efter me hes tha yin an am no fit tae lowse his buits fer him noo this aa cum aboot at bethanie on tha faur side o tha joardan whar jhone wus baptisin tha nixt day jhone saa jesus cumin up tae him an saed luk an behoul tha lamb o god that taks awa tha sin o tha warl thons tha man a wus taakin aboot whaniver a saed thairs a man cumin efter me thats o heicher stannin ner me fer he wus thair afore iver a wus boarn a didnae unnerstan masel wha he wus but it wus tae mak him kent tae israel that a cum baptisin wi watter then jhone gien this accoont a saa tha spirit cum doon frae heiven laik a doo an bide on him a wudnae a knowed him but tha yin that sent me fer tae baptise wi watter toul me whan ye see tha spirit cum doon an bide on a man its him that wull baptise wi tha halie spirit a hae saa it fer masel an am wutness tae it thon man daes be tha sinn o god tha nixt day jhone wus bak thonner wi twa o his ain follaers whaniver he saa jesus slippin bye he saed luk thons tha lamb o god whaniver tha twa follaers heerd him say this the turnt an went efter jesus lukkin roon jesus saa thaim cumin efter him an axt whut dae yis want rabbi the saed rabbi stans fer dominie whar ir ye stappin thenicht cum on an see he answert sae the went an saa whar he wus stappin an the passt tha rest o tha day wi him fer it wus aboot fower in tha efternuin andra simon peters brither wus yin o tha twa that went efter jesus whaniver the heerd whut jhone haed saed tha furst thing andra daen wus tae fin his brither simon an tell him we hae fun tha messiah mainin tha christ an he brocht him tae jesus jesus tuk a guid luk at him an he saed sae ye ir simon jhones sinn yell noo be caad cephas cephas stans fer peter mainin a roak tha nixt day jesus made up his mine tae heid fer galilee he fun philip an saed tae him follae me noo philip cum frae bethsaida tha same toon as andra an peter philip fun thannie an toul him we hae fun tha yin moses writ aboot in tha laa him that tha proaphits writ aboot forbye jesus o nazareth tha sinn o joseph nazareth cud ye iver see ocht guid cumin oot o thonner thannie axt cum an see fer yersel saed philip whan jesus saa thannie cumin he saed this aboot him noo thairs a guid israelite thairs naethin fauss aboot him hoo is it ye ken me thannie axt jesus answert a saa ye whaniver ye wur still unner tha fig tree afore philip caad ye wi that thannie declared rabbi you ir tha sinn o god sae ye ir tha king o israel jesus saed you lippen jist wi me tellin ye a saa ye unner tha fig tree weel yell see ower mair ner that an then he addit am tellin yis tha truith thairs a day cumin whaniver yell see heiven apen up an tha angels o god gaun up an cumin doon on tha sinn o man cum tha thurd day thair wus this waddin on at cana in galilee an tha mither o jesus wus at it an jesus wus axt tae tha waddin tae alang wi his follaers noo whaniver tha wine wus aa daen jesuss mither saed til him the hae nae mair wine wumman dear jesus answert whut ir ye bringin me intae it fer ma oor isnae cum yit his mither saed til tha sarvints whutiver he bids yis dae dae it noo nearhan thair wus six stane watter crocks tha soart tha jews uised fer ritual waashin that cud houl aboot twuntie tae thurtie gallon apiece jesus toul tha sarvints fill tha crocks fu o watter sae the fillt thaim fu tae tha lip then he toul thaim noo lave a drap oot an tak it tae tha heid sarvint sae the daen as the wur bid an tha heid sarvint preed a wee taste o tha watter that haed bin turnt intae wine hed nae notion whar it cum frae tha mair tha sarvints that haed brocht tha watter knowed sae he tuk tha bridegruim tae tha yin side qo he onie ither bodie wud gie oot tha guid wine at tha furst an whan fowks hae a lock o drink in thaim the bring oot tha chaip stuff but you hae kep tha guid wine tae noo this sign at cana in galilee wus tha furst that jesus wrocht in daein this his glorie wus thair fer aa tae see an his follaers believed in him efter this jesus tuk hissel doon wi his follaers tae capernaum alang wi his mither an brithers an the aa stapt thonner fer twarthie days whaniver tha time cum fer tha jews tae houl tha passower jesus gaed up tae jerusalem an in tha coortyaird o tha hoose o god he cum on men dailin in kye sheep an doos an ithers sittin at thair tables changin siller sae he put thegither a whup o coards an driv tha hale lock oot o tha temple gruns alang wi sheep an kye he skailt tha siller o tha money changers an coupt thair tables tae thaim that soul doos he saed tak aa this awa oot o here hoo dar yis mak a margymore oot o ma faithers hoose his follaers haed mine o tha scripture whar its writ all be het up wi a hungr fer your hoose sae tha jews then axt him strecht whut sign cud ye gie iz fer pruif o yer richt tae dae aa this jesus gien thaim tha answer fletten this temple an in thrie days a wull rise it agane but tha jews cum bak wi it tuk fowertiesix year tae big this temple an yer fer risin it agane in thrie days hooaniver tha temple he wus taakin aboot wus his ain bodie efter he wus ris frae tha deid his follaers haed mine o whut he saed then the put thair faith in scripture an tha wurd o jesus noo whaniver he wus in jerusalem fer tha faist o tha passower monie fowks put thair faith in his name whan the saen tha signs he daen but jesus wudnae pit his faith in thaim fer he knowed whut fowk wus laik he didnae need oniebodie tae tell him ocht aboot fowk fer he kent weel eneuch whut wus in thair hairts noo thair wus yin o tha pharisees caad nicodemus a memmer o tha heich cooncil o tha jews he cum tae jesus at nicht an saed rabbi we ken yer a taicher that haes cum frae god fer naebodie cud wark these signs ye ir daein if god wusnae wi him jesus saed bak tae him am tellin ye tha truith naebodie wull see tha kingdom o god if he isnae boarn agane hoo cud ye get boarn agane whaniver yer aareadie oul nicodemus axt shair ye cudnae gang bak intae yer mithers wame an be boarn agane cud ye jesus answert am tellin ye tha truith naebodie can get intae tha kingdom o god if he isnae boarn o watter an tha spirit whuts boarn o tha flesh is flesh but whuts boarn o tha spirit is spirit dinnae be tuk bak whaniver a tell ye yis maun be boarn agane tha wun blaas whutiver airt it wants ye hear tha sugh o it but ye dinnae ken whar its cum frae ner whar its gaun tae its tha same wi iveriebodie thats boarn o tha spirit nicodemus saed bak tae him weel hoo cud that be wi you bein a taicher o israel saed jesus yed think ye wud unnerstan these things am tellin ye tha truith whut we ir tellin ye aboot is baith whut we ken an whut we hae wutnesst but yous fowk dinnae tak onie heed o iz whan a hae toul ye aboot tha things o tha irth an yis dinnae tak ma wurd fer it hoo ir ye gaun tae believe whan a taak aboot tha things o heiven naebodie haes iver gan up tae heiven apairt frae tha yin that is cum doon frae heiven tha sinn o man wha is in heiven but jist as moses put up tha sarpent on a poul in tha wulderness tha sinn o man maun be liftit up tae sae that iveriebodie that believes on him wull no perish but wull hae ayelastin life fer god loved tha warl that much that he gien his yin an ainlie sinn sae that whaiver pits thair trust in him wull no be loast but wull leeve fer ivermair fer god niver sent his sinn intae tha warl fer tae judge it but rether fer tae save it oniebodie that believes on him is no condemned but oniebodie that daesnae believe is aareadie condemned fer he haesnae believed on tha name o gods yin an ainlie sinn an this is tha judgemen that tha licht haes cum intae tha warl but men wud rether hae tha dairk ner tha licht on accoont o thair wrangdaeins iverie wrangdaer haits tha licht an thell no cum intae tha licht fer fear thair wrangdaeins wull be fun oot but oniebodie that leeves bi tha truith cums intae tha licht sae its oot in tha apen fer aa tae see that whut he haes daen wus gods daein efter this jesus an his follaers cum intae tha kintrie o judea whar he stapt a wheen o days alang wi thaim an baptised fowks weel jhone wus baptisin fowk forbye at aenon nearhan salim fer thair wus watter aplentie thair an fowks wus cumin lukkin baptised but this wus afore jhone wus put intae jail twarthie o jhones follaers haed wurds wi a jew ower ritual waashin the cum tae jhone an saed rabbi ye mine thon man that wus wi ye on tha ither side o tha joardan ye ken tha yin ye toul iz aboot weel he is baptisin an the ir aa flockin tae him jhone saed bak tae thaim naebodie can get ocht less its gien tae him frae heiven shair yis know yersels a toul yis strecht am no tha christ a wus jist sent aheid o him tha bridegruims tha yin that tha bride belangs tae still an aa tha freen lukkin efter him stans alangside o him an bes gye gled tae listen tae tha soon o his voice noo am owercum wi joy masel he maun growe bigger an a maun get smaaer tha yin that cums frae abain is abain aa tha yin that is frae tha irth belangs tae tha irth an taaks aboot tha things o tha irth tha yin that cums frae heiven is abain aa hes toul thaim whut aa he haes saen an heerd but naebodie taks onie heed tha yin that daes tak heed o it tha same yin wud warrant that god spakes tha truith tak tent tha yin that god haes sent taaks tha wurds o god fer thairs nae limit tae tha spirit god gies him tha faither loves tha sinn an haes gien aa things intae his han an oniebodie that pits thair belief in tha sinn haes ayelastin life but oniebodie that turns thair bak on tha sinn winnae see life but tha wrath o god hings ower him tha pharisees heerd that jesus wus getherin mair follaers roon him ner jhone an he wus baptisin thaim tha mair in fect it wusnae jesus but his follaers that wus daein tha baptisin but whaniver tha loard heerd this he upt an left judea an went awa hame yinst mair tae galilee noo he beed tae gang throu samaria sae he cum tae this toon in samaria wi tha name o sychar nearhan tha wee bit o grun that jacob haed gien tae joseph jacobs wal wus thonner an jesus daen oot frae aa his trevelin sut doon agin tha wal an it wus aboot tha middle o tha day noo a samaritan wumman cum fer a go o watter oot o tha wal an jesus saed til hir gie iz a drink o yer watter his follaers wur awa intae tha toon tae buy mait tha wumman saed bak tae him hoo cum yer axin me fer a drink an you a jew an me a samaritan wumman fer tha jews haed nae truck wi tha samaritans jesus gien hir tha answer if ye haed onlie but knowed whut god haes tae gie an whas axin ye fer tha drink ye wud hae axt him an he wud hae gien ye tha leevin watter sir qo she ye hae naethin tae lave tha watter oot wi an tha wal is brave an deep whar dae ye get this leevin watter frae dae ye think yer a bigger man ner oor forefaither jacob that gien iz tha wal an drunk frae it hissel laik his sinns daen forbye an his beese anaa jesus saed til hir oniebodie that taks a drink o this watter wull aye hae a druith on thaim agane but oniebodie that taks a drink o tha watter that a gie him wull niver hae a druith agane deed ay tha watter a gie him wull be a watter spoot wallin up tae ayelastin life tha wumman saed tae him weel sir gies a drap o this watter then sae all niver hae a druith on me agane ner hae tae keep cumin bak here fer tae draa watter he toul hir awa an caa yer husban an cum bak here a hae nae husban she answert jesus saed til hir yer richt thair whaniver ye say ye hinnae a husban tha truith o tha metter is ye hae haed five husbans an tha man yer leevin wi jist noo is no yer husban ava sae ye wur richt in whut ye saed sir tha wumman saed ye maun be a proaphit oor forefaithers wurshipt on this muntin but yous jews houl that we hae tae woarship in jerusalem jesus saed believe you me wumman tha times cumin whan itll no be on this here muntin ner in jerusalem ether that yisll be woarshippin tha faither yous samaritans dinnae ken whut yis ir woarshippin we jews dae ken whut wer woarshippin fer salvation is frae tha jews yit tha oors cumin an its here noo whan tha true woarshippers wull woarship tha faither in spirit an truith fer thaims tha soart tha faithers lukkin fer tae woarship him god is spirit an thaim that woarship him maun woarship in spirit an truith tha wumman saed a ken that tha messiah him the caa christ is cumin whaniver he cums hell mak aa things clear tae iz saed jesus til hir am him tha verie yin thats taakin tae ye jist then his follaers cum bak an the wur stoondit that jesus wus taakin wi a wumman but naebodie axt him whut dae ye want wi hir or whut ir ye daein taakin tae hir sae tha wumman set hir watter jar doon an went aff bak intae tha toon thair she telt tha fowk cum an see this man that toul me aa a iver daen cud this no be tha christ sae oot the cum frae tha toon an made thair wye up tae him while this wus gaun on his follaers kep at him sayin rabbi wud ye no tak a bite tae ait but he toul thaim a hae mait tae ait that yis ken naethin aboot then his follaers saed tae yin anither cud oniebodie hae brocht him mait whaniver we wur awa ma mait saed jesus is daein tha wull o him that sent me an tae get his wark aa daen dae yis no say fower mair month an then tha hairvest am tellin ye but cast yer een oot ower tha fiels the ir ripe an readie fer tha hairst tha shearer wull get his wages pyed an wull gether tha craps fer ayelastin life sae tha sower an tha shearer wull be gled thegither sae its tha truith whut the say yin man saas an tha tither yin shears a sent ye fer tae shear whut ye hinnae wrocht at ithers hae daen aa tha haird wark an yous hae got tha guid o thair labourin a guid wheen o tha samaritans frae thon toon believed in him becas o tha wummans wutness whaniver she telt thaim he toul me iveriethin a iver daen sae whaniver tha samaritans cum tae see him the plaidit wi him tae stap a bit langr wi thaim sae he stapt wi thaim twa days monie mair believed in jesus fer whut he saed an the toul tha wumman efter we ir no believin in him onie mair jist becas o whut you telt iz we hae heerd him fer oorsels an noo we ken that this man is tha saviour o tha warl noo efter twa days jesus tuk his leave an gan aff tae galilee fer as jesus hissel haed brocht tae thair notysh nae proaphit is iver weel thocht o in his ain hametoon an whaniver he cum tae galilee tha fowk thonner gien him a guid walcum fer the haed saen iveriethin he daen in jerusalem at tha faist o tha passower whaniver the wur up at it thairsels jesus stapt aff agane at cana in galilee whar he haed turnt tha watter intae wine an this heidyin frae tha palace wus thair whase sinn wus lyin seeck at capernaum whaniver tha man heerd that jesus wus bak in galilee frae judea he cum plaidin wi jesus tae cum doon an mak his sinn better his sinn wus gye faur throu ye see yous fowk less ye get signs an wunners tae luk at jesus telt him yell niver believe tha man frae tha palace saed o sir cum doon noo afore ma weefla slips awa saed jesus gan yer wa yer sinn wull leeve tha man tuk jesus at his wurd an went on hame whan he wus on tha road his sarvints cum oot tae meet him an tell him his weefla wus aa richt sae he axt at whut oor o tha day his sinn tuk a turn fer tha better an the toul him tha faivir quit at yin oclock yesterday then tha faither knowed richt awa that it wus tha verie time o day that jesus saed tae him yer sinn wull leeve sae he becum a believer tae him an aa in his hoose this wus tha saicont miracle jesus wrocht fer a sign efter cumin bak frae judea intae galilee efter a bit jesus gaed up tae jerusalem fer a faistday o tha jews noo alangside tha sheep gate in jerusalem thairs this puil that gets tha name o bethzatha in tha aramaic tung an it haes five ruifedin waakwyes wi apen pillars richt roon it big nummers o disabelt fowk uist tae lie roon it tha blin tha crippelt an tha paralysed waitin on tha rummlin o tha watter fer an angel wud gae doon at a sartin time intae tha puil fer tae rummle tha watter tha furst yin intae tha watter efter tha rummlin wus makkit weel o whutiver ailment he haed noo yin o thaim that wus lyin thonner haed bin ailin fer thurtieecht year whan jesus saa him an kent tha lang he wus seeck he axt him dae ye want tae be made weel sir tha lameter answert a hae naebodie tae gie me a han intae tha watter whaniver its rummelt jist whan am makkin tae get in some ither bodie aye gets doon afore me then jesus saed tae him up ye get lift yer mat up an waak strecht aff tha man wus made weel he liftit his mat an waakt noo aa this happent on tha sabbath day an sae tha jews saed tae tha man that wus makkit weel its tha sabbath day an tha laa daesnae alloo ye tae cairrie a mat but he cum bak wi this tha man that made me weel saed tae me lift yer mat up an waak an the axt him whas this that toul ye tae lift it up an waak tha man that wus makkit weel haed nae notion ava o wha it wus fer jesus haed jookt aff thonner intae tha thrang o fowk a while efter jesus fun him at tha hoose o god an saed til him luk see yer weel agane sae quit yer sinnin or sumthin waur micht happen tae ye tha man went awa an toul tha jews that it wus jesus that made him weel sae on accoont o jesus daein these things on tha sabbath day tha jews wur efter him an wur oot tae pit an enn tae him but jesus saed tae thaim ma faither is aye warkin richt up tae this verie day an am warkin tae thats fer why tha jews ettled aa tha mair tae kill him no jist fer brekkin tha sabbath but forbye he wus caain god his ain faither an pittin hissel on a level wi god then jesus toul thaim am tellin ye tha truith tha sinn can dae naethin on his ain but onlie whut he sees his faither dae fer whutiver tha faither daes tha sinn daes tae fer tha faither loves tha sinn an shows him aa he daes ay hell show him even bigger things ner these things ower an abain aa ye cud tak in fer jist laik tha faither rises tha deid an gies thaim life sae tha sinn gies life tae whaiver he plaises an mair ner that tha faither daesnae judge oniebodie but haes gien aa judgemen tae tha sinn that aa micht gie honour tae tha sinn jist as the gie honour tae tha faither him that daesnae honour tha sinn daesnae honour tha faither that sent him am tellin ye tha truith whaiver hears ma wurd an believes him that sent me haes ayelastin life he wull no be condemned he haes flittit frae deith tae life heres tha truith o it tha oor is cumin ay its cum noo whan tha deid wull hear tha voice o tha sinn o god an thaim that hears wull leeve fer jist laik tha faither haes tha pooer o life in hissel sae he haes gien tha sinn tha pooer o life tae an he haes gien him tha richt tae judge becas he is tha sinn o man dinnae be put aboot bi this fer tha oor is cumin whan aa thaim thats deid an buriet wull hear his voice an cum oot o thair graves thaim that haes daen guid wull be ris tae life an thaim that haes daen ill wull be ris tae damnation on ma ain a can dae naethin a judge jist whut a hear an ma judgin is richt fer am no lukkin tae plaise masel but tae plaise him that sent me if a wutness aboot masel ma testimonie daesnae stan up but thairs anither yin that gies me a guid testimonie an a ken that his testimonie aboot me stans up yis hae sent fowk tae jhone an he haes wutnesst tae tha truith aboot me no that a need tae tak mans testimonie but a mak mention o it sae as ye micht be saved jhone wus a bricht shinin lamp an yis wur hairt gled tae leeve in tha licht o it fer a wee while but a hae testimonie that houls mair wecht ner jhones fer tha verie wark that tha faither haes gien me tae feenish thats whut a am aboot noo an its wutness tae yin an aa that tha faither haes sent me an tha faither that sent me haes testified aboot me hissel yis hae niver heerd his voice ner set yer een on him nether daes his wurd bide in ye fer ye dinnae lippen tha yin he sent yis ir aye lukkin at tha ins an oots o tha scriptures fer ye think thats tha wye yell hae ayelastin life but am tha yin tha scriptures is taakin aboot an yit ye wull no cum tae me tae hae life tha praise o man mains naethin tae me but a know richtlie whut yous ir laik a ken that yis dinnae hae tha love o god in yer hairts a hae cum in ma faithers name an ye wudnae pye onie heed tae me but if anither bodie cums in his ain name ye wud tak heed o him sae ye wud yis ir content eneuch tae tak praise frae yin anither yit yis mak nae effort tae get tha praise that cums frae tha yin an ainlie god sae nae wunner yis cannae believe me but dinnae be thinkin am fer accusin ye afore tha faither its moses thatll accuse ye tha verie yin yis ir pittin aa yer hope on if ye haed hae believed moses ye wud hae believed me fer its me he writ aboot but seein as ye dinnae believe whut he writ ye ir no gaun tae believe whut a say ir ye efter this jesus went ower tae tha ither side o loch galilee whiles caad loch tiberias an a hale thrang o fowk wus cumin behin him fer the saa tha wunners hed daen wi tha seeck sae jesus gaed up tha braeside an sut doon wi his follaers noo tha passower faist hel bi tha jews wus cumin up whaniver jesus liftit his een an saa a big nummer o fowk cumin til him he saed tae philip whar cud we buy breid tae feed aa thae fowk but he jist axt this tae try him oot fer he knowed fine weel whut he wus fer daein philip toul him twa hunner denarii wudnae be eneuch tae buy breid fer thaim aa anither o his follaers andra simon peters brither cum forrit an saed thairs a weefla here wi five barley bannocks an twa wee fish but hoo faur wud the gang amang that crood jesus saed gar tha fowk tae sut doon thair wus onie amoont o gress thonner an tha men sut doon aboot five thoosan o thaim an then jesus tuk tha bannocks gien thenks an the wur hannit roon bi his follaers tae thaim that wus sut on tha grun as much as the wantit he daen tha same wi tha fish whaniver the aa haed et thair fill he toul his follaers gether up aa tha leftowers an mine ye dinnae waste ocht sae efter iveriebodie haed et the gethert tha leains o tha five barley bannocks an fillt twal creels wi thaim an whaniver tha fowk saa tha wunner jesus wrocht the saed thairs nae doot this maun be thon proaphit the saed wud cum intae tha warl jesus knowed that the wur ettlin tae mak him king agin his wull sae he went aff on his lane tae tha muntin agane bi noo it wus dailygan an his follaers went doon tae tha loch whar the got intae a boat an set aff ower tha loch heidin fer capernaum it wus dairk got an jesus haednae turnt up yit a fierce wun wus blaain an tha watters wus reuch gettin efter the haed bin rowin thrie or fower mile the saa jesus cumin up tae tha boat waakin on tha watter an the wur wile feart but he saed til thaim its masel dinnae be feart an sae the wur gled tae tak him aboord tha boat an richt awa tha boat landit on tha shore whar the wur heidin tae tha nixt day tha fowk that haed stapt on tha ither shore o tha loch mindit that thair haed jist bin tha yin boat thonner an jesus haednae got in it alang wi his follaers but that the haed set aff on thair lane but then some boats frae tiberias landit near tae whar tha fowk et tha breid efter tha loard haed gien thenks sae tha minit tha fowk twigged that jesus an his follaers wurnae aboot the got intae tha boats an went tae capernaum tae luk fer jesus whaniver the fun him on tha ither side o tha loch the axt him rabbi whan did ye get here jesus answert am tellin yis tha truith yis ir no lukkin fer me acause ye saa wunners its becas yis et yer fill o tha loafs dinnae wark fer mait that gaes aff na wark fer mait that keeps tae ayelastin life that tha sinn o man wull gie tae ye fer god tha faither haes put tha keelmairk o his bakkin on tha sinn sae the axt him but whut maun we dae if wer tae dae tha wark that god wud hae iz dae jesus answert heres whut tha wark o god is that yis pit yer belief in tha yin he haes sent an sae the axt him whut sign cud ye gie iz sae that we micht see fer oorsels an believe ye whut ir ye fer daein oor forefaithers et tha manna in tha wulderness jist laik its writ doon in tha scriptures he gien thaim breid frae heiven fer tae ait then jesus saed tae thaim am tellin yis tha truith its no moses that gien ye tha breid frae heiven it cum frae ma faither an noo ma faither is giein ye tha true breid frae heiven fer tha breid o god is him that cums doon frae heiven an gies life tae tha warl loard the saed frae noo on thons tha breid we want an jesus saed tae thaim a am tha breid o life him that cums tae me wull niver get hungrie an him that believes in me wull niver hae a druith agane but laik a telt ye tha mair ye hae saen me yis dinnae believe aa that tha faither gies me wull cum tae me an oniebodie that cums tae me all niver turn thaim awa fer am no cum frae heiven tae dae ma ain wull but tae dae tha wull o him that sent me an this is tha wull o him that sent me that oot o aa he haes gien me thairll be nane ava loast but all rise thaim aa up on tha last day fer its ma faithers wull that oniebodie that luks tae tha sinn an pits his trust in him wull hae ayelastin life an a wull rise him up on tha last day wi that tha jews stairtit grummlin aboot him acause he saed a be tha breid that cum doon frae heiven the saed is thon no jesus him thats tha sinn o joseph shair we ken his faither an mither hoo cum hes noo sayin a cum doon frae heiven wud ye quit grummlin amang yersels jesus toul thaim naebodie can cum tae me less tha faither that sent me draas him an a wull rise him up on tha last day it is writ in tha proaphits thell aa be lairnt bi god iveriebodie that taks heed o tha faither an lairns frae him wull cum tae me naebodie haes iver saen tha faither apairt frae tha yin thats alang wi god its jist him haes saen tha faither am tellin ye tha truith thaim at believes haes ayelastin life a be tha breid o life yer forefaithers et tha manna in tha wulderness yit fer aa that the deed but this here breid that cums doon frae heiven a man can ait it an no dee a be tha leevin breid that cums doon frae heiven if oniebodie aits this breid he wull leeve fer aye this breid is ma flesh that a wull gie fer tha life o tha warl wi that tha jews stairtit an argyin match amang thairsels sayin hoo cud yer man gie iz his flesh tae ait but jesus toul thaim am tellin ye tha truith less ye ait tha flesh o tha sinn o man an drink his bluid yell hae nae life in ye whaiver aits ma flesh an drinks ma bluid haes ayelastin life an a wull rise him up on tha last day fer ma flesh is tha rael mait an ma bluid is tha rael drink whaiver aits ma flesh an drinks ma bluid bides in me an me in him jist as tha leevin faither sent me an a leeve acause o tha faither sae tha yin that feeds on me wull leeve acause o me this is tha breid that cum doon frae heiven yer forefaithers et manna an the deed but this breids no laik that him that feeds on this here breid wull leeve fer aye jesus toul thaim aa this whaniver he wus lairnin fowks in tha meetin hoose in capernaum monie o his follaers whan the heerd aa this the saed thons haird tae stomach wha cud tak it in jesus knowed in hissel that his follaers wus grummlin aboot it an he axt thaim is yer faith shuk bi this whut if ye saa tha sinn o man gang up tae whar he wus afore its tha spirit gies life tha flesh coonts fer naethin ava tha wurds a hae spauk til yis ir spirit an ther life as weel yit thairs yins amang ye that dinnae believe fer jesus knowed richt frae tha stairt whut yins o thaim wudnae believe an wha it wus that wud bethray him he went on tae say thats why a toul ye that naebodie can cum tae me less ma faither alloos it noo ower tha heid o aa this monie o his follaers turnt thair baks on him an haed naethin mair tae dae wi him yous wudnae be fer leain me tae wud ye jesus axt tha twal simon peter cum bak wi loard wha else wud we gang til its yersel haes tha wurds o ayelastin life we houl an we ken fine weel that you ir tha halie yin o god an jesus reponed did a no pick tha twal o ye but fer aa that yin o yis is a deil he wus taakin aboot judas tha sinn o simon iscariot that wus aboot tae bethray him tha mair he wus yin o tha twal efter aa this jesus trevelt roon aboot galilee an he kep hissel weel oot o judea fer tha jews thonner wur lukkin tae dae awa wi him but whaniver tha jews faist o shilters cum near jesuss brithers toul him ye shud lea here an gang tae judea sae as yer follaers can aa see tha guid warks yer daein naebodie thats lukkin tae get tae tha tap iver daes things in hidlins seein as yer aye daein these things dae thaim oot in tha apen afore tha fowk fer no een his ain brithers believed in him jesus saed bak tae thaim na fer masel tha richt time is no here yit but onie time fer yous wud dae tha warl haes nae cal tae hait yous it haits me but fer a stan wutness that tha warl daes nocht but ill awa on up yersels tae tha faist am no fer gaun up jist noo fer its no tha richt time yit fer masel whan he toul thaim that he stapt in galilee hooaniver efter his brithers haed gan up tae tha faist he went up on his lane on tha quait an no in tha apen noo at tha faist tha jews wur lukkin oot fer him an axin whars thon man thair wus a wile lock o whusperin amang tha thrang aboot him some saed thons yin guid man na saed ithers hes pittin fowk tha wrang road but fer fear o tha jews naebodie wud say ocht aboot him oot in tha apen whan tha faist wus half ower jesus gaed up tae tha coortyaird o tha hoose o god an he stairtit lairnin tha fowks tha jews wur stoondit an axt whar did yer man git sitch lairnin an him wi nae schuilin ava jesus toul thaim ma taichin is no ma ain it cums frae him that sent me if oniebodie haes a mine tae dae tha wull o god hell fin oot if ma taichin cums frae god or whuther its jist ma ain him that gies oot his ain thochts daes it fer his ain glorie but him that daes it fer tha glorie o tha yin that sent him hes a man o truith thairs nae lees aboot him ava did moses no gie ye tha laa yit thairs no yin o yis keeps tha laa whut ir ye wantin tae kill me fer ye hae a divil in ye tha thrang answert whas oot tae kill ye jesus toul thaim a daen tha yin miracle an yis ir aa dumfoonert yit moses gien ye tha laa o circumcision tha mair in fect it didnae cum frae moses ava but frae tha patriarchs afore him an acause o that yousll circumcise weans on tha sabbath day noo if yell circumcise a wean on tha sabbath day sae as tha laa o moses wull no git brauk hoo cum yisr angrie wi me fer makkin a hale man weel on tha sabbath day quit yer judgin bi tha luk o things but judge tha richt wye richt then some o tha fowk frae jerusalem begun axin yin anither is this no tha man ther lukkin tae kill luk here he is taakin oot in tha apen an ther no sayin yin wurd tae him it cudnae be that oor heidyins haes cum roon tae thinkin hes tha christ cud it but shair we ken whar this man cums frae yit whan tha christ cums naebodie wull ken whar he cums frae an sae whaniver jesus wus taichin in tha temple coorts he caad oot ay ye think ye ken me an ye think ye ken whar a cum frae but am no here on ma ain accoont him that sent me is true him yis dinnae ken but a ken him fer a cum frae him an its him that sent me efter that the haed a mine tae grup jesus but niver tha yin layed a han on him fer his oor haednae cum yit wi aa that monie o tha fowk put thair faith in him an the saed whaniver messiah cums dae ye think he wud dae onie mair miraclis signs ner this man tha pharisees heerd tha whuspers gaun roon tha crood aboot him an sae tha heid preeshts an tha pharisees sent sodgers o tha temple gaird tae tak him in jesus toul thaim am wi ye fer a wee while langer jist an then am gaun tae tha yin that sent me yell luk fer me but yell no fin me an whar a be ye cannae cum tha jews saed tae yin anither whars this man fer gaun that well niver fin him wull he gang whar oor fowks is leevin skailt amang tha greeks an taich tha greeks whut wus he taakin aboot whan he saed yell luk fer me but yell no fin me an whar a be ye cannae cum on tha last day tha big day o tha faist jesus stud up an caad oot lood if oniebodie haes a druith on thaim cum tae me an tak a drink oniebodie that lippens on me jist as scripture haes saed leevin watters wull rin oot frae his hairt he wus taakin here aboot tha spirit that his follaers wud be gien later on up tae noo tha spirit wusnae gien fer jesus haednae cum intae his glorie yit whaniver the heerd his wurds some o tha fowk saed this man fer shair maun be tha proaphit ithers saed this man is tha christ but ither yins axt hoo cud tha christ cum frae galilee dae tha scriptures no say that christ wull cum frae tha femlie o davit an fae tha toon o bethlehem whar davit leeved an sae tha fowk wus divid aboot him some wur lukkin tae lay houl o him but naebodie layed a fingr on him sae efter aa that tha sodgers o tha temple gaird went bak tae tha heid preeshts an pharisees an the wur axt hoo cum yis niver brocht him in naebodie iver taakt tha wye thon man daes tha sodgers toul thaim yer no tellin iz he haes tuk yous in anaa tha pharisees speered daes onie o iz heidyins or pharisees houl wi him na nane but thon getherup that kens naethin o tha laa an the ir damned oniehoo noo nicodemus yin o tha pharisees him that cum tae jesus afore axt thaim daes oor laa fin a bodie guiltie wioot giein him a hearin furst fer tae fin oot whut hes daen the cum bak an saed ir you frae galilee anaa luk intae it an yell fin that nae proaphit cums oot o galilee sae the aa went bak hame tae thair ain hoose hooaniver jesus gaed up tae tha moont o olives at furst licht he turnt up yinst mair in tha temple coorts whar aa tha fowk gethert roon him an he sut doon an begun lairnin thaim tha maisters o tha laa an tha pharisees brocht in a wumman catched in adulterie the gart hir tae stan in tha middle o tha getherin an the saed tae jesus taicher the catched this wumman here in tha verie ect o adulterie noo in oor laa moses bid iz tae stane sitch weemen tae deith whut dae you say but the wur quizzin him fer tae ketch him oot tae get tha gruns fer a chairge agin him but jesus stoopit doon an he stairtit tae scrieve in tha stour wi his fingr whan the kep on at him he stud up strecht an toul thaim whaiver yin o yis haes niver sinned weel let him clod tha furst stane at hir yinst mair he stoopt doon an scrievit in tha stour o tha grun whaniver the heerd this convictit in thair hairts the stairtit tae slip awa yin bi yin tha oul yins furst an tha ithers efter thaim jesus wus left on his lane wi tha wumman stannin afore him he stud up an seein naebodie bar tha wumman he saed tae hir sae whar ir the aa haes nane o thaim condemned ye naebodie loard qo she weel nether dae a condemn ye saed jesus awa ye gang an sin nae mair whaniver jesus taakt agane wi tha fowk he toul thaim a be tha licht o tha warl whaiver follaes me wull no waak in tha dairk onie mair but the wull hae tha licht o life tha pharisees saed til him thair ye ir agane pittin yersel forrit as yer ain wutness that kine o testimonie daesnae coont fer ocht but jesus cum bak wi this tha mair a gie ma ain testimonie ma testimonie stans fer a ken whar a cum frae an whar am gaun but yous hae nae notion o whar a hae cum frae or whar am gaun you mak yer ain judgemens accoardin tae tha wye man daes but a mak nae judgemens on naebodie but if a did judge ye wud fin ma judgemens wud be richt its no me ectin on ma lane fer tha faither that sent me stans alang wi me shair it says in yer ain laa that twa mens wurd is tuk as tha truith a be tha yin that wutnesses fer masel ma ither wutness is tha faither that sent me an sae the axt him whars yer faither at ye nether know me ner ma faither qo jesus if ye knowed me ye wud know ma faither forbye he telt thaim aa this whaniver he wus lairnin fowks in tha temple yaird nearhan tha kist fer tha offerins aa tha same naebodie layed a fingr on him fer his time wusnae cum yit an jesus went on tae tell thaim luk see am gaun aff yell luk fer me an yell dee in yer sin whar am gaun yis cannae cum tha jews saed amang thairsels is he gaun tae dae hissel in cud that be fer why hes sayin whar am gaun yis cannae cum but he toul thaim mair yous ir frae doon unner a be frae abain yous ir o this warl a dinnae belang tae this warl a toul ye that yis wud dee in yer sins fer less ye lippen that a be tha yin that a say that a am yisll dee in yer sins fer shair wha ir ye then the axt jist whut a hae bin tellin yis al alang jesus reponed a hae monies a thing a cud say aboot yis an tae condemn yis wi all no say it but him that sent me is siccar an its whut a hae heerd frae him that a tell tha warl still an aa the didnae unnerstan that he wus taakin aboot his faither sae jesus saed whan ye hae liftit up tha sinn o man then ye wull ken that a am tha yin a saed a wus an that a dae naethin ava on ma ain but gie wurd o whut tha faither haes tocht me an tha yin that sent me is wi me he haesnae left me on ma lane fer a aye dae whut plaises him an aa tha while jesus wus taakin monie fowk lippened on him tae tha jews at haed lippened on him jesus saed if yis houl tae whut a hae tocht ye yer ma follaers aa richt yis wull ken tha truith an tha truith wull mak ye free an the cum bak wi this luk we ir tha childer o abraham an we wur niver slaves tae naebodie sae hoo can ye say that we wull be let lowse jesus gie thaim this answer noo heres tha truith o it iveriebodie that daes wrang is a slave tae wrang sin is his maister noo a slave haes nae richt tae be a pairt o tha femlie fer iver but a sinn belangs tae tha femlie fer iver an aye sae if tha sinn maks ye free then yell be free fer shair a ken yis ir tha childer o abraham but yis ir lukkin tae kill me fer yis hae nae ruim in yer hairts fer whut a hae tae say am tellin ye whut a saa whan a wus alang wi ma faither but yous follae tha biddin o your faither abraham is oor faither the answert gin you wur tha childer o abraham qo jesus then ye wud dae whut abraham daen an yit naethinll dae yis but seein me killt me that haes toul ye tha truith a heerd frae god abraham niver wud a daen that yous jist dae whut yer ain faither daes nane o iz wus boarn ootbye a laafu femlie the answert bak we hae tha yin faither an thats god hissel jesus telt thaim if god wus yer faither ye wud love me fer a cum frae god an noo here a be am no cum on ma ain accoont it wus him that sent me hoo cum yis cannae tak in whut am tellin ye all tell ye fer why its acause yer no wullin tae listen ye belang tae your faither tha deil an yer wantin tae dae whuts in yer faithers hairt he wus a murderer richt frae tha stairt nae freen o tha truith fer thairs nae truith in him whan he tells lees he taaks his ain leid fer hes a doonricht liar ay tha faither o lees yit whaniver its me tellin ye tha truith ye dinnae believe me is thair yin amang ye can gie onie pruif am guiltie o sin an if am tellin ye tha truith hoo cum ye dinnae lippen whut a say him that belangs tae god taks tent tae whut god says tha raison yous dinnae listen is that yis dinnae belang tae god tha jews axt him ir we no richt in sayin yer a samaritan wi a divil in ye thairs nae divil in me qo jesus but a hae regaird fer ma faither an yous hae nae regaird fer me am no efter glorie fer masel but thair is yin that is lukkin it for me an he is tha yin tae judge heres tha truith o it if oniebodie houls tae ma wurd he wull niver dee wi that tha jews caad oot noo we ken fer shair that thairs a divil in ye abraham deed an tha proaphits deed as weel yit your tellin iz that if oniebodie houls tae yer wurd hell niver dee wud you be a bigger man ner oor faither abraham he deed an sae did tha proaphits wha dae you think you ir jesus reponed if a gie masel tha glorie thon glorie mains naethin ma faither that yous mak oot is your god hes tha yin at gies me tha glorie tha mair yous dinnae ken him a ken him weel if a saed a didnae that wud mak me a liar laik yous but a dae ken him an a houl tae his wurd yer faither abraham wus fu o joy at tha thocht o seein ma day cum he saa it an wus hairt gled ketch yersel on yer no fiftie yit tha jews saed tae him an yer tellin iz ye hae saa abraham am tellin ye tha truith answert jesus afore iver abraham wus boarn a be whaniver the heerd that the tuk up stanes fer tae pelt him but jesus jookt oot o sicht an left tha temple gruns yin day jesus wus waakin alang an he cum on this man blin frae tha day he wus boarn his follaers axt him rabbi wha wus it daen wrang that this here man wus boarn blin wus it hissel or wus it his mither an faither nether this man ner his mither ner his faither haes sinned he answert but it cum aboot sae that tha warks o god micht be showed in his life whan its daylicht we maun dae tha wark o him that sent me nicht is cumin whan naebodie can wark aa tha while am in tha warl a be tha licht o tha warl wi that he sput on tha grun an made some glar wi his spittle an put it on tha mans een awa he telt him an waash in tha puil o siloam siloam haes tha mainin o sent sae tha man went aff an waasht an cum bak able tae see his nighbers an thaim that knowed him as a blin beggarman axt wud this no be tha same man that uist tae sit an beg some ledged that he wus ithers saed na he jist favours him but tha man kep on tellin thaim aa its me richt eneuch sae whut wye did ye git yer een apent the axt him he reponed tha man the caa jesus made some glar an put it on ma een he toul me tae gang til tha puil o siloam an waash sae aff a went an waasht an efter that a cud see whars thon man at noo the axt him a dinnae ken qo he the brocht tha man that uist tae be blin up afore tha pharisees noo it wus a sabbath day that jesus made tha mud an apent tha mans een sae tha pharisees they quizzed him as weel aboot hoo he haed got his sicht he put glar on ma een tha man answert an a waasht an noo a can see a nummer o tha pharisees saed this man isnae frae god fer he daesnae keep tha sabbath but ithers axt hoo cud a sinner dae aa thaim miracles an the wur divid ower tha heid o it sae the turnt agane an axt tha blin man an whut dae you say aboot him fer it wus your een he apent tha man reponed he is a proaphit tha jews still didnae believe that he wus iver blin no tae the sent fer tha mans mither an faither is this yer sinn the axt thaim wud it be him yer tellin iz wus boarn blin hoo cum he can see noo we know fine weel this is oor sinn tha mither an faither reponed an we ken he wus boarn blin but hoo its cum aboot that he can see noo or wha apent his een we cannae tell ye ax him yersels hes oul eneuch tae taak fer hissel his mither an faither wus taakin that wye fer fear o tha jews fer tha jews haed thair mines made up tae pit iveriebodie oot o tha meetin hoose that allooed jesus wus tha christ thats tha raison his mither an faither saed hes oul eneuch ax him yersels then tha man at wus blin wus brocht up afore thaim a saicont time gods yer wutness sae taak tha truith noo the saed we ken this man jesus is a sinner a cudnae say qo he whuther hes a sinner or no yin thing a dae ken but yinst a wus blin an noo a can see but the kep on at him whut did he dae tae ye hoo did he apen yer een he reponed a toul ye afore an ye wudnae listen whut dae ye want tae hear it agane fer dae yous want tae stairt follaein him anaa the yaukt him an saed you ir a follaer o thon fella but we ir follaers o moses here we ken that god spauk wi moses but we dinnae even ken whar this fella cums frae tha man answert weel that bates aa ye dinnae ken whar he cums frae yit he apent ma een we ken that god daesnae listen tae sinners but he wull listen tae yin thats godfearin an daes his wull frae tha warl begun ye niver heerd tell o summodie apenin tha een o a man boarn blin did ye if this man wusnae frae god he cudnae a daen ocht ava the cum bak at him you wur boarn steepit in sin an noo ye wud dar tae taich iz an the throwed him oot jesus heerd wurd the haed throwed him oot an whaniver he fun him he axt him dae ye believe in tha sinn o man wha is he sir tha man axt tell iz sae a can believe in him ye hae saen him saed jesus in fect yer lukkin at him its him thats taakin tae ye then tha man saed loard a believe an he wurshipt him jesus saed its fer judgemen am cum intae this warl thaim that ir blin all mak tae see an thaim that can see all show thaim that the ir blin but some pharisees that wur nearhan heerd him say this an the axt whut ir ye sayin wer blin anaa jesus telt thaim weel if yis wur blin ye wudnae be guiltie o sin but noo yis mak oot ye can see yer guilt bides on ye noo heres tha truith o it qo jesus tha man that daesnae cum intae tha ree bi tha yett tae get amang tha sheep but spiels in bi some ither road ye can be shair hes a thief or a reiver tha man that cums in bi tha yett is tha hird o tha sheep tha herdhan apens tha yett fer him an tha sheep hear tha shepherds voice he caas his sheep bi name an leads thaim oot efter him whaniver he haes brocht oot aa his ain sheep he waaks aheid o thaim an his sheep follae him fer the ken his voice thell no follae a stranger but na thell rin aff whan the hear a voice the dinnae ken jesus gien thaim this picter tae pit ower his mainin but the didnae unnerstan whut he wus taakin aboot sae jesus toul thaim yinst mair heres tha truith o it a be tha yett fer tha sheep aa thaim that cum afore me wus thiefs an reivers but tha sheep tuk nae heed o thaim a be tha yett him that cums in throu me wull be saved he wull gang in an oot an fin guid gress tha thief jist cums fer tae wreck an rob an kill a hae cum that the micht hae life an hae it ower an abain a be tha guid shepherd tha guid shepherd gies his ain life fer tha sheep tha hired han is no tha shepherd an he daesnae own tha sheep ether sae whan he sees a wolf cumin he rins aff an leas thaim an then tha wolf lays hoult o tha flock an skails it tha man rins awa fer he is a hired han an he cares naethin fer tha sheep a be tha guid shepherd a ken ma sheep an ma sheep ken me jist laik tha faither kens me an a ken tha faither an a gie ma ain life fer tha sheep a hae ither sheep that daesnae belang tae this ree a maun bring thaim forbye thell tak heed o ma voice anaa an thair wull be yin hirsle an yin shepherd tha raison ma faither loves me is this a gie up ma ain life jist fer tae tak it bak agane naebodie taks it frae me but a gie it up o ma ain wull a hae tha thortie tae gie it up an a hae tha thortie tae tak it bak agane this is tha chairge a hae got frae ma faither becas o whut he saed tha jews wur at odds wi yin anither yit agane monie o thaim saed hes bin tuk ower wi a divil an hes haiverin whut wud ye listen tae him fer but ithers saed thons no tha wurds o a man taen ower wi a divil cud a divil apen tha een o tha blin roon cum tha faist o dedication it wus wuntertim an jesus wus in tha temple gruns waakin alang unner solomons airches tha jews gethert roon jesus quizzin him hoo lang wull ye keep iz wunnerin wer deein tae fin oot if yer tha christ tell iz strecht jesus reponed a hae aareadie toul ye but yis dinnae believe me tha warks a dae in ma faithers name baks me up but tha raison yis dinnae believe me is that yer no ma sheep ma sheep hears ma caa a ken thaim an the follae me a gie thaim ayelastin life an the wull niver perish naebodie can wheek thaim oot o ma han ma faither that gien thaim tae me is ower ocht naebodie can wheek thaim oot o ma faithers han me an tha faither is yin yinst mair tha jews gethert stanes fer tae clod him but jesus toul thaim a hae showed ye onie amoont o guid warks wrocht bi tha faither whut yin o thaim ir ye stanein me fer wer no stanein ye fer ocht o thaim tha jews reponed but fer blesphemie you ir jist an ordinarie man an yit ye mak yersel oot tae be god jesus answert thaim is it no writ in yer ain laa a hae toul ye yis ir gods noo if he caad thaimins that tha wurd o god cum tae gods an mine you tha scriptures stan fer iver an aye whut aboot tha yin that tha faither set apairt as his verie ain an sent intae tha warl a saed a be gods sinn an fer that yis chairge me wi blesphemie if am no daein tha things ma faither daes then dinnae believe me but if a dae thaim tha mair ye dinnae believe whut a tell ye jist believe whut tha warks thairsels tells ye that wye yisll unnerstan fer shair that tha faither is in me an me in tha faither agane the tried tae lay houl o him but he gien thaim tha slip efter that jesus gaed bak ower tha joardan tae tha place whar jhone baptised at tha furst he stapt thonner a wee while an monie fowk cum tae him the saed fer aa that jhone niver daen onie miraclis signs iveriethin jhone saed aboot this man wus tha truith an in thon place monie fowk put thair faith in jesus thair wus this man the caad lazarus an he wusnae verie weel he wus frae bethanie a wee toon whar his sisters mary an mairtha leeved noo this wus tha same mary that poored scent on tha loard an gien his feet a dicht wi hir hair it wus hir brither that wus no weel sae tha twa sisters sent wurd tae jesus sayin loard tha yin ye love is seeck whaniver jesus heerd tell o it he saed this ailment wull no enn up wi him deein na its fer tha glorie o god an fer tha sinn o god tae get tha glorie oot o it mairtha an hir sister an lazarus wus aa loved bi jesus sae tha mair he heerd lazarus wusnae weel he stapt fer twa mair days whar he wus at then efter this he toul his follaers cum on an well gang bak tae judea but rabbi the saed a wee while bak thaim jews wus gaun tae stane ye an noo yer fer gaun bak thonner jesus saed is thair no twal oors o daylicht iverie day if ye waak in tha braid daylicht yell no thrip an faa fer ye can see bi tha licht o this warl its whan yer waakin bi nicht that ye thrip up fer ye hinnae tha licht in ye efter he saed this he went on oor freen lazarus is jist sleepin but am awa fer tae waaken him up his follaers reponed weel loard if hes jist haein a sleep hell shuin be on tha men his follaers thocht he wus taakin aboot ordinarie sleep but jesus wus mainin lazarus wus deid sae then he toul thaim strecht lazarus is deid an fer your sake am gled a wusnae thair sae that you micht believe cum on noo an well gang til him then tammas caad didymus saed tae tha ither follaers cum on an well gang tae sae that we can dee alang wi him whaniver jesus got nixt bethanie he fun that lazarus haed bin fower days deid an in tha tomb bethanie wus nearhan jerusalem aboot twa mile doon tha road an a hale lock o jews haed cum tae mairtha an mary fer tae stan bye thaim in tha loass o thair brither whan mairtha got wurd that jesus wus cumin oot she went tae meet him but mary sut in tha hoose loard mairtha saed tae jesus if you haed hae bin here ma brither wudnae be deid but a ken that even noo god wull gie ye whutiver ye ax him jesus saed til hir yer brither wull rise agane mairtha answert a ken he wull rise agane in tha resurrection on tha hinmaist day jesus telt hir a be tha resurrection an tha life him that believes in me tha mair he dees yit hell leeve agane an whaiver leeves an believes in me wull niver dee dae ye believe this ay loard a dae qo she a believe that you ir tha christ tha sinn o god tha yin we wur toul wus cumin intae tha warl an efter she saed that awa she went bak hame an tuk hir sister mary tae tha yin side tha maister is here qo she an he wants ye tae cum whaniver mary heerd that up she got in a hurrie an gaed til him noo jesus haednae yit got tha lenth o tha village but wus still bak at tha spot whar mairtha haed met up wi him tha jews that wus thair in tha hoose tae offer mary sorra fer hir trouble whaniver the saa tha quick she got up an went oot up they got as weel an went oot efter hir jalousin she wus awa tae tha tomb tae greet thonner sae mary got tae whar jesus wus at an whaniver she saa him she faad doon at his feet an she saed loard if you haed hae bin here ma brither wudnae be deid whan jesus saa hir greetin an aa tha jews that wur cum alang wi hir greetin forbye he wus vext in his spirit an he wus hairt sair whar hae yis put him saed he cum an see loard the toul him wi that jesus begun tae greet tha jews saed see tha much he loved him but some o thaim saed if he cud apen tha een o thon blin man cud he no hae kep this man frae deein jesus cum tae tha tomb an his hairt wus troublet agane it wus a cave wi a stane put ower its mooth tak tha stane awa qo he but loard saed mairtha tha deid mans sister bi noo it wud stink ye oot fer hes in thair this fower days wi that jesus saed did a no tell ye that if ye believed ye wud see tha glorie o god sae the shiftit tha stane an jesus lukt up tae heiven abain an he saed faither a gie ye thenks that ye hae heerd me ye hear me ayewyes a know that but a hae saed aa this fer tha guid o tha fowk stud here sae the micht believe that you sent me whaniver he saed that jesus caad oot at tha tap o his voice lazarus cum on oot an lo an behoul tha deid man did cum oot his hans an feet lapt wi strips o linen an a cloot roon his face jesus toul thaim tak tha grave claes aff him an let him gang wi that monie o tha jews that wur cum tae be at tha wake wi mary whaniver the saa whut jesus did the put thair faith in him but ithers amang thaim went an toul tha pharisees whut jesus haed daen an sae tha heid preeshts an tha pharisees caad tha cooncil thegither is this no a hanlin whutll we dae the axt fer thon mans daein a hale wheen o miraclis signs if we let him aff wi it tha nixt thing thell aa believe on him an then tha romansll cum an dae awa wi baith oor halie place an oor kintrie on iz an then yin o thaim bi tha name o caiaphas that wus heich preesht thon yeir spauk oot yis ken naethin ava ye dinnae unnerstan that it wud be fer tha best if yin man deed fer aa tha fowk ay faur better ner fer tha hale kintrie tae be wiped oot he didnae say this o his ain accoard but as heich preesht thon yeir he foretelt that jesus wud dee fer tha hale nation an no jist fer thon nation but fer aa tha skailt childer o god tae bring thaim thegither an mak thaim yin sae frae that day an oor the collogued thegither tae dae him in an efter that jesus wudnae cum oot in tha apen onie mair amang tha jews rether he tuk hissel aff tae a pairt o tha kintrie nearhan tha wulderness tae a toon bi tha name o ephraim an he stapt ower thair wi his follaers whaniver it wus near time fer tha passower faist monie fowk frae tha kintrie went up tae jerusalem fer tae get thair ritual waash afore tha passower the kep lukkin fer jesus an as the stud roon in tha temple gruns the axt yin anither dae ye think is he fer cumin tae tha faist ava but tha heid preeshts an pharisees haed gien oarders that if oniebodie fun oot tha wharaboots o jesus the maun let thaim know sae as the cud hae him liftit six day afore tha passower jesus cum tae bethanie whar lazarus leeved him jesus haed ris frae tha deid the wur houlin a denner thonner fer jesus mairtha wus sarvin at it an lazarus wus yin o thaim roon tha boord wi jesus weel mary tuk aboot a pint o pure nard a scentit oyle that coast big money an she poored it ower jesuss feet an gien thaim a dicht wi hir hair an tha hoose wus fu o tha sweet scent o tha oyle but yin o his follaers judas iscariot him that wud bethray him later on he wus agin it hoo cum this oyle wusnae soul an tha catter gien tae tha puir itd tak ye a year tae wark fer that he didnae say that oot o peetie fer tha puir but becas he wus a thief he kep tha sillerpooch an he jist dippt intae it fer his ain use whan he wantit lea hir be jesus reponed she wus supposed tae keep this scent bak fer ma layin oot tae be buriet fer tha puir yell aye hae wi yis but yell no aye hae me bi noo a big thrang o jews haed gethert whaniver the fun oot that jesus wus thair the wurnae cum jist on accoont o jesus but wur lukkin a wee skellie o lazarus forbye him that jesus haed ris frae tha deid sae tha heid preeshts collogued thegither tae kill lazarus as weel fer it wus ower tha heid o him that monie o tha jews wur noo pittin thair faith in jesus tha nixt day a big thrang o fowk that haed cum fer tha passower heerd wurd that jesus wus makkin his road fer jerusalem an the tuk brenches o palmtrees an oot the went tae meet him cryin hosanna blisst be tha yin that cums in tha name o tha loard blisst be tha king o israel jesus fun a young cuddie an sut on its bak jist laik its writ doon dinnae be feart o dochter o zion luk see yer king is cumin sut on a young cuddie at tha stairt his follaers didnae unnerstan aa this it wusnae tae efter jesus cum intae his glorie that the twigged that thaim things wus writ aboot him an haed happent tae him noo tha crood that wus wi him whaniver he caad lazarus frae tha tomb an ris him frae tha deid wus taakin aboot it aa ower tha kintrie an that wus why sitch a crood o fowk went oot fer tae meet him acause thed heerd aboot tha miraclis sign hed daen sae tha pharisees collogued amang thairsels luk wer gettin naewhar wi this tha hale warls rinnin efter him noo thair wus some greeks amang tha fowk that haed cum up fer tha passower the made an approach tae philip wha cum frae bethsaida in galilee sir the saed wer lukkin tae hae a wurd wi jesus aff philip went an toul andra an then andra an philip thegither telt jesus tha answer jesus gien wus this noos tha time fer tha sinn o man tae cum intae his glorie heres tha truith o it less an ear o seedcoarn draps doon intae tha grun an dees it jist stays on its lane but if it dees it maks a hale lock o seeds him thats ower fand o his ain life wull loass it but him at haes nae gra fer leevin in this warl wull keep his life fer iver an aye oniebodie that wants me as thair maister maun follae me an whar am at yell fin ma sarvint thonner forbye ma faither wull gie honour tae him that sarves me an noo ma hairt is sair annoyt whut am a tae say faither save me frae this oor na fer it wus fer this verie raison that am cum tae this oor faither glorie be tae yer name an wi that a voice cum frae heiven an it saed a hae gien it tha glorie an all gie it tha glorie agane whaniver tha crood thonner heerd it the thocht it wus a rummle o thunner but ithers saed it wus an angel taakin wi him jesus saed thon voice wus fer your guid no fer mine noo is tha time o judgemen fer this warl noo tha prince o this warl wull be driv oot but whaniver am liftit up frae tha irth a wull draa iveriebodie tae masel he saed this tae pit it oot in tha apen whut wye he wus gaun tae dee tha crood saed oor laa tells iz that tha christ wull bide fer iver sae hoo cum ye can say tha sinn o man maun be liftit up this sinn o man wha wud he be oniehoo wi that jesus toul thaim yis wull hae tha licht jist a wee while langr waak in tha licht whaniver ye hae it afore tha mirk cums doon on ye thaim that waak in tha mirk dinnae ken whar ther fer pit yer trust in tha licht as lang as ye hae it sae as ye can becum childer o tha licht whan jesus wus daen taakin he went awa an hud hissel frae thaim tha mair jesus wrocht aa thae miraclis signs afore thaim the still wudnae believe in him that wus tae bring aboot whut isaiah tha proaphit haed saed loard whar ir tha yins that hae tuk oor wurd tae hairt an wha ir tha yins that hae wutnesst your pooer but the wurnae able tae believe fer laik isaiah says in anither pairt he haes made thair een blin an turnt thair hairts tae stane sae the can see naethin wi thair een ner unnerstan ocht wi thair hairts ner turn fer me tae hail thaim isaiah wus taakin aboot jesus whaniver he saed this he lukt aheid an foresaa his glorie wi aa that thair wus monies a yin did believe in him even amang tha heidyins but the wudnae own up tae thair faith afore tha pharisees fer fear o bein put oot o tha meetin hoose fer the wur mair keen on bein weel thocht o bi men ner bi god then jesus caad oot whan a bodie haes belief in me he daesnae jist believe in me masel but in tha yin that sent me him that sees me sees tha yin that sent me am cum intae tha warl as a licht sae that naebodie that believes in me shud bide in tha dairk anent oniebodie that haes heerd ma wurds but daesnae houl tae thaim am no fer makkin judgemen on him fer a didnae cum intae tha warl tae judge it but tae save it thair is a judge fer tha yin that turns his bak on me an daesnae tak ma wurds tae hairt tha verie wurds a spauk wull judge him on tha day o reckonin fer a wusnae taakin on ma ain accoont but tha faither that sent me toul me whut tae say an hoo tae say it an a know richt weel that his commauns aye roads tae iverlastin life sae ocht a say is jist whut tha faither haes bid me say noo tha passower faist wus nearhan an jesus knowed that tha time wus cum fer him tae lea this warl an gang til tha faither haein loved his ain that wus in tha warl noo he apent up tae thaim tha fu meesure o his love supper wus gettin put oot an tha deil haed aareadie put tha thocht intae tha hairt o judas iscariot sinn o simon tae bethray jesus jesus knowed that tha faither haed gien aa things intae his pooer an that he wus cum frae god an wus fer gaun bak tae god sae up he got frae tha supper tuk aff his ooter claes an roon his middle he lapt a dryin cloot efter that he teemed watter intae a boul an stairtit tae waash tha feet o his follaers an gien thaim a dicht wi tha dryin cloot lapt roon aboot him he cum tae simon peter wha axt him loard you ir no fer waashin ma feet ir ye jesus answert ye dinnae get whut am daein jist noo but later on yell unnerstan na qo peter yell niver waash ma feet jesus toul him less a gie ye a waash yell hae nae pairt wi me weel loard simon peter reponed no jist ma feet then but ma hans an ma heid anaa jesus answert a bodie that haes waasht hissel aa ower jist needs tae dae his feet fer hes aareadie clain an you follaers ir clain sae ye ir but thairs yin amang ye that isnae fer he knowed wha wud bethray him an that wus fer why he saed that no iverie last yin o thaim wus clain whaniver he wus daen waashin thair feet he put his robe bak on an he tuk his place agane dae yis no ken whut a hae daen fer ye he axt thaim yis caa me taicher an loard an yer richt fer thats wha a am an noo that a masel yer loard an taicher hae waasht yer feet you shud waash yin anithers feet tae a daen it masel tae show yis tae dae whut a hae daen fer you heres tha truith o it nae sarvint is bigger ner his maister an him at brings a message isnae bigger ner tha yin that sent him noo that yis ken these things yell be blisst if ye dae thaim am no taakin aboot yis aa a ken thaimins a hae waaled but this is tae bring aboot whuts writ doon in tha halie scriptures him that shares ma breid wi me haes turnt agin me am tellin ye noo aforehan sae that whaniver it cums aboot yisll believe that a be tha messiah thairs no twa wyes aboot it whaiver walcums oniebodie a senn walcums me an whaiver walcums me walcums tha yin that sent me efter he saed that jesuss spirit wus gye vext then he stapt an cum oot wi this am tellin ye strecht yin o yis is fer bethrayin me his follaers jist gaukt at yin anither whutch yin o thaim wus he taakin aboot yin amang thaim tha follaer that jesus loved wus leant bak agin him simon peter catched thon follaers ee an he saed whas he taakin aboot sae leanin bak agin jesus that follaer speered loard wha is it jesus answert itll be tha yin a gie this bit o breid tae efter a hae dunkt it in tha boul an he dunkt tha bit o breid an gien it tae judas iscariot tha sinn o simon tha minit judas tuk tha breid tha deil wus in him whut yer fer daein jesus telt him dae it quick but naebodie at tha supper unnerstud tha raison jesus toul him that seein as judas lukt efter tha siller yins thocht jesus wus sennin him fer whutiver needit bocht fer tha faist or tae gie sumthin tae tha puir sae efter judas haed taen tha bit o breid awa he went an it wus tha blek o nicht whaniver judas went oot jesus saed tha sinn o manll noo cum intae his glorie an god wull get tha glorie acause o him an if god gets tha glorie on accoont o his sinn god wull gie glorie tae tha sinn forbye an hell dae it strecht awa ma dear childer a wull be wi yis jist a wee while langr yell be lukkin fer me an jist laik a toul tha jews sae am tellin yous noo whar am fer gaun yis cannae cum a hae a new commaun tae gie yis love yin anither jist as a hae loved you thats hoo ye maun love yin anither an if ye love yin anither tha hale warl wull see that yer ma follaers simon peter axt him loard whar ir ye aff tae jesus reponed whar am fer ye cannae follae me noo but later on yell follae me peter axt loard hoo cum a cannae follae ye noo shair a wud dee fer ye wi that jesus answert sae yed dee fer me wud ye heres tha truith o it afore tha rooster craas thrie times ower yell say ye dinnae ken me dinnae let yer hairts be sair annoyt pit yer trust in god an lippen in me forbye in ma faithers hoose thairs monie dwallinplaces if that wusnae richt a wudnae hae toul ye that am gaun tae mak a place readie fer ye wud a noo an whaniver a hae got a place readie fer ye all cum an tak yis bak alang wi me sae that whar a be well aa be thegither yis ken whar am gaun an yis ken tha road tae whar am gaun tammas turnt an saed til him loard we hae nae notion o whar yer fer sae hoo cud we ken tha road jesus reponed a be tha road an tha truith an tha life naebodie cums tae tha faither but throu me if ye knowed me weel ye wud ken ma faither as weel frae noo on yis dae ken him an yis hae saa him forbye philip saed loard show iz tha faither an thatll be eneuch fer iz jesus answert dae ye no ken me philip tha mair a hae bin amang yis aa this time oniebodie lukkin at me haes saen tha faither sae hoo can ye say show iz tha faither philip dae ye no believe that a be in tha faither an tha faithers in me tha wurds am taakin til yis ir no jist ma ain na its tha faither leevin in me whas daein his wark tak ma wurd fer it whaniver a say that a be in tha faither an tha faither is in me or at tha laist trust me acause o tha warks yis hae saen me daein noo heres tha truith o it oniebodie that pits thair faith in me wull dae tha same warks that a dae ay an hell dae faur bigger things ner thon fer am gaun tae be wi ma faither an all dae whutiver ye ax in ma name sae as tha sinn micht bring glorie til tha faither ye can ax me fer ocht in ma name an a wull dae it if ye love me ye wull dae whut a bid ye an a wull ax tha faither an he wull gie yis an indwallin guide tae be wi yis fer aye its tha spirit o truith am taakin aboot tha warl cannae tak him in fer it nether sees him ner kens him yous wull ken him but fer he leeves wi ye noo an hell dwall in ye later on all no lea yis laik orphan weans a wull cum tae ye afore lang tha warl wull no see me nae mair but yousll see me acause a leeve yousll leeve forbye cum thon day youll be shair that a be in ma faither an you ir in me an a am in you whaiver taks ma commauns tae hairt an keeps thaim thons tha yins that love me thaim that love me wull be loved bi ma faither an forbye a wull love thaim an show masel tae thaim wi that judas no judas iscariot but he speered but loard hoo cum yer ettlin tae show yersel jist tae iz an no tae tha hale warl jesus gien tha answer if oniebodie loves me he daes whut he haes lairnt frae me ma faither wull love him an we wull cum tae him an
