mak oor hame wi him him that daesnae love me wull no dae whut a hae toul him these wurds ye hear ir no ma ain the belang tae tha faither that sent me a hae toul yis thae things while am still here amang yis but tha indwallin guide tha halie spirit that tha faither wull senn tae tak ma place he wull lairn yis aa things an bring bak tae mine iveriethin a hae toul ye peace a lea wi ye ma peace a gie ye a dinnae gie ye ocht tha wye tha warl gies dinnae let yer hairts be annoyt an dinnae be afeart ye heerd me tellin ye am leain ye an am cumin bak til yis if ye loved me ye wud be gled that am fer gaun tae tha faither fer tha faither is mair bigger ner me a hae telt ye this noo afore it cums aboot sae as whaniver it happens ye wull believe am fer taakin tae ye nae mair ner a wee bit langr fer tha prince o this warl is cumin he haes nae pooer ower me but all dae whut aa ma faither bids me dae sae as tha warl micht lairn that a love tha faither weel cum on noo well be up an awa o a truith a be tha richt vine an ma faither is tha gairdner he haes iverie brench cut aff o me that haes gien nae fruit an iverie brench that daes gie fruit he faces bak a weethin sae that it fruits aa tha mair yous ir aareadie faced on accoont o tha wurd a hae spauk tae ye bide in me an a wull bide in you nae brench can gie fruit its lane it maun be growein oot o tha vine or it cannae leeve an nether can yous gie fruit less ye bide in me a be tha vine yous ir tha brenches if a man bides in me an me in him he wull gie fruit ower ocht apairt frae me ye can dae naethin ava if a bodie daesnae bide in me he is laik a brench that is redd oot an wuthers up an dees sitch brenches is gethert up an coupt intae tha fire an brunt if ye bide in me an ma wurds bide in you ax fer ocht ava ye want an it wull be gien til ye thats tae tha glorie o ma faither that yer brustin wi fruit showin yersels tae be ma follaers jist as tha faither haes loved me sae a hae loved you bide noo in ma love if yis dae ma biddin ye wull bide in ma love jist laik a masel hae daen ma faithers biddin an bide in his love a hae toul ye aa that sae as ma joy maun be in you ay an that yer joy maun be fu an skailin heres ma commaun love yin anither laik a hae loved yous thairs nae bodie haes mair love ner this that he wud dee fer his freens you ir ma freens if ye dae ma biddin nae mair dae a caa yis sarvints fer a sarvint daesnae ken ocht o whut his maisters at na a hae caad yous freens acause iveriethin a hae lairnt frae ma faither a hae taicht yous as weel you didnae waal me na fer a waaled you an appointit ye tae gang an bair fruit fruit that wull last fer aye an then tha faither wull gie ye ocht ye ax fer in ma name heres whut a bid ye love yin anither if tha warl haits ye hae mine that it haitit me furst if ye belanged tae tha warl it wud love ye as its ain aa tha same ye dinnae belang tae tha warl but a hae waaled ye oot o tha warl thons tha raison tha warl haits ye hae mine o tha wurds a telt ye nae sarvint is bigger ner his maister if the haed it in fer me thell hae it in fer you forbye if the daen ma biddin the wull dae yours as weel thell dail wi ye thon wye acause o ma name fer the dinnae ken tha yin that sent me if a haednae cum an taakt tae thaim the wudnae be guiltie o wrangdaein hooaniver the hae nae caa fer thair sin noo him that haits me haits ma faither forbye if a haednae daen wunnerfu warks amang thaim laik naebodie else daen the wudnae be guiltie o sin but the hae saa thaim an still an aa the hae haitit baith me an ma faither this is tae bring aboot whut is writ in thair laa the haitit me an the haed nae caa fer it but all be sennin yis tha indwallin guide frae tha faither tha spirit o truith hell gang oot frae tha faither an whaniver he cums he wull gie wutness aboot me an yous maun gie wutness forbye fer yous hae bin alang wi me richt frae tha verie stairt a telt ye aa this sae that yer faith wull no be shuk the wull pit ye oot o tha meetin hooses ay tha day is cumin whan oniebodie that kills ye wull think ther daein gods wark an the wull dae tha laik o thon becas the hinnae knowed tha faither ner me a hae telt ye this sae as whaniver tha time cums an the happen yell mine that a gien ye warnin a didnae tell ye at tha stairt fer a wus still wi ye noo am awa tae him that sent me an yit nane o yis haes axt me whar ir ye aff tae na but becas a hae toul yis these things yer hairts is fu o sorra but tae tell ye tha truith its fer yer ain guid that am gaun awa fer less a gang awa tha halie guide wull no cum til yis but if a gang a wull senn him tae ye whaniver he cums he wull show tha warl that its in tha wrang anent its sin anent bein richt an anent judgemen anent sin becas the dinnae believe in me anent bein richt becas am gaun tae tha faither whar yell no see me onie mair an anent judgemen acause tha prince o this warl noo stans condemned bi god a hae a hale lock mair tae tell ye mair ner yis cud thole jist noo but whaniver tha spirit o truith cums he wull guide yis intae aa tha truith hell no spake on his ain hell tell ye jist whut he hears an hell tell ye whut is yit tae cum aboot he wull bring glorie tae me bi takkin frae whut is mine an makkin it knowed til yis aa that belangs tae tha faither is mine noo thons tha raison a telt ye tha spirit is fer takkin frae whut is mine an wull mak it knowed til ye in a wee while yell no see me onie mair an then efter anither wee bit yis wull see me some o tha follaers saed tae yin anither whuts he taakin aboot in a wee while yell see me nae mair an then efter anither wee bit yis wull see me an fer am awa tae tha faither the kep rhymin whuts he taakin aboot a wee while we dinnae unnerstan whut hes on aboot jesus saa the wur lukkin tae ax him aboot it aa sae he saed tae thaim ir ye speerin yin anither aboot me sayin in a wee while yell see me nae mair an then efter anither wee bit yis wull see me weel heres tha truith o it you wull be greetin an murnin whan tha warl ootbye is blythesum youll be hairtsair but yer sorra wull turn intae joy a wumman haein a wean is wile sair fer hir time is cum but whaniver hir babbies boarn she haes nae mair mine o tha anguish acause o hir joy that a wean is boarn intae tha warl samewyes wi yous noos your time o sorra but a wull see yis agane an yer hairts wull be singin fer joy an naebodie wull tak yer joy awa frae ye cum that day an yisll no ax me ocht onie mair heres tha wye o it strecht ma faither wull gie ye oniethin ye ax fer in ma name up tae noo yis hinnae axt fer ocht in ma name ax an yell hae it gien an yer hairts wull be fu o joy ma wye o yarnin wi ye aboot these things haes bin tae halp ye picter it aa tha day is cumin that all no taak in picters onie langr but all tell ye strecht aboot ma faither cum that day yisll ax in ma name noo am no sayin a wull then ax tha faither for ye na tha faither hissel loves ye acause yis hae loved me an hae believed that a cum frae god ay a hae cum frae tha faither intae tha warl noo am leain tha warl an gaun bak tae tha faither wi that jesuss follaers saed noo yer taakin plain taak wioot yarns an picters noo we unnerstan that you ken iveriethin an that ye hae nae need o fowk quizzin ye frae this we believe that ye hae cum frae god at lang last yis believe jesus answert but tha day wull cum an in fect its here noo whaniver yell be skailt iverie yin o yis tae yer ain hame yisll lea me aa on ma ain yit am no ma lane fer ma faither is wi me a telt ye aa thon sae that in me yis can hae peace in this warl ye wull hae nae enn o bother but dinnae be doonhairtit got cheer up a hae tha warl owercum efter these wurds jesus lukt up abain tae heiven faither he saed tha time is cum gie glorie tae yer sinn sae as yer sinn can gie glorie bak tae yersel fer ye hae gien him pooer ower aa tha fowk sae he micht gie ayelastin life tae aa thaim ye hae gien him noo this is ayelastin life that the can know you tha yin true god an jesus christ that ye hae sent a hae brocht ye glorie here on irth bi gettin aa tha wark daen ye gien me fer tae dae an noo faither bring me up intae tha glorie a haed wi ye afore tha warl begun a hae made ye known tae thaim that ye gien me oot o this warl the wur yours ye gien thaim tae me an the hae kep yer wurd noo the ken that iveriethin a hae frae your han cums frae you o a truith fer a gien thaim tha wurds ye gien tae me an the tuk thaim tae hairt weel the wut that a cum frae you an the believe that ye sent me a mak a prayer fer thaim am no prayin fer tha warl but fer thaim ye hae gien me fer they belang tae you aa thaimins a hae is yours an aa thaim you hae is mine an glorie is cum tae me throu thaim a wull bide in tha warl nae langr but they ir in tha warl yit an am fer cumin tae you halie faither luk efter thaim bi tha pooer o yer name tha name ye gien me sae the can be yin laik we be yin whaniver a wus wi thaim a lukt efter thaim an kep thaim safe an siccar bi tha name ye gien me nane haes bin loast apairt frae tha yin duimt tae be desthroyt sae as whut wus writ in tha scriptures micht cum aboot am cumin tae ye richt awa but am taakin aboot this jist noo whan am still in tha warl sae as the can hae tha fu meesure o ma joy in thair hairts a hae gien thaim yer wurd an tha warl haes haitit thaim fer ther nae mair o this warl ner a be ma prayer isnae that ye tak thaim oot o tha warl but that ye keep thaim safe frae tha wickit yin ther no o this warl jist laik am no o it set thaim apairt an keep thaim halie bi tha truith your wurd is truith laik ye sent me intae tha warl a hae sent thaim intae tha warl a set masel apairt fer you on thair accoont sae as the can be made perfait halie bi your truith anaa ma prayer isnae jist fer these follaers thairsels a mak a prayer forbye fer aa thaim at wull cum tae believe bi wye o thair message that the wull aa be yin faither jist laik you ir in me an a be in you let thaim be in iz as weel sae that tha warl micht believe that ye hae sent me a hae gien thaim tha glorie that ye gien me sae the can be yin laik we ir yin me in thaim an you in me let thaim be aa yin thegither as a wutness tae tha hale warl that you sent me an loved thaim jist laik you hae loved me faither am lukkin fer thaim that ye gien me tae be wi me whar a am tae be an tae see ma glorie tha glorie ye hae gien me acause ye loved me afore tha warl wus stairtit o faither you that aye daes whuts richt tha mair tha warl daesnae ken ye a ken ye an these follaers o mine ken that ye hae sent me a hae showed ye tae thaim apenlie an wull keep on makkin ye knowed tae thaim sae as tha love ye hae fer me can be in thaim an that a can be in thaim masel whaniver he wus daen prayin jesus tuk his follaers athort tha kidron glen on tha ither side thair wus an olive gairden an him an his follaers went intae it noo judas him that wus fer bethrayin him knowed tha place fer jesus aye cum thegither thonner wi his follaers sae judas cum tae tha gairden at tha heid o a clatter o sodgers an temple gairds sent bi tha heid preeshts an tha pharisees the haed weapons on thaim an the wur houlin bleezin torches an lamps but jesus knowed fine weel whut aa wus fer happenin tae him sae he cum forrit an axt thaim wha ir ye efter jesus o nazareth the reponed a be him qo he an judas tha bethrayer wus stud thonner alang wi thaim whaniver jesus saed a be him the bakt awa an faad tae tha grun yinst mair he axt thaim wha ir ye efter an the saed jesus o nazareth a toul ye that a be him jesus answert if its me yis ir lukkin fer then lea these men alane an let thaim gang noo that aa happent sae as tha wurds he haed spauk wud cum aboot a hinnae loast yin o thaim ye gien me wi that simon peter that haed a sword on him pued it oot an hut tha sarvint o tha heich preesht cuttin aff his richt lug the caad tha sarvint malchus jesus oardert peter pit yer sword awa in its skebbard shud a no drink frae tha bicker tha faither haes gien me an sae tha squad o sodgers wi thair offysher an tha temple gairds o tha jews that wus alang wi thaim tuk houl o jesus the tyed him up an furst o aa brocht him afore annas faitherinlaa tae caiaphas that wus tha heich preesht thon yeir caiaphas wus him that haed toul tha jews afore it wud be guid if yin man wud dee fer tha hale nation simon peter an anither follaer waakt a wyes behin jesus acause thon follaer wus akwant wi tha heich preesht he wus allooed tae gae wi jesus intae tha verie coortyaird o tha heich preesht but peter haed tae houl on ootbye at tha dure tha ither follaer that wus akwant wi tha heich preesht cum bak oot an haed a wee wurd wi tha lass that wus on tha dure an brocht peter in ye wudnae be yin o his follaers wud ye tha sarvin lass on tha dure axt peter he answert na am no thair wus nae heat in tha air an tha sarvints an tha temple gairds wur stud roon this bleeze the haed lit fer tae keep oot tha coul peter wus stud wi thaim forbye wairmin hissel whan aa this wus gaun on tha heich preesht speered jesus aboot his follaers an whut he wus taichin thaim a hae spauk oot in tha apen tae yin an aa jesus reponed a aye taicht in meetin hooses or in tha hoose o god whar aa tha jews cum thegither a saed naethin behin shut dures whut ir ye quizzin me fer ax thaim that heerd me shair they wud ken whut a saed whaniver jesus saed that yin o tha gairds got angrie an he hut him on tha face dinnae taak bak tae tha heich preesht laik that qo he if a hae saed sumthin wrang jesus saed jist tell me whut it wus if a wus tellin tha truith but whut did ye hut me fer still tyed up jesus wus sent bi annas tae caiaphas tha heich preesht noo as simon peter wus stud wairmin hissel the axt him agane you wudnae be yin o thaim follaers o his wud ye peter denied it tae thair face sayin na am naethin o tha soart but yin o tha heich preeshts sarvints a freen o tha man that peter haed cut tha lug aff he pued peter up an saed did a no see ye wi him in tha olive gairden yinst mair peter denied it an at that verie minit a rooster craad an sae tha jews convoyed jesus frae caiaphas tae tha palace o tha roman guviner bi noo it wus earlie in tha moarnin an sae as tae keep thairsels richt an no be sullied tha jews wudnae gang ower tha palace dure the wantit tae be fit tae ait tha passower sae pilate cum oot tae thaim an axt whuts tha chairges brocht agin this man if he wurnae a laa brekker the answert we wudnae a hannit him ower til ye pilate toul thaim tak him yersels an judge him wi yer ain laas but we hae nae richt tae pit oniebodie tae deith tha jews argyid aa this wus saed sae as tha wurds jesus haed spauk aboot hoo he wud dee wud cum tae pass wi that pilate went bak ben tha palace sent fer jesus an axt him ir you tha king o tha jews wud that be a notion o yer ain jesus answert or haes ithers bin taakin til ye aboot me am a a jew pilate reponed it wus yer ain fowk an yer tap preeshts that hannit ye ower til me whut is it ye hae daen ma kingdom qo jesus isnae o this warl if it wus ma gairds wud fecht tae stap me bein liftit an brocht in afore tha jewish heidyins but na ma kingdom isnae frae here sae ye wud be a king then saed pilate jesus answert yer richt eneuch sayin am a king as a metter o fect tha raison a wus boarn an fer why a cum intae tha warl wus tae gie wutness tae tha truith iveriebodie thats on fer tha truith taks tent o whut a say an whut wud tha truith be axt pilate an wi that he went oot agane tae tha jews an toul thaim a can fin nae grun fer a chairge agin him but yis hae a custom tae ax me tae let yin man oot o jail iverie passower dae yis want me tae let oot tha king o tha jews the yellt oot na no him gie iz barabbas noo barabbas wus a rebel that haed tuk pairt in a risin weel pilate tuk jesus awa tae be gien tha whup an tha sodgers plettit thoarns thegither tae mak a croon an the set it on his heid an the put a purple goon on him an the kep cumin up tae him tae jeer at him lang leeve tha king o tha jews an the skelpt him on tha face yinst mair pilate cum oot an toul tha jews luk see am bringin him oot til ye an am tellin yis agane that a can fin nae gruns fer a chairge agin him wi that jesus cum oot wi tha croon o thoarns an tha purple goon on him an pilate saed til thaim luk this is tha man tha minit tha heid preeshts an tha temple gairds saa him the shoutit oot crucyfie him crucyfie him but pilate answert weel yous can crucyfie him yersels fer a can fin nae gruns fer a chairge agin him tha jews wudnae budge we hae a laa an owin til thon laa he maun dee fer he ledged he wus tha sinn o god whaniver pilate heerd that he wus aa tha mair feart an he tuk hissel bak intae tha palace whar dae ye cum frae he axt jesus but jesus niver saed a wurd ir you refusin tae taak tae me qo pilate dae ye no unnerstan a hae tha pooer tae let ye oot or tae nail ye up on a cross jesus reponed ye wud hae nae pooer ower me nane ava if it wusnae gien til ye frae abain on accoont o that tha yin that hannit me ower tae ye is guiltie o a bigger sin frae then on pilate ettled at lettin jesus gang free but tha jews kep shoutin if ye let this man oot yer nae freen o caesars oniebodie that maks hissel oot tae be a king maun be agin caesar whaniver pilate heerd that he brocht jesus oot an sut doon on tha judges sait at a place caad tha stane fitpad in tha aramaic tung it gets gabbatha noo it wus tha day fer makkin readie fer tha passower sennicht aboot heich nuin luk heres yer king pilate saed tae tha jews but the shoutit awa wi him tak him awa crucyfie him wull a crucyfie yer king pilate axt thaim we hae nae king but caesar tha heid preeshts answert at tha enn o it aa pilate hannit him ower tae thaim fer tae be crucyfied sae jesus wus taen awa shooderin his ain cross jesus went oot tae tha place o tha skull thon place the caa golgotha in tha aramaic tung thonner the crucyfied him alang wi twa ithers yin on tha yin side an yin on tha tither wi jesus in tha middle pilate got a wee sign made an put it up on tha cross wi this writ on it jesus o nazareth tha king o tha jews monie o tha jews haed a read o thon sign fer tha place whar jesus wus crucyfied wus nearhan tha citie an tha sign wus writ in tha hebrew tha latin an tha greek tha heid preeshts o tha jews wurnae plaised an the kep on at pilate sayin dinnae jist pit tha king o tha jews on it but pit this man saed he wus the king o tha jews pilate answert whut a hae writ a hae writ whaniver tha sodgers nailt jesus on tha cross the tuk his claes an divid thaim in fower pairts yin apiece fer each o thaim wi onlie his goon left his goon wus jist tha yin bit o claith wove frae tap tae bottom wi nae seams in it we shudnae teer it up the saed cum on an well clod dice fer it an see wha gets it aa that happent sae as tha scripture wud cum aboot whar it wus writ the divid ma dishables amang thaim an the clod dice fer ma claes sae that wus whut tha sodgers daen jesuss mither an his mithers sister an mary tha guidwife o clopas an mary magdalene wur aa stud nixt tha cross that jesus wus on whaniver jesus catched sicht o his mither thonner an tha follaer that he loved nearhan he toul his mither guid wumman thons yer sinn thonner an tae tha follaer he saed an thons yer mither frae that day an oor that follaer tuk hir intae his ain hame efter this knowin in hissel that iveriethin wus noo feenished an sae as whut wus writ in tha scriptures micht cum aboot jesus saed a hae a druith on me a crock o soor wine wus thair sae the wat a spongefu put tha sponge on a staak o hyssop an raxt it up tae jesuss mooth whaniver he got tha drink jesus saed its feenished wi that he bood his heid an he gien up his spirit noo it wus tha day o makkin readie fer tha passower an tha nixt day bein a big speeshel sabbath day forbye tha jews wur no wantin tha bodies tae bide on tha crosses on tha sabbath an sae the axt pilate tae hae tha legs brauk an tha bodies tuk doon becas o that tha sodgers cum an brauk tha legs o tha furst man that wus crucyfied alang wi jesus an then tha same thing wi tha tither but whaniver the cum tae jesus an fun oot he wus aareadie deid the didnae brek his legs insteed o that yin o tha sodgers pusht a pike intae jesuss side an that brocht oot a flush o bluid an watter tha man that saa that happen haes gien wutness o it an his is a true wutness he kens that he tells tha truith an he gies wutness sae as you micht believe forbye aa this happent sae as whut wus writ in scripture wud cum aboot nane o his banes wull be brauk an as anither pairt o scripture says the wull luk on tha yin the hae pierced efter aa thae things a man caad joseph o arimathea axt pilate if he cud hae tha bodie o jesus noo joseph wus a follaer but he kep it a saicret fer fear o tha jews pilate gien him laive an he cum an tuk tha bodie awa an alang wi joseph wus nicodemus him that haed cum afore tae jesus bi nicht nicodemus brocht wi him a mix o myrrh an aloes aboot seiventiefive pun wecht takkin jesuss bodie tha twa o thaim lapt it in strips o linen claith thegither wi tha spices this wus tha ritual tha jews aye daen whan the buriet fowk thonner whar jesus wus crucyfied thair wus a gairden an in tha gairden thair wus a new tomb that haed niver bin uised sae seein it wus tha jews reddinup day fer tha passower an seein as tha tomb wus nearhan the haed jesus layed oot thonner in tha smaa oors o tha furst day o tha week whan thair wus nae licht yit mary magdalene cum tae tha tomb an saa that tha stane haed bin taen awa frae tha apenin sae she run bak tae simon peter an tha ither follaer tha yin jesus loved an she saed the hae taen tha loard oot o tha tomb an we dinnae ken whar the hae put him sae peter an tha ither follaer heidit aff fer tha tomb tha baith o thaim wus rinnin but tha ither follaer run mair quick ner peter an got tae tha tomb furst he stoopit doon an keekt in at tha linen claiths lyin thair but he didnae gan inbye then simon peter that wus behin him got thair an went strecht intae tha tomb he saa tha strips o linen lyin thonner forbye tha buryin cloot that haed bin roon jesuss heid but tha cloot wus lapt up bi itsel awa frae tha linen sae noo tha ither follaer that haed got tae tha tomb furst went inside tae he saa iveriethin an he believed the didnae unnerstan yit frae tha halie scriptures that jesus wud hae tae rise frae tha deid wi that tha follaers went bak tae thair hames but mary stud ootbye tha tomb greetin an whan she wus greetin she stoopit doon fer tae tak a luk inside tha tomb an she saa twa angels in white claes sut whar jesuss bodie haed bin yin at tha heid an tha tither at tha fit the axt hir wumman whut ir ye greetin fer the hae taen ma loard awa qo she an a dinnae ken whar the hae put him sayin that she turnt roon an saa jesus stud thonner but she didnae twig that it wus jesus wumman qo he whut ir ye greetin fer wha is it yer lukkin she thocht it wus tha gairdner an she saed sir if ye hae cairriet him awa tell iz whar ye hae put him an all get him jesus saed til hir mary she turnt roon tae him an caad oot rabboni that mains dominie in tha aramaic jesus saed dinnae be hingin ontae me noo fer am no yit gan bak tae tha faither but gang tae ma brithers an tell thaim this frae me am fer gaun bak tae ma faither an tae your faither tae ma god an tae your god mary magdalene went tae fin tha follaers an tell thaim tha guid news a hae saa tha loard an she toul thaim whut he haed saed til hir whaniver it wus dairk got on thon furst day o tha week tha follaers wur thegither behin lockt dures fer fear o tha jews an jesus cum an stud amang thaim peace be wi yis qo he an efter sayin this he showed thaim his hans an his side tha follaers wus fu o joy whaniver the saa tha loard agane jesus saed peace be wi yis jist as tha faither haes sent me am sennin yous as weel an wi that he breathed ower thaim an he saed tak tha halie spirit tae yersels if ye forgie oniebodie thair sins thell be forgien if ye dinnae forgie thaim ther no forgien noo tammas that the caad didymus yin o tha twal wusnae alang wi tha ither follaers whaniver jesus cum sae tha ither follaers toul him we hae saa tha loard but he saed til thaim less a behoul tha mairks o tha nails in his hans an pit ma fingr whar tha nails wus an less a pit ma han intae his side all niver believe it a sennicht later tha follaers wus in tha hoose agane an this time tammas wus wi thaim tha mair tha dures wus lockt jesus cum an stud amang thaim an saed peace be wi yis an then he saed tae tammas pit yer fingr here hae a luk at ma hans rax oot yer han an pit it intae ma side an quit yer dootin an believe tammas saed til him ma loard an ma god jesus telt him acause ye hae saa me ye hae believed weel fer thaim that haesnae saa but haes believed aa tha same noo jesus wrocht a hale wheen o ither miraclis signs in front o his follaers thats no bin recoardit in this here buik but these yins ir put doon sae yis can lippen that jesus is tha christ tha sinn o god an that bi believin ye can hae life throu him later on jesus appeart agane tae his follaers this time on tha loch shore o tiberias heres hoo it happent simon peter tammas caad didymus tha twun nathaniel frae cana in galilee an tha sinns o zebedee wur aa thegither thonner wi twa ither follaers am awa oot tae ketch some fish simon peter toul thaim an the saed well gang alang wi ye sae oot the went an got intae tha boat but the niver catched ocht ava tha hale nicht in tha smaa oors o tha moarnin jesus wus stud on tha shore but tha follaers didnae ken it wus him jesus caad oot tae thaim freens hae yis no catched onie fish na the reponed pit yer neyt oot qo he on tha richthan side o tha boat an yisll fin some whaniver the did the wurnae fit tae pu in tha neyt thair wus that monie fish in it an then tha follaer that jesus loved saed tae peter its tha loard sae it is tha minit simon peter heerd him say its tha loard he lapt his ooter claes roon hissel fer he haed taen thaim aff fer fishin an he lep intae tha watter tha ither follaers cum alang behin him in tha boat puin tha neyt fu o fish fer the wurnae faur frae shore nae mair ner a hunner yairds whaniver the lannit the saa a fire o bleezin coals thonner wi fish on it an some breid jesus saed til thaim bring some o thaim fish ye hae jist catched simon peter climmed aboord an dregged tha neyt tae tha shore it wus fu o big fish a hunner an fiftiethrie o thaim but tha mair it haed sae monie it wusnae tore jesus saed tae thaim cum on an hae yer brekfast nane o tha follaers dar ax him wha ir ye the knowed it wus tha loard jesus cum tuk tha breid an gien it tae thaim an he daen tha same wi tha fish noo this wus tha thurd time jesus haed appeart tae his follaers efter he wus ris frae tha deid whaniver the wur daen aitin jesus saed tae simon peter simon sinn o jhone dae ye love me mair ner aa these ither yins dae ay loard qo he ye ken that a love ye jesus saed luk efter ma lambs agane jesus saed simon sinn o jhone dae ye love me he answert ay loard ye ken that a love ye jesus saed tak guid care o ma sheep tha thurd time he saed til him simon sinn o jhone dae ye love me peter wus hurt that jesus axt him tha thrie times dae ye love me he saed loard ye ken iveriethin ye ken that a love ye jesus saed luk efter ma sheep noo heres tha truith o it whan ye wur a young yin ye put yer ain claes on bi yersel an ye went whariver ye wantit but whaniver yer oul got yell rax oot yer hans an some ither bodie wull pit yer claes on ye an tak ye whar ye dinnae want tae gang jesus saed that fer tae point oot tha wye peter wud dee an hoo he wud bring glorie tae god an then he saed til him follae me peter lukt ower his shooder an saa tha follaer that jesus loved cumin efter thaim tha yin that haed leant bak agin jesus at tha supper an axt loard whas gaun tae bethray ye whaniver peter saa that follaer he axt loard whut aboot him jesus answert if a want him tae leeve richt up tae tha day a cum bak whuts it tae dae wi you jist you follae me on accoont o this tha taak went roon tha brithers that this follaer wudnae dee but jesus niver saed that he wudnae dee he jist saed if a want him tae leeve richt up tae tha day a cum bak whuts it tae dae wi you thon follaer is tha yin that gies wutness tae aa these things an writ thaim doon we can be shair his testimonie is true jesus daen monie ither things forbye if iverie yin o thaim wus writ doon a jalouse that even tha hale warl wudnae hae ruim eneuch fer aa tha buiks that wud be scrievit
